varYatciyE Ayvu ceVyya munYnYAlY muwalvar eVtiyUrappA curYrYuppayaNam - 
mAnilawwil varYatciyE Ayvu ceVyya munYnYAlY muwalvar eVtiyUrappA puwanYkilYYamE ( ep . 27 ) muwal curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVlYkirYAr . 
munYnYAlY muwalvar eVtiyUrappA aNmEyil mAnila pAjaka walEvarAka pawavi erYrYAr . 
appowu mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavuvawAl , mAnilam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu varYatci kurYiwwu Ayvu ceVywu arYikkE alYikka ulYlYawAka weVriviwwAr . 
awanYpati puwanYkilYYamE muwal 5 nAtkalYukku mAnilawwinY pIwar , kalapurki , yAwakiri , pijAppUr , mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu , varYatciyE Ayvu ceVywu , makkalYitam kurYEkalYE kettarYinwu , awu woVtarpAnYa arYikkEyE wAkkal ceVyya ulYlYAr . cAwanYEkalYE coVlli ottu kettAr kokula inwirA 
ceVnYnYE , 
ep . 22 – 
aNNAnakar woVkuwiyil ceVywa cAwanYEkalYE coVlli aNNAnakar woVkuwi vetpAlYarum amEccarumAnYa eVs.kokula inwirA ottu kettAr . 
aNNAnakar woVkuwikku nirYEverYrYiya wittafkalYE coVlliyum makkalYitam Awaravu kettu varukirYAr . 
winYamum kAlEyilum , mAlEyilum vItu vItAka ceVnYrYu ottu kettu varukirYAr . 
ceVllum itameVllAm makkalY makilYYcciyutanY varaverYrYu Arawwi eVtukkirYArkalY . 
AfkAfke cAwanYE vilYakka poVwukkUttafkalYum natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
2 winYafkalYukku munYpu ti.pi.cawwirawwil mApeVrum werwal piraccAra poVwukkUttam natanwawu . 
inwa kUttawwil natikar rAmarAjanY pecinYAr . 
pallAyirakkaNakkil wiraNtirunwa makkalY mawwiyil jeVyalaliwA Atciyil ceVywa cAwanYEkalYE anwa pakuwiyil ceVywa cAwanYEkalYE eVs.kokula inwirA pattiyal kAtti Awaravu kettAr . 
iwanYE atuwwu marYunAlY eVm.eVm.ti.e. kAlanYiyil natanwa piramANta werwal piraccAra kUttawwil natikE vinwiyA pecinYAr . 
ifkum pallAyirakkaNakkil makkalY vanwirunwanYar . 
ifkum anwa pakuwiyil ceVywa cAwanYEkalYE coVlli Awaravu kettAr . 
iwanYE atuwwu amEnwakarE peVrumAlYkoyil pakuwiyil natanwa piraccAra poVwukkUttawwil aNNAnakar cattamanYrYa woVkuwi veVrYrYi vetpAlYarum kalYYaka makalYir aNi ceVyalAlYarum amEccarumAnYa eVs.kokula inwirA , natcawwira peccAlYar cifkamuwwu Akiyor jeVyalaliwAvinY poVrYkAla AtciyinY cAwanYEkalYE kUrYi aNNA.wi.mu.ka.vE peVruvAriyAnYa vAkku viwwiyAcawwil veVrYrYi peVrYac ceVyya kettuk koVNtAr . 
kutinIr piraccanYE , cAlE vacawikalY , minYparYrYAkkurYE marYrYum pala piraccinYEkalY ammAvinY poVrYkAla Atciyil cIrceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
wi.mu.ka. Atciyil purYakkaNikkappatta wittafkalY aNNA.wi.mu.ka. Atciyil poVwumakkalY kitEkkap peVrYrYu payanYatEnwu varukinYrYanYar . 
mINtum ammAvinY nallAtci woVtara irattE ilEkku vAkkalYiyufkalY eVnYrYu eVs.kokula inwirA kettuk koVNtAr .

niyUsilAnwukku eVwirAka vafkawecam patuwolvi - 
wi inwu . 
koVlkawwAvil natEpeVrYrYa ulakakkoppE ti20 pottiyil vafkawecawwE , niyUsilAnwu aNi 75 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil vIlYYwwi UwiwwalYlYiyawu . 
tAs veVnYrYa niyUsilAnwu aNi muwalil pet ceVywawu , kapwil inwap pottiyil illE . 
niyUsilAnwu aNiyE vafkawecam 145 ranYkalYukku mattuppatuwwiyawu , woVtarnwu Atiya vafkawecam 15.4 ovarkalYil 70 ranYkalYukkuc curuNtawu . 
vafkaweca aNiyil itawu kE vekappanwu vIccAlYar muswapicur rahmAnY 4 ovarkalYil 22 ranYkalYE mattume koVtuwwu 5 vikkeVttukalYEk kEpparYrYinYAr . 
niyUsilAnwu aNiyil mINtum E.eVs.cowi 3.4 ovarkalY vIci 21 ranYkalYukku 3 vikkeVttukalYEc cAykka , kirANt eVliyat 4 ovarkalYil 12 ranYkalYukku 3 vikkeVttukalYEk kEpparYrYinYAr . 
inwa veVrYrYi mUlam kurUp pirivu Attawwil niyUsilAnwu anYEwwu pottikalYilum veVnYrYulYlYawu . 
mikavum varYaNta pitcil , woVtakkawwil kenY villiyamnYcanY 32 panwukalYil 42 ranYkalY eVnYrYa valuvAnYa woVtakkawwE koVtuwwAr . 
muswapicur rahmAnY wanYawu muwal ovaril heVnYrYi nikolsE ( 7 ) pavultu ceVywAr . 
42 ranYkalY eVtuwwa villiyamcanY awil 5 pavuNtarikalY 1 cikcar atiwwu muswapicur rahmAnYitam pavultu AnYAr . 
kirANt eVliyat 9 ranYkalYil cuvAkawa hom pitiwwa arumEyAnYa ketcinY mUlam muswapicur 3-vawu vikkeVttEk kEpparYrYinYAr . 
pirYaku katEci ovaril mitceVl cANtnYar , newanY meVkkallam AkiyorE atuwwatuwwa panwukalYil pavultu ceVywAr muswapicur rahmAnY , mikavum nerwwiyAnYa , wulliyamAnYa , kattukkoppAnYa panwu vIccu muswapicur rahmAnYutEyawu . 
koVlinY manYro wanYawu AkroRawwEk kattuppatuwwik koVNtu natu ovarkalYil Ati 1 pavuNtari 2 cikcarutanY 33 panwukalYil 35 ranYkalY eVtuwwu al aminY hucEnY panwil pavultu AnYAr . 
rAs teVylar 24 panwukalYil 2 pavuNtari 1 cikcarutanY 28 ranYkalY eVtuwwu al aminY hucEnYitam AttamilYYanwAr . 
AnYAl manYro , teVylar kUttaNi 42 ranYkalYE 4-vawu vikkeVttukkAkac cerwwanYar . 
kori ANtarcanY ranY eVtukkAmal maRrape mortacAvinY vekam kurYEvAnYa panwil mattEyil pattu pavultu AnYAr . 
katEci ovaril muswapicur 2 vikkeVttukalYE atuwwatuwwu vIlYYwwa hetrik panwE meVklinYAkanY ciks atikka niyUsilAnwu oVru valYYiyAka 145 ranYkalYE eVttiyawu . 
AnYAl iwil 8 vikkeVttukalYEp parYikoVtuwwawu . 
awAvawu 14.5 ovarkalYil 99 / 2 eVnYrYu irunwa niyUsilAnwu katEci 6 vikkeVttukalYE 46 ranYkalYukku ilYYanwawu . 
vafkawecawwinY mocamAnYa pettif : 
3 pottikalYil wolviyatEnwu woVyvAnYa manYanilEyutanY kalYamirYafkiya vafkawecam 2-vawu ovarinY katEci panwil wamim ikpAlE ( 3 ) ranY avut mUlam ilYYanwawu . 
moVkamawu miwunY RArt wert menY wicEyil watti vittu oVru ranYnYukkAka purYappata carYrYe wayafki ota woVtafkinYAr wamim AnYAl manYrovinY wro nerAka stampE wAkka ranY avut AnYAr . 
awanY pirYaku miwunY ( 11 ) , capIr rahmAnY ( 12 ) Akiyor vafkaweca inYnYifsinY awikkpatca joti ranYkalYAka 25 ranYkalYEc cerwwanYar . 
iwil cANtnYar ovaril miwunY , capIr rahmAnY walA oVru pavuNtariyE atiwwanYar . 
innilEyil meVklinYAkanY panwE oVwufkik koVNtu Ata ninYEwwAr miwunY , ravuNt wa vikkeVttil vIciya meVklinYAkanY avarE pavultu ceVywAr . 
niwAnYam kAtta veNtiya nerawwil RAkip al hacanY ( 2 ) , cANtnYar panwE lAf AnYil wUkki atiwwu meVkkallamitam ketc koVtuwwAr . 
capIr rahmAnY pettirYku cariyAka varAwa newanY meVkkallam panwE wUkki atiwwu cANtnYarinY nalla ketcukku veVlYiyerYinYAr . 
cavumiyA carkkAr 6 ranYkalYil leVkspinYnYar cowiyitam stamp ovttu AnYAr . 
muRpikur rahim ranY eVtukkAmal kirANt eVliyat panwil pavultu AnYAr . 
iwu oVru arumEyAnYa leVk kattar . 
mahmuwullAvukku cowi arumEyAnYa kUklYiyE vIci avarawu mattEkkum kAlkAppirYkum itEye pukunwa panwu stampE woVnwaravu ceVywawu . 
48 / 7 eVnYrYa nilEyil vafkawecawwinY awikapatca skorAka cuvAkawa hom 16 ranYkalY eVtuwwAr . 
muswapicur rahmAnY 1 cikcar atiwwAr . 
15.4 ovarkalYil 70 ranYkalYukkuc curuNtu ulakakkoppE ti20 kirikkeVttil emArYrYawwutanY veVlYiyerYiyawu vafkawecam . 
Atta nAyakanYAka kenY villiyamcanY wervu ceVyyappattAr . 
waskinY akamawu , arApaw canYnYi pottiw woVtarinY itEyil watE ceVyyappattawil anwa aNi manYawalYavil veVrYuppatEnwulYlYawE inwaw wolvi kAttukirYawu . ceVnYnYE , 
varum nAtkalYil puyal eVwuvum illE eVnYrYum , weVrYku AnwirA vafkakkatalil nilEk koVNtu ulYlYa kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwi kAraNamAka , wamilYYakam marYrYum puwucceriyil anYeka itafkalYil inYrYu ( viyAlYYakkilYYamE ) malYYE peVyyum eVnYrYum vAnYilE Ayvu mEyam weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvupakuwi vatakilYYakku paruvamalYYE kAlamAnYa warYpowu wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum paravalAka nalla malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
inwa mAwam woVtakkawwilirunwu vafkakkatal pakuwiyil nilaviya kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu maNtalam , wAlYYvu pakuwi kAraNamAka wamilYYakawwinY vata katalora mAvattafkalY marYrYum palverYu itafkalYil kanYamalYYE peVywawu . 
katanwa iru winYafkalYAka malYYE alYavu kurYEnwulYlYawu . 
inwa nilEyil , weVrYku AnwirA vafkakkatal marYrYum awanYE oVttiyulYlYa pakuwiyil katanwa 16-nwewi ( wifkatkilYYamE ) kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwi uruvAnYawu . 
inwa kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwi , wIvira kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwiyAka nerYrYu munYwinYam ( ceVvvAykkilYYamE ) mArYiyawu . 
iwanYAl wamilYYakawwil oVru cila itafkalYil malYYE peVywulYlYawu . 
warYpowu anwa wIvira kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwi valukurYEnwu , awe pakuwiyil kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwiyAka nItikkirYawu eVnYrYum , iwanY kAraNamAka , wamilYYakawwil anYeka itafkalYil malYYE peVyyum eVnYrYum vAnYilE Ayvu mEyam weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
anYeka itafkalYil malYYE peVyyum 
iwu woVtarpAka ceVnYnYE vAnYilE Ayvu mEya iyakkunYar eVs.Ar.ramaNanY nerYrYu niruparkalYitam kUrYiyawAvawu : 
weVrYku AnwirA vafkakkatal marYrYum awanYE oVttiyulYlYa pakuwiyil nerYrYu ( nerYrYu munYwinYam ) nilEkoVNtirunwa wIvira kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwi , valu kurYEnwu , kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu pakuwiyAka mArYi awe pakuwiyil nItikkirYawu . 
melum , wamilYYnAttinY ulYmAvattafkalYil oVru melatukku culYYarYci nilEk koVNtu ulYlYawu . 
inwa kAraNafkalYAl , atuwwa 24 maNi nerawwil ( inYrYu ) , wamilYYakam marYrYum puwucceriyil anYeka itafkalYilum , oriru itafkalYil kanYamalYYEyum peVyyum . 
kurYippAka viruwunakar , kovE , nIlakiri ulYpata ulYmAvattafkalYil kanYamalYYE iruppawarYkAnYa vAyppu irukkirYawu . 
ceVnYnYEyE poVrYuwwavarEyil , vAnYam lecAnYa mekamUttawwutanY kANappatum . 
nakarinY cila itafkalYil malYYE peVyya vAyppu ulYlYawu . 
puyalukku vAyppu illE 
puyal ponYrYa nikalYYvukalY eVwuvum varum nAtkalYil illE . 
appatiye irunwAlum , awu nilanatukka kottukku arukil inwiya peVrufkatal pakuwiyil wAnY nilavum . 
nerYrYu kAlE 8.30 maNiyutanY mutivatEnwa 24 maNi nerawwil peVywa malYYE alYavu varumArYu : 
civakAci 10 ceV.mI. , viruwunakar 9 ceV.mI. , rAjapAlYEyam 8 ceV.mI. , kovilafkulYam , wirumayam , wirumafkalam , iluppUr , woVNti , ilYEyAfkuti , cUrafkuti Akiya itafkalYil walA 6 ceV.mI. , aruppukkottE , marufkapuri , kalYYukumalE , cAwwUr Akiya itafkalYil walA 5 ceV.mI. , cittAmpatti , vAtippatti , katalAti , melUr , paramakkuti Akiya itafkalYil walA 4 ceV.mI. malYYE peVywulYlYawu . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . wiruppUril kEparYrYappatta paNam vafki parimArYrYawwirYku koVNtu ceVllappattawe - rAjeR lakkAnYi 
ceVnYnYE 
wamilYYaka walEmE werwal awikAri rAjeR lakkAnYi wiruppUril kEparYrYappatta paNam vafki parimArYrYawwirYku koVNtu ceVllappattawe eVnYa kUrYi ulYlYAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu melum avar kUrYiyawAvawu : - 
wamilYYakawwil nerYrYu varE rU. 102 koti paNam parYimuwal ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
katanwa 3 nAtkalYil mattum paNam pattuvAtA ceVywawAka 101 per mIwu valYYakkup pawivu ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
pUw cilip kitEkkAwavarkalY 11 AvaNafkalYil oVnYrYE payanYapatuwwalAm , woVkuwikku campanwam illAwavarkalY mAlE 6 maNikkulY veVlYiyerYa veNtum . 
vAkkucAvati parYrYi vivaram arYiya 1950 eVnYrYa eVNNukku eVs.eVm.eVs anYuppa veNtum eVnYa kUrYi ulYlYAr . ulaka ceVs cAmpiyanYRip potti : 
meknYas kArlcanYutanY mowukirYAr karjAkinY - 
vAyppE ilYYanwAr AnYanw - 
wi inwu 
mAskovil natEpeVrYrYa keNti tets ceVs pottiyil raRiyAvinY ceVrji karjAkinY 8.5 pulYlYikalYutanY cAmpiyanY pattam veVnYrYAr . 
iwanY mUlam varum navampar mAwam niyUyArk nakaril natEpeVrYavulYlYa ulaka ceVs cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil natappu cAmpiyanYAnYa meknYas kArlcanYE eVwirwwu vilYEyAta wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYAr ceVrji karjAkinY . 
katEcic curYrYil karjAkinYitam wolvi kaNta ameVrikkAvinY karuNA marYrYum katEcic curYrYil tirA ceVywa inwiyAvinY visvanAwanY AnYanw Akiyor walA 7.5 pulYlYikalYutanY 2-vawu itawwEp pitiwwanYar . 
5 murYE ulaka cAmpiyanY pattam veVnYrYa visvanAwanY AnYanw , katanwa 10 ANtukalYil muwalmurYEyAka ulaka ceVs cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil vilYEyAtum vAyppE ilYYanwulYlYAr . 
2016 ulaka ceVs cAmpiyanYRip potti , ameVrikkAvinY niyUyArkkil natEpeVrYa ulYlYawu . 
navampar 11 muwal 30-m wewi varE natEpeVrYa ulYlYa inwap potti , moVwwam 12 curYrYukalYEk koVNtawAkum . 
iwil 6.5 pulYlYikalYE eVttum vIrar cAmpiyanY pattam veVlvAr . karnAtakawwil varYatci nivAraNam valYYafkuvawil murYEketu - 
karnAtakawwil varYatci nivAraNam valYYafkuvawil murYEketu natEpeVrYrYiruppawAka anwa mAnila munYnYAlY muwalvar kumAracAmi kurYrYamcAttiyulYlYAr . 
civamoVkkA mAvattawwil veVlYlYikkilYYamE natEpeVrYrYa koyil wiruvilYYAvil kalanwu koVlYvawarYku munYnYawAka ceVywiyAlYarkalYitam avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYE merYkoVlYvawil aracu wolvi atEnwulYlYawu . 
varYatciyAl vivacAyikalY katumEyAkap pAwikkappattulYlYanYar . 
AnYAl , avarkalYukku valYYafkappatum nivAraNa niwiyil murYEketu natEpeVrYrYulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl pAwikkappatta pala vivacAyikalYukku uriya nivAraNam kitEkkavillE . 
iwarYkitEye varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta mAvattafkalYE Ayvu ceVyya muwalvar ciwwarAmEyA ceVnYrYulYlYAr . 
varYatci mAvattafkalYEp pArvEyituvawil muwalvarukku ArvamillE . 
AnYAl , verYu valYYiyillAmal avar varYatci mAvattafkalYukkuc ceVnYrYulYlYAr . 
nAlY oVnYrYukku 2 mAvattafkalYukkuc ceVlvawAka UtakafkalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . 
varYatci mAvattafkalYil ulYlYa ewenYum or arafkawwil amarnwu koVNtu awikArikalY warum wakavalkalYE muwalvar peVrYrYu varukirYAr . 
iwanYAl , varYatciyAl erYpattulYlYa pAwippukalY kurYiwwu avarukku uriya wakavalkalY kitEkkAwu . 
eVnYave , mAvattam mulYYuvawum payaNam ceVywu Ayvu ceVyya veNtum . 
iwanY mUlam uNmE nilEmEyE avar weVrinwu koVlYlYa mutiyum . 
varYatci nivAraNap paNiyil mAnila aracutanY , mawwiya aracu iNEnwu paNiyArYrYa veNtum . 
katanwa mAwam payir ilYYappIttirYku mawwiya aracu valYYafkiya , rU. 1500 koti mAvatta AtciyarkalY mUlamAka pAwikkappatta vivacAyikalYukku valYYafkappattawu . 
iwilum itEwwarakarkalYinY walEyItu irunwawAka vivacAyikalY kurYrYam cAttiyulYlYanYar . 
varYatciyAl karnAtakawwil AyirawwirYkum awikamAnYa vivacAyikalY warYkoVlE ceVywu koVNtulYlYawAka munYnYAlY muwalvar eVtiyUrappA weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
aNtE mAnilamAnYa makArARtirawwil pAjaka Atciyil 2 AyirawwirYkum awikamAnYa vivacAyikalY warYkoVlE ceVywu koVNtulYlYanYar . 
afku eVnYnYa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYawu eVnYpawE eVtiyUrappA vilYakka veNtum eVnYrYAr . poVnYnYEyanYE Awariwwu cEwAppettEyil natikar manYopAlA piraccAram 
ceVnYnYE , ep . 22 – 
ceVnYnYE cEwAppettE woVkuwiyil pottiyitum aNNA.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar poVnYnYEyanYE Awariwwu natikar manYopAlA vIwivIwiyAka ceVnYrYu piraccAram ceVywAr . 
ceVnYrYa itameVllAm makkalY urYcAka varaverYpu alYiwwanYar . 
cEwAppettE woVkuwiyil poVnYnYEyanY vIwivIwiyAkavum , vItu vItAkavum ceVnYrYu irattE ilEkku Awaravu wiratti varukirYAr . 
jeVyalaliwA Atci cAwanYEkalYE makkalYitam pattiyal pottu kAtti Awaravu wiratti varukirYAr . 
ceVllum itameVllAm makkalY urYcAkawwutanYum eVlYYucciyutanYum varaverYrYu Arawwi eVtuwwu veVrYrYi wilakamitukirYArkalY . 
nerYrYu mAlE 171–vawu vArtu mAmanYrYa urYuppinYarum cukAwAra nilEkkulYYu walEvarumAnYa A.palYYanYi , 171–vawu kilYYakku vattawwirYku utpatta palverYu pakuwikalYil vAkku cekarikka erYpAtu ceVywirunwAr . 
cEwAppettE pAlawwilirunwu wirYanwa jIppil vetpAlYar poVnYnYEyanY , natikar manYopAlA , ji.ceVnwamilYYanY eVm.eVl.e , meyar cEwE wurEcAmi , tAktar jeVyavarwwanY eVm.pi , pakuwi ceVyalAlYar eVnY.eVs.mAkanY utpata palar ceVnYrYArkalY . 
ArokkiyamAwA 1–vawu weVru , 2–vawu weVru , wAmas nakar , kallarYE cAlE , srInakar kAlanYi , rafkarAjapuram 1 muwal 6–vawu weVru varE , veVfkatApuram , velYacceri cAlE , wAtaNtanY nakar aracu UlYYiyar kutiyiruppukalY , aracu paNNE , jowiyammAlY nakar Akiya pakuwikalYil vIwivIwiyAka ceVnYrYu Awaravu wirattinYArkalY . 
erAlYamAnYa aNNA.wi.mu.ka. woVNtarkalY koVtikalYE pitiwwu koVNtum irattE ilEyE kEyil enwiyapatiyum irattE ilEkku vAkkalYiyufkalY eVnYrYu koRam eVlYYuppiyavArYu ceVnYrYArkalY . 
ammAvinY nallAtci woVtara , nAtu ceVlYYikka , makkalY valYamutanY , makilYYcciyutanY vAlYYa irattE ilEkku vAkkalYiyufkalY eVnYrYu manYopAlA kettuk koVNtAr . 
ceVnYrYa itameVllAm makkalY vIttE vittu veVlYiye vanwu irattE viralE kAtti irattE ilEkke eVfkalY ottu eVnYrYu urYuwi kUrYinYArkalY . 
cukAwAra nilEkkulYYu walEvar A.palYYanYi erYpAtu ceVywa inwa ottu cekarippil woVkuwi ceVyalAlYar manYokar , cEwE eVm.eVm.pApu , eVnY.ke.vawcalA , e.comacafkaranY , vatta ceVyalAlYar por eVm.ravi , peravE FAnYamuwwu , cEwE ji.cArawi , poVwukkulYYu urYuppinYar cEwE ci.eVm.cAmi , Rek apwullA , kapIr , kort e.panYnYIr , cinYnYamalE wAs , paramacivam , cEwE uwayakumAr , arYivalYYakanY , colE arulYpirakAR utpata erAlYamAnYa per ceVnYrYArkalY . ti20 makalYir ulakak koppE : 
irYuwippottiyil Aswireliya aNi - 
wi inwu 
makalYir ti20 ulakak koppE arEyirYuwi Attawwil ifkilAnwu aNiyE 5 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil worYkatiwwu Asreliya aNi irYuwippottikku munYnYerYiyawu . 
teVlli peVroRA kotlA mEwAnYawwil natEpeVrYrYa inwa Attawwil muwalil pet ceVywa Aswireliya aNi 20 ovarkalY mutivil 6 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 132 ranYkalY eVtuwwawu . 
lenYif 50 panwil , 6 pavuNtarikalYutanY 55 ranY vilYAcinYAr . 
alissA hIli 25 , villAnYi 19 ranYkalY eVtuwwanYar . 
ifkilAnwu warappil natAli 2 vikkeVt kEpparYrYinYAr . 
133 ranYkalY ilakkutanY ifkilAnwu aNi vilYEyAtiyawu . 
keptanY cArlat eVtvarts , tAmi pi amavunYt joti cirYappAnYa woVtakkam koVtuwwawu . 
cArlat 29 panwukalYil 31 ranYnYum , tAmi 40 panwukalYil 32 ranYnYum eVtuwwu AttamilYYanwanYar . 
atuwwu vanwa natAli 0 , nEt 1 ranYkalYil veVlYiyerYinYar . 
katEci 3 ovarkalYil 31 ranYkalY eVtuwwAl veVrYrYi nilEyil natcawwira vIrAfkanYEyAnYa cArA teVylar 21 ranYkalYil AttamilYYanwAr . 
iwEw woVtarnwu vanwa purunYt 11 , hanY 1 ranYkalYil veVlYiyerYa 20 ovarkalY mutivil ifkilAnwu aNi 7 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 127 ranYkalY mattume eVtuwwawu . 
AswireliyA warappil mekanY 2 vikkeVt vIlYYwwinYAr . 
Atta nAyakiyAka lenYif wervAnYAr . 
5 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil veVrYrYi peVrYrYa natappu cAmpiyanYAnYa Aswireliya aNi 4-vawu murYEyAka irYuwippottikku munYnYerYiyawu . vitAwu peVyyum kanYamalYYEyAl ceVnYnYE veVlYlYawwil miwakkirYawu 
ceVnYnYE , 
itEvitAwu peVyyum kanYamalYYEyAl ceVnYnYE veVlYlYawwil miwakkirYawu . 
iwanYAl poVwumakkalYinY iyalpu vAlYYkkEyil pAwippu erYpattulYlYawu . 
vafkakkatalil anwamAnY aruke uruvAnYa kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu nilE merYku nokki nakarnwu , weVnYmerYku vafkakkatalil nilEkoVNtiruppawAl nerYrYu iravu muwal ceVnYnYEyil paravalAka kanYamalYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
vitiya , vitiya itEvitAmal koVttiwwIrwwa kanYamalYYEyAnYawu , ippowu varEyil peVywu varukirYawu . 
malYYEyAl nakarinY palverYu itafkalY veVlYlYakkAtAka kAtciyalYikkirYawu . 
wirumpum wicE eVllAm malYYEnIr cUlYYnwu , ceVnYnYE nakaram wIvukalYinY nakarampola veVlYlYawwil miwakkirYawu . 
pirawAnYa cAlEkalY anYEwwilum malYYEnIr vatiya itaminYrYi peVrukkeVtuwwu otukirYawu . 
eVfku pArwwAlum malYYEnIr wefki kulYampol kAtci alYikkirYawu . 
wAlYYvAnYa itafkalYil ulYlYa kutiyiruppu pakuwikalYukkulY malYYEnIr pukunwawu . 
eVlYYumpUr , puracEvAkkam , kIlYYppAkkam , aNNAnakar , wirumafkalam , mukapper , vepperi , koyampetu , cewwuppattu , viyAcarpAti , kiNti , cinwAwirippettE , rAyappettE , wiyAkarAyanakar , kotampAkkam , ayanYAvaram , peVrampUr , pANti pajAr , mayilAppUr ulYpata palverYu itafkalYilum cAlEkalY marYrYum kutiyiruppu pakuwikalYil veVlYlYam cUlYYnwawu . 
malYYEnIr wefkiyawinY kAraNamAka pirawAnYa cAlEkalY anYEwwilum katumEyAnYa pokkuvarawwu neVrical kANappattawu . 
irulY cUlYYnwu kANappattawAl vAkanYafkalY mukappu vilYakkE eVriyavittappati aNNA cAlE , pUnwamalli neVtuFcAlE ulYlYitta palverYu mukkiya cAlEkalYil vAkanYafkalY meVwuvAka Urnwu ceVlkirYawu . 
cAlEkalYil veVlYlYa nIr peVrukkeVtuwwu otukirYawu . 
ceVnYnYEyil malYYE kAraNamAka peVrumpAlAnYa katEkalY atEkkappattu ulYlYawu . 
veVlYiye varuvawarYku payanwu poVwumakkalY vIttileye mutafkiyawAl cila itafkalYil wirYanwirunwa katEkalYilum kUta viyApAram illE . 
iwanYAl viyApArikalY cIkkiramAkave katEkalYE atEwwuvittu wafkalYawu vItukalYukku wirumpinYar . 
nakarinY palverYu itafkalYil pAwukAppu karuwi minYcAra iNEppukalY wuNtikkappattanYa . 
pakal nerawwil koVcukkati verYu irunwAl poVwumakkalY katum ciramappattanYar . 
poVwumakkalYinY iyalpu vAlYYkkE katumEyAka pAwikkappattawu . 
iyalpu nilEkku wirumpa inYnYum oriru winYafkalY Akum eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . wiruppUril kaNteVynYaril koVNtu ceVllapatta rU. 570 koti parYimuwal 
wamilYYaka cattacapEkku nAlYEmarYunAlY werwal natakkirYawu . 
iwE atuwwu araciyal katciyinYar vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam marYrYum paricu poVrutkalY koVtuppawE watukka vAkanYa cowanYE wIvirappatuwwappattu irukkirYawu . 
iwarYkAka oVvvoVru mAvattawwilum kUtuwal parYakkumpatE amEkkappattu 24 maNi neramum wIvira vAkanYa cowanYE natawwappattu varukirYawu . 
inwa cowanYEkalYil paNam marYrYum paricu poVrutkalY parYimuwal ceVyyappattu varukirYawu . 
awircci 
inwiyAvil verYu eVfkum illAwa alYavukku wamilYYakawwil mattum iwuvarE rU. - 102 koti varE paNam cikkiyirukkirYawu . 
eVnYave werwal neVrufkivittawAl paNam pattuvAtA awikalYavil natEpeVrYum eVnYpawAl cowanYE wIvirappatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
wiruppUr vatakku woVkuwi parYakkumpatE wAcilwAr vijayakumAr , cap - inYspeVktar kiruRNanY marYrYum wuNE rANuvawwinYar nalYlYiravu 12.20 maNiyalYavil kovE - peVrumAnallUr rotu kunYnYawwUr pEpAs cAlEyil vAkanYa cowanYEyil Itupattu koVNtu irunwanYar . 
appowu kovE cAlEyilirunwu oVru coVkucu kArE woVtarnwu 3 kaNteVynYar lArikalY awarYku pinYnYAl 2 coVkucu kArkalY vanwawu - . 
canwekam atEnwa parYakkumpatEyinYar anwa kAr marYrYum kaNteVynYar lArikalYE nirYuwwa muyanYrYanYar . 
AnYAl nirYkAmal avE ceVnYrYawu . 
iwE atuwwu parYakkumpatE awikArikalY uyar awikArikalYukku wakaval koVtuwwanYar . 
pinYnYar anwa kaNteVynYar lArikalYE 3 kilomIttar wUram viratti ceVnYrYu ceVfkappalYlYi eVnYrYa itawwil matakkinYar . 
parYakkumpatEyinYar kaNteVynYar lAriyil irunwavarkalYitam vicAraNE natawwinYar . 
appowu avarkalY munYnYukkuppinY muraNAka pecinYar . 
anwa nerawwil kaNteVynYar lArikku munYnYAl ceVnYrYu koVNtirunwa coVkucu kAril irunwavarkalY oti vanwanYar . 
avarkalY parYakkumpatE awikArikalYitam kovEyilirunwu weciya mayamAkkappatta oVru vafkiyilirunwu AnwirA mAnilam vicAkappattinYawwukku kaNteVynYarkalYil paNam koVNtu ceVlvawAka weVriviwwanYar . 
anwa nerawwil wiruppUr mAvatta polIs cuppiraNtu carojkumAr wAkUr , wuNE kamiRanYar wiRApattel marYrYum mAvatta varuvAy awikAri caNmukam Akiyor ceVfkappalYlYi pakuwikku virEnwu vanwanYar . 
pinYnYar avarkalY 3 kaNteVynYar lArikalYEyum wirYanwu pArwwanYar . 
awil kattukattAka rU. 570 koti iruppawu kaNtupitikkappattawu . 
murYEyAnYa AvaNafkalY illE 
woVtarnwu avarkalYitam vicAraNE natawwiya powu 3 coVkucu kAril vanwavarkalYum wAfkalY AnwirA polIs eVnYrYum kaNteVynYar lArikalYil koVNtu ceVllappatum paNam weciya mayamAkkappatta oVru vafkikku coVnwamAnYawu eVnYrYum weVriviwwu cila AvaNafkalYE kAttinYar . 
AnYAl anwa AvaNafkalYil wewi wavarYAka irunwawu . 
melum polIcAr eVnYrYu coVnYnYavarkalYitam atEyAlYa attEyum illE . 
iwE atuwwu rU. 570 kotiyutanY 3 kaNteVynYar lArikalYum , awotu vanwa 3 coVkucu kArkalYEyum parYakkumpatEyinYar parYimuwal ceVywu wiruppUr kaleVktar aluvalakawwukku koVNtu vanwanYar . 
afku 3 kaNteVynYar lArikalYE curYrYiyum watuppu amEwwu wuNE rANuvawwinYar pAwukAppu paNi merYkoVNtu varukirYArkalY . inwa campavam wiruppUril peVrum paraparappE erYpatuwwi ulYlYawu .

irYuwippottiyil ifkilAnwu - 
wi inwu . 
ti20 ulakak koppE arEyirYuwi Attawwil niyUsilAnwu aNiyE 7 vikkeVt viwwiyAcawwil vIlYYwwi ifkilAnwu aNi irYuwippottikku munYnYerYiyawu . 
teVlli peVroRA kotlA mEwAnYawwil natEpeVrYrYa inwa Attawwil tAs veVnYrYa ifkilAnwu keptanY morkanY pIltifkE wervu ceVywAr . 
muwalil pet ceVywa niyUsilAnwu aNi 8 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 153 ranYkalY cerwwawu . 
kapwil 12 panwil , 15 ranY cerwwu villi panwil AttamilYYanwAr . 
atuwwu kalYamirYafkiya kAlinY munYro , villiyamcutanY iNEnwu cIrAka ranY cerwwAr .

ceVnYnYE : 
vafkakkatalil uruvAnYa kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu nilE , wAlYYvu maNtalamAka valuppeVrYrYawAl , wamilYYakawwil paravalAka malYYE peVywu varukirYawu .

kAlE muwale woVtarnwu lecAnYa malYYE peVywuvarukirYawu .

kanYnYiyAkumari , ep . 22 – 
rAjAkkamafkalam oVnYrYiyawwil kanYnYiyAkumari woVkuwi aNNA.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar eVnY.walYavAycunwaram cUrYAvalYi piraccAram merYkoVNtu wirYanwa jIppil kirAmam kirAmamAka ceVnYrYu irattE ilEkku Awaravu wirattinYAr . 
muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA nallalAciyutanY kanYnYiyAkumari woVkuwiyil pottiyitum kalYYaka vetpAlYarum mAvatta kalYYaka ceVyalAlYarumAnYa eVnY.walYavAycunwaram woVkuwikutpatta rAjAkkamafkalam oVnYrYiyam puwwalYam perUrAtciyil piraccAram ceVywAr . 
paNikkanYkutiyiruppu canwippil peVrunwiralYAka wiraNtirunwa peVNkalYitam Awaravu wirattinYAr . 
peVNkalY Arawwi eVtuwwu vetpAlYar walYavAycunwarawwirYku urYcAka varaverYpu alYiwwanYar . 
pinYnYar avar appakuwiyil vItu vItAka ceVnYrYu aracinY cAwanYEkalYE kUrYi irattE ilE cinYnYawwil vAkkukalY cekariwwAr . 
munYnYawAka akaswIsvaram UrAtci oVnYrYiyam werUr perUrAtci werUr uwirappatti kirAmawwilirunwu wanYawu werwal piraccArawwE woVtafkinYAr . 
woVtarnwu avar werUr vaNtimalEcci ammanYkovil , pAlakiruRNanYpuwUr , werUr weVrYku , werUr vatakku , vAnYamwattu , cuppiramaNiyapuram , makarAjApuram , eVs.eVl.puram , kaswUripAy kirAmam , waNtanAyakkanY , koNam Akiya pakuwikalYil vItu vItAka ceVnYrYu Awaravu wiratti irattE ilE cinYnYawwirYku vAkkukalY cekariwwAr . 
100 kirAmafkalYil 8230 ; pinYnYar avar cewupawiyUr ilanwavilYE , nEnYApuwUr , panYafkoVttAnY vilYE , mAlEyaNinwAnY kutiyiruppu , ucaravilYE , coVwwavilYE , ampalapawi , vIrapAkupawi , wivilYE , weVrYkupaNikkanY kutiyiruppu , kaNiyAnYvilYE , vatakkuwivilYE , uwwaNtanY kutiyiruppu , cifkayeyarpuri , weVfkampuwUr muslim weVru ulYpata cumAr 100kkum merYpatta kirAmafkalYil kirAmam kirAmamAka wirYanwa jIppil ceVnYrYu Awaravu wiratti irattE ilE cinYnYawwirYku vAkkukalY cekariwwAr . 
vetpAlYar walYavAycunwaram ceVnYrYa itafkalYil eVllAm peVriyorkalY ANkalY , peVNkalY avarukku cAlvE aNiviwwu urYcAka varaverYpu alYiwwanYar . 
vAkku cekarippil rAjAkkamafkalam oVnYrYiya kalYYaka ceVyalAlYar Ar.kiruRNawAs , puwwalYam perUr kalYYaka ceVyalAlYar cureR , puwwalYam perUrAtci walEvar ciwamparawevi , woVkuwi iNE ceVyalAlYar muwwukumAr , mAvatta valYYakkarYiFar pirivu iNEcceVyalAlYarkalY ceVllam , Awilifkam , mAvatta amEppucArA ottunYar aNi wuNEc ceVyalAlYar rAjAcif , mAvatta peravE poVrulYAlYar eV.eV.racAk , valYYakkarYiFarkalY veVrYrYiceVlvanY , civakumAr , IwwAmoVlYYi vIttuvacawi kUtturYavu cafka walEvar maNi , mAvatta eVm.ji.Ar. manYrYa iNEc ceVyalAlYarkalY eVnYjinYiyar leVtcumaNanY , weVnYkarEmakarAjanY , mAvatta wakaval woVlYYil nutpa pirivu ceVyalAlYarkalY i.eVnY.cafkar , mAvatta ilYEFaraNi wuNEcceVyalAlYarkalY eVs.ci.veVfkateR utpata palar utanY ceVnYrYanYar . oVlimpik pottikku civA wapA wakuwi - 
wi inwu 
oVlimpik pottikkAnYa Aciya kuwwuccaNtE wakuwiccurYrYu pottiyil inwiya vIrar civA wapA irYuwippottikku munYnYerYinYAr . 
iwanY mUlam avar oVlimpik pottiyil vilYEyAta wakuwi peVrYrYAr . 
makalYir pirivil inwiyAvinY meri kom awircci wolviyatEnwAr . 
cInYAvinY kiyAnY ' 
anYnakaril natEpeVrYrYu varum wakuwi curYrYu pottiyil Atavar pirivinY 56 kilo eVtE pirivu arEyirYuwiyil inwiyAvinY civA wapA , 2013-m ANtu ulaka kuwwuccaNtE pottiyil veVNkala pawakkam veVnYrYa kajakaswAnYinY hErAttE worYkatiwwu irYuwippottikku munYnYerYinYAr . 
iwanY mUlam Akast mAwam natEpeVrYum oVlimpik pottiyil vilYEyAta civA wapA wakuwi peVrYrYAr . 
nAlYE natEpeVrYum irYuwippottiyil wAylAnwinY cAtRAy puttiyE canwikkirYAr civA wapA . 
civA wapA oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYuvawu iwu iraNtAvawu murYEyAkum . 
meri kom wolvi 
civA wapA oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYa awevelYEyil meri kom vAyppE ilYYanwulYlYAr . 
51 kilo eVtE makalYir pirivu arEyirYuwiyil avar cInYAvinY reVnYnYitam wolviyatEnwAr . 
inwa wakuwicurYrYu pottiyil wafkam marYrYum veVlYlYi pawakkam peVrYum vIrAfkanYEkalY mattume oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYa mutiyum . 
arEyirYuwiyil wolviyatEnwa meri kom veVNkala pawakkame peVrYrYawAl oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYum vAyppE ilYYanwAr . 
avarukku katEciyAka inYnYum oVru vAyppu ulYlYawu . 
me mAwam natEpeVrYum ulaka cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYalAm . jappAnYil payafkara nilanatukkam : 
9 per pali ; 860 per patukAyam - 
wi inwu 
nilanatukkawwAl pAwippatEnwa jappAnYinY weVnYmerYku wIvAnYa kEyURuvil mItpu paNikalY woVtarnwu wIviramAka natanwu varukinYrYanYa . 
jappAnYinY weVnYmerYku wIvup pakuwiyAnYa kEyURuvil iru winYafkalYukku munY 6.5 riktar alYavil cakwivAynwa nilanatukkam erYpattawu . 
vItukalY , kattitafkalY itinwu vilYYunwawil iwuvarE 9 per uyirilYYanwiruppawAka kUrYappatukirYawu . 
patukAyamatEnwa 860-kkum merYpattor maruwwuvamanYEyil anYumawikkappattulYlYanYar . 
peVrumpAlAnYa atukkumAti vItukalYil nilanatukkawwAl virical erYpattiruppawAl Ayirawwukkum merYpatta makkalY pAwukAppAnYa itafkalYil waFcam atEnwulYlYanYar . 
awiveka pullat rayilkalY watam puraNtawu mattuminYrYi , rayil nilEyafkalYinY kUrEkalYum atiyotu cAynwulYlYanYa . 
iwanYAl jappAnYinY oVru cila pakuwikalYil rayil pokkuvarawwum wuNtikkappattulYlYawu . 
melum atuwwatuwwu nila awirvukalYum erYpattu varuvawAl poVwumakkalY mikunwa pIwiyatEnwulYlYanYar . 
itipAtukalYil cikkiyavarkalYE mItkum paNikalY woVtarnwu natanwu varukinYrYanYa . 
iwanYAl pali eVNNikkE uyaralAm eVnYa aFcappatukirYawu . 
iwarYkitEyil itipAtukalYil cikki uyirukku porAti koVNtirunwa eVttu mAwa peVN kulYYanwEyE ArYu maNi nerawwukku pinY nerYrYu mItpu kulYYuvinYar uyirutanY mIttanYar . 
kutumpawwinYar itipAtukalYilirunwu eVppatiyo wappi pilYYEwwa nilEyil kulYYanwE mattum itipAtukalYil cikkik koVNtawu . 
eVnYinYum utalil eVnwavoVru kAyamum kulYYanwEkku erYpatavillE . 
iwanYAl kutumpawwinYar makilYYcci atEnwulYlYanYar . 
itipAtukalYil cikki uyirutanY iruppavarkalYE atEyAlYam kANpawarYkAka moppa nAy uwaviyutanY mItpu kulYYuvinYar iravu , pakalAka paNiyArYrYi varukinYrYanYar . kUttaNiyil ceruvawarYkAka eVnYakku paNa AcE kAttinYArkalY 
pottutEkkum vijayakAnw 
ceVnYnYE we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar vijayakAnw , iNEyaw walYam oVnYrYu alYiwwa pettiyil kUrYi iruppawAvawu : 
wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalil kUttaNi ceruvawarYkAka eVnYakku paNa AcE kAttinYArkalY . 
a.wi.mu.ka , wi.mu.ka , pArawIya janYawA katcikalY cArpil eVnYakku paNam waruvawAka peram pecappattawu . 
AnYAl nAnY paNawwukku mukkiyawwuvam koVtukkavillE . 
paNawwukku mayafkAmal nAnY makkalY nalak kUttaNiyutanY cernwenY . 
pArawIya janYawA katciw walEvarkalY eVnYakku muwal-manwiri pawaviyE waruvawAka kUrYinYArkalY . 
eVnYrYAlum nAnY makkalY nalak kUttaNiyEye wervu ceVywenY . 
awil nAnY urYuwiyAkavum irunwenY . 
makkalY nalakkUttaNiyil nAnY eVnwa eVwirpArppum vEwwirukkavillE . 
oVruvelYE avarkalY eVnYnYE muwal-amEccar vetpAlYarAka arYivikkAmal irunwu irunwAlum kUta nAnY anwa aNiyilwAnY cernwu iruppenY . 
a.wi.mu.ka.vum wi.mu.ka.vum inwa nAttE pAlYYpatuwwi vittArkalY . 
appatippatta a.wi.mu.ka , wi.mu.ka.vutanYA nAnY kUttaNi cera veNtum ? 
oVrupowum nAnY avarkalYutanY poka mAttenY . 
2011-m ANtu werwalil kUta avarkalYil oVruvarutanY kUttaNi vEwwu vittu , mUnYrYe mAwafkalYil nAnY kUttaNiyilirunwu veVlYiyil vanwu vittenY . 
inwa watavE woVfku cattacapE erYpatalAm eVnYrYu cilar coVlvawE erYka iyalAwu . 
makkalY 16-nwewi wafkalY wIrppE valYYafka ulYlYanYar . 
eVnYave 19-nwewi varE nAm poVrYuwwu irukkalAm . 
cattacapEyil jeVyalaliwA allawu karuNAniwi mattumwAnY irukka veNtumA ? 
werwalukkup pirYaku wi.mu.ka. allawu a.wi.mu.ka.vutanY kUttaNi amEkkum wittam eVwuvum illE . 
makkalY inYiyum wi.mu.ka.vukku a.wi.mu.ka.vukkum vAkkalYiwwAl awu maN kuwirEyE nampi ArYrYil kuwiwwa kawEyAkivitum . 
a.wi.mu.ka. aracu makkalYE emArYrYum aracu . 
avarkalY mINtum veVrYrYi peVrYrYu makkalYE curaNtave virumpukirYArkalY . 
ivvArYu vijayakAnw kUrYinYAr . 29 pattafkalY veVnYrYu jokovic cAwanYE - 
wi inwu 
mAtrit opanY teVnYnYis potti Atavar pirivil nampar oVnY vIrarAnYa ceVrpiyAvinY novAk jokovic cAmpiyanY pattam veVnYrYAr . 
iwanY mUlam mAstars woVtaril 28 pattafkalY veVnYrYirunwa natAlinY cAwanYEyE murYiyatiwwAr . 
speVyinYinY mAtrit nakaril natEpeVrYrYa inwa pottiyinY irYuwic curYrYil 2-m nilE vIrarum natappu cAmpiyanYumAnYa ifkilAnwinY AnYti murrevE 6-2 , 3-6 , 6-3 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYwwi pattam veVnYrYAr jokovic . 
inwa Attam 2 maNi neram 6 nimitafkalY natEpeVrYrYawu . 
AnYti murre wolviyatEnwawAl teVnYnYis waravaricE pattiyalil 2-vawu itawwE cuvitcarlAnwinY rojar peVtararitam parYikoVtuwwulYlYAr . 
jokoviccukku eVwirAka murre wolviyE canwippawu iwu 23-vawu murYEyAkum . 
awilum katanwa 2014 muwal warYpowu varE iruvarum 13 Attawwil vilYEyAti ulYlYanYar . 
iwil murre oVru Attawwil mattume veVrYrYi peVrYrYulYlYAr . 
12 Attawwilum jokovicce Awikkam ceVluwwiyulYlYAr . 
inwa ANtil jokovic kEpparYrYum 5-vawu pattam iwuvAkum . 
mAtrit opanYil jokovic pattam veVlvawu iwu 2-vawu murYEyAkum . 
katEciyAka avar 2011l koppE veVnYrYirunwAr . 
warYpowu pattam veVnYrYulYlYawanY mUlam jokovic puwiya cAwanYEyum patEwwulYlYAr . 
mAstars anwaswu peVrYrYa woVtaril avar veVllum 29-vawu pattam iwuvAkum . 
iwanY mUlam mAstars woVtaril 28 pattafkalY veVnYrYirunwa natAlinY cAwanYEyE murYiyatiwwAr . pali eVNNikkE 41Aka uyarvu : 
nilanatukkawwukku payanwu kAril wUfkum jappAnYiya makkalY 
tokkiyo : 
jappAnYil iruwinYafkalYAka woVtarnwu erYpatta nilanatukkawwukku paliyAnYavarkalYinY eVNNikkE 41Aka uyarnwulYlYa nilEyil mINtum nilanatukkam wAkkalAm eVnYrYa accawwil palar vItukalYukku ceVllAmal cAlEyoramAka kArukkulYlYeye patuwwu wUfkuvawAka wakavalkalY veVlYiyAkiyulYlYanYa . 
munYnYawAka , jappAnYil nerYrYu munYwinYam erYpatta nilanatukkawwAl pawwu per uyirilYYanwu , cumAr 650 per kAyamatEnwanYar . 
anwa awircciyilirunwu makkalY mIlYAwa nilEyil jappAnYinY weVnYmerYku wIvAnYa kiyURu pakuwiyil nerYrYu awikAlE erYpatta nilanatukkam riktar alYavil 7.3 alakukalYAka pawivAnYawu . 
mikamocamAnYa inwa nilanatukkawwinY vilYEvAka pala atukkumAti vItukalYum , wanYi vItukalYum itinwu vilYYunwanYa . 
cAlEkalYil pilYavu erYpattu , pala pakuwikalYil pokkuvarawwu pAwippatEnwulYlYawu . 
nerYrYEya nilanatukkawwAl kiyURu wIvukku arukAmEyil ulYlYa oVru eVrimalE veVtiwwu , wIppilYYampE kakki varuvawAka ulYlYUr UtakafkalY ceVywi veVlYiyittulYlYanYa . 
kattita itipAtukalYil cikki uyirilYYanwa 19 pirewafkalY mItkappattawAkavum , melum palarE uyirutanY mItkum muyarYciyil peritar nivAraNam marYrYum wIyaNEppu patEyinYar mulYYuvIccil Itupattu varuvawAkavum aracu vattArafkalY weVriviwwanYa . 
kAyamatEnwa cumAr 800 per AspawwirikalYil cikiccE peVrYrYu varuvawAka ulYlYAtciwurYE cukAwAra awikArikalY nerYrYu kUrYinYar . 
innilEyil , inYrYu ( 17-m wewi ) kAlE nilavarappati , ivviru nilanatukkafkalYilum 41 per paliyAnYawAkavum , cumAr 1500 per kAyamatEnwawAkavum awikArappUrvamAka arYivikkappattulYlYawu . 
ivarkalYil kumAmAtto nakaril mattum 32 per itipAtukalYil cikki uyirilYYanwawAkavum , cumAr 200 vItukalY warEmattamAki kitappawAkavum UtakafkalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . 
innakaril cumAr 4 latcam vItukalYil vacikkum makkalY kutinIr kitEkkAmal wiNtAtuvawAkavum , cumAr oVru latcam vItukalY minYcAraminYrYi irulYil mUlYYki kitappawAkavum anwa ceVywikalY kurYippitukinYrYanYa . 
iwarYkitEyil , mINtum nilanatukkam wAkkalAm eVnYrYa accawwil palar vItukalYukku ceVllAmal , kutumpawwArutanY cAlEyoramAka kArukkulYlYeye patuwwu wUfkuvawAka wakavalkalY veVlYiyAkiyulYlYanYa . pA.valYarmawiyitam ‘ irattE ilEkku ’ ottu eVnYrYu makkalY urYuwi 
ceVnYnYE , ep . 22 – 
Ayiram vilYakku woVkuwi aNNA.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarAnYa amEccar pA.valYarmawiyitam woVkuwi makkalY jeVyalaliwA ceVywa uwavikalY , cAwanYEkalYukku nanYrYi kUrYi irattE ilEkkuwwAnY eVfkalY ottu eVnYrYu urYuwi kUrYinYArkalY . 
valYarmawi ceVnYrYa itameVllAm makkalY urYcAkawwutanYum , makilYYcciyutanYum varaverYrYArkalY . 
AyiramvilYakku woVkuwiyil mINtum pottiyitum amEccar pA.valYarmawi katanwa 5 ANtukalYil woVkuwikku erAlYamAnYa wittafkalYE koVNtu vanwu nirYEverYrYi irukkirYAr . 
erAlYamAnYa nalawwitta uwavikalYE valYYafki irukkirYAr . 
malYYE vanwapowum , veVlYlYam vanwapowum veVlYlYa nIril nInwic ceVnYrYu cerYum cakawiyum kalYYivunIr kalanwa pakuwikalYukku natanwu ceVnYrYu makkalYitam kurYEkalYE kettu utanYatiyAka nivAraNa paNikalYE minYnYal vekawwil natavatikkE eVtukka erYpAtu ceVywawE anwa pakuwi makkalY marYakkavillE . 
anwa paNikalYE nirYEverYrYappattirukkirYawA eVnYrYu pala itafkalYil neril ceVnYrYum valYarmawi urYuwi ceVywAr . 
eVnYave iwanYE eVllAm makkalY eVNNip pArkkirYArkalY . 
vItu vItAka ceVnYrYu jeVyalaliwA cAwanYEkalYE coVlli valYarmawi Awaravu wiratti varukirYAr . 
oVvvoVru vIttilum wafkalY vIttu peVN eVnYrYa nilEyil makilYYcciyutanY varaverYkirYArkalY . 
jeVyalaliwA cAwanYEkku nanYrYi 
wafkalY woVkuwikku ceVywa wittafkalY , ceVywa uwavikalYE nanYrYiyutanY woVkuwi makkalY kUrYukirYArkalY . 
jeVyalaliwA koVNtu vanwa wittafkalYinY palanYkalYE makilYYcciyutanY eVtuwwu kUrYukirYArkalY . 
eVfkalY vIttil ammA wanwa mikci , kirENtar , minYvicirYi ulYlYawu eVnYavum pilYlYEkku koVtuwwa leptAp irukku eVnYavum jeVyalaliwA valYYafkiya wittawwinY palanYE peVrYrYa makkalY nanYrYiyutanY ammAvukkuwwAnY eVfkalY ottu , irattE ilEkkuwwAnY oVttu eVnYrYu kUrYinYArkalY . 
eVfku pArwwAlum jeVyalaliwAvinY wittafkalYE coVlli nanYrYi kUrYuvawE kANa mutinwawu . 
jeVyalaliwA mIwu makkalY mulYYu nampikkE vEwwirukkirYArkalY . 
mINtum muwalamEccarAka vara veNtum eVnYrYu virumpukirYArkalY . 
eVfkum makkalY manYanilE iwuponYrYu ulYlYawu . 
malYYE , veVlYlYam vanwa nerawwil ceVywa uwavikalY , kurYEkalYE coVnYnYAl utanYatiyAka anwa pakuwikku vanwu awanYE cIrceVywawE eVllAm makkalY ninYEvu pArwwu nanYrYi kUrYi irattE ilEkkuwAnY ottu eVnYrYu makilYYcciyutanY kUrYinYArkalY . 
inYrYu kAlE 7 maNikku kotampAkkam mempAlam aruke ulYlYa 112–vawu kilYYakku vattam pakuwiyil ulYlYa cupewAr kArtanY , varawarAjapettE , mEnYar tirastpuram Akiya pakuwikalYil vItu vItAka ceVnYrYu Awaravu kettAr . 
kAlE 7 maNikku ceVnYrYa valYarmawi 11 maNi varE woVtarnwu Awaravu kettAr . 
malar wUvi varaverYpu 
palverYu vItukalYil peVNkalY malar wUvi makilYYcciyutanY varaverYrYArkalY . 
Arawwi eVtuwwArkalY . 
wafkalY ottu irattE ilEkkuwAnY eVnYpawE kAtta erAlYamAnYa vItukalYil irattE ilE kolam pottirunwanYar . 
ceVnYrYa itameVllAm eVlYYucci varaverYpu alYikkappattawu . 
pA.valYarmawiyutanY pakuwi ceVyalAlYar nufkE mArYanY eVm.ci , woVkuwi ceVyalAlYar ti.civarAj eVm.ci , mAmanYrYa urYuppinYar puRpA nakar ArYumukam , maNtala kulYYu walEvar eVs.cakwi , mAmanYrYa urYuppinYarkalY yu.karYpakam , pi.cinYnYEyanY , cAnwi pAskar marYrYum vatta ceVyalAlYar varawE muwwuparaNi , nufkE mUrwwi , pArwwacArawi , valYYakkarYiFar Ar.cawAcivam , rAmamUrwwi , cinYnYEyA , colE umApawi , Atiyo rakIm , nufkE manYokar , aNNA Atto ottunYar woVlYYirYcafka ceVyalAlYar ji.panYnYIrceVlvam , poVnY ceV.kumAr , manYcUr akamawu , jeVyapal , pi.ilYEyamArYanY , eVm.cekar , jArj utpata palar utanY ceVnYrYArkalY . 
iwarYkAnYa erYpAtukalYE vatta ceVyalAlYar varawE muwwuparaNi ceVywirunwAr . mAnila cap–jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu : 
ceVnYnYE mAvatta aNikalY arYivippu 
ceVnYnYE , mAvattafkalYukku itEyilAnYa mAnila jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu cAmpiyanYRip potti ceVnYnYE neru stetiyawwil nAlYE ( veVlYlYikkilYYamE ) muwal 25–nwewi varE natakkirYawu . 
inwa pottikkAnYa ceVnYnYE mAvatta ANkalY marYrYum peVNkalY aNiyE ceVnYnYE mAvatta kUtEppanwu cafka ceVyalAlYar eVs.eVs.nicAr arYiviwwulYlYAr . 
aNi varumArYu : 
ANkalY aNi : ayUp apwullA , arvinw , ajiw , tenYiyar riccarts , harirAm ( keptanY ) , jeVyacUryA , jocuvA rocAriyo , kAlYiwAs , nanwakumAr , cAm jos canYnYi , canwoR maNi , srIrAm , payirYciyAlYar : lokanAwanY , mAnYejar : cacikumAr . 
peVNkalY aNi : aRmi mariyA pepi , avanwi varwanY , wIpikA , kAyawri , EsvaryA , monYiRAkumAri , monYikA , niRAnwi ( keptanY ) , poVnYcavunwaryA latcumi , riyA RaronY , cinYekA , srIriswi curenY , payirYciyAlYar : pAp tevis , mAnYejar : rAmaccanwiranY . paFcAfkawwil puyal parYrYiya kaNippu 
ceVnYnYE , 
vAnYawwil culYYalum navakirakafkalYinY iyakkam , awanYAl ulakil erYpatum mArYrYafkalY AkiyavE woVtarpAnYa kurYippukalY atafkiyawu ‘ paFcAfkam ’ eVnYrYu alYYEkkappatukirYawu . 
paNtEya kAlawwil navInYa vAnYiyal AyvukkaruvikalY illAwa cUlYYnilEyil , munYivarkalY nava kirakafkalYinY iyakkawwE wulliyamAka kaNiwwanYar . 
wafkalYawu kaNippukalYE culokafkalYAka ( pAtalkalYAka ) eVlYYuwiyum vEwwulYlYanYar . 
iwanY atippatEyil ANtuworYum wamilYY ANtupirYappE atippatEyAka vEwwu paFcAfkam kaNikkappatukirYawu . 
inwa paFcAfkafkalYinY uwaviyutanY jAwakam kaNippawu , eVwirkAla palanYkalYEc coVlvawu ponYrYavarYrYE jowitarkalY ceVykinYrYanYar . 
paFcAfkam iruvakEppatum . 
1 . wirukkaNiwa paFcAfkam , 2 vAkkiyappaFcAfkam . 
inwa iraNtu paFcAfkafkalYinY kaNippukalYukku itEye 6 maNi 48 nimitam viwwiyAcam irukkum . 
pallAyiram ANtukalYukku munYpu munYivarkalY eVlYYuwiya culokafkalY atippatEyil eVlYYuwappatuvawu ‘ vAkkiya paFcAfkam ’ eVnYappatum . 
canwiranYinY iyakkawwE atippatEyAkak koVNtu eVlYYuwappatuvawu ‘ wirukkaNiwa paFcAfkam ’ Akum . 
vAkkiya murYE paFcAfkawwE palverYu jowitarkalYum veVlYiyittu varukirYArkalY . 
avvArYu veVlYiyAnYa oVru vAkkiya paFcAfkawwil katanwa 14-nwewi ( canYikkilYYamE ) anYrYu “ puwiya kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu maNtalam uruvAkum ” eVnYrYu kurYippitappattulYlYawu . 
awanYpati warYpowu kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu nilE erYpattu wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum paravalAka palawwa malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
iwupola anwa paFcAfkawwil varukirYa 21-nwewi ( canYikkilYYamE ) “ oVru vAram malYYE peVyyum ” eVnYrYum , 22-nwewi ( FAyirYrYukkilYYamE ) anYrYu “ puyal palamAka ceVnYnYEyE ulukkum ” eVnYrYum kurYippitappattulYlYawu . wamilYYakawwil wifkatkilYYamE vAkkuppawivu ; 
anYEwwu erYpAtukalYum wayAr ; 
ottuppawivu nAlYil minYwatE kUtAwu eVnYrYu uwwaravu ; 
walEmE werwal awikAri wakaval 
ceVnYnYE , 
wamilYYaka cattacapEkku oVre kattamAka varukirYa wifkatkilYYamE werwal natEpeVrYukirYawu . 
awikArikalY mummuram 
werwal piracAram inYrYu ( canYikkilYYamE ) mAlE 6 maNiyutanY mutivatEkirYawu . 
234 woVkuwikalYilum moVwwam 3,776 vetpAlYarkalY pottiyitukirYArkalY . 
ivarkalYil 320 per peVNkalY . 
1,566 per cuyeccE vetpAlYarkalY . 
inwa werwalil 5 kotiye 82 latcam vAkkAlYarkalY ottuppota irukkirYArkalY . 
vAkkuppawivukkAnYa irYuwikkatta paNikalYil werwal kamiRanY awikArikalY mummuramAka ulYlYanYar . 
iwu kurYiwwu wamilYYaka walEmE werwal awikAri rAjeR lakkAnYi nerYrYu walEmEc ceVyalakawwil niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : - 
erYpAtukalY wayAr 
wamilYYakawwil iwuvarE 86.44 cawavIwa ‘ pUw cilippukalY vinYiyokikkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
‘ pUw cilip ’ kitEkkAwavarkalY werwal kamiRanY erYkanYave arYiviwwulYlYa 11 AvaNafkalYE kAtti vAkkalYikkalAm . 
werwalukkAka anYEwwu erYpAtukalYum wayAr nilEyil ulYlYanYa . 
cattacapE werwalil 100 cawavIwa vAkkuppawivukkAnYa eVllA erYpAtukalYum ceVyyappattu ulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum moVwwam 66 Ayirawwu oVru vAkkuccAvatikalY amEkkappattu irukkinYrYanYa . 
vAkkuppawivukkAka oVru latcawwu 4 Ayirawwu 500 minYnYaNu eVnwirafkalY wayAr nilEyil ulYlYanYa . 
ivE wavira 20 cawavIwa eVnwirafkalY kUtuwalAka vEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
minYnYaNu vAkkuppawivu eVnwirafkalY marYrYum werwalukku wevEyAnYa mE , AvaNafkalY ulYpata anYEwwu poVrutkalYum FAyirYrYukkilYYamE ( nAlYE ) kAlE muwal iravu varE anwanwa vAkkuccAvatikalYukku polIs pAwukApputanY koVNtu ceVllappatum . 
malYYE peVywAl ... 
wamilYYakawwinY weVnY mAvattafkalYil warYpowu lecAka malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
wamilYYakawwil ulYlYa anYEwwu vAkkuccAvatikalYum kattitafkalYilwAnY amEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
irunwapowilum vAkkuppawivu winYawwanYrYu malYYE peVywAl awE camAlYikka vAkkuccAvati munYpu pilYAstik kUrE pota uwwaravitappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAka powiya niwi oVwukkappattu irukkirYawu . 
ceVlponYukku watE 
pawarYrYamAnYa vAkkuccAvatikalYinY eVNNikkE , 
katanwa werwalE vita ippowu kurYEvAka irunwAlum avE wIviramAka kaNkANikkappatum . 
vAkkuccAvatikalYukkulY vAkkAlYarkalY ceVlponYkalYE koVNtu ceVlla watE viwikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
mIrYi koVNtu ceVnYrYAl parYimuwal ceVyyappatum . 
AnYAl vAkkuccAvati werwal awikAri mattum ceVlponY vEwwukkoVlYlYalAm . 
AnYAl awEyum vAkkuppawivu kurYiwwu werwal awikArikalYukku weVriyappatuwwuvawarYku mattume payanYpatuwwa veNtum . 
verYu yArukkum wakaval koVtukka payanYpatuwwak kUtAwu . 
iwepol werwal mukavarkalYum ceVlponYkalYE koVNtu ceVllak kUtAwu . 
vAkkuppawivinY powu itEyil avarkalY veVlYiye vara anYumawi illE . 
vAkkuppawivu winYamAnYa 16-nwewi mAlE 6 maNi varE minYveVttu erYpatAmal kavanYamutanY ceVyalpatumArYu minYvAriya awikArikalYukku uwwaravitappattu ulYlYawu . 
poVmmE vAkkuppawivu eVnwirafkalY parYimuwal 
waFcAvUr mAvattam pApanAcam eVnYrYa itawwil araciyal katciyinYar koVNtu vanwa 50 poVmmE minYnYaNu vAkkuppawivu eVnwirafkalY parYimuwal ceVyyappattu irukkinYrYanYa . 
ivE puwucceriyil wayArikkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
ivE piracArawwukkAka wAnY koVNtu varappattu ulYlYanYa . 
awu wavarYu kitEyAwu . 
AnYAl awuparYrYi munYkUttiye werwal kamiRanYukku wakaval weVriviwwirukka veNtum . 
AnYAl avarkalY wakaval weVrivikkAwawAl poVmmE vAkkuppawivu eVnwirafkalY parYimuwal ceVyyappattu ulYlYanYa . 
anwa eVnwirafkalY koVNtu varappatta vAkanYawwil piracArawwukku wevEyAnYa poVrutkalY irunwanYa . 
avarYrYE awikArikalY parYimuwal ceVywu valYYakkuppawivu ceVywu ulYlYanYar . 
cUwAttam 
ceVnYnYE eVlYYumpUril oVru lAtjil cUwAttam natappawAka vanwa wakavalE woVtarnwu , parYakkumpatEyinYar campava itawwukku virEnwu ceVnYrYu vicAriwwanYar . 
appowu afku rU. 2 latcam irunwawu . 
AnYAl vicAraNEyil afku werwal woVtarpAnYa cUwAttam natakkavillE eVnYpawAlum , anwa paNawwukku cariyAnYa kaNakku kAttappattawAlum anwa paNam wiruppi koVtukkappattawu . 
katanwa 12-nwewi oVre nAlYil oVru kotiye 43 latcam rUpAy parYimuwal ceVyyappattu ulYlYawu .

virAt koli vilYakkam ! - 
peVfkalYUr aNiyil kirYis keVyl itampeVrYAwawarYkuk kAraNam , oyvu alla , pawilAka avar nIkkappattulYlYAr eVnYrYu anwa aNiyinY keptanY virAt koli petti alYiwwulYlYAr . 
pirapala kirikkeVt vIrar kirYis keVyil , AN kulYYanwEkkuw wanwEyAnYavutanY wanYawu coVnwa Urukkuk kilYampinYAr . 
pirYaku epral 25 anYrYu EpieVl pottiyil kalanwukoVlYlYa inwiyAvukkuw wirumpinYAr .

keVyl aNiyil itampeVrYAwawarYku peVfkalYUr aNi keptanY virAt koli kUrYiyawAvawu : 
kirYis keVylukku oyvalYikkappatavillE . 
pawilAka avar nIkkappattulYlYAr .

nAnYum rAkulum woVtakka vIrarkalYAka nanYrYAka vilYEyAti varukirYom . 
tirAvis heVt mitil Artaril nanYrYAka vilYEyAtuvAr . 
culYYarYpanwu vIccukkum uwavuvAr eVnYrYAr . 
carparAs kAnY aNiyil itampeVrYAwawu kurYiwwu koli kUrYumpowu : 
avarukkuk kAyam eVwuvum erYpatavillE . 
utalnilEw wakuwiyil , wAnY eVppati munYnYerYrYam kANa veNtum eVnYpawE avar arYinwulYlYAr . 
HpIltifkinY powu vekamAka oti Enwu ArYu ranYkalYEw watukkum vIrarkalYe namakkuw wevE . 
carparAs kAnY awEp purinwukoVNtulYlYAr . 
avarukkup pawilAka aNiyil itampeVrYrYulYlYa caccinY pepi , nalla utalwakuwiyutanY cirYappAka HpIltif ceVypavar . 
nIfkalY pavular illE eVnYrYAl pettif marYrYum HpIltifkilum cirYappAka irukka veNtum . 
AtukalYawwil 120 % munYEpputanY ulYlYa vIrarEye nAnY wervu ceVyvenY eVnYrYAr . varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta uwwarappirawecawwukku utanYati nivAraNam : 
moti uwwaravu - 
puwuwilli : 
varYatciyAl katumEyAka pAwikkappatta uwwarappiraweca mAnilawwukku wevEyAnYa nivAraNa uwavikalYE utanYatiyAka valYYafkumpati pirawamar narenwira moti uwwaravittulYlYAr . 
varYatci nilE kurYiwwu eVtuwwurEwwu nivAraNa uwavi peVrYuvawarYkAka uwwarappiraweca muwalvar akileR yAwav inYrYu pirawamar narenwira motiyE canwiwwup pecinYAr . 
inwa canwippinY powu , akileR yAwav , nIr AwArafkalY kurYiwwu vivAwiwwAr . 
awarYku pirawamar narenwira moti mawwiya aracum , mAnila aracum iNEnwu iwarYkAnYa paNiyE munYnYeVtuwwu , varYatci kAraNamAka makkalY canwikkum piracnYEkalYE wavirkka veNtum eVnYrYu kUrYiyawAka pirawamar aluvalakam weVriviwwulYlYawu . 29–nwewi vilYYuppurawwil jeVyalaliwA pecukirYAr 
ceVnYnYE , ep . 21 – 
muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY werwal piraccArawwil mArYrYam ceVywu aNNA.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
29–nwewi vilYYuppurawwil natEpeVrYum poVwukkUttawwil jeVyalaliwA pecukirYAr . 
awanYpati , me 3-nwewi vilYYuppurawwil natEpeVrYa irunwa werwal piraccAram immAwam 29n–wewikku mArYrYam ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
natEpeVrYa ulYlYa cattamanYrYa werwalil aNNA.wi.mu.ka. kUttaNiyil aNNA.wi.mu.ka. 227 itafkalYilum , kUttaNi katcikalY 7 itafkalYilum pottiyitukinYrYanYa . 
iwarYkAnYa aNNA.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar pattiyal katanwa 4-nwewi veVlYiyitappattawu . 
anYrYEya winYam mAlEyileye aNNA.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwalamEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwAvinY werwal piraccAra curYrYuppayaNa wittam kurYiwwu arYivippu veVlYiyAnYawu . 
awanYpati , katanwa 9-nwewi ceVnYnYEyil woVtafkiya avarawu piraccAram me 12-nwewi varE natEpeVrYuvawAka arYivikkappattawu . 
ceVnYnYE , viruwwAcalam , warmapuri , aruppukkottE , kAFcipuram , celam Akiya 6 itafkalYil wanYawu werwal piraccArawwE jeVyalaliwA nirYEvu ceVywulYlYAr . 
inwa nilEyil werwal piraccArawwil cirYiya mArYrYam ceVywu aNNA.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam arYivippu veVlYiyittulYlYawu . 
awAvawu , me 3-nwewi vilYYuppuram mAvattawwil merYkoVlYvawAka irunwa werwal piraccAram immAwam 29–nwewikku mArYrYam ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu aNNA.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYi iruppawAvawu : 
16.5.2016 anYrYu natEpeVrYa ulYlYa wamilYYnAtu , puwucceri marYrYum keralYa mAnila cattacapE poVwuwwerwalkalYE munYnYittu , aNNA.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwalamEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwAvinY werwal piraccAra curYrYuppayaNam erYkeVnYave arYivikkappattu irunwawu . 
awil pinYvarumArYu wiruwwi amEkkappattulYlYawu . 
10-m nAlY werwal piraccAram immAwam 29-nwewi ( veVlYlYikkilYYamE ) vilYYuppurawwil natEpeVrYukirYawu .

kAyam kAraNamAka meksveVl vilakal 
9-vawu E.pi.eVl. pottiyil kifsleVvanY paFcAp aNiyil AswireliyAvE cernwa awirati vIrar meksveVl vilYEyAti varukirYAr . 
anwa aNi erYkanYave pilYe Ap curYrYu vAyppE ilYYanwu vittawu .

carAcari 19.88 Akum . ceVnYnYE , 
ilafkE - kanYnYiyAkumari itEye nilavukinYrYa melatukku culYYarYci kAraNamAka wamilYYnAtu marYrYum puwucceriyil inYrYu ( canYikkilYYamE ) aneka itafkalYil malYYE peVyyum eVnYrYum , arapikkatalil uruvAnYa puyal wIviram atEnwulYlYawu eVnYrYum vAnYilE mEya iyakkunYar eVs.Ar.ramaNanY weVriviwwAr . 
valYYakkamAka vatakilYYakku paruvamalYYE woVtafkiyawum vafkakkatalil kurYEnwa kArYrYalYYuwwa wAlYYvu nilE uruvAkuvawum awanY kAraNamAka palawwa malYYEpeVyvawum uNtu . 
wamilYYnAttil katanwa 28-nwewi muwal vatakilYYakku paruvamalYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
inYrYum wamilYYnAtu marYrYum puwucceriyil aneka itafkalYil malYYE peVyyum eVnYrYu vAnYilE mEyam arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
aneka itafkalYil malYYE peVyyum 
iwu kurYiwwu ceVnYnYE vAnYilE maNtala ArAycci mEya iyakkunYar eVs.Ar.ramaNanY kUrYiyawAvawu : 
vafkakkatalil ilafkE aruke nerYrYu munYwinYam melatukku culYYarYci irunwawu . 
awanY kAraNamAka wamilYYnAttil aneka itafkalYil malYYE peVywulYlYawu . 
ilafkE aruke irunwa melatukku culYYarYci , afkirunwu merYku nokki nakarnwu kanYnYiyAkumari aruke ceVnYrYulYlYawu . 
inwa melatukku culYYarYci kAraNamAka wamilYYnAtu marYrYum puwucceriyil inYrYu ( canYikkilYYamE ) aneka itafkalYilum , katalora weVnYmAvattafkalYilum , ulYmAvattafkalYilum oriru itafkalYil kanYamalYYE peVyyum . 
wIviram atEnwa puyal 
arapikkatalil uruvAnYa capAlA eVnYrYa puyal , wIviram atEnwu ulYlYawu . 
awu nerYrYu kAlE 8-30 maNi nilavarappati omanY nAttil ulYlYa calAlA nakarukku kilYYakkil weVnYkilYYakkil 850 kilo mIttar wUrawwil ulYlYawu . 
anwap puyal melum wIviram atEnwu awi wIvira puyalAka mArYalAm . 
awu navampar 2-nwewi omanY - emanY nAtukalYukku itEye karEyE katakka vAyppu ulYlYawu . 
ivvArYu eVs.Ar.ramaNanY weVriviwwAr . 
nerYrYu kAlE 8-30 maNiyutanY mutivatEnwa 24 maNi nerawwil peVywa malYYE alYavu varumArYu : 
pApanAcam 9 ceV.mI. pApanAcam 9 ceV.mI. , makApalipuram 8 ceV.mI. , pUwappANti 5 ceV.mI. , ceVnYnYE ti.ji.pi.aluvalakam , ceVfkottE , mElAti walA 4 ceV.mI. , pAmpanY , aNNApalkalEkkalYYakam , wAmparam walA 3 ceV.mI. , ceVnYnYE nufkampAkkam , rAmesvaram , nAkappattinYam , mayilAtuwurYE , srIvEkuNtam , waFcAvUr , wiNtivanYam , nanYnYilam walA 2 ceV.mI. weVnYkAci , maNimuwwArYu , ceVnYnYE vimAnYanilEyam , kArEkkal , ceVfkunYrYam , wiruvAlafkAtu , parafkippettE , Aykkuti , jeVyafkoVNtam , peVrufkalUr , kanwavarkottE , wiruwwaNi , vilYAwwikkulYam , ciwamparam , wakkalE , wAmarEppAkkam , pUNti , wiruwwurYEppUNti , muwwuppettE , pulYlYampAti , kulYYiwwalE , viruwunakar walA 1 ceV.mI. malYYE peVywulYlYawu . ceVnYnYE , ‘ ‘ 
eVnYawu kanYaveVllAm wamilYYarkalY vAlYYvAfku vAlYYa veNtum . 
234 woVkuwikalYilum nAnYe vetpAlYarAka kalYawwil nirYkirYenY ’’ eVnYrYu weVriviwwulYlYa muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA , kaNwuFcAmal a.wi.mu.ka. woVNtarkalY katamEyArYrYita veNtum eVnYrYum veNtukolY vituwwulYlYAr . 
a.wi.mu.ka. poVwuc ceVyalAlYarum , muwal-amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA nerYrYu veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYi iruppawAvawu : 
araciyal payaNam 
wamilYYnAtu cattamanYrYap peravEkkAnYa poVwuwwerwal vAkkuppawivu 16-5-2016 anYrYu natEpeVrYa ulYlYa nilEyil , awarYku munYnYar nIfkalY anYEvarum ArYrYa veNtiya inYrYiyamEyAwa paNikalY cilavarYrYEyum , avarYrYE nIfkalY wirYampata ceVywita veNtum eVnYpawE ninYEvUttavum inwa matalinYE ufkalYukku varEkirYenY . 
natEpeVrYa irukkum wamilYYnAtu cattamanYrYap peravE poVwuwwerwal eVwirkAla wamilYYakawwinY araciyal payaNawwirYku wicEkAttiyAka amEyap pokum werwal eVnYpawE ninYEvil koVlYlYufkalY . 
kUtA natpu 
ilafkEyil latcakkaNakkil wamilYY makkalY koVnYrYu kuvikkappatak kAraNamAka irunwa or araciyal kUttaNi ‘ ‘ kUtA natpu ’’ eVnYrYu kUrYi pirinwawu ; 
inYrYu ‘ ‘ oVttip pirYanwavarkalY ’’ eVnYrYu kUrYikkoVNtu makkalY munY kEkorwwu nirYkirYawu . 
ilafkEyil wanY urimEkalYE mItteVtukka porAtik koVNtirukkum wamilYY makkalYinY muyarYcikalYukku inwak kUttaNi perApawwAy mutiyum eVnYpawE vAkkAlYarkalYukku eVtuwwuk kUrYufkalY . 
kutumpa araciyal eVnYnYum naccu maram wanY verkalYEyum , vilYYuwukalYEyum valuppatuwwik koVlYlYumeyAnYAl , awu wamilYYnAttil wanYi manYiwa cuwanwirawwirYku ApawwAnYawAka amEnwuvitum eVnYpawEyum ; pawwirikEkalY , vAnYoVlikalY , woVlEkkAtcikalY , wirEppataw wayArippu , wirEppata veVlYiyItu , kirikkeVt pottikalY natawwum urimE ulYlYitta anYEwwuw woVlYYil muyarYcikalYum oVru kutumpawwinY kattuppAttirYkulY ceVnYrYa koVtiya nilEyE 2011 varE wamilYYakam anYupaviwwawEyum vAkkAlYarkalYukku ninYEvUttufkalY . 
nila apakarippu 
2006 muwal 2011 varEyilum natEpeVrYrYa wi.mu.ka. Atciyil , AlYum katciyinY nirvAkikalY , kilYE , Ur , mAvattam eVnYrYu anYEwwu nilEkalYilum AfkAfke ‘ ‘ watiyeVtuwworkalY eVllAm waNtalkArarkalYAki ’’ nila apakarippu ulYlYitta makkalYinY urimEkalYEyum , utEmEkalYEyum atiwwup parYikkum avalanilE wamilYYakawwil kANappattawE , makkalY marYanwirukka mAttArkalY . 
iruppinYum , makkalYukku anwaw wuyarafkalYE nIfkalY vItu vItAkac ceVnYrYu eVtuwwuk kUrYuvawu mikavum avaciyam . 
merYcoVnYnYa varalArYrYup pilYYEkalYEyum , manYnYikka mutiyAwa pala kurYrYafkalYEyum ceVywitta wi.mu.ka , avarYrYE makkalY manYawilirunwu akarYrYita , 2-ji alEkkarYrYE ulYlYitta pala UlYYalkalYil campAwiwwa peVrum paNawwEk koVNtu oVru cila UtakafkalY valYYiyAkavum , pawwirikEkalY valYYiyAkavum muyarYcikkirYawu . 
wIya cakwi 
inwap piracAraw wanwirawwil wIya cakwiyinY kutumpap parivArafkalY merYkoVNtirukkum muyarYcikalYE , a.wi.mu.ka. woVNtarkalYAkiya nIfkalY ufkalYutEya ayarAwa ulYYEppinY mUlam murYiyatikka veNtum . 
ufkalY anYpuc cakowariyAkiya eVnYawu Atciyil , palverYu nilEkalYilum cirYanwa mAnilamAka wamilYYnAtu vilYafki varukirYawu . 
anYEwwu kutumpafkalYum payanYpeVrYum vakEyil palverYu kurYukiya kAla marYrYum nINtakAla payanY alYikkum wittafkalYE nAnY veVrYrYikaramAka ceVyalpatuwwi irukkirYenY . 
wamilYYaka makkalY yArukkum aFcitAmal wafkalY uyirukkum , utEmEkkum pAwukAppu peVrYrYu ; cattawwinY Atci warukinYrYa camUkap pAwukAppinYEyum peVrYrYu makilYYcciyotu vAlYYkirYArkalY . 
inwa cAwanYEyE ufkalY anYpuc cakowariyinY aracu nikalYYwwi iruppawE wamilYYaka vAkkAlYarkalYukku eVtuwwuk kUrYufkalY . 
puwiya velE vAyppukalY 
inwiyAvil verYu eVnwa mAnilawwilum illAwa vakEyil wamilYYnAttil wAnY katanwa EnwANtukalYil oVnYrYarE koti puwiya velE vAyppukalY uruvAnYawEyum ; cirYu , kurYu woVlYYirYcAlEkalY inwiyAvileye wamilYYnAttil wAnY awika alYavil woVtafkappattiruppawEyum ; wakaval woVlYYilnutpaw wurYEyil wamilYYakam woVtarnwu munYnYerYik koVNtiruppawEyum pala pulYlYi vivarafkalY cuttikkAttukinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYakawwinY palverYu wittafkalYEp pArAtti mawwiya aracu katanwa EnwANtukalYil erAlYamAnYa viruwukalYEyum , paricukalYEyum valYYafki irukkirYawu . 
eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa a.wi.mu.ka. aracu nirYEverYrYi irukkum pala wittafkalYE inwiya mAnilafkalY palavum pinYparYrYa muyarYcikkinYrYanYa eVnYrYa uNmEyE wamilYYaka vAkkAlYarkalYukku vivaramAka eVtuwwuc coVllufkalY . 
a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkE inwac cAwanYEkalY woVtarum vakEyil , natEpeVrYa ulYlYa cattamanYrYap poVwuw werwalE munYnYittu , a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyinYE veVlYiyittirukkirYawu . 
wamilYYaka makkalYukkAkave nAlYworYum cinwiwwu ulYYEwwu varum ufkalY anYpuc cakowariyAkiya nAnY , AlYYnwu yociwwu inwaw werwal arYikkEyinYE wayAriwwirukkirYenY .

vivacAyak katanYkalY rawwu ; 
puwiwAka 40 Ayiram koti rUpAy vivacAyawwirYku katanYuwavi ; 
mANavarkalYinY kalvik katanY cumEyE arace erYpawu ; 
anYEwwu kutumpa attEwArarkalYukkum vilEyillA ceVlponY ;

vattiyillA culapaw wavaNE katanY vacawi warum ‘ ‘ ammA pefkif kArtu ’’ ponYrYa pala amcafkalYE ulYlYatakkiya a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyinY cirYappu amcafkalYE accittu , vItuworYum awanYEk koVNtu cerwwu , vAkku ketka veNtiya peVrum katamE a.wi.mu.ka. woVNtarkalYAkiya ufkalY oVvvoVruvarukkum irukkirYawu . 
nAnYe vetpAlYarAka nirYkirYenY 
‘ ‘ makkalYAl nAnY , makkalYukkAkave nAnY ’’ , 
‘ ‘ ufkalYAl nAnY , ufkalYukkAkave nAnY ’’ 
eVnY ninYEppeVllAm wamilYYaka makkalYinY uyarvEp parYrYiye . 
eVnY kanYaveVllAm wamilYYarkalY vAlYYvAfku vAlYYnwu cirYakka veNtum eVnYpawarYkAkave . 
eVnY muyarYcikku oVwwulYYEwwu , merYkUrYiya paNikalYE wirYampata ceVywu mutiwwu , a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalY anYEvarum makawwAnYa veVrYrYi peVrYum vakEyil , nIfkalY oVvvoVruvarum kaN wuFcAmal katamEyArYrYita veNtum eVnYrYu , eVnY uyirinYum melAnYa eVnYawarumE a.wi.mu.ka. woVNtarkalY oVvvoVruvarEyum kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
234 woVkuwikalYilum ufkalY anYpuc cakowariyAkiya nAnYe vetpAlYarAka kalYawwil nirYkirYenY eVnYrYa uNarvotu nIfkalY anYEvarum paNiyArYrYita veNtum eVnYpawE ufkalYukku mINtum ninYEvUttukirYenY . 
veVrYrYi mIwu veVrYrYi vanwu nammEc cerattum . 
ivvArYu jeVyalaliwA kUrYiyulYlYAr . iraNtu nopAlkalYAlwAnY AttawwinY mutivu eVfkalYukku cAwakamAka amEnwawu : 
leVNtil cimmanYs karuwwu - 
wi inwu 
ti20 ulakak koppE 
inwiyAvukku eVwirAnYa arEyirYuwiyil iraNtu nopAlkalYAlwAnY AttawwinY mutivu eVfkalYukku cAwakamAka amEnwawAka merYkinwiyawwIvukalY petsmenY leVNtil cimmanYs weVriviwwAr . 
ti20 ulakak koppEyil inwiyAvukku eVwirAnYa arEyirYuwi Attawwil 18 , 50 ranYkalYil AttamilYYakka veNtiya merYkinwiyawwIvukalY aNiyinY petsmenY leVNtil cimmanYs iru nopAlkalYAl Attamilirunwu wappiwwu kitEwwa vAyppE melum cirYappAka payanYpatuwwi 51 panwil 82 ranY vilYAci aNiyE veVrYrYi peVrYa vEwwAr . 
iwu woVtarpAka leVNtil cimmanYs kUrYiyawAvawu : 
iraNtu nopAlkalYwAnY Attam eVfkalYukku cAwakamAka amEya uwaviyawu eVnYrYu ninYEkkirYenY . 
woVtakka vIrarAnYa cArlas muwalil neVrukkatiyE kurYEwwAr . 
cUlYYnilEyE nanYku arYinwu koVNtu awarYku wakunwapati vilYEyAti pavuNtarikalY atiwwAr . 
pettifkil nAnY kalYamirYafkum powu eVnYnYa ceVyya veNtum eVnYpawil weVlYivAka irunwenY . 
enYeVnYil ilakkE wurawwuvawarYkAka nAfkalY wittam amEwwirunwom . 
inwa nAlY eVnYawu nAlYAka amEnwirunwawu . 
awirRtamum eVnY pakkam irunwawu . 
awanY valYYiye ceVnYrYu nAnY virumpiya AttawwE vilYEyAtinYenY . 
eVfkalY aNi wanYippatta eVnwa oVru vIrarinY AttawwEyum cArnwawillE . 
kirYis keVylukku Attam cirYappAka amEyAwa powum AttawwinY pokkE nirvakiwwu veVrYrYi kaNtulYlYom . 
peVriya ilakkE nokki wurawwum powu keVyl AttamilYYanwAlum porAti veVrYrYi peVrYum wirYanY eVfkalYitam ulYlYawu . 
anwa vakEyilAnYa AttawwE veVlYippatuwwum wirYamEyAnYa vIrarkalY aNiyil ulYlYanYar . 
irYuwippotti natEpeVrYum koVlkawwA mEwAnYam iwe ponYrYu pettifkirYku cAwakamAka irukkAwu . 
afku viwwiyAcamAnYa cUlYYnilE irukkum . 
EpieVl woVtarwAnY eVnYnYE cirYanwa vIrarAka mempata ceVywawu . 
mumpE inwiyanYs aNikkAka vAnYkate mEwAnYawwil awika AttafkalYil vilYEyAti ulYlYawAl mEwAnYawwinY wanYmEyE nanYku arYinwirunwenY . 
iwu cirYappAka ceVyalpata uwaviyawu .

ceVnYnYE : 
wamilYYakawwil velUr , warmapuri , wirucci , mawurE , pAlYEyafkottE ulYpata palverYu pakuwikalYil katanwa cila nAtkalYAkave anYal kArYrYu vIciyawu . 
awanY veVppanilEyum awikariwwu kANappattawu . 
iravu nerafkalYil kUta veVppam kurYEyAmal irunwawu . 
iwanYAl poVwumakkalY vItukalYileye mutafki kitanwanYar . 
inwa nilEyil warYpowu anYalkArYrYu vIcuvawu carYrYu kurYEnwu kANappatuvawAl wamilYYakawwinY oVru cila pakuwikalYil iwamAnYa kAlanilE nItikkirYawu . 
varum 4-nwewi aknYinatcawwiram eVnYrYa kawwiriveVyil woVtafkavirukkum nilEyil mINtum veVppakArYrYu vIca vAyppu ulYlYawA ? eVnYpawu kurYiwwu ceVnYnYE vAnYilE maNtala ArAycci mEya aluvalaka awikArikalYitam kettawarYku avarkalY alYiwwa pawil varumArYu : 
wamilYYnAttil weVrYku marYrYum weVnYkilYYakku pakuwiyilirunwu oralYavukku Irappawam kalanwa kArYrYu vIcukirYawu . 
anwa kArYrYu woVtarnwu atuwwa 2 nAtkalYukku vIcum . 
awanYkAraNamAka wamilYYakawwil atuwwa 2 nAtkalYukku anYal kArYrYu vIca vAyppu illE eVnYpawAl veVppawwinY wIviram carYrYu kurYEyum . 
kAlanilEyum iyalpE ottiye irukkum . 
kotE malYYEyE poVrYuwwavarEyil wamilYYakawwinY utpakuwiyil atuwwa 48 maNi nerawwirYkulY oVru cila pakuwikalYil itiminYnYalutanY malYYE peVyya vAyppu ulYlYawu . 
ceVnYnYEyE poVrYuwwavarEyil 94 muwal 96 tikiri varE veVppam irukkum . 
kArYrYu awikam vIca vAyppu ulYlYawu eVnYpawAl mInYavarkalYum kavanYamAka katalukku ceVnYrYu wirumpa veNtum .

vijayakAnw makkalY nalak kUttaNiyutanY utanYpAtu ceVywawAl awirupwi atEnwa eVm.eVl.e.kkalY canwirakumAr , eVs.Ar.pArwwipanY , ci.eVc.cekar marYrYum 4 mAvatta ceVyalAlYarkalY we.mu.wi.ka.vukku eVwirAka porkkoVti uyarwwinYar . 
wi.mu.ka.vutanY kUttaNi amEkka veNtum eVnYrYu valiyurYuwwiya avarkalYE katciyilirunwu vijayakAnw nIkkinYAr . 
iwE atuwwu we.mu.wi.ka.vil ulYlYa awirupwi nirvAkikalYE canwirakumAr oVnYrYuwiratti ceVnYnYEyil kUttam natawwi AlocanYE natawwinYAr . 
awil makkalY we.mu.wi.ka. eVnYrYa iyakkawwE cAnwirA kumAr walEmEyilAnYa awirupwi koRti uruvAkkiyawu . 
cAnwirA kumAr , eVs.Ar.pArwwipanY , ci.eVc.cekar ulYlYitta nirvAkikalY nerYrYu wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi , mu.ka.stAlinY AkiyorE canwiwwu wafkalYawu AwaravE weVriviwwanYar . 
appowu avarkalY cattacapE werwalil pottiyita vAyppu wArufkalY eVnYrYum veNtukolY vituwwanYar . 
awE erYrYu makkalY we.mu.wi.ka.vEc cernwa 3 eVm.eVl.e.kkalYukkum 3 woVkuwikalY oVwukka wi.mu.ka. munYvanwawu . 
awanYpati canwirakumArukku katanwa werwalil pottiyitta Irotu kilYYakku woVkuwiyum eVs.Ar.pArwwipanYukku mettUr woVkuwiyum , ci.eVc.cekarukku kummitippUNti woVkuwiyum oVwukka kettuk koVNtanYar . 
iwu woVtarpAka makkalY we.mu.wi.ka.vinYar mu.ka.stAlinYE inYrYu mINtum canwiwwu pecinYArkalY . 
awil kummitippUNti woVkuwiyil wi.mu.ka. cArpil veNu pottiyita mutivAki iruppawAl makkalY we.mu.wi.ka.vukku anwa woVkuwi oVwukkappata mutiyAwa nilEyil iruppawAka weVrivikkappattawu . 
iwe pol canwirakumAr ketkum Irotu kilYYakku woVkuwiyil wi.mu.ka. cArpil munYnYAlY amEccar muwwucAmi pottiyita iruppawAl anwa woVkuwi oVwukkuvawilum cikkal iruppawAka weVrivikkappattawu . 
melum Irotu kilYYakku woVkuwi kettu inYrYu muwwucAmi aNNA arYivAlayam vanwAr . 
avarutanY nIfkalYe pecik koVlYlYufkalY eVnYrYu wi.mu.ka. warappil canwirakumAritam weVrivikkappattawu . 
iwE atuwwu muwwucAmiyum , canwirakumArum cirYiwu neram wanYiyAka canwiwwu pecinYArkalY . 
eVnYrYAlum utanYpAtu parYrYi awikArapUrvamAka arYivikkappatavillE . 
canwirakumAr canwiwwup peciya pinYpu mu.ka.stAlinY niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
aNNA arYivAlayawwirYku vanwa makkalY we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar canwirakumAr niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
awanY viparam varumArYu : 
– kelYvi : 
mu.ka.stAlinYutanY peccuvArwwE natawwi irukkirYIrkalYe , mutivu ewum erYpattulYlYawA ? 
pawil : 
wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinYE canwiwwu pecinYom . 
makkalY we.mu.wi.ka , wi.mu.ka. kUttaNiyil iNEnwu cattamanYrYa werwalil pottiyita veNtiya avaciyam parYrYiyum , eVfkalYawu karuwwukkalY cilavarYrYEyum eVtuwwu kUrYinYenY . 
oVrucila woVkuwikalYil pottiyituvawu kurYiwwum avaritam peciyulYlYenY . 
niccayamAka kalEFaritam peci nalla mutivE coVlvawAka weVriviwwu ulYlYAr . 
eVnYave niccayamAka nalla mutivE weVrivippAr eVnYrYa nampikkE ulYlYawu . 
kelYvi : 
eVwwanYE woVkuwikalY nIfkalY kettu irukkirYIrkalY ? 
pawil : 
nAfkalY eVwwanYE itam eVnYrYu kurYippittu ketkavillE . 
ufkalYE nampi vanwu irukkirYom . 
eVfkalYukku eVnwa alYavu ceVywAl cariyAka irukkum , nallawAka irukkum eVnYpawu avarkalYukku weVriyum . 
eVfkalYE vita araciyalil nalla anYupavam vAynwavar mu.ka.stAlinY . 
eVnYave avaritam nIfkalY eVnYnYa coVlkirYIrkalYo 
awE ketka wayArAka irukkirYom eVnYrYu kUrYi irukkirYom .

woVkuwi utanYpAtu oVppanwawwil eVppowu kEyeVlYYuwwituvIrkalY ? 
pawil : 
veVku virEvil irukkum . 
kelYvi : 
eVnweVnwa woVkuwiyil pottiyituvawu eVnYrYu mutivu ceVywu vittIrkalYA ? 
pawil : 
erYkanYave nAfkalY 5 ANtu eVm.eVl.e.kkalYAka paNiyArYrYi vittom . 
eVnYave awE eVwirpArwwu varavillE . 
mINtum cattamanYrYa werwalil pottiyita veNtum eVnYrYa AcEyil vanwawAka ninYEkka veNtAm . 
makkalY we.mu.wi.ka.vukku oVru afkIkAram veNtum . 
awuvum eVwarYkAka eVnYrYAl wamilYYaka makkalY Atci mArYrYawwE virumpukirYArkalY . 
anwa Atci mArYrYawwE wi.mu.ka.val mattume koVtukka mutiyum . 
awarYkAka wamilYYaka makkalYotu nAfkalYum oVrufkiNEnwu ceVyalpata eVfkalYukku oVru vAyppu koVtufkalY eVnYrYu kettu irukkirYom .

kelYvi : 
vijayakAnwukku vicuvAcamAka iruppawAka kUrYukirYIrkalY . 
AnYAl wi.mu.ka. kUttaNiyil pottiyitumpowu neritEyAka avarEye eVwirwwu pottiyitum cUlYYnilE uruvAkume ? 
pawil : 
keptanYE eVwirwwu pottiyitum eVNNam illE . 
eVfkalYE avar eVwiriyAka pArkka veNtiya avaciyam illE . 
we.mu.wi.ka. woVNtarkalY wi.mu.ka. kUttaNiyEwAnY virumpukirYArkalY . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . caccinY kAlil vilYYunwu Aci vAfkiya yuvarAj cif vicAkappattanYam mumpE inwiyanYs aNikku eVwirAnYa pottiyil Atiya canYrEcars hEwarApAw aNiyinY vIrar yuvarAj cif , mEwAnYawwil caccinY teVNtulkarEp pArwwawum avaritam kAlil vilYYunwu vaNafki Aci peVrYrYAr . 
caccinY eVnYrYAl pAcawwEk koVttum vIrarkalYil yuvarAjum oVruvar . 
caccinY kAlil vilYYunwu vaNafkuvawE oVru campirawAyamAkave mArYrYi vittAr yuvarAj . 
eVnwa itawwilum caccinYEp pArwwuvittAl patAreVnYa kAlil vilYYunwu vitukirYAr . 
vicAkappattanYawwilum iwe campavam nerYrYu natanwawu . 
mumpE inwiyanYs aNikkum hEwarApAw aNikkum itEyilAnYa EpieVl potti nerYrYu natanwawu . 
awil Rikar wavAnY , vArnYar , yuvarAj Akiyor cirYappAka AtiyawAl hEwarApAw aNi apAra veVrYrYi peVrYrYawu . 
potti mutinwawum iru aNikalYinY vIrarkalYum peVviliyanY wirumpinYar . 
appowu pavuNtari lEnYil ninYrYapati mumpE vIrarkalYE varaverYrYuk koVNtirunwAr caccinY . 
avarEp pArwwa yuvarAj arukil ceVnYrYu takkeVnYa kAlil vilYYunwu woVttuk kumpittAr . 
yuvarAjutanY vanwu koVNtirunwa hEwarApAw vIrar kanYe villiyamcanY , yuvarAj , caccinY kAlil vilYYuvawE ninYrYu vetikkE pArwwAr . 
caccinYukkuwwAnY roVmpa cafkojamAki vittawu . 
cafkojawwil neVlYinwa caccinY , vekamAka yuvarAjEw watuwwu pitiwwu nirYuwwinYAr . 
ippottiyil Rikar wavAnY awiratiyAka Ati AttamilYYakkAmal 82 ranYkalYEk kuviwwAr . 
yuvarAj cifkum cirYappAka Ati 39 ranYkalYEk kuviwwAr eVnYpawu kurYippitawwakkawu . vAlpArYE aruke awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYcciyil kuviyum curYrYulA payaNikalY 
vAlpArYE aruke ulYlYa awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYcciyil curYrYulA payaNikalY kuvinwa vaNNam ulYlYanYar . 
awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYcci 
kovE mAvattam vAlpArYEyilirunwu keralYa mAnilam cAlakkuti ceVllum cAlEyil ulYlYa vanYappakuwiyil awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYcci ulYlYawu . 
keralYa mAnilawwinY mukkiya curYrYulA walamAka inwa nIrvIlYYcci vilYafkukirYawu . 
wamilYYaka – keralYa mAnilawwE iNEkkum pakuwiyil nIrvIlYYcci amEnwu ulYlYawu . 
ifku wamilYYakam , keralYA mattuminYrYi nAttinY palverYu pakuwikalYil irunwum curYrYulA payaNikalY awikalYavil varukirYArkalY . 
inwa nIrvIlYYcciyinY alYYaku wamilYY cinYimAvilum kAttappattu ulYlYawu . 
punYnYakE manYnYanY patawwil inwa nIrvIlYYcciyinY alYYaku palverYu koNafkalYil kAttappattawu . 
nIrvIlYYcciyil Arppariwwu koVttum waNNIr veVlYlYiuruki koVttuvawu ponYrYu mikavum rammiyamAka kAtci alYikkum . 
kulYukulYuveVnYa irukkum vAlpArYEkku varum curYrYulA payaNikalY peVrumpAlum awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYccikku ceVnYrYuwAnY wirumpuvArkalY . 
kuviyum curYrYulA payaNikalY vAlpArYEyE curYrYi pArwwu vittu colEyAr aNEppakuwi valYYiyAka awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYccikku ceVnYrYu iyarYkE alYYakE curYrYulA payaNikalY raciwwu vittu keralYa mAnilawwil ulYlYa curYrYulA walafkalYukku ceVlkirYArkalY . 
keralYa mAnilawwilirunwu awika alYavil inwa nIrvIlYYccikku varukirYArkalY . 
pinYnYar avarkalY vAlpArYE pakuwiyil ulYlYa palverYu curYrYulA walafkalYE curYrYi pArkkirYArkalY . 
wamilYYakam , keralYA mattuminYrYi inwiyAvinY palverYu pakuwikalYil warYpowu palYlYi , kallUrikalYukku kotE vitumurYE alYikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl awirappalYlYi nIrvIlYYccikku varum curYrYulA payaNikalYinY eVNNikkE awikarikka woVtafki ulYlYawu . 
veVyilinY wAkkam awikamAka ulYlYawAl nIrvIlYYcciyil waNNIr kurYEnwu kANappatukirYawu . 
ifku avvappowu lecAnYa malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
iwanYAl nIrvIlYYcci amEnwulYlYa vanYappakuwiyilirunwu kitEkkum iwamAnYa kArYrYEyum , kAlacUlYYnilEyEyum anYupavikka erAlYamAnYa curYrYulA payaNikalY kuvikinYrYanYar . varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYEc ceVyalpatuwwuvawil alatciyam kAttum awikArikalY mIwu natavatikkE : 
karnAtaka muwalvar ciwwarAmEyA 
varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYEc ceVyalpatuwwuvawil alatciyam kAttum awikArikalY mIwu natavatikkE eVtukkappatum eVnYa karnAtaka muwalvar ciwwarAmEyA eVccariwwAr . 
peVfkalYUru viwAnYa cOwAvil wifkalYkilYYamE muwalvar ciwwarAmEyA walEmEyil kUtuwal , muwanYmEc ceVyalarkalY kUttam natEpeVrYrYawu . 
iwil kalanwukoVNtu avar peciyawu : 
mAnilawwil katum varYatci erYpattulYlYawu . 
varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYukku wevEyAnYa niwiyE mAnila aracu oVwukkiyulYlYawu . 
eVnYave , awikArikalY wuriwa kawiyil varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa veNtum . 
katamE ceVyvawil alatciyam kAttum awikArikalY mIwu katum natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
patjeVttil makkalY nalaw wittafkalY pala arYivikkappattulYlYanYa . 
anwa wittafkalY mAnilawwinY eVllEyil ulYlYa katEkkoti kutimakkalYEyum ceVnYrYatEya veNtum . 
awikArikalY uriya nerawwil aluvalakawwukku vanwu poVwumakkalYinY piracnYEkalYEw wIrkka natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum . 
poVwumakkalYinY manYukkalY , pukArkalYukku uriya kAlawwil pawil alYikka veNtum . 
awikArikalY cirYappAka paNi ceVywAl mattume aracukku nalla peVyar kitEkkum . 
mAnilawwil oVrucila itafkalYil malYYE peVyyaw woVtafkiyulYlYawu . 
awuponYrYa pakuwikalYil vivacAyikalYukkuw wevEyAnYa viwEkalYE utanYatiyAka valYYafka veNtum eVnYrYAr . 
kUttawwil , walEmEc ceVyalar aravinw jAwav , kUtuwal walEmEc ceVyalar lawA kiruRNarAv ulYlYittor kalanwu koVNtanYar . karuNAniwi mIwu natikE vinwiyA wAkku

wi.mu.ka. munYpu wirutuvawarYku wittam pottArkalY .

natEpayirYci piracAram

vAkku cekarippu 
mu.ka.stAlinY wanYnYutEya vIttileye peVrumpAlum nAlYiwalYYkalYE patippawu valYYakkam .

wiNNE piracAram

koVlkawwAvil nerYrYu natEpeVrYrYa EpieVl pottiyil mINtum virAt koli , tivilliyars joti piriwwu meya 9 vikkeVttukalY viwwiyAcawwil koVlkawwAvE vIlYYwwiyawu peVfkalYUru . 
muwalil pet ceVywa koVlkawwA kampIr , pANte arEcawafkalYutanY 5 vikkeVttukalY ilYYappukku 183 ranYkalY eVtukka , woVtarnwu Atiya peVfkalYUru aNi 1 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 186 ranYkalY eVtuwwawu . 
virAt koli 75 nAttavut , tivilliyars 59 nAttavut . 
munYnYawAka kirYis keVyil 31 panwukalYil 49 ranYkalY eVnYrYu HpArmE kaNtupitiwwuk koVNtAr . 
ilakkEw wurawwum powu keVyil 7 panwukalYil 1 ranY eVnYrYu niwAnYiwwAr , AnYAl awanY pirYaku peVriya RAtkalY kEkUtinYa . 
awanY pirYaku avarukkeyuriya pANiyil pavuNtarikalY vara 21 panwukalYil 35 ranYkalYE avacarakawiyil eVtuwwAr . 
itEye virAt koli oVru arumEyAnYa inYcEtu avut RAttil eVkstrA kavaril ciks atiwwirunwAr . 
keVyil 2 cikcarkalYE atiwwa pirYaku cunYil narEnY avarE eVl.pi. ceVywu veVlYiyerYrYinYAr . 
appowu koli , tivilliyars oVnYrYucernwanYar , koVlkawwA panwu vIccE avvappowu eVccarikkEyutanY aNukumArYu pAvlA ceVywAlum avvappowu pavuNtarikalYEyum atiwwu vanwanYar . 
anYkit rAjpuw marYrYum RAkip al hacanYE tivilliyars kavanYiwwuk koVlYlYa Anwre racalE koli kavanYiwwAr .

appowu 56 panwukalYil 90 ranYkalY veVrYrYikkuw wevEppattawu . 
RAkip , cAvlA iruvarum pavuNtari koVtukkAmal iru ovarkalYE vIca awanY pirYake koli , tivilliyars mutivutanY irYafkinYar . 
koli kirIsil nirYpawEw wavirwwAr . 
iruvarum mArYi mArYi atikka 24 panwukalYil 40 eVnYrYavArYu camanYpAtu mArYiyawu . 
inwaw woVtaril wanYawu 8-vawu arEcawawwE koli eVtukka , tivilliyars 28 panwukalYil arEcawam kaNtAr . 
iruvarum iNEnwu 67 panwukalYil 115 ranYkalYEc cerkka 8 panwukalY mIwamulYlYa nilEyil peVfkalYUru veVrYrYi peVrYrYawu . 
iwanY mUlam virAt koli oVre EpieVl cIcanYil 733 ranYkalYEk kuviwwu mEk hassi , kirYis keVyilEk katanwu cAwanYE purinwulYlYAr .

10.3 ovarkalYil 90 / 1 eVnYrYu arumEyAkac ceVnYrYu koVNtirunwa powu rAyal cAlaFcars aNi pavularkalY muttukkattE pottanYar . 
10 panwukalYil 3 vikkeVttukalY cAynwawu . 
kampIr , pANte , yUcup pawwAnY Akiyor atuwwatuwwu veVlYiyerYinYar . 
125 / 5 eVnYrYa nilEyil Anwre rasal 19 panwukalYil 2 pavuNtari 3 cikcarutanY 39 ranYkalYE vilYAca , RAkip al hacanY 11 panwukalYil 18 ranYkalYE eVtukka iruvarum iNEnwu 28 panwukalYil 58 ranYkalYE vilYAca koVlkawwA cavAlAnYa 183 ranYkalYE eVttiyawu , AnYAl virattal manYnYanY virAt irukkum pArmirYku cavAl eVnYpawe illAmal ponYawu . 
AttanAyakanYAka virAt koli wernweVtukkappattAr . 
rAyal cAlaFcars peVfkalYUru 12 pulYlYikalYutanY 5-m itawwirYku munYnYerYiyawu . 
teVlli ter teVvilsE pinYnYukkuw walYlYi warYpowu nikara ranY vikiwa atippatEyil peVfkalYUru 5-m itawwirYku munYnYerYiyulYlYawu . varYatci erYpatuwwum miratci ! 
nikalYYANtil paruva malYYE mikak kurYEvAka irukkum eVnYrYu inwiya vAnYilE mEyam kaNiwwulYlYawu . 
peVyya veNtiya malYYEyalYavil 12 % kurYEvAka malYYE peVyyum eVnYpawe avarkalYawu kaNippu . 
inwak kaNippu uNmEyAka irukkum patcawwil , 1950 muwalAka inwiyA eVwirkoVlYlYa neritta varYatcikalYil iwu 12-Avawu varYatciyAka irukkum . 
munwEya kAlakattafkalYil vAnYilE mEyawwinY kaNippukalY palavum wavarYAkip ponYawuNtu . 
AnYAl , warYpowu ceVyarYkEkkolY mUlam mikaw wulliyamAka puvikkolYawwinY mArYrYafkalYEk kaNikka mutikirYawu eVnYpawAl , nikalYYANtil paruva malYYE 12 % kurYEyum eVnYrYa kaNippu poVyppawu ariwu . 
anYal kArYrYAl cumAr 2,000 per irYanwu ponYawAlum , keralYawwil woVtafka veNtiya weVnYmerYkup paruva malYYE cumAr oVru vAram walYlYip pokirYawu eVnYpawAlum mattume iwwakEya malYYEk kurYEvu , varYatci kaNikkappatavillE . 
puvi veVppa mArYupAtum oVru kAraNamAkac coVllappatukirYawu . 
merYcoVnYnYa kAraNafkalY mattume malYYEk kurYEvukkAnYa kAraNafkalY illE eVnYrYum , ivE nAnYku ANtukalYukku oVrumurYE culYYarYci murYEyil vanwu koVNtiruppawuwAnY eVnYrYum cila vallunarkalY karuwwu weVrivikkinYrYanYar . 
iwil kAraNam eVwuvAnYa powilum , malYYE valYYakkawwEvitak kurYEvAkawwAnY peVyyum eVnYpawu mattum urYuwi . 
inwa malYYEk kurYEvu kaNippu kurYiwwu mawwiya velYAN wurYE amEccar rAwA mokanY cif kUrYumpowu , 
ceVnYrYa ANtum kUta valYYakkawwEvita malYYE kurYEvAkap peVywawu eVnYrYa powilum , velYAN urYpawwi 2 % mattume kurYEnwawu ; 
inwa ANtu powumAnYa uNavuw wAnYiyafkalY , viwEkalY kEyiruppil ulYlYanYa ; 
Akave , malYYEk kurYEvu parYrYi accappataw wevEyillE eVnYrYu kurYippittulYlYAr . 
malYYEk kurYEvu allawu varYatci erYpatumpowu vivacAyam peVriwum pAwikkappatum . 
kutinIrw wattuppAtu erYpatum . 
inwa iraNtEyum or aracu camAlYiwwuvita mutiyum eVnYrYAl , anwa varYatciyE valiyinYrYik katanwuvita mutiyum . 
awarYkAnYa munYnYerYpAtukalYE ippowe mawwiya aracum , mAnila aracukalYum merYkoVNtAlwAnY varavirukkum varYatciyEc camAlYikka iyalum . 
velYANmEyEp poVruwwavarE , erYkeVnYave nirNayikkappatta ilakkukalYE eVttuvawil Arvam kAttAmal , vivacAyikalY emArYrYamatEyAwa vakEyil , varYatciyEw wAfkum payirkalYukku mattume munYnYurimE wara valiyurYuwwa veNtum . 
payirk kAppItu , kurYukiyakAla cAkupati AkiyavarYrYE Ukkappatuwwi coVttunIrp pAcanYa murYEkalYukku munY eVppowEyum vita warYpowu awikak kavanYam wara veNtum . 
isrel ponYrYa nAtukalYil mikak kurYEnwa alYavu pAcanYa nIril nirYEvAnYa cAkupati ceVyyum woVlYYilnutpafkalY kurYiwwu inwiya velYAN aluvalarkalY pala kulYYukkalYAka neril poyp pArwwu vanwapowilum , awanY wAkkam vivacAyikalYitam paravalAkac ceVnYrYu ceravillE . 
ippowAkilum awwakEya pAcanYa nIr melANmE kurYiwwa nutpafkalYE vivacAyikalYitam koVNtupoyc cerwwu , avaravar pakuwiyil , nilawwatiyil kitEkkum nIrE eVvvArYu mulYYumEyAka velYANmEkkup payanYpatuwwi , varYatciyinY wIvirawwEk kurYEkka mutiyum eVnYpawE vilYakkuvawu avaciyam . 
varYatcik kAlafkalYil , anYrYAta camEyalukkAnYa kAykarYikalYinY vilE awikarippawu iyalpu .

oVvvoVru mAvattawwilum , eVnwa alYavukku malYYE peVyyumpowu eVfkeVllAm nilawwati nIr uyarkirYawu , eri kulYafkalYil ( nila merYparappil ) wefkum nIr eVvvalYavu eVnYpawu kurYiwwa pulYlYivivaramum , malYYE kurYEyumpowu eVnweVnwak kulYam , erikalY kAynwupokinYrYanYa , eVnwap pakuwiyil katum varYatciyilum nIr varYrYAmal wafkukirYawu ponYrYa pulYlYivivarafkalYum makkalYitam peccuvalYYakkil , anYupavawwAl irukkirYawe wavira , mAvatta nirvAkawwitam AvaNamAka illE . 
wiruneVlveli keVcattiyar wayAriwwa Afkileyar eVc.Ar.pet , eVnweVnwap pakuwiyil eVnwa alYavu malYYE peVywAl eVnweVnwa cirYrYArYukalYil eVvvalYavu veVlYlYam varum , wAmiravaruNiyil eVnwa alYavu veVlYlYam varum eVnYrYu pawivu ceVywirunwAr .

iwarYkAka vAnYilE , nIr melANmE vallunarkalYEk koVNtawAka wanYiw wurYE amEkkappatuwal veNtum . wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanYE Awariwwu mawwiya manwiri smiriwi irAnYi piracAram ;

wi inwu . 
rom nakaril natEpeVrYrYa iwwAli opanY teVnYnYis makalYir irattEyar pirivil nampar oVnY jotiyAnYa inwiyAvinY cAnYiyA mircA , svitcarlAnwinY mArttinYA hifkis joti pattam veVnYrYawu .

AnYAl iwwAli opanYil raRya jotiyinY katum neVrukkatiyE camAlYiwwe koppEyE kEpparYrYa mutinwawu . jappAnYil 6.1 riktar alYavukkoVNta nilanatukkam , cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitappatavillE 
tokkiyo , jappAnYinY kinYki pirAnwiya pakuwiyil 6.1 riktar alYavukkoVNta nilanatukkam erYpattu ulYlYawu .

pacipik katarYpakuwiyil cumAr 10 kilomIttar AlYYawwil mEyam koVNtu nilanatukkam erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
nilanatukkawwinYAl cewam ewuvum erYpattawA eVnYpawu woVtarpAnYa wakavalkalY utanYatiyAka veVlYiyAkavillE... 
nilanatukkawwE woVtarnwu jappAnYil awiveka reVyil cevEyil watE erYpattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYu muwalkatta wakavalkalY veVlYiyAki ulYlYanYa . melum 9 wurYEkalYil nirYEverYrYiya wittafkalY pattiyal : 
viwi eVN 110–nY kIlYY arYiviwwa wittafkalY anYEwwum ceVyalAkkawwil ulYlYanYa jeVyalaliwA arYikkE 
ceVnYnYE ,
