iwu kurYiwwu , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwal–amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
poVy piracAram 
katanwa 5 ANtukalYil cattapperavE viwi 110–nY kIlYY nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVwuvume nirYEverYrYappatavillE eVnYa kurYrYaFcAtti karuNAniwiyum , wi.mu.ka.vinYarum poVy piracAram ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . 
110 viwikalYinY kIlYY nAnY arYiviwwavE anYEwwum ceVyalAkkawwirYku eVtuwwuk koVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
iwuvarE 20 wurYEkalYil veVlYiyitappatta arYivippukalYinY mIwu eVtukkappatta natavatikkEkalYE nAnY weVriviwwulYlYenY . 
warYpowu eVFciya 9 wurYEkalYil nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVvvArYu nirYEverYrYappattirukkinYrYanYa eVnYpawu parYrYiya vivarafkalYE nAnY alYikka virumpukirYenY . 
kAlnatE parAmarippu , pAlvalYam marYrYum mInYvalYawwurYE kAlnatE parAmarippu , pAlvalYam marYrYum mInYvalYaw wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
mInYvalYawwirYku eVnYa , ‘ ‘ mInYvalYap palkalEkkalYYakam ’’ oVnYrYu nAkappattinYawwil nirYuvappattu , ceVyalpattu varukirYawu . 
katal mInYavarkalY pAwukAppirYku watEyillA wakaval woVtarpu vacawi erYpatuwwi waruvawarYkum marYrYum vi.eVc.eVp. marYrYum eVc.eVp. karuvikalY valYYafkuvawu woVtarpAka mawwiya kampiyillA witta ANEyawwinY urimam peVrYrYita anYumawi peVrYappattulYlYawu . 
virEvil mInYavarkalYukku vi.eVc.eVp. karuvikalY valYYafkappatum . 
ceVnYnYE cewwuppattu eriyil ‘ ‘ poVlYYuwupokku wUNtil mInYpitippu marYrYum pacumE pUfkA ’’ amEkkappattu makkalY payanYpatuwwi varukinYrYanYar . 
ceVnYnYE mInYpiti wurYEmukam 75 koti rUpAy ceVlavil navInYamayamAkkappattulYlYawu . 
katal mInYavarkalYukku weciya mInYavar cemippu marYrYum nivAraNa woVkE 1,800 rUpAyilirunwu 2,700 rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu 13 katalora mAvattafkalYE cernwa 1,94,436 katal mInYavarkalYukku 34.99 koti rUpAy nivAraNawwoVkE weciya minYnYaNu paNa parimArYrYam mUlam vafki kaNakkil neratiyAka ceVluwwappattulYlYawu . 
katal mInYava makalYirukku cemippu marYrYum nivAraNa woVkE 1,800 rUpAyilirunwu 2,700 rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu , 13 katalora mAvattafkalYEc cernwa 1,76,786 katal mInYava makalYirukku 31.82 koti rUpAy nivAraNaw woVkE weciya minYnYaNu paNa parimArYrYam mUlam vafki kaNakkil neratiyAka ceVluwwappattulYlYawu . 
kurYu , cirYu marYrYum natuwwara woVlYYil nirYuvanYafkalY wurYE kurYu , cirYu marYrYum natuwwara woVlYYil nirYuvanYafkalY wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
wamilYYnAttil ulYlYa wanYiyAr nirYuvanYafkalYinY urYpawwiyE awikappatuwwuwal , potti warawwE mempatuwwuwal marYrYum wirYanY valYarwwal AkiyavarYrYE kulYYuma mempAttu wittawwinY mUlam ceVyalpatuwwa , wamilYYnAtu cirYu woVlYYil valYarcci nirYuvanYawwE wamilYYaka aracu mukavarAka niyamiwwu , 17 kulYYumafkalY ceVyalpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
iwarYkAka 10 uwavi valYarcci aluvalarkalY paNiyamarwwappattulYlYanYar . 
kiNti aracinYar woVlYYilnutpa payilakam , wiNtukkal karuvi poVrYiyiyal payilakam marYrYum viruwwAcalam pIfkAnY woVlYYilnutpa payirYci nilEyam Akiya payirYci nilEyafkalYinY utkattamEppu vacawikalY mempatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
mAnilam mulYYuvawum mAvatta woVlYYil mEyafkalYukkAnYa 11 puwiya marYrYum 18 kUtuwal kattitafkalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
woVlYYil valYarcciyil pinYwafkiyawAka arYivikkappattulYlYa pakuwikalYil amEkkappatum kurYu , cirYu marYrYum natuwwara nirYuvanYafkalY , anYEwwu pakuwikalYilum amEkkappatum kurYunwoVlYYil nirYuvanYafkalY marYrYum anYEwwu vattArafkalYilum amEkkappatum velYANcAr kurYu , cirYu marYrYum natuwwara urYpawwiw woVlYYil nirYuvanYafkalY AkiyavarYrYirYku avarYrYinY eVnwirafkalY marYrYum walYavAtafkalYukku valYYafkappatum mAnYiyam moVwwa mawippil 15 cawavIwawwilirunwu 25 cawavIwamAka awikarikkappattulYlYawu . 
puwiya woVlYYirYpettEkalY amEwwita , wamilYYnAtu cirYu woVlYYil valYarcci nirYuvanYawwinY mUlamAka nila vafki amEkka cumAr 3,044 ekkar parappilAnYa nilam kaNtarYiyappattu natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYawu . 
puwiya woVlYYirYpettEkalY amEppawil erYpatum kAla wAmawawwinYE wavirkkum poVruttu walEmEc ceVyalAlYar walEmEyil mAnila alYavilAnYa oVrYrYEccAlYara wIrvu kulYYu oVnYrYu amEkkappattulYlYawu . 
wamilYYnAtu cirYu woVlYYil valYarcci nirYuvanYawwirYku , kUtuwalAka 16 koti rUpAy aracinY pafku mUlawanYamAka valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
wiruvalYlYUr mAvattam , wirumalYYicEyil , cirYuwoVlYYil munYEvor woVlYYirYkUtafkalYE amEwwita 20 koti rUpAy ceVlavil atukkumAtiw woVlYYil valYAkam katti mutikkappattulYlYawu . 
kUtturYavu , uNavu , marYrYum nukarvor pAwukAppuwwurYE kUtturYavu , uNavu , marYrYum nukarvor pAwukAppuw wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
woVtakka velYANmE kUtturYavu katanY cafkafkalY marYrYum velYANmE urYpawwiyAlYar kUtturYavu virYpanYE cafkafkalYukku 1,166 puwiya cemippu kitafkukalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
1,24,100 meVtrik tanY koVlYlYalYavu koVNta 1,044 puwiya cemippu kitafkukalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
139 nalivatEnwa woVtakka velYANmE kUtturYavu katanY cafkafkalYil muwalkattamAka 72 cafkafkalYukku cirYappu kAcu katanY 36 koti rUpAy anYumawi valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
woVtakka velYANmE kUtturYavu katanY cafkafkalYil ulYlYa 20 Ayiram makalYir urYuppinYarkalYinY katanY peVrYum wakuwiyinYE awikarikka 2,500 rUpAy vIwam 5 koti rUpAy pafku mUlawanYa mAnYiyam urYuppinYarkalYukku valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
kUtturYavuc cafkap paNiyAlYarkalYukkum maruwwuvak kAppIttuwwittam natEmurYEppatuwwappattulYlYawu . 
vaNika varikalY marYrYum pawivuwwurYE 
vaNika varikalY marYrYum pawivuwwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
vaNikar nala vAriyawwinY urYuppinYarkalY eVNNikkE awikariwwulYlYawE karuwwil koVNtu , aracAl valYYafkappatum woVkuppu niwi 2 koti rUpAyilirunwu 5 koti rUpAyAka uyarwwappattulYlYawu . 
rANippettE , viruwwAcalam , kalYlYakkurYicci , ceVFci , arUr , ariyalUr , wiruppUr , ampAcamuwwiram , nAfkuneri marYrYum wirucceVnwUr Akiya 10 itafkalYil ulYlYa 16 vaNikavari aluvalakafkalYukkAka 12 kotiye 50 latcam rUpAy ceVlavil coVnwa kattitafkalY kattappattulYlYawu . 
elYYEkalY marYrYum natuwwara makkalY payanYpeVrYum vakEyil , uNavaka wafkumita vacawikku Atampara vari ceVluwwuvawilirunwu vilakku peVrYuvawarYkAnYa uccavarampu 199 rUpAyilirunwu 499 rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu 1–7–2013 muwal ceVyalAkkawwirYkuk koVNtu varappattulYlYawu . 
niwiwwurYE 
niwiw wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
aracu UlYYiyarkalYukku valYYafkappatum paNtikE munYpaNam 2 Ayiram rUpAyilirunwu 5 Ayiram rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
25 ANtu kAlam appalYYukkarYrYa paNiyinYE mutiwwa aracu UlYYiyarkalYukku roVkkap paricu valYYafkum wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
wamilYYnAtu aracu UlYYiyarkalY marYrYum AciriyarkalYukkAnYa akavilEppati , mawwiya aracu akavilEppatiyE uyarwwi arYivippu veVlYiyittawum , awe alYavu uyarwwi utanYukkutanY arYivippu veVlYiyitappattu varukirYawu . 
ulY , mawuvilakku marYrYum AyawwIrvEwwurYE ulY , mawuvilakku marYrYum AyawwIrvEw wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
kAvalwurYE , wIyaNEppuw wurYE marYrYum cirYEwwurYE paNiyAlYarkalYukku ‘ ‘ ufkalY coVnwa illam ’’ wittawwinY kIlYY kAFcIpuram mAvattam melakkottEyUril 2,673 vItukalY katti mutikkappattu , cIrutEp paNiyAlYarkalYukku oVwukkItu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
ariyalUr , kiruRNakiri , mawurE , civakafkE , waFcAvUr marYrYum viruwunakar Akiya 6 mAvattafkalYil walA 10 ekkar itam oVwukkItu ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
kAFcIpuram mAvattam kIlYYkottEyUr , warmapuri , rAmanAwapuram , wiruccirAppalYlYi , katalUr , nAmakkal , celam , wenYi , marYrYum wiruvaNNAmalE Akiya 8 mAvattafkalYilum nilam wervu ceVyyappattu nila mArYrYam ceVyyum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
kAval patEkku uwavuvawarYku wamilYYnAtu cirYappu kAval ilYEFar patE oVnYrYu uruvAkkappattu , ceVyalpattu varukirYawu . 
ippatEyil or ANtu paNi nirYEvu ceVywa 8,500 per wamilYYnAtu cIrutEp paNiyAlYar wervANEyawwinY poVwuwwervu mUlam iraNtAm nilE kAvalarAka , wamilYYnAtu cirYappu kAval patEyil paNi niyamanYam ceVyyappattu , warYpowu kAvalarkalYukkAnYa atippatE payirYci merYkoVNtu varukinYrYanYar . 
‘ ‘ kAval wurYEyinYarukkAka erYpatuwwappatta palpoVrulY afkAtikalY ’’ mUlam poVrutkalYE kurYEnwa vilEyil peVrYum vacawi wIyaNEppu marYrYum mItpup paNikalY wurYEyil paNipuriyum 6,800 aluvalarkalYukkum nIttikkappattulYlYawu . 
vIttu vacawi marYrYum nakarppurYa valYarcciwwurYE vIttuvacawi marYrYum nakarppurYa valYarcciw wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
ceVnYnYE – peVfkalYUr neVtuFcAlEyil ulYlYa wirumalYYicEyil , 2,160 koti rUpAy mawippIttil , 12 Ayiram atukkumAti kutiyiruppukalYutanY kUtiya wuNEkkolY nakaram amEppawarYkAnYa paNikalY natEppeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
ceVnYnYE acokpillar arukil , wamilYYnAtu vIttu vacawi vAriyawwirYku coVnwamAnYa maravelE pirivil kAliyAka ulYlYa 3.73 ekkar nilapparappil panYnYatukkumAti kutiyiruppukalY kattuvawarYkAnYa paNikalY woVtafkappattu , natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
ceVnYnYE koyampetu weVrYkAciya vilYEyAttu kUttamEppu kirAmawwil 5.6 ekkar nilaparappil panYnYatukku kutiyiruppukalY kattuvawarYku uNtAnYa ANEkalY veVlYiyitappattulYlYanYa . 
virEvil oVppanwappulYlYi korappatavulYlYawu . 
kuticEp pakuwi mArYrYu vAriyam mUlam kattappatum atukkumAti kutiyiruppukalYE nanYmurYEyil parAmarippawarYku niwi AwAram erYpatuwwum poVruttu nanwanYam pakuwiyil 17 atukku , aluvalaka valYAkam vAriya niwiyilirunwe amEwwita natavatikkE eVtukkappattulYlYawu . 
oVppanwappulYlYi korappatavulYlYawu . 
woVlYYil wurYE woVlYYil wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
kUtturYavu marYrYum poVwuwwurYE carkkarE AlEkalYil , Uwiya oVppanwawwinY kIlYY Uwiyam peVrYrYu varum paNiyAlYarkalYukku Uwiya uyarvu valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
kiruRNakiri mAvattam ocUril 2,740 ekkar parappalYavil puwiya wayArippu maNtalam nirYuvita natavatikkE eVtukkappattu nila eVtuppu natavatikkEkalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
wiruvalYlYUr mAvattawwil poVnYnYeri wAlukAvil ulYlYa kAttUr marYrYum eVprahAmpuram kirAmafkalYil ulYlYa cumAr 700 ekkar parappalYavil kanYaraka eVnwira urYpawwi mEyam oVnYrYE amEwwita natavatikkE eVtukkappattu , nilam kEyakappatuwwum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
‘ ‘ woVlYYil kattamEppu woVkuppu niwi ’’ oVnYrYu erYpatuwwappattu , cipkAt valYAkafkalYil ulYlYa woVlYYil pUfkAkkalYil utkattamEppu mempatuwwum paNikalY ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAttil muwanYmuwalAka ulaka muwalIttAlYar mAnAtu cila mAwafkalYukku munY natawwappattawu . 
iwil 2,42,160 koti rUpAy muwalItu ceVywawarYkAnYa purinwuNarvu oVppanwafkalY kEyeVlYYuwwu itappattanYa . 
iwil 45 nirYuvanYafkalY mUlam 22,595 koti rUpAy muwalItukalY ceVyyappattu palar velEvAyppukalY peVrYrYulYlYanYar . 
marYrYa nirYuvanYafkalY nilam kEyakappatuwwuvawu , niwi AwArafkalYEp peVrYuvawu ponYrYa paNikalYE merYkoVNtu varukinYrYanYar . 
virEvileye ivEkalYum wafkalY woVlYYilkalYE nirYuva natavatikkEkalYE eVtuwwu vitum . 
inwa muwalIttAlYarkalY mAnAtu natEpeVrYuvawarYku munYpe , 33 purinwuNarvu oVppanwafkalY mUlam 31,706 koti rUpAy muwalItukku vakE ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
valYYikAttum mEyam mUlam 57 wittafkalYil , 12,233 koti rUpAy IrkkappattulYlYawu . 
neVtuFcAlEkalY marYrYum cirYu wurYEmukafkalY wurYE neVtuFcAlEkalY marYrYum cirYu wurYEmukafkalY wurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
wUwwukkuti muwal kanYnYiyAkumari mAvattam aFcu kirAmam varEyil ulYlYa 113 ki.mI cAlE , iruvalYYippAwEyAka akalappatuwwi , mempAtu ceVyyum paNikalYil 6 woVkuppukalYil cAlEp paNi natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
iru woVkuppukalYil nilam kEyakappatuwwum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
celam mAvattam eVtappAti nakaril , 8.60 ki.mI. nIlYawwirYkAnYa purYavalYYic cAlE amEkkum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
civakafkE nakaril , 10.60 ki.mI. nIlYa purYavalYYiccAlE amEkka 5 kirAmafkalYil wevEyAnYa nila eVtuppu paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
ceVnYnYE peVrunakara pakuwikalYil , ulYvatta cAlEyil kOwwUr pakuwiyil irattEeri arukil peVrampUr – ceVfkunYrYam cAlE canwippil iraNtAm kattamAka , valawu purYaccAlEyil mempAlap paNi 35 koti rUpAy mawippil merYkoVlYlYappatuvawu kurYiwwa paNikkAnYa nirvAka oVppuwal aracAl valYYafkappattu mawippItu wayArikkappattulYlYawu . 
oVppanwam paricIlanYEyil ulYlYawu .

uyar nIwimanYrYawwil cuRil kumAr valYYakku - 
wi inwu 
riyo oVlimpik malyuwwa pottiyil 74 kilo eVtE pirivil inwiya warappilirunwu yAr kalanwu koVlYvawu eVnYpawil naracif yAwav , cuRil kumAr itEye mowal eVlYYunwulYlYawu . 
inwa vivakArawwil aracu walEyitAwu eVnYrYu mawwiya amEccar weVriviwwawE woVtarnwu cuRil kumAr teVlli uyarnIwimanYrYawwE nAtiyulYlYAr . 
inwiyAvinY munYnYaNi malyuwwa vIrar cuRil kumAr . 
74 kilo eVtEppirivil kalanwu koVNtu vilYEyAti varum ivar katanwa iru oVlimpikkil veVNkalam marYrYum veVlYlYi pawakkafkalY veVnYrYulYlYAr . 
ivar riyo oVlimpikkil kalanwu koVlYlYum kanYavil irunwAr . 
AnYAl riyo oVlimpikkil kalanwukoVlYlYa veNtumeVnYrYAl lAs vekAsil natEpeVrYrYa ulaka cAmpiyanYRip malyuwwa pottiyil wanYawu wirYamEyE nirUpikka veNtiya cUlYYnilEyil irunwAr . 
anwa camayawwil avarukku wolYpattEyil kAyam erYpattawu . 
iwanYAl lAs vekAs ulaka cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil cuRil kumAr kalanwu koVlYlYavillE . 
awe pirivil kalanwu koVNta naracif yAwav cirYappAka ceVyalpattu oVlimpik pottiyil kalanwu koVlYlYa wakuwi peVrYrYAr . 
inwa pirivil oVruvar mattume kalanwu koVlYlYa veNtum eVnYrYa nipanwanYE iruppawAl inwiya malyuwwa cafkam naracif yAwavE riyo pottikku anYuppuvawarYku erYpAtu ceVywawu . 
innilEyil avarukku pawilAka oVlimpik pottikku wanYnYEye anYuppa veNtum eVnYrYum , illEyeVnYil wanYakkum , naracif yAwavukkum itEyil potti vEwwu awil veVrYrYi peVrYupavarE oVlimpik pottikku anYuppa veNtum eVnYrYum korikkE vituwwAr . 
inwa korikkEyE inwiya malyuwwa cafkam erYka marYuwwuvittawu . 
iwanYAl cuRil kumAr mawwiya aracukku katiwam eVlYYuwinYAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu mawwiya vilYEyAttuwwurYE amEccar carpAnYanwA conYAvAl kUrYumpowu 
‘ ‘ inwa piraccinYEyil mawwiya aracu ceVyvawarYku oVnYrYumillE . 
inwiya malyuwwa cafkam wanYnYAtci awikAram peVrYrYawu . 
awuwAnY irYuwi mutivE eVtukkum ' ' eVnYrYAr . 
mawwiya aracu kEviriwwuvitta nilEyil cuRil kumAr teVlli uyarnIwimanYrYawwil nerYrYu manYu wAkkal ceVywAr . 
awil , oVlimpik pottikku cirYanwa vIrarE wervu ceVyvawarYku naracif yAwavutanY wAnY mowum pottiyE natawwa inwiya malyuwwa cafkawwukku uwwaravita veNtum eVnYa koriyulYlYAr . 
inwa manYu inYrYu vicAraNEkku varum eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
iwuwoVtarpAka cuRil kumAr kUrYumpowu , 
‘ ‘ yAr pafkerYka veNtum eVnYpawE erYkeVnYave mutivu ceVywirunwAl , inwiya malyuwwa cafkam eVnYnYE neril alYYEwwu weVriviwwirukkalAm . 
melum mawwiya vilYEyAttu amEccaka vilYEyAttu wittawwil irunwum eVnYawu peVyarE nIkkiyirukkalAm . 
nAnYum katanwa oVru varutamAka katumEyAka payirYci ceVywirukka veNtiyawillE . 
melum aracukkum awika paNam virEyam AkiyirukkAwu , payirYcikkAka ceVlavitta eVnYawu neram vINAkiyirukkAwu ' ' eVnYrYAr . 
iwarYkitEye malyuwwa cafkam inYrYu avaraca kUttawwukku erYpAtu ceVywulYlYawu . makArARtirawwil varYatciyE camAlYikka iraNtu nawikalYE iNEkka wittam : 
mawwiya aracu wakaval 
makArARtirawwil erYpattulYlYa varYatciyE camAlYippawarYkAka afku otum pImA marYrYum maFcArA ArYukalYE iNEkka mawwiya aracu wittamittulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu mAnilafkalYavEyil wifkalYkilYYamE ketkappatta kelYvikku , mawwiya nIrvalYaw wurYE iNEyamEccar canYvAr lAl jAt pawilalYiwwup peciyawAvawu : 
makArARtirawwil marAwvAtA , punwelkaNt ulYlYitta mAvattafkalYil katum varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
inwa varYatciyE camAlYikkum viwamAka mawwiya aracu palverYu wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwavulYlYawu . 
iwanY oVru pakuwiyAka , makArARtirawwil otum ArYukalYAnYa pImA marYrYum maFcArA AkiyavarYrYE iNEkka aracu mutivu ceVywulYlYawu . 
iwanY mUlam appakuwi makkalYukku powiya alYavu waNNIr kitEkkum . 
melum , awika varYatciyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa marAwvAtA , punwelkaNt Akiya mAvattafkalYil nilawwati nIr AwAra Ayvu marYrYum melANmEw wittawwE ceVyalpatuwwa aracu wayArAka ulYlYawu . 
iwanYpati , afku nilawwati nIrAwArafkalY kaNtarYiyappattu avarYrYEp peVrukkum natavatikkEkalY merYkoVlYlYappatum . 
melum , malYYEnIr cekarippu amEppukalY uruvAkkappatum eVnYrYAr canYvAr lAl . wamilYYaka makkalY makilYYak kUtiya mArYrYam erYpatuvawu urYuwi ; 
anYpumaNi rAmawAs arYikkE 
ceVnYnYE , wamilYYakawwil makkalY makilYYak kUtiya mArYrYam erYpatuvawu urYuwi eVnYrYu tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
pA.ma.ka. ilYEFaraNi walEvar tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs eVm.pi. , nerYrYu veVlYiyitta arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
amEwiyAnYa vAkkuppawivu 
wamilYYnAttil cattapperavEw werwal vAkkuppawivu amEwiyAka natEpeVrYrYu mutinwirukkirYawu . 
wamilYYakawwinY peVrumpAlAnYa pakuwikalYil koVttum malYYEyEyum poVrutpatuwwAmal nINta varicEyil ninYrYu vAkkalYiwwulYlYanYar . 
iwanYAl wamilYYakawwil vAkkuppawivu awikariwwirukkirYawu . 
kurYippAka nAnY pottiyitum peVnYnYAkaram woVkuwiyil wamilYYakawwileye mika awikamAka vAkkukalY pawivAki ulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYakawwil vAkkuppawivu inwa alYavu awikariwwawarYku kAraNamAnYa makkalYukku nanYrYikalY . 
munYnYerYrYawwukkAnYa vAkkukalY poVwuvAkave inwa werwalil varalArYu kANAwa alYavukku paNam vilYEyAtiyawu . 
a.wi.mu.ka.vum , wi.mu.ka.vum cernwu rU. 16 Ayiram kotikkum awikamAnYa paNawwE vAri irYEwwanYar . 
oVru ottukku rU. 500 muwal rU. 5 Ayiram varE paNam warappattawu . 
AnYAl , awarYkeVllAm mayafkAmal wamilYYaka vAkkAlYarkalY wiraNtu vanwu mArYrYawwE erYpatuwwa veNtum eVnYpawarYkAka vAkkalYiwwulYlYanYar . 
wamilYYaka vAkkAlYarkalY alYiwwa vAkku mArYrYam marYrYum munYnYerYrYawwirYkAnYa vAkku Akum . 
vAkkAlYarkalYukku nanYrYi 
wamilYYakawwinY anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilirunwum kitEkkum wakavalkalYEk koVNtu pArkkum powu 50 ANtukalYukku pirYaku wamilYYakawwil makkalY makilYYak kUtiya mArYrYam erYpatuvawu urYuwi eVnYpawu weVlYivAkirYawu . 
iwarYku viwwitta wamilYYakawwinY anYEwwu woVkuwikalYinY vAkkAlYarkalYukkum pA.ma.ka. cArpil eVnYawu neVFcArnwa nanYrYikalYE weVriviwwukkoVlYkirYenY . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYiyulYlYAr . teVlli - punYe aNikalY inYrYu mowal - 
wi inwu 
EpieVl woVtaril inYrYu iravu 8 maNikku vicAkappattinYawwil natEpeVrYum Attawwil teVlli tertevils , punYe cUpparjayaNts aNikalY mowukinYrYanYa . 
punYe aNi erYkeVnYave pilYe Ap curYrYukku munYnYerYum wakuwiyE ilYYanwu vittawAl inYrYEya AttawwinY mutivu anwa aNikku eVnwa vakEyilum pAwippE erYpatuwwAwu . 
mArYAka teVlli aNikku inwa Attam mukkiyawwuvam vAynwawAka ulYlYawu . 
11 Attawwil pafkerYrYulYlYa teVlli 6 veVrYrYikalYutanY 12 pulYlYikalY peVrYrYulYlYawu . 
pilYe Ap curYrYukku munYnYerYa veNtumAnYAl inYnYum iru veVrYrYikalYE peVrYrYAka veNtum eVnYrYa neVrukkatiyil ulYlYawu . 
teVlli aNi wanYawu katEci Attawwil 80 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil mumpEyitam wolvi kaNtirunwawu . 
awe mEwAnYawwil wAnY inYrYu punYe aNiyEyum canwikkirYawu . 
pettifkil kuyiNtanY ti kAk mattume cIrAnYa AttawwE veVlYippatuwwi varukirYAr . 
caFcu cAmcanY , karuN nAyar ulYlYitta ilYam vIrarkalY poVrYuppE uNarnwu mINtum cirYappAnYa AttawwE veVlYippatuwwum patcawwil aNikku valucerkkalAm . 
panwuvIccil jAkIrkAnYinY anYupavam kEkoVtukkirYawu . 
irYuwikkatta ovarkalYil avar nerwwiyAka ceVyalpattu varukirYAr . 
culYYarYpanwuvIccil amiw misrA palam cerkkirYAr . 
avar inwa woVtaril 13 vikkeVt kEpparYrYiyulYlYAr . 
AlravuNtar kirYis morisUm cirYanwa pafkalYippE valYYafki varukirYAr . 
avar 11 vikkeVt cAywwulYlYAr . 
punYe aNiyil rahAnYe mattume ranY cerppavarAka ulYlYAr . 
wonYi inwa woVtaril keptanYAkavum , petsmenYAkavum katumEyAka wiNarYi varukirYAr . 
koVlkawwAvukku eVwirAnYa Attawwil wonYiyAl 22 panwukalYil 8 ranYkalY mattume cerkka mutinwawu . 
awuvum teVst potti ponYrYu avarukku arukil nirYuwwappattirunwa pIltif valYEyawwilirunwu mINtu varamutiyAmal waviwwawu avarawu pettif wirYanY melum kurYEnwu varuvawEye kAttiyawu . 
cavurap wivAri , wiRarA peVrerA Akiyorum ranY kuvikka ciramappatukinYrYanYar . 
veVrYrYi peVrYrYAka veNtum eVnYrYa neVrukkati illAwawAl inYrYAvawu oralYavu cirYappAnYa AttawwE koVtukka punYe aNi muyarYcikkakkUtum eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . inwonYeRiyAvil 7.9 riktar alYavu koVNta cakwivAynwa nilanatukkam , cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattawu 
jakArwwA , inwonYeRiyAvil 7.9 riktar alYavu koVNta cakwivAynwa nilanatukkam erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
nilanatukkawwE atuwwu cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYawu . 
inwonYeRiyAvinY weVnYmerYke cakwi vAynwa nilanatukkam erYpattulYlYawu . 
iwu riktar alYavukolil 7.9 Aka pawivAkiyulYlYawu . 
cakwivAynwa nilanatukkawwE atuwwu cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYawu . 
cumawrA wIvirYku merYku pakuwiyil nilanatukkam erYpattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYu ameVrikka puviyiyal Ayvu mEyam weVriviwwu ulYlYawu . 
merYku cumawrA , vatakku cumawrA , AR Akiya pakuwikalYukku muwalkattamAka cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYawu . 
patAfkilirunwu weVnYmerYke 808 kilo mIttar woVlEvil nilanatukkam pUmikku atiyil 10 ki.mIttar AlYYawwil mEyam koVNtu erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
innilanatukkawwinYAl erYpatta cewa vivarafkalY kurYiwwa wakaval veVlYivaravillE , cewafkalY irukkakkUtum eVnYrYu ceVywikalY veVlYiyAki ulYlYawu . 
inwiyAvirYku Apawwu illE 
inwonYeRiyAvil cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYanilEyil , inwiyAvirYku Apawwu illE eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
EwarApAw nakaril ulYlYa cunYAmi munYnYeVccarikkE mEyam inwiyAvE warYpowu cunYAmi wAkkuvawarYku vAyppu illE eVnYrYu weVriviwwu ulYlYawu . 
nilanatukkawwinYAl erYpatum pAwippE unYnYippAka kavanYiwwu varuvawAkavum weVriviwwu ulYlYawu . veVllap povawu yAr ? 
15 % natunilEyAlYarkalYinY vAkkukalY yArukku ? 
1967-l natanwa wamilYYaka cattamanYrYaw werwalil wimuka veVrYrYipeVrYrYu AtciyEp pitiwwa pirYaku , wamilYYakawwil vAkkuvafki araciyal uruvAnYawu . 
1977-l natanwa wamilYYaka cattamanYrYaw werwalil aiawimuka AtciyEk kEpparYrYiya pirYaku , wamilYYakawwil vAkkuvafki urYuwi ceVyyappattawu . 
1991-l wimukavum , 1996-l aiawimukavum wamilYYaka cattamanYrYaw werwalkalYil patuwolviyEc canwiwwAlum , wafkalYinY vAkkuvafkiyE ilYYakkavillE . 
wamilYYakaw werwal kalYawwEp poVruwwavarE koVlYkEkalY , kotpAtukalY , werwal arYikkEkalY , alEkalY eVwuvum eVvviwa mArYrYawwEyum erYpatuwwivitavillE . 
wimuka marYrYum aiawimukavutanY mArYi mArYi kUttaNi vEkkum katcikalYinY vAkkuvafki , iraNtu katcikalYukkum camanilEyE erYpatuwwiyulYlYanYa . 
AlYufkatcikku eVwirAnYa eVwirmarYE vAkkukalYwAnY katanwa 5 cattamanYrYaw werwalkalYilum veVrYrYi wolviyEw wIrmAnYiwwulYlYanYa . 
AnYAl inwa murYE , kUttaNiyAkac ceVyalpatum eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatta katcikalY pirinwu nirYkinYrYanYa . 
awanYAl , vAkkuvafkic camanilE pAwikkappattu , AlYufkatcikku eVwirAnYa vAkkukalYum piriyum cUlYYal erYpattulYlYawu . 
vAkkuvafki eVnYpawu wamilYYakam mulYYumEkkumAnYa cawavikiwamAkap pArkkappatukirYawu . 
AnYAl , vAkkuvafkiyEw wIrmAnYippawu vAkkuc cAvatikalYwAnY . 
oVru kurYippitta vAkkuccAvatiyil 1300 vAkkAlYarkalY irunwAl , avarkalYil 300 - 350 per aiawimukavinYarAkavum , 275 - 325 per wimukavinYarAkavum ulYlYanYar . 
paNavalimEyAl , vAkkuc cAvati vAkkuvafkiyEw wimukavum aiawimukavum urYuwippatuwwivittanYa . 
pirYa katcikalYEc cernwavarkalY oVttumoVwwamAkak kUtinYAlum , 150 - 250 per varE mattume ulYlYanYar . 
125 - 175 per natunilEyAlYarkalYAka ulYlYanYar . 
mIwi per AkkalYikka mAttArkalY . 
wamilYYaka vAkkuccAvatikalYil 85 cawavikiwam , merYpati kaNakkIttinYpatiwAnY katcikalYinY palam ulYlYawu . 
wemuwikavinY vAkkuvafki anYEwwu vAkkuc cAvatikalYilum paravalAka irunwAlum , wimukavEyum aiawimukavEyum munwukirYa alYavukku illE . 
mawimuka , pAjaka , pAmaka , wamAkA , vituwalEc cirYuwwEkalY , itawucArikalY yAvarukkum kurYippitta cila vAkkuc cAvatikalYil vAkkuvafki valimEyAka ulYlYawu . 
AnYAl , awe ponYrYa valimEyAnYa vAkkuc cAvatikalY woVkuwi mulYYuvawum illE eVnYpawAlwAnY , avarkalYAl wanYiwwu veVrYrYi peVrYa mutiyAwa cUlYYal ulYlYawu . 
merYpati vAkkuvafkik kaNakkIttEw wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum virivupatuwwip pArwwAl , awimukavukku 30 cawavikiwam muwal 35 cawavikiwam varEyilum , wimuka - kAfkiras kUttaNikku 28 cawavikiwam muwal 33 cawavikiwam varEyilum , wemuwika – makkalYnalakkUttaNi – wamAkAvukku 15 muwal 20 cawavikiwam varEyilum , pAjaka marYrYum pAmakavukku 3 muwal 6 cawavikiwam varEyilum vAkkuvafki pawivAkalAm . 
nAm wamilYYar katciyinY vAkkuvafki inwaw werwalilwAnY weVriyavarum . 
merYpati vAkkuvafkiyEk koVNtirunwAl mattum , wimukavum awimukavum AtciyEp pitiwwuvita mutiyAwu . 
enYeVnYil , natunilEyAlYarkalY 15 cawavikiwam yArukku vAkkalYippArkalY eVnYpawuwAnY ippowEya muwanYmEyAnYa eVwirpArppAkum . 
natunilEyAlYarkalYEp poVruwwavarEyil , mUnYrYu viwamAkac cinwiwwuwwAnY iwuvarE vAkkalYiwwu irukkirYArkalY , 
1. nermEyAnYavarkalYukkum puwiyavarkalYukkum vAkkalYippawu . 
2. veVrYrYipeVrYap pokum aNikku vAkkalYippawu . 
3. AlYufkatcikku eVwirAka , eVwirmarYEyAka vAkkalYippawu . 
pAjaka marYrYum pAmakavEp poVruwwavarE , woVkuwi vAriyAka 30 muwal 35 cawavikiwam vAkkukalYEp peVrYuvawarYkuriya vAkkuvafki illE eVnYpawAl , ivarkalYAl AtciyEp pitikkamutiyAwu . 
AnYAl , kurYippitta cila vAkkuc cAvatikalYil palamAnYa vAkkuvafkiyEp peVrYrYulYlYawAl , anwak kurYippittaw woVkuwikalYE veVlvawarYkAnYa vAyppukalY ulYlYanYa . 
AnYAl , wimuka marYrYum aiawimuka inwaw woVkuwikalYil kUtuwal kavanYam ceVluwwukinYrYanYa eVnYpawum kavanYikkappata veNtiyawAka ulYlYawu . 
wemuwika – makkalY nalak kUttaNi – wamAkA , aiawimuka marYrYum wimukavukku atuwwu vAkkuvafkiyEp peVrYrYulYlYanYa . 
AnYAl , ivarkalY vacamulYlYa 20 cawavikiwa vAkkukalY 35 cawavikiwamAka mArYuvawu eVppati ? 
puwiya vAkkAlYarkalY wafkalY aNikku vAkkalYippArkalY eVnYrYu nampukirYArkalY . 
nermEyAnYavarkalYukkum puwiyavarkalYukkum vAkkalYikka veNtum eVnYrYu ninYEkkirYa natunilEyAlYarkalY , ivarkalY pakkam cAyvawarYku vAyppukalY uNtu . 
awecamayam , AlYufkatcikku eVwirAnYa eVwirmarYE vAkkukalYum ivarkalYukkuc ceVlvawarYku vAyppukalY uNtu . 
eVnYinYum , kurYEvAnYa vAkkukalY viwwiyAcawwil veVrYrYiyE ilYYakkap pokum woVkuwikalY ivarkalYukku nirYEyave ulYlYanYa . 
wimuka , aiawimukavukku mArYrYAnYavarkalY veNtum eVnYrYa puwiya puratci alE oVnYrYu wamilYYaka makkalY manYawwil uruvAki irukkume AnYAl , ivarkalY veVlvawarYku vAyppu uNtu . 
AnYAl ArYu mAwawwil anwap puratci alE erYpattirukkumA ? eVnYrYa canwekam eVlYYunwAlum , wimuka , aiawimukavinY veVrYrYi wolvikalYE nirNayikkappokum ArYrYal utEyavarkalY eVnYpawE urYuwiyAka meVyppikkappokirYArkalY . 
aiawimukavEp poVruwwavarE ammA kutinIr , ammA uNavakam ponYrYa nalla wittafkalYukkum , ilavacaw wittafkalYukkum makkalY vAkkalYippArkalY eVnYrYu AlYufkatciyinYar ninYEkkalAm . 
AnYAl , katanwa Enwu cattamanYrYaw werwalkalYilum eVwirmarYEyAlYar vAkkukalYe veVrYrYi wolviyE nirNayiwwulYlYanYa eVnYpawE marYanwuvita mutiyAwu . 
2014-l natanwa makkalYavEw werwalil wanYiwwu ninYrYu veVrYrYipeVrYrYawum aiawimukavinY wanYnYampikkEyAka irukkalAm . 
AnYAl , makkalYavEw werwal verYu , cattamanYrYaw werwal verYu eVnYpawEwwAnY wamilYYaka makkalY palverYu werwalkalYil pAtamAkac coVlliyirukkirYArkalY . 
vAkkuvafki valimE illAwa katcikalYutanY kUttaNiyum AlYufkatcikkup pinYnYatEvEw waralAm . 
eVlYiwil canwikka mutiyAmE , 
iraNtAm kattaw walEvarkalYe illAmal ceVywuvittawu , 
werwal nerawwil mattume makkalYEc canwippawu , 
UlYYal kurYrYaccAttukalY , 
AlYufkatcikku eVwirAnYa vAkkukalY ponYrYa parappurEkalYEw wANti aiawimuka veVrYrYipeVrYrYuvittAl , akkatciyinY vAkkuvafki acEkka mutiyAwa ArYrYalAkivittawu eVnYrYu urYuwiyAka nampalAm . 
wimukavEp poVruwwavarE , 2014 makkalYavEw werwalil oVru woVkuwiyilkUta veVrYrYipeVrYa mutiyAmal ponYAlum , wafkalYukkAnYa 90 latcam vAkkukalYEp peVrYrYuvittawAl , wanYawu vAkkuvafki palYYuwAkivitavillE eVnYrYa nampikkEyutanY ulYlYawu . 
ilafkEw wamilYYarukku eVwirAnYa katci eVnYrYu muwwirE kuwwappatta pirYakum , kAfkiras katci 2014 makkalYavEw werwalil , wamilYYakawwil 17 latcam vAkkukalYEp peVrYrYu , wanYnYutEya vAkkuvafkiyE cirYukavenYum meVyppiwwulYlYawu . 
AnYAl , wamAkAvinY pirivu eVnwa alYavukku vAkkuvafkiyEp piriwwirukkarYawu eVnYpawu inwaw werwalilwAnY weVriyum . 
wamilYYaka natunilE vAkkAlYarkalY AlYufkatcikku eVwirAkawwAnY vAkkalYippArkalY eVnYrYa nampikkEyum ivarkalYukku ulYlYawu . 
AnYAl , kutumpa araciyal , 2ji alEkkarYrYE murYEketu kurYrYaccAttu , ilafkEw wamilYYar patukoVlEyinYpowu meVwwanYam ponYrYa nikalYYvukalYE natunilEyAlYarkalY marYanwuvittirunwAl , ivarkalYinY veVrYrYiyum kelYvikkurYiyE eVlYYuppAwu . 
wamilYYakaw werwal kurYiwwu varukirYa karuwwuk kaNippukalY nampukirYa vakEyil illE . 
enYeVnYil , natunilEyAlYarkalY yArukku vAkkalYippawu eVnYpawE inYnYum mutivu ceVyyavillE . 
15 cawavikiwa natunilEyAlYarkalYinY vAkkukalY oVttumoVwwamum oVre aNikku vilYYunwuvitappovawillE . 
anwa vAkkukalYum ciwarYappokinYrYanYa . 
nottAvilum vilYYappokinYrYanYa . 
AnYAl , araciyal katcikalYinY vAkkuvafkiyE veVrYrYivafkiyAka mArYrYakkUtiya vallamE ivarkalYitam mattumwAnY uNtu . 
iwuvarE veVrYrYipeVrYappokum aNikke vAkkalYiwwu vanwa natunilEyAlYarkalY , inwa murYE wafkalYinY vAkkukalY mUlam veVrYrYipeVrYum aNiyEw wIrmAnYikkappokirYArkalY .

inwiya makalYir aNi veVrYrYi -

makalYirukkAnYa upar koppE pAtmiNtanY pottiyil inwiyA muwal Attawwil AswireliyAvE 5-0 eVnYrYa kaNakkil vIlYYwwiyawu . 
cInYAvinY hUnYRAnY nakaril natEpeVrYrYu varum inwa pottiyil oVrYrYEyar pirivil waravaricEyil 8-vawu itawwil ulYlYa inwiyAvinY cAynYA neVvAl , 74-vawu itawwil ulYlYa AswireliyAvinY hacunY - yu veVNti ReVnYE 22-20 , 21-14 eVnYrYa nerceVttil vIlYYwwinYAr . 
iraNtAvawu Attawwil pi.vi.cinwu 21-12 , 21-11 eVnYrYa nerceVttil jAy lAyE worYkatiwwAr . 
inwa Attam veVrYum 25 nimitafkalYil mutivatEnwawu . 
iwanYAl 2-0 eVnYa inwiyA munYnYilE vakiwwawu . 
irattEyar pirivil inwiyAvinY jUvAlA kattA-asvinYi poVnYnYappA joti , AswireliyAvinY hacunY - kuronYyA jotiyE 21-9 , 21-15 eVnYrYa nerceVttil worYkatiwwawu . 
atuwwu natEpeVrYrYa oVrYrYEyar pirivu Attawwil inwiyAvinY ruwvikA RivAnYi 21-5 , 21-11 eVnYrYa kaNakkil tipAnYiyE veVnYrYAr . 
katEciyAka natEpeVrYrYa irattEr pirivu Attawwil inwiyAvinY Rikki reVtti , pi.vi.cinwu joti 21-12 , 21-12 eVnYrYa kaNakkil jAy lAy - lianYe jotiyE vIlYYwwiyawu . 
inwiya makalYir aNi wanYawu iraNtAvawu Attawwil jeVrmanYiyutanY inYrYu mowukirYawu . varYatciyAl erYpatta poVrulYAwAra ilYYappu rU. 6,50,000 koti - 
katanwa iru ANtukalYil nAttil erYpatta varYatciyAl wecawwukku rU. 6 latcawwu 50 Ayiram koti poVrulYAwAra ilYYappu erYpattulYlYawu eVnYrYu weVriyavanwulYlYawu . 
iwu woVtarpAka inwiya woVlYYil varwwakak kUttamEppu aNmEyil natawwiya Ayvil melum kUrYappattulYlYawAvawu : 
nAttil katanwa iru ANtukalYAka paruvamalYYE powiya alYavu illE . 
aNEkalY , nIrwwekkafkalY peVrumalYavil varYaNtu kANappatukinYrYanYa . 
nilawwati nIrum kurYEnwuvittawu . 
iwanYAl makArARtiram , karnAtakam ulYlYitta 10 mAnilafkalYil katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
varYatciyAl 256 mAvattafkalYEc cernwa 33 koti per katumEyAka pAwikkappattulYlYanYar . 
iwanYAl wecawwukku poVrulYAwArarIwiyAka rU. 6 latcawwu 50 Ayiram koti ilYYappu erYpattulYlYawu . 
eVnYinYum inwa ANtu paruvamalYYE valYYakkamAnYa alYavil irukkum eVnYrYu vAnYilE Ayvu mEyam kaNiwwulYlYawAl , wecawwinY poVrulYAwAra ilYYappu kurYEyum . 
paruva malYYE poVywwuppovawu , varYatci ponYrYa kAraNafkalY camUka , poVrulYAwAra alYavil palverYu woVtar vilYEvukalYE erYpatuwwukinYrYanYa . 
varYatci pakuwikalYil powiya uNavu , kutinIr kitEkkAwawAl peVNkalY , kulYYanwEkalYinY utalnilE pAwikkappatukirYawu . 
uNavu , wAnYiya urYpawwi kurYEvawAl avarYrYinY vilEkalY uyarnwu nAttil paNavIkkam awikarikkirYawu . 
iwu aracukku peVrum neVrukkatiyE alYikkirYawu eVnYrYu anwa Ayvil cuttikkAttappattulYlYawu . werwal ANEyam janYanAyaka murYEyil werwalE natawwavillE : 
vijayakAnw kurYrYaccAttu - 
wi inwu 
werwal ANEyam janYanAyaka murYEyil werwalE natawwavillE eVnYrYu wemuwika walEvar vijayakAnw kurYrYaccAttiyulYlYAr . 
wemuwika walEvar vijayakAnw nerYrYu veVlYiyitta arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
wamilYYaka cattapperavEw werwalE janYanAyaka murYEyil werwal ANEyam natawwavillE . 
puwiya vAkkAlYarkalY , ilYam walEmurYEyinYar , natunilEyAlYarkalYitam wemuwika - makkalY nalakkUttaNi wamAkA aNi erYpatuwwiya wAkkawwE poVrYuwwuk koVlYlYa mutiyAwa awimukavum , wimukavum palverYu murYEketukalYil ItupattanYa . 
wamilYYakawwinY anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum paNam viniyokam ceVyyappattawu . 
iwu woVtarpAka alYikkappatta pukArkalY mIwu werwal ANEyam eVnwa natavatikkEyum eVtukkavillE . 
vAkkuccAvatikku vanwa vAkkAlYarkalYukku uriya pAwukAppu alYikkappatavillE . 
wemuwika vetpAlYarkalY , avarkalYutEya kutumpawwinYar , wemuwika werwal aluvalakam mIwu awimukavinYar wAkkuwal natawwinYar . 
wamilYYakam mulYYuvawume paNap pattuvAtA ceVyyappatta nilEyil , aravakkurYicci marYrYum waFcE woVkuwikalYil mattum werwal walYlYi vEkkappattulYlYawu erYkawwakkawu alla . 
cattapperavEw werwal mutivukalY 19-m wewi veVlYiyAka ulYlYa nilEyil , aravakkurYicci , waFcAvUr Akiya woVkuwikalYil 23-m wewi vAkkuppawivu natEpeVrYum eVnYrYu werwal ANEyam arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
iwu wirumafkalam , cafkaranY koyil , srIrafkam , Ar.ke.nakar itEwwerwal vakEyileye mINtum amEyum . 
eVnYave , 19-m wewikku munYpe iru woVkuwikalYilum werwalE natawwa veNtum . 
ivvArYu arYikkEyil kUrYappattulYlYawu . stArk , hecilvuttutanY kaminYsum iNEnwAl Asi.yE kaNtu eVwiraNikalY aFcum : 
riyAnY hAris - 
wi inwu . 
kAyawwinYAl pAwikkappattu aNikkulY varuvawum povawumAka irunwu varum Aswireliya vekappanwu vIccAlYar pet kaminYs warYpowu mulYYumEyAka kuNamatEnwu vittAr . 
virEvil aswireliyA e aNikkAka pet kaminYs mINtum teVst pottikalYukkuriya panwil vIca varukirYAr eVnYrYu avar kAyawwilirunwu mIlYavum wanYawu palYYEya vekappanwu vIccE mINtum peVrYavum uwaviya vekappanwu vIccAlYar riyAnY hAris weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
pet kaminYs otivanwu panwE vIcum viwam kAyafkalY erYpata peVrum kAraNamAka amEnwawE atuwwu riyAnY hAris avarawu panwu vIccu murYEyil puwumEyEp pukuwwiyulYlYAr . 
oVru murYE ifkilAnwinY pilYiNtAHp kAyawwilirunwu wappa valYYi weVriyAwu watumArYiya powu , AlanY tonYaltu avarukku uwavi purinwAr . 
awAvawu panwu vIcum powu munYnYafkAlE nanYrYAkaw wUkki warEyil atippawum , appowu valawu kAl pAwam pakkavAttil wirumpiyiruppawu pilYiNtAHp kAyafkalYukku pirawAnYa kAraNam eVnYrYu kaNtarYinwa weVnY Appirikka munYnYAlY vekappanwu vIccAlYar AlanY tonYaltu , munYnYafkAlE awikam wUkkAmal nerAka vEwwuk koVlYlYavum , valawu pAwam pakkavAttil wirumpAmal awuvum panwu vIcum powu nerAka varumArYu wiruwwi amEwwAr . 
awanY pirYake avar rivars svifkil peVriya alYavukku ulaka vIrarkalYE accurYuwwinYAr . 
AswireliyAvE patuwwi eVtuwwAr pilYiNtAHp . 
warYpowu inwak koNawwilwAnY pet kaminYs atikkati kAyamatEyAmal irukkavum AnYAl vekawwEk kurYEkkAmal vIcavum riyAnY hAris uwavi purinwulYlYAr . 
innilEyil pet kaminYs kurYiwwu riyAnY hAris kUrYumpowu , 
“ avarAl inYnYamum eVnYnYa mutiyum eVnYpawE ninYEkkum powu accamUttuvawAka ulYlYawu . 
avaritam accamUttum oVru wirYamE ulYlYawu . 
oVrunAlY pottikalYil avar oti vanwu nalla vekawwutanY vIciyawEp pArwwom . 
niccayam ippowu puwwuNarvu peVrYrYu puwiya panwu vIccu murYEyutanY kalYam kANum pet kaminYs , Aswireliya aNikku mikap peVriya varappiracAwamAkaw wikalYYvAr . 
awuvum mitceVl stArk , joR hecilvut , jems pettinYcanY AkiyorutanY ivarum cernwAl eVnwa oVru aNiyum Aswireliya aNiyE canwikka accafkoVlYlYum . 
panwu vIccil AkRanY carivara amEyavillE eVnYil kAyafkalY erYpatuvawu iyalpu . 
AnYAl warYpowu puwwuNarvu peVrYrYu Aswireliya aNikkAka Ata mulYYu urYcAkawwutanY wayArAka ulYlYAr kaminYs ” eVnYrYAr riyAnY hAris . mAnilam mulYYuvawum 29 Ayiram kirAmafkalY varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYAka arYivikkappatum

mumpE , 
mAnilam mulYYuvawum 29 Ayiram kirAmafkalY varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYAka arYivikkappatum eVnYrYu Ekorttil mAnila aracu weVriviwwawu . 
waNNIr parYrYAkkurYE 
marAttiyawwil nilavum kutinIr wattuppAttE pokka wakunwa natavatikkEkalY eVtukka mAnila aracukku uwwaravita kori palverYu poVwunala manYukkalY mumpE Ekorttil woVtarappattanYa . 
iwanYE vicAriwwa Ekorttu , kutinIr wattuppAttE pokka marAttiya aracu merYkoVNtu varum natavatikkEkalYE weVriyappatuwwumArYu uwwaravittawu . 
iwanYperil , inwa valYYakku camIpawwil mINtum vicAraNEkku vanwawu . 
appowu , marAttiya aracu warappil wAkkal ceVyyappatta piramANappawwirawwil , ‘ ‘ mAnilawwil 29 Ayiram kirAmafkalY varYatciyAl pAwikkappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
ivE anYEwwum varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwiyAka arYivikkappatum . 
2009–m ANtEya varYatci melANmE wittawwinYpati , nivAraNam valYYafkappatum ’’ eVnYrYu kUrYappattirunwawu . 
anYEwwu mAvattawwukkum cAwwiyamalla 
melum , varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil palverYu nalawwittafkalYE katanwa vAram wIviramAka natEmurYEppatuwwiyawAkavum , waNNIr parYrYAkkurYEyE kattuppatuwwa palverYu natavatikkEkalYE eVtuwwu varuvawAkavum awil kurYippitappattulYlYawu . 
awecamayam , anYEwwu mAvattafkalYukkum aracAl waNNIr vinYiyokam ceVyvawu cAwwiyamarYrYawu eVnYrYum , irunwAlum , cIrAnYa atippatEyil waNNIr vinYiyokam ceVyyappatum eVnYrYum atvaket jeVnYaral rokiw wiyo vAwittAr . 
vAwawwE kettarYinwa nIwipawikalY , atuwwakatta vicAraNEyE varukirYa 24–nwewikku walYlYivEwwanYar . hariR rAvaw mINtum muwalvarAkirYAr 
puwuteVlli , me . 11 – 
uwwarakANt mAnila cattacapEyil Atcikku eVwirAnYa palapparItcEyil kAfkiras katci veVrYrYi peVrYrYawE atuwwu , janYAwipawi AtciyE vApas peVrYuvawAka mawwiya aracu cuprIm korttil inYrYu weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
iwEyatuwwu , ammAnilawwil janYAwipawi Atci rawwu ceVyyappattawu . 
muwalvarAka hariR rAvaw mINtum pawavi erYkirYAr . 
uwwarakANt mAnilawwil hariR rAvaw walEmEyilAnYa kAfkiras aracukku eVwirAka akkatciyEc cernwa 9 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY ceVyalpattanYar . 
avarkalYE capAnAyakar wakuwi nIkkam ceVywu uwwaravittAr . 
iwanYAl nampikkE vAkkeVtuppu natawwi peVrumpAnYmEyE nirUpikka veNtiya cUlYYnilE aracukku erYpattawu . 
inwa nilEyil awirupwi eVm.eVl.e.kkalYutanY hariR rAvaw peram peciyawAka kurYrYam cAttappattawu . 
iwE kAraNam kAtti afku janYAwipawi Atci amalpatuwwappattawu . 
iwu woVtarpAnYa valYYakkil uwwarakANt cattacapEyil nerYrYu ( ceVvvAykkilYYamE ) nampikkE vAkkeVtuppu natawwa cuprIm korttu uwwaravittawu . 
wakuwi nIkkam ceVyyappatta 9 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY wafkalY mIwAnYa natavatikkEyE rawwu ceVyyakkori uwwarakANt Ekorttil munYnYar manYuwAkkal ceVywu irunwanYar . 
Ekorttu nIwipawi wayAnYi pirYappiwwa uwwaravil , hariR rAvaw Atcikku eVwirAnYa awirupwi eVm.eVl.e.kkalYE wakuwi nIkkam ceVywa capAnAyakarinY natavatikkE ceVllum eVnYrYum , 9 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY cArpil wAkkal ceVyyappatta manYuvE walYlYupati ceVyvawAkavum arYiviwwAr . 
EkorttinY inwa wIrppE eVwirwwu 9 awirupwi eVm.eVl.ekkalY cArpil cuprIm korttil melmurYEyItu ceVyyappattawu . 
ivarkalYinY manYuvE avacara manYuvAka karuwi vicArikka veNtum eVnYrYum korikkE vitukkappattawu . 
inwa manYuvE vicAriwwa nIwipawikalY 9 eVm.eVl.ekkalYE wakuwi nIkkam ceVywa capAnAyakarinY natavatikkE ceVllum eVnYrYa uwwarakANt Ekorttu uwwaravukku watE viwikka marYuwwuvittanYar . 
melum , nampikkE vAkkeVtuppil 9 eVm.eVl.ekkalYum kalanwukoVlYlYa mutiyAwu eVnYrYum weVriviwwanYar . 
cuprIm korttu erYkanYave pirYappiwwulYlYa uwwaravinY atippatEyil uwwarakANt mAnila cattacapEyil nampikkE vAkkeVtuppu natakkum eVnYa arYiviwwa capAnAyakar iwarYkAnYa cirYappu kUttawwukku erYpAtu ceVywAr . 
wakuwinIkkam ceVyyappatta 9 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY cattacapEkku varamutiyAwa nilEyil cattacapEyil warYpowEya moVwwa urYuppinYarkalYinY palam 61Aka ulYlYawu . 
iwil , kAfkiras katcikku 27 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY ulYlYanYar . 
cattacapEyil peVrumpAnYmEyE nirUpikka 32 eVm.eVl.e.kkalYinY Awaravu wevE eVnYrYa nilEyil pi.ti.pi , katciyE cernwa ArYu eVm.eVl.e.kkalY wanYawu walEmEyilAnYa Atcikku Awaravu weVrivippawAka hariR rAvaw kUrYi vanwAr . 
eVwirkkatciyAnYa pArawIya janYawAvukku 28 eVm.eVl.e.kkalY ulYlYa nilEyil nerYrYEya nampikkE vAkkeVtuppu inwiya araciyal arafkil peVrum eVwirpArppE erYpatuwwiyawu . 
innilEyil , nerYrYu kAlE cattamanYrYawwinY cirYappu kUttam woVtafkiyawu . 
neVrYrYiyil wilakawwutanY cattamanYrYawwukku vanwa hariR rAvaw , makkalY eVfkalYutanY irukkirYArkalY . 
kewarnAw , kafkowri , yamunYowri , pawrinAw AlayafkalYil ulYlYa weVyvafkalYinY AciyutanY inwa vAkkeVtuppil nAfkalY veVrYrYi peVrYuvom eVnYa nampikkE weVriviwwAr . 
kAlE 10.30 maNiyalYavil hariR rAvawwinY AtciyinYmIwu nampikkE korum vAkkeVtuppu woVtafkiyawu . 
cattacapE marYrYum pArAlYumanYrYa vivakArafkalYukkAnYa muwanYmE ceVyalAlYar merYpArvEyil natEpeVrYrYa inwa vAkkeVtuppil cattacapEyil AjarAnYa 61 eVm.eVl.e.kkalYum AtciyE Awariwwum , eVwirwwum wafkalYawu kEkalYE uyarwwi , vAkkalYiwwanYar . 
cumAr panYnYireVNtu maNivarE nItiwwa nerYrYEya vAkkeVtuppu hariR rAvawwinY Atcikku cAwakamAkave amEnwawAkavum , wafkalYawu AtciyE eVwirkkum pArawIya janYawAvinY muyarYci wolviyil mutinwawAkavum vAkkeVtuppil pafkerYrYa kAfkiras eVm.eVl.ekkalY weVriviwwanYar . 
vAkkeVtuppukku pinYnYar ceVywiyAlYarkalYE canwiwwa hariR rAvaw , uwwarakANtE curYrYiyulYlYa nampakawwanYmEyarYrYa mekafkalY nAlYE ( inYrYu ) marYEnwuvitum eVnYa kurYippittAr . 
inwa vAkkeVtuppinY viparawwE arYikkEyAka wayAriwwa cattacapE marYrYum pArAlYumanYrYa vivakArafkalYukkAnYa muwanYmE ceVyalAlYar , anwa arYikkEyE cIlitta kavarukkulY pottu inYrYu anwa kavarE cuprIm korttil camarppiwwAr . 
innilEyil , inYrYu cuprIm korttil AjarAnYa mawwiya aracinY walEmE valYYakkarYiFar mukul rohatki , uwwarakANt cattacapEyil nerYrYu natEpeVrYrYa nampikkE vAkkeVtuppil hariR rAvaw wanYakkulYlYa peVrumpAnYamEyE nirUpiwwulYlYawAka kurYippittAr . 
33 eVm.eVl.e.kkalYinY AwaravutanY avar veVrYrYipeVrYrYawAkavum avar weVriviwwAr . 
iwEyatuwwu , ammAnilawwil natEmurYEyil irukkum janYAwipawi AtciyE inYrYe wirumpappeVrYa mawwiya aracu mutiveVtuwwulYlYawAkavum avar weVriviwwAr . 
mawwiya aracinY inwa mutivE varaverYpawAka hariR rAvawwinY cArpil inwa valYYakkil AjarAnYa pirapala vakkIl kapil cipal weVriviwwAr . 
iwE erYrYukkoVNta cuprIm kort , uwwarakANtinY muwalvarAka hariR rAvaw mINtum pawavi erYka anYumawiyalYiwwawu . 
iwanY mUlam , uwwarakANttil warYpowu amalil ulYlYa janYAwipawi Atci inYrYu rawwu ceVyyappatum . 
hariR rAvaw walEmEyilAnYa kAfkiras amEccaravE virEvil afku pawavi erYkum eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . virAt koliyinY ‘ mAstar kilYAs ’ mUlam nirYEya karYrYukkoVNtenY : 
stIv smiw 
- wi inwu . 
camIpawwil mutinwa ulakakkoppE ti20 pottiw woVtaril AswireliyAvE veVlYiyerYrYiya koliyinY arumEyAnYa 82 ranY inYnYifs wanYakku nirYEya karYrYuk koVtuwwawAka Aswireliya keptanY stIv smiw kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
anYrYu virAt koli 39 panwukalYil 50 ranYkalYE eVtuwwAr , awanY pirYaku 12 panwukalYil melum 32 ranYkalYE vilYAci 5 panwukalY mIwamulYlYa nilEyil inwiyAvukku veVrYrYi wetiw wanwAr , 
AswireliyA veVlYiyerYiyawu . 
inwa inYnYifsil 2 cikcarkalYEye koli atiwwAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu Aswireliya Utakam oVnYrYirYku smiw kUrYiyawAvawu : 
anYrYu koli Atiya inYnYifsE ninYEwwup pArkkumpowu nAnY pArwwawileye cirYanwa inYnYifs awu eVnYrYu karuwukirYenY . 
niccayamAka nAnY neratiyAkap pArwwa eVnYakku eVwirAnYa oVru mikaccirYanwa inYnYifs eVnYrYAl awu virAt koli anYrYu AtiyawuwAnY . 
kalYawwinY itEveVlYikalYil avar panwukalYE ceVluwwiya viwam AccariyamUttuvawAka irunwawu . 
oVvvoVru murYE avar panwE atikkum powum awu pavuNtarikkuc ceVllum eVnYpawu pol AtinYAr . 
AnYAl peVriya alYavil risk eVtukkavillE . 
awu oVru ‘ kilYAs ’ inYnYifs . 
awuvum cakwi vAynwa RAtkalYe wevE eVnYrYu ninYEkkappatum ti20 kirikkeVttil ippatiyoVru inYnYifs mikavum AccariyamAnYa oVnYrYu . 
anwa oVru inYnYifsE pArwwa alYavileye nAnY nirYEya avaritamirunwu karYrYuk koVNtawAka uNarkirYenY . 
nam aNikku awwakEya oVru inYnYifcE Ata veNtum eVnYrYu eVnYnYulY uwvekam pirYanwawu . 
rEcif punYe cUppar jeVyaNts aNikkAka nAnY EpieVl woVtaril atiwwa cawam awwakEya muyarYciye . 
koli polwAnY kalYaviyUkawwinY itEveVlYikalYE cAmarwwiyamAka payanYpatuwwi AtinYenY . 
awe velYEyil nalla kirikkeVt RAtkalYE AtinYenY . 
inwiyAvukku eVwirAka virAt koli atiwwu noVrYukkiya powu mitceVl stArk irunwirunwAl oVruvelYE namakku cAwakamAka mArYiyirukkalAm , AnYAl awuvum namakku urYuwiyAkaw weVriyAwawe . 
ivvArYu kUrYinYAr stIv smiw . hAcanY mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyita ceVnYrYa manwiri eVm.pi.pattIlE murYrYukEyittu kirAma makkalY porAttam walYlYumulYlYu – 
paraparappu cikkamakalYUru , 
hAcanY mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyita ceVnYrYa manwiri eVm.pi.pattIlE murYrYukEyittu kirAma makkalY porAttawwil ItupattanYar . 
avarkalYE watukka vanwa polIcArukkum , kirAma makkalYukkum itEye walYlYumulYlYu erYpattawu . 
iwanYAl afku paraparappu erYpattawu . 
mAnilawwil katumEyAnYa varYatci 
karnAtakawwil warYpowu katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
iwanYAl mAnilawwil palverYu mAvattafkalYil makkalY kutinIr kitEkkAmal avawippattu varukinYrYanYar . 
mAnilawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyita muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA walEmEyil , manwirikalY atafkiya 4 kulYYukkalY amEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
anwak kulYYuvinYar mAnilam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyittu varukinYrYanYar . 
ciwwarAmEyAvum pala pakuwikalYil pArvEyittu makkalYinY kurYEkalYE kettarYinwu varukirYAr . 
walYlYumulYlYu – paraparappu 
inwa nilEyil hAcanY mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyituvawarYkAka manwiri eVm.pi.pattIl ceVnYrYAr . 
avarutanY aracu awikArikalYum ceVnYrYirunwanYar . 
palverYu itafkalYE pArvEyitta manwiri eVm.pi. pattIl , pinYnYar ceVnYnYarAyappattaNA wAlukAvil ulYlYa pAkUr pakuwiyE pArvEyita ceVnYrYAr . 
appowu appakuwi kirAma makkalY manwiri eVm.pi.pattIlE murYrYukEyittu porAttawwil ItupattanYar . 
iwanYAl afku paraparappu erYpattawu . 
iwEp pArwwa manwiriyinY pAwukAppirYkAka ceVnYrYirunwa polIcAr , kirAma makkalYE watukka muyanYrYanYar . 
iwanYAl afku walYlYumulYlYu erYpattawu . 
pawarYrYamAnYa cUlYYnilE uruvAnYawE woVtarnwu manwiri afkirunwu utanYe purYappattAr . 
manwiri purYappattu ceVnYrYAr 
AnYAl avarE afkirunwu ceVlla vitAmal kirAma makkalY cUlYYnwu koVNtu porAttam natawwinYar . 
iwukurYiwwu wakaval arYinwa ceVnYnYarAyappattaNA polIcAr virEnwu vanwu porAttawwil ItupattavarkalYitam peccuvArwwE natawwinYArkalY . 
AnYAl kirAma makkalY porAttawwE kEvita marYuwwawAl afku mINtum kirAma makkalYukkum , polIcArukkum walYlYumulYlYu erYpattawu . 
inwa walYlYumulYlYuvinY powu manwiri eVm.pi.pattIl kIlYYe vilYYa muyanYrYAr . 
avarE polIcAr wAfki pitiwwu pawwiramAka mIttu alYYEwwuc ceVnYrYanYar . 
iruppinYum avarE pinYwoVtarnwu kirAma makkalY koRafkalYE eVlYYuppi vanwanYar . 
inwa nilEyil , kAril erYiya manwiri eVm.pi. pattIlum , aracu awikArikalYum varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyitAmaleye afkirunwu purYappattu ceVnYrYanYar . 
inwa campavam nerYrYu afku peVrum paraparappEyum , pawarYrYawwEyum erYpatuwwiyawu . merYku vafkAlYawwil mINtum muwalvar AkirYAr mamwA pAnYarji - 
acAmil pA.ja.ka. munYnYilE : 
karuwwuk kaNippu puwuteVlli : 
ci ottar , 
e.pi.pi. AnYanwA marYrYum inwiyA tUte natawwiya vAkkuppawivukku pinwEya karuwwukkaNippil merYku vafkAlYawwil wiriNAmul kAfkiras katci mINtum AtciyE pitikkum eVnYrYu weVriyavanwulYlYawu . 
e.pi.pi. AnYanwA karuwwukkaNippil wiriNAmul kAfkiracukku 163 itafkalYum , ci - ottaril 167 itafkalYum , inwiyA tute 243 itafkalYum kitEkkum eVnYa weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
iwanY mUlam mamwA pAnYarji mINtum AtciyE pitippawu urYuwiyAkiyulYlYawu . 
acAmil muwalmurYEyAka pA.ja.ka. AtciyE pitikkum eVnYrYu vAkkup pawivukku pinwEya karuwwukkaNippil kUrYappattulYlYawu . 
ci - ottar karuwwu kaNippil pA.ja.ka . kUttaNikku 57 itafkalY kitEkkum eVnYrYu kUrYappattulYlYawu . 
e.pi.pi. AnYanwA karuwwu kaNippil 81 itafkalY kitEkkum eVnYrYum , inwiyA tute karuwwukkaNippil 79 muwal 93 itafkalY kitEkkum eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl warYpowu acAmil Atciyil irukkum kAfkiras AtciyE ilYYakkappovawu urYuwiyAkiyulYlYawu . karnAtakawwil katum varYatci illE : manwiri karuwwAl carccE 
peVfkalYUru , karnAtaka mAnilawwil 136 wAlukAkkalYil katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
inwa pakuwikalYE mAnila aracu varYatci pakuwikalY eVnYa arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
awwutanY afku varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE aracu merYkoVNtu varukirYawu . 
varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil manwirikalY walEmEyilAnYa kulYYuvinYar Ayvu ceVywu varukirYArkalY . 
inwa nilEyil karnAtaka paFcAyawwurAj marYrYum kirAma valYarcciwwurYE manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl kalapurakiyil niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwa powu , karnAtakawwil katum varYatci illE eVnYa kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
melum avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
vatakarnAtaka makkalY mika mocamAnYa varYatciyE anYupaviwwu ulYlYanYar . 
1972-m ANtu waNNIr , wIvanYam , uNavu illAmal kAlnatEkalY , makkalY maraNam atEnwanYar . 
awwakEya nilEyE pArwwavarkalYukku warYpowEya varYatci mocamAnYawu kitEyAwu . 
varYatci eVnYrYAl nilawwil viwEkkappatta viwE mulYEkkAwu . 
vilYEccal kEkku varAwu . 
awE wAnY varYatci eVnYrYu coVlkirYom . 
AnYAl ippowu veVyilinY wAkkam awikamAka ulYlYawu . 
iwE katum varYatci eVnYrYu coVlla mutiyAwu . 
mAnilawwil katum veVyil atiwwu varuvawAl nilawwati nIrmattam nAlYukku nAlY kurYEnwu varukirYawu . 
iwu AwafkawwE erYpatuwwum viRayam ” eVnYrYAr . 
warYpowu varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA , manwirikalY curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varum nilEyil mAnilawwil katum varYatci illE eVnYrYu manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl kUrYiya karuwwu karnAtakawwil peVrum carccEyE erYpatuwwiyulYlYawu . maruwwuva kallUri nulYYEvuwwervu piraccinYEyil iwuvarE jeVyalaliwA natavatikkE eVtukkAwawu enY ? 
karuNAniwi kelYvi 
ceVnYnYE , maruwwuva kallUri nulYYEvuwwervu piraccinYEyil iwuvarE muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA natavatikkE eVtukkAwawu enY ? eVnYrYu karuNAniwi kelYvi eVlYYuppiyulYlYAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu , wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi nerYrYu veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
nulYYEvuwwervu piraccinYE 
a.wi.mu.ka. aracu mINtum amEnwavutanY maruwwuvap patippu – pal maruwwuvap patippukalYukku nulYYEvuw wervu illAmaleye mANavarkalY cerkkEkku natavatikkE eVtukkappatum eVnYrYu nerYrYEyawinYam muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA arYiviwwirukkirYAr . 
awarYkeVnYa wanYiye oVru cattawwEye koVNtu varuvArkalYAm . 
nulYYEvuwwervu parYrYiya piraccinYE eVwwanYE mAwafkalYAka natEpeVrYukirYawu ? 
anwap piraccinYE vanwavutanYeye warYpowu wiruneVlvelikkup poyc coVlkinYrYa muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA , wamilYYakawwile oVru avacaraccattam pirYappippawE yAr watuwwawu ? 
mINtum Atcikku vanwAl natavatikkE eVtukkappatum eVnYrYu eVllorEyum emArYrYukirYa jeVyalaliwA , iwuvarE natavatikkE eVtukkAmal irunwawarYkAka wakunwa waNtanYEyE mANavarkalYitam irunwum , peVrYrYorkalYitamirunwum peVrYa veNtAmA ? 
kAraNamAnYavarkalY yAr ? 
warYpowu kUta uccanIwimanYrYawwile nulYYEvuwwervu parYrYiya valYYakku natanwu koVNtirunwa powu , marYrYa mAnilafkalYinY cArpil vAwAtiya valYYakkarYiFarkalY eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAka wafkalY eVwirppE uccanIwimanYrYawwil wAkkal ceVywapowu , wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil uccanIwimanYrYawwile eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAnYa eVwirppEw wAkkal ceVyyAwawu enY ? 
awarYku kAraNamAnYavarkalY yAr ? 
muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA inwa mukkiyamAnYa valYYakkil wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil vAwAtiya valYYakkarYiFarotu vivAwiwwu wamilYYakawwinY eVwirppE wanYiye oVru manYu mUlam eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAka uccanIwimanYrYawwile weVriviwwirukka veNtAmA ? 
jeVyalaliwA pecumpowu , ‘ ‘ inwa valYYakkil wamilYYaka aracu eVwir manYuwArarAkac cerkkappatAwa nilEyilum ’’ wamilYYaka aracinY valYYakkarYiFar vAwAtiyawAkavum , wAnY vAwAtiyawE eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAka wAkkal ceVywulYlYawAkavum kUrYiyirukkirYAr . 
mukkiyamAnYa inwa valYYakkil wamilYYaka aracE eVwir manYuwArarAka cerkka veNtum eVnYrYu valiyurYuwwi uccanIwimanYrYawwil wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil korappattawA ? 
korappatavillE eVnYkirYapowu , awarYku kAraNam eVnYnYa ? 
wamilYYaka aracEyum eVwir manYuwArarAkac cerkkumpati , wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil uccanIwimanYrYawwil enY valiyurYuwwavillE ? 
eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAka wAkkal 
avvArYu valiyurYuwwAwa nilEyilwAnY , valYYakkil wamilYYaka aracu eVwir manYuwArarAkac cerkkappatAwa nilEyilwAnY wamilYYaka aracukkAka valYYakkarYiFar kurYukkittup peci , avar peciyawE eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAkaw wAkkal ceVywirukkirYAre wavira , nulYYEvuwwervu wevEyillE eVnYrYu wamilYYaka aracu 2006–m ANtu koVNtu vanwa cattam parYrYiyo , anwac cattam janYAwipawiyinY oVppuwalEp peVrYrYawu eVnYpawu parYrYiyo mawwiya aracinY verYu eVnwa cattamum , arYivikkEyum wamilYYaka aracinY cattawwEp parYrYi kelYvi ketkavo , awE nIrwwuppokac ceVywitavo mutiyAwu eVnYpawu parYrYiyo eVlYYuwwuppUrvamAka wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil enY wAkkal ceVyyavillE eVnYrYuwAnY nAnY kelYvi kettirunwenY . 
awarYku muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA neVllE kUttawwil eVnwa pawilum kUrYavillE . 
mawwiya aracu amEccakafkalY pawivu ceVywirunwa kurYippurEkalYinY atippatEyil , janYAwipawiyinY oVppuwalEp peVrYrYawarYkup pirYaku , wamilYYaka aracinY cattawwE mawwiya aracinY verYu eVnwac cattamum oVlYYufku murYE ANEkalYum kattuppatuwwita iyalAwu eVnYpawEw wanYawu vAwawwil wamilYYaka aracu enY eVtuwwurEkkavillE ? 
itEkkAlaw watE 
jeVyalaliwA pecumpowu , inwiya maruwwuva kavunYcil 2010–m ANtu nulYYEvuw wervEk koVNtuvanwu arYivikkE veVlYiyittapowu mawwiya kAfkiras kUttaNi aracil irunwawu wi.mu.ka. wAnY eVnYrYum , awEw watukka itEkkAlaw watE vAfki eVnYnYa payanY eVnYrYum kUrYiyirukkirYAr . 
21–12–2010 anYrYu inwiya maruwwuva kavunYcil ivvArYu arYivikkE veVlYiyittavutanY , anwa arYivikkEkku eVwirAka , ceVnYnYE uyarnIwimanYrYawwil wi.mu.ka. aracu valYYakkuw woVtuwwawu . 
anwa valYYakkil ceVnYnYE uyarnIwimanYrYam , wi.mu.ka. aracinY eVwir vAwafkalYE erYrYukkoVNtu , wamilYYaka aracu nulYYEvuw wervinYE rawwu ceVywu koVNtu vanwa cattawwE verYu eVnwa arYivikkEkalYum kattuppatuwwa mutiyAwu eVnYrYu wIrppalYiwwawu . 
melum wi.mu.ka. aracu koriyapati , inwiya maruwwuvak kavunYcilinY arYivikkEkku watE uwwaravEyum uyarnIwimanYrYam valYYafkiyawu . 
AnYAl jeVyalaliwA neVllEp peccile inwa uNmEkalYE eVllAm appatiye marYEwwuvittu , wi.mu.ka. aracEk kurYE kUrYip peciyirukkirYAr . 
uNmE eVnYrYAle uppAkak karikkum jeVyalaliwAvukku . 
mawwiyil appowu irunwa kAfkiras kUttaNi aracil nAnY peci arYivikkEyE enY watukkavillE eVnYrYu jeVyalaliwA kettirukkirYAr . 
mAnila aracukalYutanY AlocanYE 
mawwiya aracitam , appowu irunwa wi.mu.ka. aracu valiyurYuwwiya kAraNawwAlwAnY , appowu mawwiya manYiwavalYa mempAttuw wurYE manwiriyAka irunwa kapilcipal , mAnila aracukalYutanY AlocanYE natawwiya pirYake poVwu nulYYEvuw wervu viRayawwil irYuwi mutivu eVtukkappatum eVnYrYu weVriviwwirunwAr . 
awu mAwwiramalla ; 
mawwiya makkalY nalvAlYYvuw wurYE manwiriyAka irunwa kulAm napi AcAw EwarApAwwil makkalY nalvAlYYvuw wurYE amEccarkalY mAnAttE natawwiya powu , maruwwuvap poVwu nulYYEvuw wervu natawwum wittawwE awikArappUrvamAka nirYuwwi vEppawu eVnYrYa oVru wIrmAnYawwEye oVrumanYawAka nirYEverYrYinYArkalY . 
AnYAl inwa uNmEkalYum yArukkuw weVriyappokirYawu eVnYrYa akafkAra manYappAnYmEyotu , wi.mu.ka. wamilYYakawwil mINtum Atcikku vanwAl nulYYEvuw wervinYEw watukka eVllA muyarYcikalYEyum eVtukkum eVnYrYu nAnY katanwa 10–nwewiyanYrYu arYikkE veVlYiyittavutanY witIreVnYrYu kaN vilYYiwwuk koVNtu neVllEkkuc ceVnYrYu nulYYEvuwwervu parYrYi , Atcikku vanwAl cattam koVNtuvarap povawAka valYYakkamAnYa kawEyEc coVlli makkalYE emArYrYa ninYEkkirYAr jeVyalaliwA . 
awanYAl wAnY inwa arYikkEyinY woVtakkawwil ‘ ‘ wumpE vittuvittu vAlEp pitikka muyalukirYAr ’’ eVnYrYu kurYippittenY . 
awu uNmEwAnYe ? 
rawwu ceVyya cattam 
muwal–amEccar jeVyalaliwA neVllEyil pecumpowu , 
‘ ‘ 2006–m ANtu oVru puwiya cattam iyarYrYappattu , 2007–m ANtu muwal 12–m vakuppu mawippeVN atippatEyileye maruwwuvam marYrYum pal maruwwuvam pattappatippukalYukku mANavarkalY cerkkappatukinYrYanYar ’’ eVnYrYu kUrYiyirukkirYAr . 
2006–m ANtu puwiya cattam iyarYrYappattawAkak kUrYukirYIrkalYe , awu eVnwa Atciyil natEpeVrYrYawu ? 
wi.mu.ka. Atciyil wAnYe ? 
awE enY marYEkka muyarYcikkirYIrkalY ? 
2006–m ANtu EnwAvawu murYEyAka wi.mu.ka. Atcikku vanwavutanY wAnY nulYYEvuwwervu murYEyE rawwu ceVywu cattam iyarYrYappattawu . 
nulYYEvuw wervE rawwu ceVywita uruppatiyAka oVru kAriyawwEyum ceVyyAwa jeVyalaliwA , ippowu werwal eVnYrYawum , nulYYEvuw wervEp parYrYi ewewo peci ‘ ‘ nuNalum wanY vAyAl keVtum ’’ eVnYpawE nirUpiwwirukkirYAr . 
ivvArYu karuNAniwi kUrYiyulYlYAr . Rikar wavaN , ARis neVhrA acawwal :

pulYlYikalY pattiyalil 2-vawu itawwukku munYnYerYrYam 
wi inwu . 
EpieVl woVtaril mumpE aNiyE 85 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil EwarApAw aNi worYkatiwwawu . 
inwa veVrYrYiyAl EwarApAw aNi pulYlYikalY pattiyalil 2-vawu itawwukku munYnYerYiyawu . 
vicAkappattinYawwil nerYrYu natEpeVrYrYa inwa Attawwil muwalil pet ceVywa EwarApAw aNi 20 ovarkalY mutivil 3 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 177 ranYkalY eVtuwwawu . 
Rikar wavaN 57 panwukalYil 10 pavuNtarikalY , 1 ciksarutanY 82 ranYkalY vilYAci AttamilYYakkAmal irunwAr . 
vArnYarutanY iNEnwu muwal vikkeVttukku avar 9.5 ovaril 85 ranYkalY cerwwAr . 
vArnYar 33 panwil , 7 pavuNtarikalY , 1 ciksarutanY 48 ranY eVtuwwu harpajanYcif panwil poltAnYAr . 
atuwwu vanwa villiyamcanY 2 ranYnYil AttamilYYanwu emArYrYam alYiwwAr . 
3-vawu vikkeVttukku Rikar wavaNutanY iNEnwa yuvarAjcif awiratiyAka vilYEyAti 23 panwil , 3 pavuNtarikalY , 2 ciksarutanY 39 ranYkalY kuviwwu valuvAnYa skorE cerkka uwavinYAr . 
avar 19.4-vawu ovaril meVkli nYahanY panwil ‘ hit vikkeVt ' murYEyil AttamilYYanwAr . 
atuwwu vanwa heVnYriks iru panwil 1 ranY mattume eVtuwwAr . 
mumpE warappil harpajanY cif iru vikkeVt kEpparYrYinYAr . 
178 ranYkalY ilakkutanY pet ceVywa mumpE aNikku Arampame awircciyAka irunwawu . 
muwal ovarinY katEci panwil ranY eVwum eVtukkAwa nilEyil pArwwiv patelE eVlpitapilYyU AkkinYAr puvanYeRvar kumAr . 
atuwwa ovarinY muwal panwil rohiw carmA 5 ranYnYil ARis neVhrA panwil poltAnYAr . 
atuwwu kalYampukunwa ampAtti rAyutuvE ranY eVwum eVtukkAwa nilEyilum , jAs patlarE 2 ranYnYilum veVlYiyerYrYinYAr neVhrA . 
4 ovaril 30 ranYkalYukku 4 vikkeVtkalYE ilYYanwu mumpE aNi waviwwawu . 
awanY pinYnYar vanwa kirunYAl pANtiyA 17 , poVllArtu 11 , harwik pANtiyA 7 , tim cavuwwi 3 , meVklinYahanY 8 , pumrA 6 ranYkalYil AttamilYYakka mumpE aNi 16.3 ovaril 92 ranYkalYukku curuNtawu . 
EwarApAw warappil neVhrA , mustApisUr rahmAnY walA 3 vikkeVt vIlYYwwinYar . 
85 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil veVnYrYa EwarApAw aNi 6-vawu veVrYrYiyE pawivu ceVywawu . 
inwa veVrYrYiyinY mUlam anwa aNi 12 pulYlYikalYutanY pattiyalil 2-vawu itawwukku munYnYerYiyawu . 
AttanAyakanYAka neVhrA wervAnYAr . ceVnYnYE , katalUr , puwucceriyil rU. 3 koti mawippulYlYa veVlYlYa nivAraNa uwavikalYE natikar vijay valYYafkinYAr 
ceVnYnYE , 
ceVnYnYE , katalUr , puwucceri Akiya itafkalYil malYYE veVlYlYawwAl pAwikkappattavarkalYukku rU. 3 koti mawippulYlYa veVlYlYa nivAraNa poVrutkalYE natikar vijay valYYafkinYAr . 
malYYE veVlYlYa pAwippu 
katanwa 3 vArafkalYukku munYpu ceVnYnYE , katalUr , puwucceri pakuwikalYil peVywa kanYamalYYE kAraNamAka AyirakkaNakkAnYavarkalY pAwikkappattArkalY . 
pAwikkappattavarkalYukku wanYawu makkalY iyakkam cArpil rU. 3 koti mawippulYlYa veVlYlYa nivAraNa poVrutkalYE valYYafka natikar vijay munYvanwAr . 
cila itafkalYukku vijay neril ceVnYrYu uNavum , nivAraNa poVrutkalYum valYYafkinYAr . 
pAwikkappattavarkalYukku arici , kAykarYi , roVtti , piskat , kowumE mAvu , ravE , pAl pAkkeVt marYrYum malYikE poVrutkalYE vijay valYYafkinYAr . 
vetti , celE , panYiyanY , porvE , awwiyAvaciya pAwwirafkalY AkiyavE vijayinY makkalY iyakkam cArpil valYYafkappattanYa . 
avEkalYE makkalY iyakka nirvAkikalY vItu , vItAkac ceVnYrYu valYYafkinYArkalY . 
nivAraNa poVrutkalY 
iwuvarE rU. 3 koti mawippulYlYa veVlYlYa nivAraNa poVrutkalY valYYafkappattulYlYawAka vijayinY makkalY iyakkam nirvAki oVruvar weVriviwwAr . 
malYYE veVlYlYawwAl pAwikkappatta vijayinY makkalY iyakka urYuppinYarkalY 150 perukku walA rU. 4 Ayiram valYYafkappattawAkavum avar weVriviwwAr . nAnY cirYu vayawil ulYYEwwawE vita 100 matafku mu.ka.stAlinY ulYYEkkirYAr 
ceVnYnYEyil natanwa poVwukkUttawwil karuNAniwi peVrumiwam 
ceVnYnYE , 
mu.ka.stAlinY eVnYakku makanYAka pirYanwawu nAnY ceVywa wavappuNNiyam eVnYrYum nAnY cirYu vayawil katcikku ulYYEwwawE vita 100 matafku mu.ka.stAlinY ulYYEkkirYAr eVnYrYu ceVnYnYEyil natanwa poVwukkUttawwil karuNAniwi pecinYAr . 
mu.ka.stAlinY ulYYEppu

appowu avar peciyawAvawu : - 
arukil ulYlYa katal ifke pukunwawo eVnYkirYa alYavukku veVlYlYam pol ifke kUtiyirukkirYIrkalY . 
kOwwUril wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY pottiyitukirYAr . 
avar inYrYu metEkku varavillE . 
UreVllAm ceVnYrYu uwaya cUriyanYukkum , kE cinYnYawwirYkum vAkku ketkum paNiyil Itupattu irukkirYAr eVnYpawAl mu.ka.stAlinY ifke illE , avar illAvittAlum avarukku pawilAka nAnY ifke irukkirYenY . 
enYeVnYrYAl inwa werwalil pAwi ulYYEppE , pAwi velEkalYE wanY mIwu ilYYuwwu pottukkoVNtu allumpakalum ulYYEwwukkoVNtu irukkirYAr , stAlinY eVnY makanY eVnYpawarYkAka coVllavillE . 
makanYAka illAvittAlum wi.mu.ka.vinY cAwAraNa woVNtanY eVnYrYa alYavil avar ArYrYum paNi eVnYnYEye poVrYAmE koVlYlYa ceVykirYawu . 
eVnY makanY mIwu eVnYakku poVrYAmE varukirYawu eVnYrYAl , cirYuvayawil nAnY inwa iyakkawwirYkAka ulYYEwwawE vita 100 matafku melAka mu.ka.stAlinY anwa paNiyE ArYrYi varukirYAr . 
wavappuNNiyam 
ewo vanwom , ceVnYrYom eVnYrYu illAmal inYrYEkku wanYiyAr ti.vi.yil kUta avar koVtuwwa pettiyE kUta unYnYippAka kavanYiwwenY .

appatippatta mu.ka.stAlinY kOwwUr woVkuwiyil uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwil pottiyitukirYAr .

afke cimlA muwwucolYYanY pottiyitukirYAr .

EpieVl pulYlYikalY pattiyal : 
witIr carYukkalil reVynYA aNi ! 
EpieVl kirikkeVt pottiyinY 34-vawu lIk Attawwil 5 vikkeVt viwwiyAcawwil kujarAw layanYsEw worYkatiwwawu canYrEsars hEwarApAw . 
iwuvarE 8 AttafkalYil vilYEyAtiyulYlYa hEwarApAw 5-Avawu veVrYrYiyEp peVrYrYulYlYawu . 
awenerawwil muwalil vilYEyAtiya 7 AttafkalYil oVnYrYil mattume worYrYirunwa kujarAw aNi , katEciyAka vilYEyAtiya 3 AttafkalYilum wolviyE canwiwwulYlYawu . 
inwa veVrYrYiyinYAl pulYlYikalY pattiyalil 4-m itawwukku munYnYerYiyulYlYawu hEwarApAw aNi . 
wolviyatEnwAlum iraNtAmitawwil nItikkirYawu kujarAw aNi . 
iruppinYum woVtarnwu wolviyatEnwu koVNtiruppawu anwa aNiyEk kavalE koVlYlYa ceVywulYlYawu . 
curukkamAnYa skor kujarAw 126 / 6 AronY HpiFc 51 ( 42 ) , cureR reVynYA 20 ( 10 ) , puvanYesvar kumAr 2 vi / 28 hEwarApAw 129 / 5 Rikar wavanY 47 ( 40 ) , tevit vArnYar 24 ( 17 ) , kulkarnYi 2 vi / 17 pulYlYikalY pattiyal aNikalY pottikalY veVrYrYi wolvi pulYlYikalY neVt ranYret koVlkawwA 9 6 3 12 + 0.359 kujarAw 10 6 4 12 -0.267 teVlli 8 5 3 10 + 0.407 hEwarApAw 8 5 3 10 + 0.115 mumpE 9 5 4 10-0.009 puNe 9 3 6 6 + 0.181 peVfkalYUr 7 2 5 4-0.031 paFcAp 8 2 6 4-0.753 wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam - 
puwiwAka woVtafkappattulYlYa wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil wamilYYakawwinY waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam , mAmallapuram katarYkarE koyil ulYpata 25 ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY itam peVrYrYulYlYanYa . 
nAttil ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYil wUymEyEp parAmarikkum vakEyil , poVwumakkalY pukArkalYEw weVrivippawarYkAka wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyali ' woVtafkappattulYlYawu . 
iwEyoVtti puwu williyil wifkalYkilYYamE natEpeVrYrYa vilYYAvil puwiya ceVyaliyE woVtafkivEwwu mawwiya curYrYulA marYrYum kalAcAra iNEyamEccar ( poVrYuppu ) tAktar makeR carmA peciyawAvawu : 
nAttil ulYlYa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYEw wUymEyAka vEwwiruppawil curYrYulAp payaNikalYum , poVwumakkalYum mukkiyap pafkalYippu ceVyya veNtiyulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl , curYrYulA itafkalY , awEc curYrYiyulYlYa pakuwikalY AkiyavE cukAwAramarYrYa vakEyil irunwAlo , kuppEkalY irunwAlo awu kurYiwwa pukArkalYE poVwumakkalY weVrivikka vacawiyAka mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakam inwa wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyE uruvAkkiyulYlYawu . 
inwaw wittam veVrYrYipeVrYa anYEvarawu oVwwulYYEppum avaciyamAkum . 
aNmEyil woVtafkappatta curYrYulA inYpolEnY ' mUlam winYamum 18 Ayiram pawilkalY varukinYrYanYa . 
iwu ponYrYu curYrYulAp payaNikalYinY vacawikkAka palverYu wittafkalY curYrYulA amEccakam mUlam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
ulYnAttu curYrYulAw wurYEyum panYnYAttu curYrYulA pola awikamAnYa vAyppukalYEp peVrYrYulYlYawu . 
awanYAlwAnY inwa ceVllitappeci ceVyali valYYiyAka poVwumakkalY , curYrYulAp payaNikalY Akiyoritamirunwu AlocanYEkalY ketkappatukinYrYanYa eVnYrYAr amEccar . 
curYrYulA ucci mAnAtu : 
mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakawwinY ceVyalar vinYow sutRi peciyawAvawu : 
2016 ANtAnYawu curYrYulAw wurYEkku nalla vAypputanY woVtafkiyulYlYawu . 
inwa ANtu mApeVrum curYrYulA ucci mAnAtu jUlE , Akastil natEpeVrYum eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
inwa mAnAtu curYrYulAw wurYEyE Ukkuvikkum . 
warYpowu arYimukappatuwwappattulYlYa wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyE veVrYrYikaramAnYawAka uruvAkka mawwiya curYrYulA marYrYum kalAcAra amEccakam iNEnwu natavatikkEkalYE merYkoVlYlYum . 
ceVyaliyinY payanYpAtu : 
inwa ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil inwiyaw woVlliyil wurYEyAl pAwukAkkappatum nAttil ulYlYa 25 cirYanwa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY cerkkappatum . 
melum , cila ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYum woVtarnwu inwac ceVyaliyil cerkka natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY ulYlYa pakuwikalYil cukAwAram illAmal irunwAlo , kuppEkalY ewum irunwAlo awE curYrYulAp payaNikalY marYrYum poVwumakkalY inwac ceVyaliyEp payanYpatuwwi pukEppatam eVtuwwu , wafkalYawu kurYippukalYutanY pawiverYrYam ceVyyalAm . 
iwEyatuwwu , ceVyaliyAnYawu campanwappatta inwiyaw woVlliyal wurYEyinY oVrufkiNEppAlYarukku kurYunwakavalAka anYuppappatum . 
awanYpirYaku , campanwappatta itawwil wUymEp paNi merYkoVlYlYa natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
awu woVtarpAnYa wakavalum pukArwArarukku kurYunwakaval mUlam anYuppivEkkappatum . 
inwac ceVyali kUkulY wetuwal poVrYi iyanwirawwil ' svac paryattanY ' ( ‘ swachh Paryatan ’ ) eVnYum peVyaril ulYlYawu eVnYrYAr avar . 
wamilYYakak koyilkalY : 
inwaw wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil williyil ulYlYa kuwUp minYAr valYAkam , himAyUnY kallarYE , willi ceVfkottE , wamilYYakawwil ulYlYa waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam , mAmallapuram katarYkarEkkoyil , AkrAvil ulYlYa wAjmakal , HpawepUr cikri , karnAtakawwil ulYlYa hampi ulYpata 25 cirYanwa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY itam peVrYrYulYlYanYa . varYatci pakuwikalYE pArvEyita muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA inYrYu cikpalYlYAppUrukku varukE 
mAvatta kaleVktar petti kolAr wafkayaval , 
varYatci pakuwikalYE pArvEyituvawarYkAka muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA inYrYu cikpalYlYAppUrukku ceVlkirYAr . 
iwuwoVtarpAka cikpalYlYAppUr mAvatta kaleVktar veVfkateR nerYrYu niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
cikpalYlYAppUrukku ciwwarAmEyA varukE 
cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattawwirYku nerYrYu munYwinYam muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varYatci paNikalYE pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVyvawarYkAka varuvawAka irunwawu . 
AnYAl kolAr mAvattawwileye neram awikamAnYawAl avar cikpalYlYAppUr curYrYuppayaNawwE rawwu ceVywuvittu peVfkalYUruvukku ceVnYrYuvittAr . 
awanYAl inYrYu ( viyAlYYakkilYYamE ) cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattawwirYku muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varukE purikirYAr . 
kAlE 11 maNi muwal mawiyam 2 maNi varE avar cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattawwil ulYlYa koVlamanYahalYlYi , reVttikoVlavehalYlYi , pIrecanwirA marYrYum pAkepalYlYi wAlukAvil ciwrAvawi aNi Akiya itafkalYE pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVykirYAr . 
melum varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYEyum avar pArvEyitukirYAr . 
palawwa polIs pAwukAppu pinYnYar mawiyam mAvatta paFcAyawwu aluvalakawwil eVm.eVl.e.kkalY marYrYum awikArikalYutanY varYatci nivAraNa paNikalY kurYiwwu AlocanYE natawwukirYAr . 
awEyatuwwu poVwumakkalYE canwiwwu kurYEkalYE kettarYinwu avarkalYitam irunwu manYukkalYE peVrYukirYAr . 
iwarYkAnYa anYEwwu erYpAtukalYum ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
muwal–manwiriyinY varukEkkAka palawwa polIs pAwukAppum potappattulYlYawu . 
ivvArYu mAvatta kaleVktar veVfkateR kUrYinYAr . 
munYnYawAka avar muwal–manwiri pArvEyita ulYlYa koVlamanYahalYlYi kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYu pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVywAr . 
appowu aracu awikArikalY palarum utanYirunwanYar . ilavacafkalYE koVtuwwu nAttinY valYarcciyE keVtuwwu vittanYar ; 
mawwiya manwiri smiriwi irAnYi kurYrYaccAttu 
ceVnYnYE , 
ilavacafkalYE koVtuwwu ottukalYE peVrYrYu nAttinY valYarcciyE keVtuwwu vittanYar eVnYa mawwiya manwiri smiriwi irAnYi kurYrYam cAttinYAr . 
mawwiya manwiri piracAram 
rAyapuram cattamanYrYa woVkuwi pA.janYawA vetpAlYar tAktar eVm.Ar.jeVmilAvukku Awaravu kettu rAyapurawwil natEpeVrYrYa poVwukkUttawwil mawwiya manYiwa nala mempAttuwwurYE manwiri smiriwi irAnYi peciyawAvawu : 
a.wi.mu.ka. , wi.mu.ka. ilavacafkalYE koVtuwwu oVttukalYE peVrYrYu ottu potta makkalYinY kutumpawwE varYumE nilEkku walYlYi , nAttinY valYarcciyE keVtuwwu vittanYar . 
oVru kApi vilE 10 rUpAy eVnYrYa nilEyil pirawamar moti mAwam 1 rUpAykku AyulY kAppIttu wittawwE koVtuwwu ulYlYAr . 
varYumE kottukku kIlYYe ulYlYa mInYavarkalY , wAlYYwwappattavarkalY , mArYrYuwwirYanYAlYikalYukku E.E.ti. varE ilavaca kalviyE moti alYiwwu ulYlYAr . 
mawwiya aracinY wittafkalY mAnilawwilum peVrYa wAmarE cinYnYawwil tAktar eVm.Ar.jeVmilAvukku vAkkalYiyufkalY . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . 
munYnYawAka vetpAlYar tAktar eVm.Ar.jeVmilA peciyawAvawu : 
woVlEnokku wittafkalY wamilYYakam mawuvAl atimEppattu kitakkinYrYawu . 
mawuvukku atimEyAnYavarkalY cAlEkalYilum , cAkkatEyilum vilYYunwu kitakkinYrYanYar . 
wirAvita katcikalYukkum , kAfkiracukkum murYrYuppulYlYi vEkka pA.janYawA Atcikku varaveNtiyawu ulYlYawu . 
rAyapuram woVkuwi munYmAwiri woVkuwiyAka mArYa peVNkalY , ilYEFarkalY , mANavarkalY , muwiyorkalY , mInYavarkalYukku eVnYa woVlEnokku wittafkalY vEwwu ulYlYenY . 
eVnYakku wAmarE cinYnYawwil vAkkalYiwwu veVrYrYipeVrYa ceVywAl rAyapuram woVkuwi makkalY 5 ANtukalYil anYEwwu atippatE vacawikalYEyum peVrYrYu wanYnYirYEvu peVrYrYa woVkuwiyAka mArYrYuvenY .

wamilYYaka ANkalY aNi ‘ cAmpiyanY 
puwucceri , 
puwucceri mAnila kUtEppanwu cafkam cArpil uppalYam rAjIv kAnwi ulYvilYEyAttu arafkawwil 67-vawu weciya jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu ‘ cAmpiyanYRip ’ potti natanwawu . 
iwil ANkalY pirivil 26 mAnilafkalYE cernwa aNiyinYarum , peVNkalY pirivil 22 mAnilafkalYE cernwa aNiyinYarum kalanwu koVNtanYar . 
iwanY ANkalY pirivil irYuwippottiyil wamilYYnAtu - keralYA aNikalY mowinYa . 
iwil wamilYYaka aNi 88-77 eVnYrYa pulYlYi kaNakkil keralYAvE vIlYYwwi cAmpiyanY pattawwE wanYawAkkiyawu . 
peVNkalY pirivil irYuwippottiyil karnAtakam - wamilYYnAtu aNikalY palapparItcE natawwinYa . 
iwil karnAtaka aNi 64-44 eVnYrYa pulYlYi kaNakkil wamilYYakawwE cAywwu cAmpiyanY pattawwE kEpparYrYiyawu . veVyilinY wAkkam wAnY awikamAka ulYlYawu 
karnAtakawwil katum varYatci illE manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl karuwwAl carccE 
karnAtakawwil veVyilinY wAkkam wAnY awikamAka iruppawAkavum , katum varYatci illE eVnYrYum manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl kUrYiya karuwwu peVrum carccEyE erYpatuwwiyulYlYawu . 
136 wAlukAkkalYil varYatci 
karnAtaka mAnilawwil 136 wAlukAkkalYil katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
inwa pakuwikalYE mAnila aracu varYatci pakuwikalY eVnYa arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
awwutanY afku varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE aracu merYkoVNtu varukirYawu . 
varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil manwirikalY walEmEyilAnYa kulYYuvinYar Ayvu ceVywu varukirYArkalY . 
melum muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA erYkanYave 8 mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varYatci pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVywulYlYAr . 
ippowu melum 5 mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtulYlYAr . 
manwirikalYinY kulYYukkalYum mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varYatciyE Ayvu ceVywu varukirYawu . 
katum varYatci illE 
inwa nilEyil karnAtaka paFcAyawwu rAj marYrYum kirAma valYarcciwwurYE manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl kalapurakiyil nerYrYu niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwa powu , karnAtakawwil katum varYatci illE eVnYa kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
melum avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
vatakarnAtaka makkalY mika mocamAnYa varYatciyE anYupaviwwu ulYlYanYar . 
1972-m ANtu waNNIr , wIvanYam , uNavu illAmal kAlnatEkalY , makkalY maraNam atEnwanYar . 
awwakEya nilEyE pArwwavarkalYukku warYpowEya varYatci mocamAnYawu kitEyAwu . 
varYatci eVnYrYAl nilawwil viwEkkappatta viwE mulYEkkAwu . 
vilYEccal kEkku varAwu . 
awE wAnY varYatci eVnYrYu coVlkirYom . 
nIr AwArafkalY wetuwal 
AnYAl ippowu veVyilinY wAkkam awikamAka ulYlYawu . 
iwE katum varYatci eVnYrYu coVlla mutiyAwu . 
mAnilawwil katum veVyil atiwwu varuvawAl nilawwati nIrmattam nAlYukku nAlY kurYEnwu varukirYawu . 
iwu AwafkawwE erYpatuwwum viRayam . 
katum veVyilAl aNEkalY marYrYum nawikalYil ulYlYa waNNIr vekamAka kAliyAki varukirYawu . 
mAnilawwil cumAr Ayiram kirAmafkalYukku tefkar lArikalY mUlam kutinIr vinYiyokam ceVyyappattu varukirYawu . 
isro uwaviyutanY nIr AwArafkalYE wetum paNi natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
iwanY atippatEyil 18 AlYYkulYYAy kiNarYukalYE amEwwom . 
iwil 12 AlYYkulYYAy kiNarYukalYil waNNIr kitEwwulYlYawu . 
ivvArYu eVc.ke.pattIl kUrYinYAr . 
carccE warYpowu varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA , manwirikalY curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varum nilEyil mAnilawwil katum varYatci illE eVnYrYu manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl kUrYiya karuwwu karnAtakawwil peVrum carccEyE erYpatuwwiyulYlYawu . 
cattacapE werwalil wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi kUtuwal itafkalYE pitikkum 
rAjanAyakam walEmEyilAnYa makkalY Ayvu iyakkam karuwwu kaNippu mutivu veVlYiyItu 
ceVnYnYE , 
cattacapE werwalil wi.mu.ka. kUtuwal itafkalYE pitikkum eVnYrYu pAwiriyAr ca.rAjanAyakam walEmEyilAnYa makkalY Ayvu iyakkam karuwwu kaNippE veVlYiyittulYlYawu . 
werwal karuwwu kaNippu veVlYiyItu 
ceVnYnYE nufkampAkkam layolA kallUriyinY munYnYAlY perAciriyarum pAwiriyArumAnYa ca.rAjanAyakam walEmEyilAnYa makkalY Ayvu iyakkam cattacapE werwalil vAkkalYikkap pokum makkalYinY manYanilE eVnYnYa eVnYpawE neratiyAka Ayvu natawwiyawu . 
inwa karuwwu kaNippu mutivE nerYrYu ceVnYnYEyil veVlYiyittawu . 
karuwwu kaNippu woVtarpAka perAciriyar rAjanAyakam kUrYiyawAvawu : 
8 Ayiram perkalYitam karuwwu ketpu 
wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalEyoVtti 177 cattacapE woVkuwikalYilum ( anYEwwu nAtAlYumanYrYa woVkuwikalYilum ) epral 24–nwewi muwal me mAwam 10–nwewi mutiya 18 nAtkalY 8 Ayirawwu 64 perkalYitam karuwwu kaNippu natawwappattawu . 
inwa karuwwukaNippil pulYlYi vivarafkalYE cekariwwavarkalY 35 per . 
avarkalY anYEvarum makkalY Ayvu eVnYrYa amEppE cernwavarkalY . 
inwa karuwwu kaNippu eVnYawu walEmEyil eVnYawu AlocanYEyil natawwappattawu . 
muwal murYEyAka vAkkalYikka ulYlYavarkalY 11.9 cawavIwam per . 
30 vayawu varE vAkkalYippor 26 cawavIwam ulYlYanYar . 
31 muwal 45 vayawu varE ulYlYavarkalY 35.3 cawavIwam per . 
46 vayawu muwal 60 vayawu varE ulYlYavarkalY 21.7 cawavIwam . 
mIwam ulYlYavarkalY 60 vayawukku merYpattavarkalY .

a.wi.mu.ka. Atci kurYiwwa mawippItu 
katanwa 5 ANtu a.wi.mu.ka. AtciyE kurYiwwa makkalYinY mawippItu , aracinY mIwu peVriya alYavil veVrYuppo , peVriya alYavil nirYEvo illE . 
a.wi.mu.ka. Atci mika nanYrYu eVnYrYu 12.5 cawavIwam perkalYum , nanYrYu eVnYrYu 33.9 cawavIwam perkalYum , mocam eVnYrYu 15.3 cawavIwam perkalYum , mika mocam eVnYrYu 15.6 cawavIwam perkalYum karuwwu weVriviwwanYar . 
katanwa janYavari mAwawwE oVppitukEyil katanwa oriru mAwafkalYil makkalYE camAwAnYam ceVyvawil a.wi.mu.ka. aracu oralYavu munYnYerYrYam kaNtulYlYawu . 
eVnYinYum vAkkAlYarinY katci cArpEyum , Atci kurYiwwa mawippIttEyum kurYukkAka attavaNE patuwwinYAl a.wi.mu.ka. AwaravAlYarkalY AtciyE uyarvAkavum mArYrYukkatciyinYar eVwirAkavum mawippitukinYrYanYar .
