ottumoVwwamAka werwal ANEyawwinY ceVyalpAtukalYukku pArAttE vita kaNtanYam awikamAka veVlYippatukirYawu . 
werwal ANEyawwinY ceVyalpAtu mika nanYrYu – 7.1 nanYrYu – 15.9 carAcari – 14.7 mocam – 31.8 mika mocam – 27.3 ivvArYu pAwiriyAr rAjanAyakam weVriviwwAr . weciya jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu : wamilYYakam cAmpiyanY - 
puwucceriyil natEpeVrYrYa weciya jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu pottiyinY Atavar pirivil wamilYYakamum , makalYir pirivil karnAtakamum cAmpiyanY pattam veVnYrYanYa . 
puwucceri uppalYam rAjIv kAnwi ulYvilYEyAttarafkil 67-Avawu arEs weciya jUnYiyar kUtEppanwu potti katanwa 1-Am wewi woVtafkiyawu . 
iwil nAtu mulYYuvawum irunwu 26 mAnila Atavar aNikalY , 22 mAnila makalYir aNikalY pafkerYrYanYa . 
lIk marYrYum nAk avut murYEyil natEpeVrYrYa pottikalYinY arEyirYuwi AttafkalY canYikkilYYamE iravu natEpeVrYrYanYa . 
Atavar pirivil natappuc cAmpiyanY wamilYYakam 83-79 eVnYrYa pulYlYikalY kaNakkil hariyANAvE porAti veVnYrYawu . 
wamilYYaka keptanY harirAm 32 , tenYiyal 20 , pAlA 17 pulYlYikalY kuviwwu aNiyinY veVrYrYikku viwwittanYar . 
marYrYoVru Attawwil keralYa aNi 72-68 eVnYrYa pulYlYikalY kaNakkil willi aNiyEw worYkatiwwawu . 
keralYa vIrarkalY pirem 28 , cirAs 14 pulYlYikalYEk kuviwwanYar . 
makalYir pirivu : 
makalYir pirivu arEyirYuwiyil natappuc cAmpiyanY cawwIskar aNi 57-63 eVnYrYa pulYlYikalY kaNakkil wamilYYakawwitam worYrYawu . 
wamilYYakawwinY avanwi 18 , EsvaryA 15 pulYlYikalYE kuviwwanYar . 
marYrYoVru arEyirYuwiyil karnAtaka aNi 73-63 eVnYrYa kaNakkil makArARtira aNiyE vIlYYwwiyawu . 
karnAtaka aNiyil paNtavayA 24 , pUmikA 13 pulYlYikalY kuviwwanYar . 
wamilYYakam cAmpiyanY : irYuwi AttafkalY FAyirYrYukkilYYamE natEpeVrYrYanYa . 
Atavar pirivil natappu cAmpiyanY wamilYYakamum , keralYamum mowinYa . 
iwil wamilYYakam 88-77 eVnYrYa pulYlYikalY kaNakkil keralYawwE veVnYrYu cAmpiyanY pattam veVnYrYawu . 
wamilYYaka aNiyil keptanY harirAm , tenYiyal ulYlYitta vIrarkalY cirYappAka vilYEyAtinYar . 
makalYir pirivil wamilYYakamum - karnAtaka aNiyum mowinYa . 
iwil karnAtaka makalYir aNi cirYappAka vilYEyAti 64-44 eVnYrYa pulYlYikalY kaNakkil wamilYYakawwE vIlYYwwiyawu . 
arEyirYuwiyil natappuc cAmpiyanY cawwIskarE vIlYYwwiya wamilYYakam , irYuwi Attawwil eVwirpArwwa alYavukku vilYEyAtavillE . 
veVrYrYipeVrYrYa aNikalYukku inwiya kUtEppanwu cammelYanYaw walEvar ke.kovinwarAj , arEs inYtastrIs walEvar Awav arjunYA Akiyor paricukalYE valYYafkinYar . 
pANticceri poVrYiyiyal kallUri muwalvar ti.cunwarrAjanY walEmE vakiwwAr . 
woVlYYilawipar vi.rAjacekar , puwucceri kUtEppanwu cafkaw walEvar jAnY pAsko , ceVyalar vi.rakowwamanY ulYlYittor pafkerYrYanYar . iyarYkE valYYiwwatafkalYE marYEwwu kattitafkalYE katti ulYlYawe ceVnYnYE malYYE veVlYlYa pAwippukalYukku kAraNam 
puwuteVlli , 
ceVnYnYEyEc curYrYiyulYlYa erikalYinY eVllEkalY nAlYukku nAlY curukkikkoVNte ceVlkirYawu . 
oVrupakkam AkkiramippukalY , marYupakkam curYrYuccUlYYal mAcupAtu Akiya kAraNafkalYAl inwa nIr AwArafkalY alYYivE nokki ceVnYrYu koVNtirukkinYrYanYa . 
velYacceri eri , nafkanallUr eri , AwampAkkam eri , ulYlYakaram eri , pulYYuwivAkkam eri , wiricUlam eri , mInYampAkkam eri , mUvaracampattu eri , matippAkkam eri , kIlYYkkattalYE eri , nanYmafkalam eri , aswinYApuram eri , neVmilicceri eri , kovilampAkkam eri , palYlYikkaraNE eri , kovilampAkkam wAfkal , nArAyaNapuram eri , palYlYikkaraNE aNE eri , palYlYikkaraNE ciwweri , rAjakIlYYppAkkam eri , metavAkkam eri , jallatiyanYpettE eri , peVrumpAkkam eri , aracanYkalYYanYi eri , aracanYkalYYanYi wAfkal , ciwwAlappAkkam eri , colYYifkanallAr eri , ciwweri , oVttiyampAkkam eri , nAvalAr eri , akaram weVnY eri ponYrYa 31 nIr AwArafkalYAnYa erikalYEk kAkka veNti ulYlYawu . 
1975-m ANtil irunwa erikalYinY varEpatawwEk koVNtu pArkkum powu ivarYrYil peVrumpAlAnYa erikalY 200 ekkar parappalYavu koVNtavE . 
AnYAl inYrYEkku 50 ekkarAka curufkivittanYa . 
warYpowu erYpatta malYYE veVlYlYawwil ceVnYnYE nakaramum , purYanakarp pakuwikalYum nIril mUlYYkippoka mukkiya kAraName , erikalY marYrYum erik kAlvAykalY Akkiramippu ceVyyappattawe . 
ceVmparampAkkam eri . 
inwa eri nirampiyawAl ceVnYnYEyinY purYanakarkalY palavum mUlYYkip poyinYa . 
atEyArYu ArYrYEyoVtti peVrum pAwippu erYpattawu . 
ceVmparampAkkam eri nirYEnwAl awilirunwu varum waNNIr nerAka porUr erikkup poka veNtum . 
AnYAl awarYkAnYa kAlvAy pala itafkalYil AkkiramikkappattulYlYawu . 
palYlYikkaraNEyilum natanwawu . 
afkulYlYa eri wUrvArappatavillE . 
afkulYlYa cawuppu nilam pala itafkalYil Akkiramikkappattu vittawu . 
vIttu manYEkalYAkki vittanYar . 
manYiwa Akkiramippu makAk koVtUramAka natanwu varukirYawu . 
iwuve appakuwi veVlYlYakkAtAka kAraNam . 
erikalYE vita mika mika mukkiyamAnYawu avarYrYinY kAlvAykalYwAnY . 
kAraNam , eri nirampumpowu awanY upari nIr inwa kAlvAykalY mUlamAkawwAnY atuwwatuwwa erikalYukku poka mutiyum . 
avE kittawwatta mulYYu alYavil Akkiramippu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
ceVnYnYEyinY malYYE veVlYlYa pAwipinY mukkiya pAwippu kurYiwwu inwiya arYiviyal marYrYum curYrYuccUlYYal mEya tEraktar cunYiwA nArAyaNanY iwuparYrYi kUrYiyawAvawu : 
paruva nilE mArYrYawwAl cila itafkalYil eVwirpArAwa alYavukku awika malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
ceVnYnYEyil peVriya alYavil malYYE peVywawarYku iwuwAnY kAraNam . 
inwiya wuNE kaNtam mulYYuvawume iwu ponYrYa vAnYilE mArYrYafkalY erYpattuk koVNtu irukkinYrYanYa . 
inwiya nakarafkalYil iyarYkEyAnYa nIramEppukalYE pAwukAkka uriya natavatikkEkalY eVtukkappatavillE . 
kurYippAka ceVnYnYE , mumpE , koVlkawwA , teVlli , srInakar ponYrYavarYrYil inwa viRayafkalYil cariyAka kavanYam ceVluwwavillE . 
iwuparYrYi nAfkalY erYkanYave kUrYi irukkirYom . 
poVwuvAka eri , kulYafkalYilirunwu veVlYiyerYum waNNIrum , ArYrYu , otE waNNIrum iyarYkEyAkave valYYiw watafkalYE amEwwu irukkum . 
veVlYlYam erYpatumpowu anwa valYYiw watafkalYil waNNIr ceVnYrYu katalil kalanwu vitum . 
iwanYAl peVriya pAwippukalY erYpatAwu . 
AnYAl , ceVnYnYE ponYrYa nakarafkalYil iyarYkE valYYiwwatafkalYE marYEwwu kattitafkalYE katti ulYlYanYar . 
iwanYAl waNNIr ceVlvawarYku valYYiyillAmal kutiyiruppukalYukkulY waNNIr pukunwu peVrum pAwippE erYpatuwwi vittanYa . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . 
arYiviyal curYrYucUlYYal mEya wuNE witta melAlYar cuRmiwA ceVnY kupwA kUrYum powu , nakarafkalY amEnwulYlYa itafkalYil munYpu AfkAfke nIr wefki iruppawarYku kulYam , kuttEkalY irunwanYa . 
avarYrYEyum alYYiwwu vittawAl nIr wefkuvawarYku vAyppu illE . 
iwanYAl nilawwati nIr varYrYi katal nIr ulYlYe pukunwulYlYawu . 
iwu ponYrYa kAraNafkalYAl wAnY ceVnYnYEyil kutinIr wattuppAtu erYpattawarYku kAraNam . 
ceVnYnYEyil wefkum malYYE nIr cariyAka vatinwu ceVlvawarYku uriya vAykkAl vacawikalY ceVyyappatavillE . 
iwuwAnY veVlYlYawwukku kAraNamAka ulYlYawu eVnYrYu kUrYinYAr . 
arYiviyal mEyam wakavalpati ceVnYnYEyil 1980 vAkkil 600 eri , kulYafkalY irunwanYa . 
ippowu avarYrYil oVru pakuwi mattume miFci irukkirYawu . 
1130 heVkter parappalYavil 19 peVriya erikalY irunwanYa . 
avE warYpowu 649 heVkterAka curufki ulYlYawu eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 160 woVkuwikalYE kEpparYrYi we.mu.wi.ka. makkalY nalakkUttaNi Atci amEkkum ; 
piremalawA vijayakAnw peccu 
srIpeVrumpuwUr ,

meVkA kUttaNi 
srIpeVrumpuwUr cattamanYrYa woVkuwiyil we.mu.wi.ka , makkalY nalakkUttaNi wa.mA.kA. aNi cArpil vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katci vetpAlYar mA.vIrakkumAr pottiyitukirYAr . 
ivarE Awariwwu cufkuvArcawwiram perunwu nilEyam aruke nerYrYu piremalawA vijayakAnw piracArawwil ItupattAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
wamilYYakawwil katanwa 50 ANtukalYAka wi.mu.ka.vum , a.wi.mu.ka.vum mArYi mArYi AtciyamEwwu varukinYrYanYa . 
inwa nilE mArYaveNtum eVnYpawarYkAkave wamilYYakawwil keptanY walEmEyilAnYa meVkA kUttaNi uruvAkiyulYlYawu . 
inwa kUttaNi uruvAnYapowu 3-vawu aNi eVnYa coVllappattu vanwawu .

wamilYYakawwil Atci amEkkappokum aNiyum iwuwAnY . 
ilYEFarkalYukku velEvAyppu 
woVtarnwu veVlYiyAkum karuwwukkaNippukalYE parYrYi yArum kavalEppata veNtAm . 
pulanYAyvuwwurYE mUlam kitEwwa wakavalpati namawu kUttaNi 130 muwal 160 woVkuwikalY varE veVrYrYi peVrYrYu Atci amEkkappokirYawu .

iwwoVlYYirYcAlEkalYil ulYlYUr ilYEFarkalYukku velEvAyppu valYYafkappatuvawillE . 
namawu kUttaNi Atci amEnwavutanY ulYlYUr ilYEFarkalYukku velEvAyppu valYYafkappatum . 
eVnYave we.mu.wi.ka. makkalY nalakkUttaNi Atci amEkka srIpeVrumpuwUr woVkuwiyil pottiyitum mA.vIrakkumArukku mowiram cinYnYawwil vAkkalYikkaveNtum . 
ivvArYu piremalawA vijayakAnw kUrYinYAr . inwiya oVlimpik vilviwwE aNiyil wIpikA kumAri 
puwuteVlli , me. 17 - 
pirecilinY riyoti jeVnYIro nakaril varukirYa Akastu mAwam oVlimpik potti natakkirYawu . 
oVlimpik pottikkAnYa vilviwwE panwayawwil inwiya peVNkalY aNiyinYar mUnYrYu wanYinapar marYrYum oVru kulYYu pirivukkAnYa itawwE urYuwi ceVywirunwanYar . 
inwa nilEyil anwa vAyppil kalYam irYafkuvawu yAr - yAr ? eVnYrYa vivarawwE inwiya vilviwwE cafkam nerYrYu arYiviwwawu . 
iwanYpati natcawwira vIrAfkanYEkalY wIpikA kumAri , pampEyalA wevi , latcumi rANi Akiyor aNiyil itam pitiwwulYlYanYar . 
katanwa mUnYrYarE mAwafkalYAka natanwa wakuwiw wervu atippatEyil wervAki irukkum ivarkalY wanYinapar pirivilum aNi pirivilum pafkerYpArkalY . 
inwiya ANkalY vilviwwE aNiyil iwuvarE oVru wanYinapar oVlimpik itam mattume kitEwwulYlYawu . 
atuwwa mAwam wurukkiyil natakkum ulaka koppE ( 3-m nilE ) vilviwwE pottiyil jeVyanwA walukwar , awAnYu wAs , mafkalY cif cAmpiyA Akiyor atafkiya inwiya aNiyinYar kalanwu koVlYkirYArkalY .

makkalY makilYYcci - ceVnYnYE : 
ceVnYnYEyil rAyappettE , nufkampAkkawwil cAral malYYE peVywu varuvawAl makkalY makilYYcciyatEnwulYlYanYar . 
wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalukkAnYa vAkkuppawivu inYrYu kAlE muwal viruviruppAka natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYawu . 
innilEyil ceVnYnYE rAyappettE , nufkampAkkawwil cAral malYYE peVywu varuvawAl makkalY makilYYcciyutanY wafkalY vAkkE pawivu ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . nAfkuneri woVkuwi pAttAlYi makkalY katci vetpAlYar a.wi.mu.ka.vil iNEnwAr 
neVllE , nAfkuneri woVkuwi pAttAlYi makkalY katciyinY vetpAlYar wiruppawi , munYnYAlY amEccar nayinYAr nAkenwiranY munYnYilEyil a.wi.mu.ka.vil iNEnwAr . 
pA.ma.ka. vetpAlYar natEpeVrYa ulYlYa cattacapE werwalil wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum ulYlYa 234 woVkuwikalYilum pA.ma.ka. wanYiwwu pottiyitukirYawu . 
inwa katciyinY cArpil neVllE mAvattawwil ulYlYa nAfkuneri cattacapE woVkuwiyil pA.ma.ka. vetpAlYarAka wiruppawi reVttiyAr arYivikkappattu irunwAr . 
avar vetpumanYu wAkkal ceVywu werwal piracArawwil Itupattu vanwAr . 
inwa nilEyil nerYrYu vetpAlYar wiruppawi reVttiyAr witIreVnYrYu wanYawu werwal piracArawwE nirYuwwivittu neVllEkku wanYawu AwaravAlYarkalYutanY vanwAr . 
pinYnYar munYnYAlY amEccarum , neVllE woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarumAnYa nayinYAr nAkenwiranY munYnYilEyil a.wi.mu.ka.vil iNEnwAr .

awE cAwi katciyAkave makkalY pArkkirYArkalY .

katEciyAkak kitEwwa wakavalkalYinY pati cunYAmi eVccarikkE wirumpap peVrYappattawu . 
inwonYeciyAvinY merYkup pakuwiyAnYa cumawwirAvil katalukku atiyil payafkara nilanatukkam erYpattulYlYawEyatuwwu cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattulYlYawu . 
cumawwirAvinY weVnYmerYke , pawAf nakarukku pala nUrYu kimI woVlEvil katalukku atiyil erYpatta inwa nilanatukkam riktar alYavil 7.9 eVnYrYu pawivAkiyulYlYawAka ameVrikka puviyiyal Ayvu mEyam yu.eVs.ji.eVs. weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
inwiya nerappati mAlE 6.20 maNiyalYavil inwa nilanatukkam erYpattulYlYawu . 
katalukku atiyil 10 ki.mI AlYYawwil inwa nilanatukka mEyam irunwawu . 
iwuvarE cewam marYrYum uyirilYYappukalY parYrYiya wakavalkalY illE . 
iwanYE atuwwu merYku cumawwirA utpata cumawwirAvinY pakuwikalY , vatakku cumawwirA , ace Akiya itafkalYukku cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYawu . 
awika katal AlYYamillAwa pakuwiyil erYpatum nilanatukkafkalY katum cewam vilYEvikkak kUtiyavE , AnYAl inwa nilanatukkam muvArA cEparut nilappakuwikku 662 kimI woVlEvil erYpattulYlYawAl pAwippu kurYEvAkave erYpatalAm eVnYrYu ameVrikka puviyiyal Ayvu mEyamAnYa yu.eVs.ji.eVs. weVriviwwulYlYawu . pA.ma.ka. Atci vanwAl 2 wuNE muwalamEccar pawavi uruvAkkappatum ; tAktar rAmawAs petti 
ceVnYnYE , pA.ma.ka . Atcikku vanwAl 2 wuNE muwalamEccar pawavi uruvAkkappatum eVnYrYu tAktar rAmawAs kUrYinYAr . 
pA.ma.ka. nirYuvanYar tAktar rAmawAs niruparkalYukku nerYrYu petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
walEkkunYivu 
wamilYYakawwil carvAwikAra AtciyE jeVyalaliwA natawwi varukirYAr . 
avarinY Atcikku UlYYal awikArikalYum wuNE poy ulYlYanYar . 
wamilYYakawwil UlYYalE arYimukappatuwwiyawe karuNAniwi wAnY .

50 ANtukAla wi.mu.ka , a.wi.mu.ka. Atcikku makkalY murYrYuppulYlYi vEkka veNtum .

eVNNippArufkalY . 
wi.mu.ka , a.wi.mu.ka. inwa 2 katcikalYinY UlYYalkalYE makkalY mawwiyil pA.ma.ka. mikaccariyAka eVtuwwurEwwawu . 
inwa 2 katcikalYAl wAnY kurYippitta cawavIwa makkalY inYnYum vAkkalYikkave virumpavillE . 
inYrYEkku mArYrYu araciyalE munYeVtuwwu ceVllum pA.ma.ka. mIwum , muwalamEccar vetpAlYar tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs mIwum makkalYukku nampikkE vanwulYlYawu . 
tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAcE makkalY Awarikka munYvanwu irukkirYArkalY . 
paNam pawukkal 
eVppatiyAvawu AtciyE pitiwwu vita veNtum eVnYrYu AlYum katciyum , ANta katciyum paNawwE vAri irYEkkirYawu . 
iwuvarE 100 koti rUpAy parYimuwal ceVyyappattu iruppawAka wakaval veVlYiyAki ulYlYawu . 
AnYAl 10 Ayiram koti rUpAy alYavukku inwa iraNtu katcikalYum pawukki vEwwu irukkirYArkalY . 
inwiyAvileye paNawwAl vAkkukalYE vAfkum mAnilafkalYil wamilYYakam 2-vawu itawwil ulYlYawu . 
eVnYnYutEya vItu amEnwulYlYa wiNtivanYawwil kUta anwa iru katcikalYum paNawwE vAri irYEkkirYArkalY . 
paNam koVtukkAmal veVrYrYi peVrYa mutiyAwu eVnYrYa nilEkku wi.mu.ka.vum , a.wi.mu.ka.vum vanwu vittawu . 
eVnYave wAnY paNawwE alYlYi vIcukirYArkalY . 
2 wuNE muwalamEccar minYwatEyAl wamilYYakawwirYku vara veNtiya woVlYYil muwalIttAlYarkalY verYu mAnilawwirYku ceVnYrYu vittArkalY . 
pA.ma.ka. Atcikku vanwawum woVlYYil muwalIttAlYarkalY wamilYYakawwirYku varakkUtiya nilEyE uruvAkkuvom . 
eVfkalY muwalamEccare neratiyAka muwalIttAlYarkalYitam peci , wamilYYakawwil awikalYavil woVlYYil muwalItukalYE IrppAr . 
pA.ma.ka. werwal arYikkEyil kurYippitta wittafkalYE nAfkalY nirYEverYrYuvom . 
makkalYukkAka puwiya wittafkalYE uruvAkkuvom . 
pA.ma.ka. veVrYrYi peVrYrYu tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs muwalamEccarAka pawaviyerYkumpowu 2 wuNE muwalamEccar pawavi uruvAkkappatum . 
oVru wuNE muwalamEccar weVnY mAvattawwE cernwavarAkavum , marYrYoVru wuNE muwalamEccarAka peVN oVruvarum wernweVtukkappatuvArkalY . 
urYuwimoVlYYi 
nAlYE ( inYrYu ) eVfkalY katciyinY vetpAlYarkalY meVrinYA katarYkarE kAnwi cilE munYpu ‘ paNi ceVyvom allawu pawavi vilakuvom ’ eVnYrYa urYuwimoVlYYiyE makkalY mawwiyil eVtukka ulYlYanYar . 
pA.ma.ka. Atcikku vanwawum wUymEyAnYa , veVlYippatEyAnYa nirvAkam ceVyalpatum . 
ivvArYu tAktar rAmawAs kUrYinYAr .

kavuwam kAmpIr karuwwu - 
wi inwu . 
cirYappAnYa panwuvIccAl EpieVl pottiyil punYe aNiyE veVnYrYom eVnYrYu koVlkawwA nEtrEtars aNiyinY keptanY kavuwam kAmpIr kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
EpieVl kirikkeVt woVtaril koVlkawwAvil nerYrYu munYwinYam natanwa pottiyil punYe cUppar jeVyaNts aNiyutanY koVlkawwA nEtrEtars aNi mowiyawu . 
ippottiyil punYe aNi muwalil pettif ceVywawu . 
koVlkawwA panwu vIccAlYarkalYinY cirYappAnYa panwu vIccAl punYe aNiyAl awika ranYkalYEk kuvikka mutiyavillE . 
anwa aNiyil peVyli mattum oralYavu cirYappAka Ati 27 panwukalYil 33 ranYkalYEk kuviwwAr . 
marYrYa vIrarkalY anYEvarum coVrYpa ranYkalYil avutAka punYe aNi 17.4 ovarkalYil 6 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 103 ranYkalYE eVtuwwu irunwapowu malYYE kurYukkittawu . 
appowu wonYi 22 panwukalYil 8 ranYkalYotum , asvinY 4 panwukalYil ranY ewum eVtukkAmalum AtikkoVNtirunwanYar . 
koVlkawwA aNiyil awikapatcamAka piyUR cAvlA 2 vikkeVtkalYE vIlYYwwinYAr . 
malYYE kAraNamAka Attam nINtaneram pAwikkappattawAl ovarkalY kurYEkkappattanYa . 
mINtum Attam woVtafkiyapowu koVlkawwA aNi veVrYrYipeVrYa 9 ovarkalYil 66 ranYkalYE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYa ilakku nirNayikkappattawu . 
anwa aNiyinY yUcup pawAnY 18 panwukalYil 37 ranYkalYEk kuvikka , 5 ovarkalYileye 2 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 66 ranYkalYEk kuviwwu koVlkawwA veVrYrYipeVrYrYawu . 
inwa veVrYrYiyutanY 14 pulYlYikalYEp peVrYrYu koVlkawwA aNi 2-vawu itawwukku munYnYerYiyawu . 
inwa veVrYrYiyEp parYrYi niruparkalYitam peciya koVlkawwA aNiyinY keptanY kAmpIr , “ inYrYEya pottiyil eVfkalY vekappanwu vIccAlYarkalY cirYappAnYa woVtakkawwEw wanwArkalY . 
awEp pinYparYrYi culYYarYpanwu vIccAlYarkalYum cirYappAkap panwuvIci punYevEk kattuppatuwwinYArkalY . 
piyUR cAvlA , cunYil narEnY Akiyor mIwu nAnY mikunwa nampikkE vEwwulYlYenY . 
anwa nampikkEyE avarkalY kAppArYrYi vittArkalY .

cunYAmi eVccarikkE 
kuvitto : 
weVnY ameVrikkAvinY vatakku katarYkarEyora nakaramAnYa Ikkuvetar nAttil inYrYu atuwwatuwwu wAkkiya iru nilanatukkafkalYAl 30 per paliyAkiyulYlYanYar . 
walEnakar kuvittovilirunwu 173 kilomIttar vatamerYke pUmiyinY atiyil cumAr irupawu kilomIttar AlYYawwil muwalil oVru miwamAnYa nilanatukkamum , awarYkatuwwa cila nimitafkalYil cakwivAynwa marYrYoVru nilanatukkamum erYpattawAka pacipik peVrufkatal cunYAmi eVccarikkE mEyam arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
( inwiya nerappati ) inYrYu kAlE cumAr 6.30 maNiyalYavil muwalil erYpatta nilanatukkam 4.8 riktarAkavum , iraNtAvawAka erYpatta nilanatukkam 7.8 riktarAkavum pawivAkiyulYlYawu .

pIwi atEnwa makkalY vItukalYE vittu oti vanwu vIwikalYil waFcam atEnwanYar .

manYttA nakaril ulYlYa vimAnYa nilEyawwil kattuppAttu arYE kopuram cAynwu vilYYunwawu . 
merYkaNta mUnYrYu nakarafkalYilum pala vItukalY itinwu nAcam atEnwa nilEyil , itipAtukalYil cikki cumAr 30 per paliyAnYawAka ulYlYUr UtakafkalY ceVywi veVlYiyittulYlYanYa . 
inwa nilanatukkawwinY wAkkam aNtE nAtAnYa peVruvinY vatapakuwikalYilum uNarappattawAka anwa ceVywikalY kurYippitukinYrYanYa . 
inYrYEya nilanatukkam wAkkiya pakuwiyilirunwu cumAr 300 kilomIttar curYrYalYavil ulYlYa katalorap pakuwikalYil peralEkalY eVlYYak kUtum eVnYa mawippitappattu ulYlYawAl , appakuwikalYil cunYAmi eVccarikkE vitukkappattulYlYawu . a.wi.mu.kavinY werwal arYikkE ceVywi veVlYiyitta ayarlAnwu pawwirikE ceVnYnYE , wamilYYaka werwal kalYawwil , immurYE cila pirawAnYa katcikalY ilavaca arYivippukalYE wavirwwAlum , AlYum awimuka katci ilavacafkalYE wavirkkavillE . 
iwu kurYiwwu wi ErIs tEms ( The Irish Times ) eVnYnYum ayarlAnwu nAlYiwalYYil ceVywi veVlYiyittu ulYlYawu .

oVlimpik pottiyil pafkupeVrYum inwiya malyuwwa vIrarkalYukkAnYa payirYci mukAm puwanYkilYYamE conYepattil woVtafkavulYlYawu . 
inwa mukAmil kalanwu koVlYlYum vIrarkalYinY pattiyalil iraNtu murYE oVlimpikkil pawakkam veVnYrYavarAnYa cucil kumArinY peVyar itam peVrYavillE . 
iwu riyo oVlimpik pottiyil kalanwukoVlYlYum avarawu kanYavukku peVrum pinYnYatEvAka karuwappatukirYawu . 
74 kilokirAm eVtEppirivil cucil kumArukku pawilAka narcif yAwavinY peVyar inwap pattiyalil itampeVrYrYulYlYawu . 
inwiya malyuwwa kUttamEppinY nirvAki oVruvar iwukurYiwwu ceVywi nirYuvanYam oVnYrYitam kUrYumpowu , “ inwa payirYci mukAm riyo oVlimpik pottiyil kalanwu koVlYlYa erYkeVnYave wernweVtukkappatta varkalYukkAka natawwappatukirYawu . 
inwa mukAmil kalanwu koVlYlYa cucil kumAr virumpinYAl avarE varaverYpom ” eVnYrYAr . 
oVlimpikkil kalanwu koVlYlYum vIrarE wernweVtukka cucil kumArukkum , narcif yAwavukkum itEye potti natawwumArYu aracu valiyurYuwwi ulYlYawA eVnYrYa kelYvikku , iwuparYrYi aracitam irunwu iwuvarE uwwaravu ewum varavillE ” eVnYrYu avar kUrYinYAr . makArARtira varYatci nilEkku uwava munYvanwa cInYa walEvarukku patnYAvis pArAttu 
mumpE , 
makArARtirAvil ulYlYa varYatci cUlYYnilEyE karuwwil koVNtu uwavi ceVyya munYvanwa cInYa walEvarukku muwalmanwiri wevenwira patnYAvis wanYawu pArAttukalYE weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
cInYAvil ulYlYa cInYa kamyUnYistu katciyinY urYuppinYar marYrYum RAfkAy nakara kulYYu walEvarAnYa henY jeVf marYrYum patnYAvis iruvaritEye inYrYu mumpEyil canwippu natanwawu . 
inwa canwippu kurYiwwu tuvittaril karuwwu weVriviwwulYlYa patnYAvis , varYatci cUlYYalE kurYiwwu karuwwil koVNtu makArARtirAvilulYlYa varYatci pAwikkappattulYlYa mAvattafkalYukku uwavi ceVyya munYvanwulYlYawarYku ufkalYukku mikka nanYrYi henY . 
mumpE marYrYum RAfkAy Akiya iru nakarafkalYukku itEye oVwwulYYEppE awikarikkum valYYikalY kurYiwwum marYrYum oVppanwam erYpatuwwi koVlYvawarYkAnYa kUttu wittawwinYE uruvAkka veNtiya wevE kurYiwwum AlocanYE natawwinYom eVnYa kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
mumpE marYrYum RAfkAy nakarafkalYukku itEye oVwwulYYEppirYkAnYa natavatikkEkalYE merYkoVNtu ulakirYku or eVtuwwukkAttAka awanYE amEya ceVyyum nokkil irukkirYom . 
inwa kUttam cirYapputanY amEnwawu eVnYa awil avar weVriviwwulYlYAr . anYal parYakkum piracAram nAlYE oykirYawu ; 
wifkatkilYYamE vAkkuppawivu 
ceVnYnYE , wamilYYaka cattacapEkku varukirYa 16-nwewi ( wifkatkilYYamE ) werwal natEpeVrYa ulYlYawu . 
3,776 vetpAlYarkalY iwarYkAnYa vetpu manYu wAkkal katanwa mAwam 22-nwewi woVtafki 29-nwewi varE natEpeVrYrYawu . 
iwEw woVtarnwu katanwa me 2-nwewi irYuwi vetpAlYar pattiyal veVlYiyitappattawu . 
234 woVkuwikalYilum 3,776 per pottiyitukirYArkalY . 
wamilYYaka araciyal kalYawwil eVppowum illAwa alYavukku 6 munYE potti nilavukirYawu . 
anYEwwu katcikalYum wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum wafkalY katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu wIvira piracAram merYkoVNtu varukinYrYanYa . 
walEvarkalY piracAram 
muwalamEccarum , a.wi.mu.ka . poVwuc ceVyalAlYarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA katanwa mAwam 9-nwewi ceVnYnYE wIvuwwitalil piracArawwE woVtafkinYAr . 
katanwa 6-wewi wAnY pottiyitum Ar.ke.nakar woVkuwiyil venY mUlam vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu piracAram ceVywAr . 
nerYrYu munYwinYam ceVnYnYEyil 16 woVkuwikalYil avar vIwi vIwiyAka wIvira piracArawwil Itupattu , vAkku cekariwwAr . 
nerYrYu neVllE pAlYEyafkottEyil natanwa werwal piracAra kUttawwil avar kalanwu koVNtu pecinYAr . 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum piracAra poVwukkUttawwil pafkerYrYu wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalYukku Awaravu wirattinYAr . 
nerYrYu avar wiruvArUril piracAram merYkoVNtAr . 
wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu wi.mu.ka. marYrYum awanY kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYukku Awaravu wiratti varukirYAr . 
moti - rAkulkAnwi iwepol we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar vijayakAnw , ma.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYar vEko , wa.mA.kA. walEvar ji.ke.vAcanY , vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katci walEvar wirumAvalYavanY , mArkcist kamyUnYistu katciyinY mAnila ceVyalAlYar ji.rAmakiruRNanY , inwiya kamyUnYistu katciyinY mAnila ceVyalAlYar muwwaracanY Akiyor wafkalY kUttaNi vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu piracAram merYkoVNtu ulYlYanYar . 
pA.ma.ka. nirYuvanYar tAktar rAmawAs , pArawIya janYawA katci walEvar tAktar wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanY , nAm wamilYYar katciyinY oVrufkiNEppAlYar cImAnY Akiyorum wIvira piracAram merYkoVNtu varukinYrYanYar . 
pirawamar narenwiramoti , pArawIya janYawA weciya walEvar amiwRA marYrYum mawwiya manwirikalY , kAfkiras walEvar conYiyAkAnwi , wuNEwwalEvar rAkulkAnwi , pakujanY camAj katciyinY walEvar mAyAvawi Akiyorum wamilYYnAttukku vanwu piracAram ceVywanYar . 
nAlYE oykirYawu 
katanwa 10 nAtkalYukkum melAka natanwu varum werwal piracAram uccakkattawwE neVrufki ulYlYawu . 
araciyal katcikalYinY anYal parYakkum piracAram nAlYE ( canYikkilYYamE ) mAlE 6 maNiyutanY oykirYawu . 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi nAlYE ceVnYnYE cinwAwiripettEyil wanYawu piracArawwE nirYEvu ceVykirYAr . 
wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY kOwwUr woVkuwiyilum , ma.wi.mu.ka. poVwuc ceVyalAlYar vEko wUwwukkutiyilum , we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar vijayakAnw velYacceriyilum , tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs peVnYnYAkarawwilum , pArawIya janYawA walEvar wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanY virukampAkkawwilum , wa.mA.kA. walEvar ji.ke.vAcanY mayilAppUrilum , vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY walEvar wirumAvalYavanY kAttumanYnYArkovililum , nAm wamilYYar katciyinY oVrufkiNEppAlYar cImAnY katalUrilum piracArawwE nirYEvu ceVykirYArkalY . 
mawukkatEkalYE mUta uwwaravu nAlYE mAlE 6 maNi muwal 16-nwewi mAlE 6 maNi varE karuwwuk kaNippu natawwavum , karuwwuk kaNippu mutivukalYE veVlYiyitavum watE viwikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
melum nAlYE muwal 16-nwewi varE werwal woVtarpAnYa eVnwa kUttafkalYo , UrvalafkalYo natawwak kUtAwu eVnYrYum uwwaravitappattu ulYlYawu . 
awwutanY camUka valEwwalYafkalY marYrYum kurYuFceVywikalY mUlamAka piracAram ceVyyak kUtAwu eVnYrYum arYivurYuwwappattu irukkirYawu . 
oVvvoVru woVkuwiyilum veVlYiyUrkArarkalY wafki irukkak kUtAwu eVnYrYum , vAkkAlYarkalY allAwavarkalY nAlYE mAlE 6 maNikkup pirYaku woVkuwiyE vittu veVlYiyerYi vita veNtum eVnYrYum arYivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
mawukkatEkalYE mUtavum uwwaravitappattu ulYlYawu . 
parYakkumpatEkalY iwarYkitEye ottuppawivukkAnYa erYpAtukalYE werwal kamiRanY ceVywu mutiwwu ulYlYawu . 
wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum ulYlYa 5 kotiye 82 latcam vAkkAlYarkalYukkAka cumAr 66 Ayiram ottuccAvatikalY amEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
iwil pawarYrYamAnYa pakuwikalY Ayvu ceVywu pattiyal wayArikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
werwal erYpAtukalY ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYa nilEyil , vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNappattuvAtA ceVyyappatuvawE watukkavum werwal kamiRanY wIvira natavatikkEkalY eVtuwwu irukkirYawu . 
paNappattuvAtAvE watuppawarYkAka 234 woVkuwikalYilum 8 Ayirawwu 112 parYakkumpatEkalY amEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
wifkatkilYYamE vAkkuppawivu 
werwalE amEwiyAkavum cumukamAkavum natawwuvawarYkAka 30 Ayiram wuNE rANuvawwinYar wamilYYnAttukku vanwu ulYlYanYar . 
avarkalY 234 woVkuwikalYilum wayAr nilEyil irukkirYArkalY . 
anYEwwu ottuccAvatikalYukkum uriya minYnYaNu eVnwirafkalY wayAr nilEyil vEkkappattu irukkinYrYanYa . 
vAkkuppawivukku moVwwam 1½ latcam minYnYaNu eVnwirafkalY payanYpatuwwappata ulYlYanYa . 
ottuppawivu wifkatkilYYamE kAlE 7 maNikku woVtafki mAlE 6 maNi varE natEpeVrYum . 
awanYpirYaku anYEwwu minYnYaNu eVnwirafkalYum ottu eVNNum mEyafkalYukku koVNtu ceVllappatum .

mawwiya aracu arYivippu 
puwuteVlli , 
nAtu mulYYuvawum varYatci pAwikkappatta mAvattafkalYil vivacAyikalY payirkkatanY ceVluwwuvawu 5 ANtukalYukku oVwwivEkkappatuvawAka mawwiya aracu arYiviwwawu . 
varYatciyil 300 mAvattafkalY marAttiyam , rAjaswAnY , weVlufkAnYA , oVticA , jArkaNt , karnAtakA ulYlYitta mAnilafkalYil warYpowu katum varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
inwa mAnilafkalYinY 300 mAvattafkalY varYatci pAwikkappatta mAvattafkalYAka arYivikkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
iwanYAl warYpowu cAkupati ceVyyappattu ulYlYa payirkalY pAcanYa vacawi inYrYi cewam atEnwulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu nerYrYu pArAlYumanYrYawwil kelYvi nerawwinY powu viRNu wayAlY rAm , jakwAmpikA pAl , pirakalAwa pattel , kalonYal conYA rAm ( pA.janYawA ) , kalikeR nArAyaN cif wiyo ( pijU janYawA walYam ) , vIrappamoVyli ( kAfkiras ) , cupriyA cule ( weciyavAwa kAfkiras ) , vinYowkumAr ( weVlufkAnYA rARtiriya camiwi ) Akiya eVm.pi.kkalY wafkalYawu kavalEkalYEw weVriviwwu pecinYar . 
viRNu wayAlY rAm pecumpowu , wanYawu mAnilawwirYku ( jArkaNt ) kurYEnwa niwiyEye mawwiya aracu oVwukkItu ceVykirYawu eVnYrYAr . 
vIrappamoVyli , pala ANtukalYAka illAwa varYatci karnAtakAvil erYpattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYAr . 
iwEw woVtarnwu peciya mawwiya velYAN manwiri rAwAmokanY cif kUrYiyawAvawu : 
5 ANtukalY oVwwivEppu 
nAttinY pala mAnilafkalY katumEyAnYa varYatcikku ulYlYAki iruppawAl vafkikalYil vivacAyikalY vAfkiya payirkkatanYE wiruppic ceVluwwuvawE oVwwivEppawu eVnYrYu mawwiya aracu mutivu ceVywu irukkirYawu . 
30 cawavIwam varE cewamatEnwa payirkalYukkAnYa katanYE vivacAyikalY wiruppic ceVluwwuvawu 2 ANtukalYukku walYlYivEkkappatukirYawu . 
iwepol 50 cawavIwamum , awarYku melAka cewamatEnwa payirkalYukkAnYa katanYE wiruppic ceVluwwa 5 ANtukalYum oVwwivEkkappatukirYawu . 
varYatci nilEmEyE camAlYikka nIrpAcanYa vacawiyE peVrukkuwal , kutinIr wattuppAtinYrYi kitEkkac ceVywal , varYatci pAwikkappatta mAvattafkalYil kAlnatEkalYukku wIvanYam kitEkkac ceVywal ponYrYa natavatikkEkalYE mawwiya aracu eVtuwwu varukirYawu . 
niwi oVwukkItu 
vivacAyam eVnYpawu mAnilafkalY woVtarputEya viRayam eVnYrYAlum kUta varYatci nilEyEk karuwwil koVNtu mawwiya aracu uwavi ceVywu varukirYawu . 
weciya peritar nivAraNa niwi marYrYum iwara inYafkalYinY vAyilAka kUtuwal niwiyE oVwukkItu ceVykirYawu . 
varYatci pAwikkappatta 300 mAvattafkalYil 5 latcam heVkteril cAkupati ceVyyappatta payirkalYE pAwukAkka mAvatta nIrpAcanYa wittam ceVyalpatuwwappatum . 
mAnilafkalYinY wevEyE pUrwwi ceVyvawil munwEya Ekkiya murYpokku kUttaNi aracE vita moti aracu cirYappAka ceVyalpatukirYawu . 
24 maNi nerawwil patjeVt oVwukkIttu niwiyE mAnilafkalYukku valYYafka mawwiya aracu mutivu ceVywu ulYlYawu . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . a.wi.mu.ka. aracu mINtum amEnwavutanY maruwwuva patippukku nulYYEvuw wervu illAmale mANavarkalYE cerkka natavatikkE ; 
jeVyalaliwA urYuwi neVllE , 
a.wi.mu.ka. aracu mINtum amEnwavutanY maruwwuva patippukku nulYYEvuw wervu illAmale mANavarkalYE cerkka natavatikkE eVtukkappatum eVnYrYu muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA urYuwiyalYiwwAr . 
jeVyalaliwA piracAram 
wamilYYaka cattamanYrYa werwalEyoVtti , a.wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu katanwa mAwam ( epral ) 9-nwewi ceVnYnYEyil muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA piracArawwE woVtafkinYAr . 
woVtarnwu , viruwwAcalam , warmapuri , aruppukkottE , kAFcIpuram , celam , wirucci , puwucceri , mawurE , vilYYuppuram , kovE , peVrunwurYE , waFcAvUr , arakkoNam Akiya nakarafkalYil natanwa piracAra poVwukkUttawwil jeVyalaliwA pecinYAr . 
inwa nilEyil , nerYrYu mAlE pAlYEyafkottEyil natanwa piramANta werwal piracAra poVwukkUttawwil muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA pafkerYrYu , wiruneVlveli , wUwwukkuti marYrYum kanYnYiyAkumari mAvattafkalYil ulYlYa 20 woVkuwikalYil pottiyitum a.wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu pecinYAr . 
appowu avar peciyawAvawu : 
vettu wi.mu.ka.vum , kAfkiracum kUttaNi amEwwu ufkalYE kaNNIril wavikkavittanYa . 
awE mArYrYi ufkalYE kE wUkki vittu , ufkalYawu kaNNIrE wutEwwu , ufkalYawu mukafkalYil malarcciyE erYpatuwwiyawu a.wi.mu.ka. eVnYave , wi.mu.ka. - kAfkiras kUttaNikku alYikkappatum eVnwa oVru ottum , ufkalY nalanYukku nIfkalYe vEwwuk koVlYlYum vettu eVnYpawE marYanwuvitAwIrkalY . 
nulYYEvuwwervu rawwu 
maruwwuvam marYrYum pal maruwwuva pattapatippukalYukku nulYYEvuwwervu natawwappatuvawu elYYE , eVlYiya kirAmappurYa mANavarkalYukku pAwakamAka irukkum eVnYpawAl , awwakEya nulYYEvuwwervukku a.wi.mu.ka. eVppowum eVwirppu weVriviwwu vanwulYlYawu . 
anwa atippatEyileye , katanwa 2005-m ANtu nulYYEvuwwervE rawwu ceVywu oVru aracANE veVlYiyittawotu , 2006-m ANtu pipravari mAwam oVru wanYi cattawwE , eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa appowEya a.wi.mu.ka. aracu koVNtu vanwawu . 
inwa aracANEyum , cattamum , ceVnYnYE uyarnIwimanYrYawwAl rawwu ceVyyappattanYa . 
iwanY atippatEyileye 2006-m ANtu oVru puwiya cattam iyarYrYappattu , 2007-m ANtu muwal 12-m vakuppu mawippeVN atippatEyileye maruwwuvam marYrYum pal maruwwuvam pattapatippukalYukku mANavarkalY cerkkappatukinYrYanYar . 
inwa nilEyil , 27-12-2010 anYrYu akila inwiya alYavil maruwwuva patippukalYukkAnYa nulYYEvuwwervu natawwappata veNtum eVnYa inwiya maruwwuvak kulYYumam oVru arYivikkEyE veVlYiyittawu . 
iwanYE eVwirwwu palverYu mAnila uyarnIwimanYrYafkalYil wAkkal ceVyyappatta anYEwwu rit manYukkalYEyum uccanIwimanYrYam vicAriwwawu . 
pirawamarutanY neril canwippu 
wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa aracAl cariyAnYa vAwafkalY vEkkappattawanY atippatEyil , 18-7-2013 anYrYu poVwu nulYYEvu wervu natawwum arYivikkEyE uccanIwimanYrYam walYlYupati ceVywawu . 
inwa uccanIwimanYrYaw wIrppinYE erYrYukkoVlYlYAmal munwEya Ekkiya murYpokku kUttaNi aracu marYu Ayvu manYuvE wAkkal ceVywawu . 
inwa marYu Ayvu manYuvE wirumpap peVrYa veNtum eVnYrYu appowEya pArawa pirawamarukku nAnY katiwam eVlYYuwinYenY . 
mawwiyile pArawIya janYawA aracu amEnwa pinY , 2014-m ANtu jUnY mAwam pArawa pirawamarE neril canwiwwu , nAnY alYiwwa korikkE manYuvilum munwEya Ekkiya murYpokku kUttaNi aracinY mutivE marYuparicIlanYE ceVywu uccanIwimanYrYawwil wAkkal ceVyyappatta marYu Ayvu manYuvE wirumpap peVrYumArYu nAnY kettukkoVNtenY . 
mINtum vicAraNE iwanYE valiyurYuwwi woVtarnwu katiwafkalY eVlYYuwi vanwenY . 
inwa nilEyil , 11-4-2016 anYrYu uccanIwimanYrYam nulYYEvuwwervE rawwu ceVywu , 2013-m ANtu valYYafkiya wIrppE wirumpap peVrYrYu , mINtum muwalilirunwu vicAraNE merYkoVlYlYappatum eVnYa uwwaravittawu . 
anwa vicAraNE inYnYamum woVtafkappatavillE . 
inwa nilEyil , marYrYoVru valYYakkE vicAriwwa 3 nIwipawikalY atafkiya amarvu itEkkAla ANEyAka , maruwwuva pattappatippu mANavar cerkkEkku akila inwiya alYavil nulYYEvu wervu natawwappata veNtum eVnYa 9-5-2016 anYrYu uwwaravittulYlYawu . 
inwa valYYakkil wamilYYaka aracu eVwirmanYuwArarAka cerkkappatAwa nilEyilum , iwil valYYafkappatum uwwaravu wamilYYakawwirYku pAwakamAka amEnwuvitak kUtAwu eVnYpawAl , wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil mUwwa valYYakkarYiFarkalY AjarAki wamilYYaka aracAl nirYEverYrYappatta cattam parYrYiyum , awarYku janYAwipawi oVppuwal valYYafkiyawu parYrYiyum , poVwu nulYYEvuwwervAl kirAmappurYa mANavarkalY eVvvArYu pAwikkappatuvArkalY eVnYpawu parYrYiyeVllAm virivAka eVtuwwuk kUrYiyawutanY , avarYrYE eVlYYuwwup pUrvamAkavum wAkkal ceVywulYlYanYar . 
araciyal AwAyam AnYAl , uccanIwimanYrYam inwa cattam parYrYiyum , wamilYYaka aracinY vAwafkalY parYrYiyum , eVwEyum weVrivikkAmal , anYEwwu mAnilafkalYukkum poVwuvAnYa oVru nulYYEvuw wervE ci.pi.eVs.i. natawwa veNtum eVnYa uwwaravittulYlYawu . 
eVnwa oVru viRayawwilum araciyal AwAyam pArkkum karuNAniwi , iwu parYrYiyum or arYikkE veVlYiyittulYlYAr . 
awil , uccanIwimanYrYawwil wamilYYaka aracinY cArpil cariyAka vAwAtappatavillE eVnYrYeVllAm oVru poVyyE weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
inwiya maruwwuvak kavunYcil 2010-m ANtu nulYYEvuw wervE koVNtu vanwu arYivikkE veVlYiyitta powu mawwiya kAfkiras kUttaNi aracil irunwawu wi.mu.ka. wAnY . 
karuNAniwi ninYEwwirunwAl appowe pArawap pirawamaritam eVtuwwuc coVlli inwa arYivikkEyE wirumpap peVrYrYirukka iyalum . 
wanYic cattam kurYEnwapatcam wamilYYnAttil ulYlYa natEmurYEyEyum , cattawwEyum parYrYiyAvawu eVtuwwuccoVlli , wamilYYnAttukkAvawu anwa arYivikkEyilirunwu vilakku peVrYrYirukka mutiyum . 
AnYAl , karuNAniwiyinY cinwanYE eVllAm 2jiyEp parYrYiye irunwa kAraNawwAl , iwu woVtarpAka eVnwa natavatikkEyEyum karuNAniwi eVtukkavillE . 
wumpE vittuvittu vAlEp pitippawu pol , anwa arYikkEkku uyarnIwimanYrYawwil itEkkAla watE vAfki eVnYnYa payanY ? 
ufkalYawu AwaravutanY a.wi.mu.ka. aracu mINtum amEnwavutanY , maruwwuva patippu marYrYum pal maruwwuvap patippukalYukku nulYYEvuwwervu illAmaleye woVtarnwu mANavarkalY cerkkappatum vakEyil natavatikkEkalY eVtukkappatum eVnYrYa urYuwiyE inwa nerawwil nAnY ufkalYukku alYikkirYenY . 
wevEyeVnYil iwarYkeVnYa wanYiye oVru cattawwEyum a.wi.mu.ka. koVNtu varum eVnYpawEyum weVriviwwukkoVlYkirYenY . 
werwal arYikkE 
wafkalYawu werwal arYikkEyE wi.mu.ka.vinYar wAnY cUppar hIro eVnYrYum , kavarccikaramAnYa werwal arYikkE eVnYrYum kUrYi vanwanYar . 
emArYrYu arYikkEkalYE veVlYiyitupavarkalY wAnY ivvArYeVllAm wafkalY werwal arYikkEyEp parYrYi kUrYik koVlYvArkalY . 
eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkE cAmAnYiya makkalYukkAnYa werwal arYikkE . 
valYarccikkAnYa werwal arYikkE . 
eVnYave wAnY , inwaw werwal arYikkEkku eVnwa atEmoVlYYiyum wevEyillE . 
eVfkalY wittafkalYil iwu cariyillE awu cariyillE eVnYrYu cawA carva kAlamum kUrYi varukirYAr karuNAniwi . 
enY ? 
5 murYE muwalamEccarAka irunwa karuNAniwi , elYYE eVlYiyorE kE wUkkivituvawarYkAnYa eVnwaw wittafkalYEyum nirYEverYrYavillE . 
enY , ceVywirukkalAme ? 
elYYEkalYinY poVrulYAwArawwE mempatuwwa a.wi.mu.ka. aracu ceVyalpatuwwiyawEp pol , AtukalY karYavE mAtukalY valYYafkuwal kalvi upakaraNafkalY valYYafkuwal eVnYa karuNAniwiyum wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwi irukka mutiyume . 
avvArYu enY ceVyyavillE ? 
ceVyyavitAmal yAr watuwwArkalY ? 
uNmE eVnYnYaveVnYrYAl avvArYu ceVyvawarYku karuNAniwikku manYamillE . 
eVwil AwAyam kitEkkum ? 
eVwEyAvawu ilavacamAka valYYafkinYAl awilirunwu wafkalYukku eVnYnYa AwAyam kitEkkum eVnYrYu pArwwu wAnY vaNNaw woVlEkkAtci peVttiyE karuNAniwi valYYafkinYAr . 
elYYE , eVlYiyor mIwu wi.mu.ka.vukku akkarYEyillE . 
eVnYave wAnY , elYYEkalYukku payanY warum vAkkurYuwikalY avarkalY werwal arYikkEyil illE . 
awu mAwwiram allAmal elYYE , eVlYiya makkalYukkAnYa wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwa mAttom eVnYrYu neratiyAkak kUrYum wEriyamum karuNAniwikku illE . 
eVnYave wAnY , ammA uNavakawwE nAfkalY woVtarnwu natawwa mAttom eVnYa neratiyAkak kUrYAmal , inwu camaya arYanilEyaw wurYEyutanY iNEnwu oVruvelYE uNavukkum valYYiyillAwavarkalYukku ‘ ‘ aNNA uNavakam ’’ amEppom eVnYa makkalYE emArYrYum viwamAka coVlli irukkirYArkalY . 
vAkkurYuwi eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkEyil eVwEyum veVlYippatEyAkaw wAnY coVlliyulYlYom . 
katanwa cattamanYrYa werwalil alYiwwa vAkkurYuwikalYE eVllAm nAfkalY nirYEverYrYiyulYlYom . 
nAnY coVnYnYawE ceVywenY . 
coVllAwa pala wittafkalYEyum nAnY ceVyalpatuwwi ulYlYenY . 
coVllAwa pala wittafkalYEyum , elYYE , eVlYiyor nalanY kAkkum vakEyil nAnY koVNtu vanwenY . 
eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkEyil weVriviwwulYlYa vAkkurYuwikalY mUlam makkalYE emArYrYa ninYEppawAka wi.mu.ka.vinYar coVlvawE yArum nampa mAttArkalY . 
nAnY coVnYnYawE ceVyvenY eVnYpawu wamilYYaka makkalYukke weVriyum . 
ceVyvawEw wAnY inwa jeVyalaliwA coVlluvAlY eVnYpawu wamilYYaka makkalYukku nanYrYAkaw weVriyum . 
eVnYave , vAkkAlYa peVrumakkalYe , ippoVlYYuwu nAnY arYiviwwa wittafkalYEk kettuvittu ivvalYavu wAnY eVnYrYu karuwivitAwIrkalY . 
iwu mattum allAmal , inYnYum iwEvita cirYanwa wittafkalYE , iwE vita unYnYawamAnYa wittafkalYE , nIfkalY karYpanYE kUta ceVywu pArkka mutiyAwa pala wittafkalYE ufkalYukkAka nAnY koVNtu varuvenY . 
nAnY ceVyalpatuwwuvenY eVnYrYa vAkkurYuwiyE ufkalYukku inwa nerawwil alYikkirYenY . 
ivvArYu jeVyalaliwA pecinYAr . skuvAR : 
inwiyAvukku veVlYlYippawakkam - 
wi inwu 
wEpe nakaril Aciya skuvAR cAmpiyanYRip pottikalY natEpeVrYrYanYa . 
iwil peVNkalYukkAnYa kulYYu pirivil nerYrYu natanwa irYuwi Attawwil inwiya aNi maleciyAvE eVwirwwu Atiyawu . 
iwil muwal Attawwil inwiyAvinY cajikA 7 11 6 11 10 12 eVnYrYa ner ceVtkalYil maleciyAvinY civacafkari cuppiramaNiyawwitam worYrYAr . 
marYrYoVru pottiyil inwiyAvinY munYnYaNi vIrAfkanYEyAnYa josnYA cinYnYappA , maleciyAvinY teVliyA arnYAltitam 9 11 , 13 11 , 11 8 , 11 9 eVnYrYa kaNakkil porAti worYrYAr . 
iwanY mUlam maleciya aNi 2-0 eVnYrYa kaNakkil inwiyAvE vIlYYwwi wafkap pawakkam veVnYrYawu . 
irYuwip pottiyil worYrYa inwiyAvukku veVlYlYippawakkam kitEwwawu . kolAr wafkavayal , kolAr mAvattawwil muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varYatci pakuwikalYE pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVywAr . 
pinYnYar avar poVwumakkalYitam kurYEkalYEyum kettarYinwAr . 
muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kolAr mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyita muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA nerYrYu kAlE 11.30 maNikku kolArukku vanwAr . 
muwalil avar kolAr wAlukA woVttavalYlYapE kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYu varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYE pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVywAr . 
afku vivacAyikalYE canwiwwu kurYEkalYE kettarYinwAr . 
appowu afkirunwa vivacAyikalY wafkalY pakuwiyil kutinIr piraccinYE mikavum katumEyAka ulYlYawu . 
awE wIrkka veNtum eVnYrYu kUrYinYArkalY . 
6 nimitafkalY mattume afkirunwa ciwwarAmEyA , pinYnYar afkirunwu purYappattu kalkare kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYAr . 
afku vivacAyikalYE canwiwwu pecinYAr . 
appowu afkirunwa vivacAyikalY varYatciyAl nAfkalY mikavum pAwikkappattulYlYom , melum warYpowu katumEyAnYa kutinIr piraccinYEyum ulYlYawu eVnYrYu kUrYinYar . 
afku 2 nimitafkalY mattume vivacAyikalYE canwiwwa ciwwarAmEyA , pinYnYar afkirunwu purYappattu kallipurA kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYAr . 
AlocanYE kUttam afku vivacAyi oVruvar coVttu nIrppAcanYa wittawwinY mUlam amEwwirunwa kAykarYikalY wottawwE pArvEyittAr . 
pinYnYar afkulYlYa vivacAyikalYitam pecinYAr . 
awEyatuwwu avar cukattUr kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYu afku kirAma makkalYE canwiwwu kurYEkalYE kettarYinwAr . 
appowu kirAma makkalY wafkalY pakuwiyil aracu Aspawwiri veNtum , kutinIr piraccinYEyE wIrkka veNtum eVnYrYu korikkE vituwwanYar . 
awanY pinYnYar avar mAvatta paFcAyawwu aluvalakawwil natEpeVrYrYa varYatci marYrYum apiviruwwi paNikalY woVtarpAnYa AlocanYE kUttawwil kalanwu koVNtu pecinYAr . 
kUttawwirYku kolAr mAvatta kaleVktar wirilok canwirA walEmE wAfkinYAr . 
mAvatta poVrYuppu manwiri rAmalifkareVtti , pArAlYumanYrYa urYuppinYarum , munYnYAlY mawwiya manwiriyumAnYa ke.eVc.munYiyappA , eVm.eVl.e.kkalY nArAyaNacAmi , koVwwUr maFcunAw , kotihalYlYi maFcunAw , rameR kumAr , rAmakkA , varawwUr pirakAR , cikpalYlYAppUr eVm.eVl.e. cuwAkar , munYnYAlY eVm.eVl.ci. cuwarcanY ulYpata awikArikalY marYrYum mAvatta paFcAyawwu urYuppinYarkalY , mAvatta polIs cUppiraNtu wivyA kopinAw Akiyor kUttawwil kalanwu koVNtanYar . 
warNA porAttam kUttam mutinwa pirYaku muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kolAr jUnYiyar kallUri valYAkawwil poVwumakkalYE canwippawarYkAka ceVnYrYAr . 
afku wiraNtirunwa erAlYamAnYa poVwumakkalYE avar canwiwwu kurYEkalYE kettarYinwu manYukkalYE peVrYrYukkoVNtAr . 
appowu afkirunwa AwiwirAvitar amEppinYar ciwwarAmEyAvinY munYpu amarnwu warNA porAttawwil ItupattanYar . 
iwanYAl afku paraparappu erYpattawu . 
avarkalY , mulpAkal wAlukA maNNehalYlYi kirAmawwil wAlYYwwappattavarkalYukku eVwirAka , pirYa camUkawwinYar palverYu woVnwaravukalYE koVtuwwu varukirYArkalY eVnYrYum , iwukurYiwwu natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYum korikkE vituwwanYar . 
avarkalYinY korikkEyE erYrYa ciwwarAmEyA utanYe iwuparYrYi natavatikkE eVtuppawAka urYuwi alYiwwAr . 
43 ANtukalYil illAwa varYatci pinYnYar avar niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
karnAtaka mAnilawwil katanwa 43 ANtukalYil illAwa alYavil inwa ANtu katumEyAnYa varYatci erYpattulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl porkkAla atippatEyil mAnila aracu palverYu wittafkalYE wItti varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVNtu varukirYawu . 
kutinIr piraccinYEyE wIrkka powumAnYa alYavu niwikalY oVwukkappattu paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
nAnY erYkanYave 16 mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu muwal wakaval arYikkEyE peVrYrYulYlYenY . 
awanY atippatEyil varYatci nivAraNa paNikalY marYrYum kutinIrukkAka kUtuwalAka niwikalY oVwukki ulYlYenY . 
mAnila wuNE manwiri kulYYuvum , mAnilam mulYYuvawum palverYu pirivukalYAka pirinwu ceVnYrYu varYatci paNikalYE pArvEyittu arYikkEkalYE koVtuwwu varukirYArkalY . 
kaNtanYawwirYku uriyawu AnYAl mawwiya aracu , karnAtaka mAnila aracukku varYatcippaNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa powumAnYa alYavu niwikalYE oVwukkavillE . 
nAfkalY mulYYumEyAnYa wakavalkalYE koVtuwwa pinYpum mawwiya aracu niwikalYE oVwukkAwawu enY eVnYrYu weVriyavillE . 
iwu kaNtanYawwukku uriyawu . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . 
pinYnYar avar afkirunwu peVfkalYUruvukku purYappattu ceVnYrYAr . 
cikpalYlYAppUr curYrYuppayaNam rawwu 
ciwwarAmEyA nerYrYu kolAr marYrYum cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattafkalYil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyituvawAka irunwawu . 
kAlE 11 maNi muwal mawiyam 3 maNi varE kolArilum , awanY pinYnYar avar cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattawwilum curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varYatcip pakuwikalYE pArvEyittu makkalYitam kurYEkalYE kettarYivawAka arYivikkappattirunwawu . 
AnYAl kolAr mAvattawwileye mAlE 5 maNikkum mel Akivittawu . 
iwanYAl avar cikpalYlYAppUr curYrYuppayaNawwE rawwu ceVywuvittu peVfkalYUruvukku ceVnYrYuvittAr . 
virEvil avar cikpalYlYAppUr mAvattawwil varYatcippakuwikalYE pArvEyita varuvAr . 
awarYkAnYa wewi pinYnYar arYivikkappatum eVnYrYu aracu awikArikalY weVriviwwanYar . wi.mu.ka. Atci amEnwAl vivacAyikalY katanY cumE wIra valYYivakE ceVyyappatum ; 
wiruvArUr piracArawwil karuNAniwi peccu 
wiruvArUr , 
wi.mu.ka. Atci amEnwAl vivacAyikalY katanY cumE wIra valYYivakE ceVyyappatum eVnYrYu wiruvArUr woVkuwiyil natanwa werwal piracArawwinY powu karuNAniwi pecinYAr . 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi 2-m kattamAka wanYawu coVnwa woVkuwiyAnYa wiruvArUril 2 nAtkalY piracAram merYkoVlYvawarYkAka ceVnYnYEyilirunwu reVyil mUlamAka nerYrYu munYwinYam wiruvArUr varukE vanwAr . 
muwal nAlY piracArawwE vilYamalil woVtafki paviwwiramANikkawwil nirYEvu ceVywAr . 
2-vawu nAlYAka nerYrYu mAlE wiruvArUr pas nilEyawwil wanYawu piracArawwE woVtafkiya wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi makkalY mawwiyil uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwirYku vAkku kettu peciyawAvawu : 
AlYYiwwer katanwa werwalil pottiyittu veVrYrYi peVrYrYa nAnY wiruvArUr woVkuwi makkalYinY nanYmE , wImEkalYE arYinwu avarYrYE nirYEvu ceVywu irukkirYenY . 
wiruvArUril puwiya maruwwuvakkallUri woVtafkappattu rU. 100 koti mawippil awarYkAnYa kattitafkalY kattappattulYlYanYa . 
wiruvArUr wiyAkarAjar kovilukku puwiya wiruwwer uruvAkkappattulYlYawu . 
1989-m ANtu wiruvArUr mempAlam kattappattawu . 
wiruvArUr kaleVktar aluvalakam rU. 6 kotiye 91 latcam ceVlavil kattappattulYlYawu . 
palverYu aracu kattitafkalYum kattappattulYlYanYa . 
nINtakAlamAka vatam pitiwwu otAmal kitappil kitanwa AlYYiwwer palYYuwupArkkappattu otavitta peVrumE wi.mu.ka. AtciyE cArum . 
ippati wiruvArUr woVkuwi makkalYinY wevEkalYE nirYEverYrYiya Atci wi.mu.ka. Atci . 
anwa Atci mINtum uwayamAnYAl ufkalYutEya wevEkalYE arYinwu palverYu vacawikalY ceVywu warappatum . 
katanwa kAla anYupavafkalYE eVNNi pArwwu wi.mu.ka.virYku Awaravu alYiwwu uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwirYku vAkkalYiwwu maNNinY mEnwanYAnYa eVnYakku veVrYrYiyE wetiwwara veNtum . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr 
pulivalam 
pinYnYar pulivalawwil makkalY mawwiyil karuNAniwi peciyawAvawu : 
wiruvArUr woVkuwiyil ufkalYE nampi ufkalY AwaravE eVwirpArwwu oVru vetpAlYarAka nAnY nirYkirYenY . 
katanwa wi.mu.ka. Atciyil katanwa kAla cAwanYEkalYE nIfkalY eVNNi pArwwu ufkalY vIttu pilYlYEyAka , ufkalY urYavukkAranYAka eVnYnYE pAviwwu eVnYakku veVrYrYiyE wetiwwara veNtum . 
wi.mu.ka. veVrYrYi peVrYrYu Atci amEkkumAnYAl pulivalam peVrumAlY kulYawwE wUr vAri , watuppuccuvar amEwwu warappatum eVnYrYu urYuwi alYikkirYenY . 
wi.mu.ka.virYku nIfkalY woVtarnwu Awaravu wara veNtum eVnYrYAr . 
woVtarnwu mAfkutikku ceVnYrYa karuNAniwikku wi.mu.ka.vinYar urYcAka varaverYpu alYiwwanYar . 
afku wiraNtu irunwa makkalY mawwiyil karuNAniwi peciyawAvawu : 
katanwa werwalil uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwirYku vAkku alYiwwu eVnYakku veVrYrYiyE wetiwwanwIrkalY . 
mANavarkalY payanYpeVrYum vakEyil wiruvArUril maruwwuva kallUri , mawwiya palkalEkkalYYakam wi.mu.ka. Atciyil koVNtu varappattawu . 
inwa werwalil wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarAka pottiyitum maNNinY mEnwanYAnYa eVnYakku uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwil vAkkalYiwwu veVrYrYi peVrYa ceVyya veNtum eVnYa kettuk koVlYkirYenY . 
wi.mu.ka. Atci amEnwAl kUtUr kAttArYrYu pAlam akalappatuwwappatum . 
veVttArYrYinY kurYukke pAlam kattappatum . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . 
walYlYupati woVtarnwu karuNAniwi vatakarE , kIlYYamaNali , pUnwAlYYafkuti , karuppUr , kamalApuram Akiya itafkalYil piracAram ceVywAr . 
valYYi neVtukka AyirakkaNakkAnYa makkalY avarukku malar wUviyum pUraNa kumpa mariyAwE alYiwwum varaverYrYanYar . 
appowu avar peciyawAvawu : 
wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyil cirYu , kurYu vivacAyikalYukku payirkkatanY walYlYupati ceVyyappatum eVnYa arYivikkappattirunwawu .

iwE nIfkalY payanYpatuwwi koVlYlYalAm . 
wi.mu.ka. Atci amEnwAl vivacAyikalY peVruvAlYYvu vAlYYa avarkalYawu katanY cumE wIra valYYivakE ceVyyappatum . 
katanwa wi.mu.ka. Atciyil cAwi verYupAtu inYrYi anYEwwu makkalYinY wevEkalYE arYinwu nirYEverYrYi wanwulYlYom . 
vItu vAlYYa , nAtu vAlYYa , vivacAyikalY , woVlYYilAlYikalY , pAttAlYi makkalY anYEvarum ufkalYawu vAkkukalYE varukirYa 16-nwewi uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwil alYiwwu eVnYnYE veVrYrYi peVrYa ceVyya veNtum .

ilavaca poVrutkalYE waramAttom eVnYrYu eVnwa katciyAlum coVlla mutiyumA ? eVnYrYu pA.ma.ka. muwal-amEccar vetpAlYar anYpumaNi rAmawAs kUrYinYAr .

makkalYukku vituwalE 
a.wi.mu.ka. , wi.mu.ka. Akiya iru katcikalYEyum vIttukku anYuppinYAlwAnY makkalYAkiya ufkalYukku vituwalE .

ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . pANtyAvE kattuppatuwwa mutiyavillE : 
teVlli keptanY jAkIrkAnY petti 
vicAkappattinYam , me . 17 - 
E.pi.eVl. kirikkeVt pottiyil , vicAkappattinYawwil nerYrYu munYwinYam iravu natanwa lIk Attawwil mumpE inwiyanYs aNi 80 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil teVlli terteVvilcE panwAtiyawu . 
iwil muwalil pet ceVywa mumpE aNi 4 vikkeVt ilYYappukku 206 ranYkalY kuviwwawu . 
kuNAl pANtyA 86 ranYnYum ( 37 panwukalYil 7 pavuNtari , 6 cikcarutanY ) mArttinY kapwil 48 ranYnYum , keptanY rokiw carmA 31 ranYnYum vilYAcinYar . 
woVtarnwu Atiya teVlli aNi , mumpE vIrarkalYinY apAra panwu vIccE wAkkuppitikka mutiyAmal 19.1 ovarkalYil 126 ranYnYil curuNtu patuwolvi atEnwawu . 
86 ranYkalY kuviwwawutanY 2 vikkeVttum vIlYYwwi Al-ravuNtarAka muwwirE pawiwwa mumpE vIrar kuNAl pANtyA AttanAyakanY viruwu peVrYrYAr . 
E.pi.eVl. varalArYrYil mumpE inwiyanYs aNi pawivu ceVywa 80-vawu veVrYrYi iwu Akum . 
iwanY mUlam awika pottiyil veVnYrYu irunwa ceVnYnYE cUppar kifcinY ( 79 veVrYrYi ) cAwanYEyE murYiyatiwwawu . 
veVrYrYikku pirYaku mumpE keptanY rokiw carmA alYiwwa pettiyil , ‘ iwu eVfkalYukku mikavum avaciyamAnYa veVrYrYi Akum . 
nAfkalY cila AttafkalYil cirYappAka ceVyalpattAlum , nilEyAnYa AttawwE veVlYippatuwwavillE . 
muwal panwil irunwe eVfkalYukku neVrukkati irunwawu . 
eVllA vIrarkalYum wafkalYawu poVrYuppE uNarnwu aNiyinY wevEkku wakunwapati cirYappAka pettif ceVywanYar . 
inwa Attawwil peVriya viwwiyAcawwil veVrYrYi peVrYa veNtum eVnYrYu virumpinYom . 
anYEwwum wittamittapati cariyAka amEnwawu . 
kuNAl pANtyA arYpuwamAkavum , accaminYrYiyum RAtkalYE AtinYAr ’ eVnYrYAr . 
wolvi kurYiwwu teVlli aNiyinY keptanY jAkIrkAnY karuwwu weVrivikkEyil , 
‘ 200 ranYkalYukku melAnYa ilakkE ‘ cecif ’ ceVyvawu eVnYpawu eVppoVlYYuwum katinYamAnYawu . 
inwa potti woVtaril eVfkalY aNiyinY panwu vIccu nanYrYAkave irunwu varukirYawu . 
inwa nAlY eVfkalYukku katinYamAnYa oVnYrYAka amEnwu vittawu . 
3-vawu vekappanwu vIccAlYar illAwawAl kuNAl pANtyAvinY awiratiyE kattuppatuwwa mutiyAmal poy vittawu . 
kuNAl pANtyA culYYarYpanwu vIccE cirYappAka eVwirkoVNtu vilYEyAtinYAr . 
eVFciya 3 AttafkalYil iraNtil veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl atuwwa curYrYukku wakuwi peVrYa mutiyum . 
eVfkalYukkuriya ulYlYUr AttafkalYukku wervu ceVyyappatta rAyppUril iru AttafkalY natakka iruppawu eVfkalYukku cAwakamAnYa amcam Akum ’ eVnYrYAr . curYrYulA payaNikalY cifkavAl kurafkukalYE woVnwaravu ceVyyakkUtAwu vanYawwurYEyinYar eVccarikkE 
vAlpArYEkku varum curYrYulA payaNikalY cifkavAl kurafkukalYE woVnwaravu ceVyyakkUtAwu eVnYrYu vanYawwurYEyinYar eVccarikkE vituwwulYlYanYar . 
cifkavAl kurafku 
vAlpArYEyil ulYlYa vanYappakuwiyil puli , cirYuwwEppuli , yAnYE , kAtteVrumE , karati , cifkavAlkurafku , pAmpukalY ulYlYitta vanYavilafkukalY vAlYYnwu varukinYrYanYa . 
inwa vanYavilafkukalYil pala ariyavakE vanYavilafkukalY alYYinwu varum vilafkukalY pattiyalil ulYlYanYa . 
kurYippAka merYku woVtarcci malEppakuwiyil mattume kANappatum ariyavakE cifkavAl kurafkukalY vAlpArYE pakuwiyil kANappatukirYawu . 
vAlpArYEyil irunwu poVlYlYAcci ceVllum malEppAwEyil puwuwwottam eVstet pakuwiyil awikalYavil ivE vAlYYnwu varukinYrYanYa . 
ivEkalYE pAwukAkka vanYawwurYEyinYar natavatikkE merYkoVNtu ulYlYanYar . 
pAwukAkka natavatikkE 
AnYEmalE pulikalY kAppaka kalYa iyakkunYar kanwacAmi uwwaravupati , mAvatta vanYa aluvalar cuppEyA arYivurEyinY peril vAlpArYE vanYaccarakar caravaNanY , mAnYAmpalYlYi vanYaccarakar cekar Akiyor walEmEyil puwuwwottam , ayyarpAti marYrYum kurafkumuti , varYattuppArYE , mAnYAmpalYlYi Akiya eVstet pakuwiyilum vettEwwatuppu kAvalarkalYE paNiyil amarwwi cifkavAl kurafkukalYE pAwukAkkum paNiyil vanYawwurYEyinYar Itupattu varukinYrYanYar . 
vAlpArYE - poVlYlYAcci meVyinY rottE oVttiya pakuwiyAnYa puwuwwottam , pAralYE eVstet pakuwiyil vanYawwurYEyinYarutanY cernwu iyarYkE vanYavalYa pAwukAppu mEya paNiyAlYarkalYum cifkavAl kurafkukalYE pAwukAkkum paNiyil Itupattu ulYlYanYar . 
avarkalY winYamum anwa pakuwikalYil ronwu ceVlkirYArkalY . 
palverYu itafkalYil cifkavAl kurafkukalYE pAwukAkka veNtum eVnYpawu kurYiwwa eVccarikkE palakEkalYum vEkkappattu ulYlYanYa . 
pukEppatam eVtukkum curYrYulA payaNikalY 
AnYAl vAlpArYEkku varum curYrYulA payaNikalY malEppAwEyil varumpowu cifkavAl kurafkukalYE pArwwAl vAkanYafkalYE nirYuwwi avarYrYE pukEppatam eVtukkirYArkalY . 
AtkalYE pArwwawum cifkavAl kurafkukalY vAkanYawwinY mIwu erYi amarnwu koVlYkirYawu . 
avarYrYukku curYrYulA payaNikalY uNavu koVtuppawutanY pukEppatam eVtukkirYArkalY . 
pinYnYar curYrYulA payaNikalY vAkanYawwE ottic ceVlkirYArkalY . 
appowu vAkanYawwil irunwu kIlYYe kuwikkum kurafkukalYukku atipattu kAyam erYpatukirYawu . 
melum , eVwire varum vAkanYafkalYil cikki irYakkavum neritukirYawu . 
eVccarikkE ariyavakE vilafkinYamAnYa cifkavAl kurafkE pAwukAkka palverYu pAwukAppu natavatikkEkalYE vanYawwurYEyinYarum iyarYkE ArvalarkalYum eVtuwwuvarum cUlYYnilEyil curYrYulA payaNikalY oVwwulYYEppu koVtuppawu illE . 
eVnYave vAlpArYEkku curYrYulA varum payaNikalY valYYiyil pArkkum vanYavilafkukalY , cifkavAl kurafku ponYrYa ariyavakE vilafkukalYukku uNavu koVtuppawutanY avarYrYE woVnwaravu ceVyyAmal irukka veNtum eVnYrYu vanYawwurYEyinYar kUrYi ulYlYanYar . 
melum , iwE mIrYupavarkalY mIwu katum natavatikkE eVtukkap patum eVnYrYu eVccarikkE vitukkappattu ulYlYanYar . cAmrAjnakar mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE manwirikalY pArvEyittanYar . 
manwirikalY kulYYu karnAtakawwil warYpowu katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE neril pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVyvawarYkAka muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA walEmEyil , manwirikalY atafkiya 4 kulYYukkalY amEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
anwak kulYYuvinYar mAnilam mulYYuvawum palverYu itafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE neril pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVywu varukirYArkalY . 
awanYpati nerYrYumunYwinYam manwirikalY makAweva piracAw , ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA , makAwevappA , winYeR kuNturAv Akiyor atafkiya kulYYuvinYar cAmrAjnakar mAvattawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE pArvEyita vanwanYar . 
mAwesvaranY malEkku ceVnYrYu cAmi waricanYam ceVywa avarkalY pinYnYar , aracu virunwinYar mAlYikEkku ceVnYrYu afku poVwumakkalYE canwiwwanYar . 
awikArikalYukku uwwaravu 
avarkalYitam kurYEkalYE kettarYinwa manwirikalY , avarkalY koVtuwwa manYuvEyum peVrYrYukkoVNtanYar . 
pinYnYar avarkalY mAwesvaranY malE marYrYum kopinawwam Akiya itafkalYil vanYappakuwiyE oVtti amEnwulYlYa pakuwikalYukku ceVnYrYanYar . 
afku nilavum kutinIr paFcam , atippatE vacawikalY kurYEpAtu AkiyavarYrYE avarkalY pArvEyittu Ayvu ceVywanYar . 
melum afkulYlYa makkalYinY piraccinYEkalYEyum kettarYinwanYar . 
pinYnYar kavutalYlYi kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYa avarkalY woVttakeVre eri cIramEppu paNikalYE pArvEyittanYar . 
melum appakuwiyil ulYlYa anYEwwu erikalYukkum waNNIr vita natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYu awikArikalYukku uwwaravittanYar . 
watEyillA minYcAram ... 
awEyatuwwu pIttars kAlanYikku ceVnYrYa avarkalY , afku natEpeVrYrYu varum kutinIr witta paNikalYE pArvEyittanYar . 
pinYnYar keVmpEyanYahatti , munYiyappanYawoVtti , poVnYnYanYawoVtti Akiya pakuwiyil ulYlYa kirAma makkalYE canwiwwu kurYEkalYE kettarYinwanYar . 
appowu afkulYlYa makkalY wafkalY pakuwikku watEyillA minYcAram valYYafka veNti korikkE manYu koVtuwwanYar . 
manYuvE peVrYrYukkoVNta manwirikalY virEvil appakuwikku watEyillA minYcAram valYYafka natavatikkE eVtuppawAka urYuwi alYiwwanYar . 
rU. 7.60 koti varYatci niwi 
pinYnYar afkirunwu mAvatta kaleVktar aluvalakawwirYku vanwa manwirikalY kulYYuvinYar afku anYEwwu wurYE awikArikalYutanY AlocanYEyil ItupattanYar . 
kUttawwil mAvatta kaleVktar ulYpata anYEwwu wurYE aracu awikArikalYum kalanwu koVNtanYar . 
kUttawwil manwirikalY kUrYukEyil , 
rU. 7.60 koti varYatci nivAraNa niwi ulYlYawu . 
awE vEwwu kutinIr piraccinYE ulYlYa pakuwikalYil AlYYkulYYAy kiNarYukalY amEkkavum , kirAmap pakuwikalYil atippatE vacawikalYE merYkoVlYlYavum awikArikalY natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum . 
kamaravAti eri ulYpata palverYu erikalYil waNNIr nirappa veNti ulYlYawu . 
kapinYi aNEyilirunwu cAmrAjnakar mAvattawwil ulYlYa erikalYil waNNIr nirappa natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum . 
oVnYrYucernwu ceVyalpata veNtum 
kirAma kaNakkAlYar , varYatci nivAraNa woVkEyE cariyAka vivacAyikalYukku koVtuppawillE eVnYrYu pukArkalY varukinYrYanYa . 
melum melnilE nIrwwekkaw woVttiyum nirYEya itafkalYil parAmarippinYrYi kitakkinYrYanYa . 
ivarYrYE eVllAm cariceVyya veNtum . 
awarYku aracu awikArikalY anYEvarum oVwwulYYEkka veNtum . 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE ceVyvawil araciyal ceVyyAmal anYEvarum oVnYrYucernwu ceVyalpata veNtum . 
appowuwAnY varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE nAm wirYamEyAka kEyAlYa mutiyum eVnYrYu kUrYinYar . 
mEcUrukku ceVnYrYanYar 
iwEyatuwwu manwirikalY 4 perum mEcUru mAvattawwirYku ceVnYrYanYar . 
afku varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta unYcUr , eVc.ti.kottE wAlukAvirYku utpatta pakuwikalYE pArvEyittanYar . 
melum afkulYlYa nIr AwArafkalYE Ayvu ceVywu kutinIr piraccinYEyE pokka awikArikalYutanY AlocanYE natawwinYar . 
pinYnYar naFcanYkUtu , ti.naracippurA , piriyappattaNA Akiya pakuwikalYukku ceVnYrYu pArvEyittanYar . 
appowu mAvatta kaleVktar RikA appakuwiyil varYatciyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa makkalYinY nilE kurYiwwu manwirikalYukku vilYakkinYAr . 
waNNIr nirappa veNtum 
iwEyatuwwu mEcUruvil ulYlYa kavarnYar mAlYikEyil anYEwwu wurYE aracu awikArikalYutanY manwirikalY AlocanYE natawwinYar . 
appowu , mAnilawwil 200-kkum merYpatta kirAmafkalYil kutinIr paFcam erYpattulYlYawu . 
muwalkattamAka kutinIr piraccinYEyE pokka natavatikkE eVtukkappattu varukirYawu . 
awanYpati mAvattawwil kutinIr paFcam ulYlYa itafkalYil AlYYkulYYAy kiNarYukalY amEkka awikArikalYukku uwwaravitappattulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAka rU. 17 koti niwi oVwukkappattulYlYawu . 
aNEkalYilirunwu mAvattawwil ulYlYa erikalY , kulYafkalY AkiyavarYrYil waNNIr nirappa veNtum . 
appowuwAnY malYYE vanwAlum , varAvittAlum inYnYum 2 mAwafkalYukku kutinIr piraccinYE erYpatAmal irukkum . 
iwarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalYE awikArikalY utanYatiyAka merYkoVlYlYa veNtum eVnYrYu manwirikalY kUrYinYar .

amiw RA wAkku - 
mawwiyil Atciyil irunwa kAfkiras walEmEyilAnYa munwEya Ekkiya murYpokkuk kUttaNi AtciyAlYarkalY , aracuk karuvUlawwE kAliyAka vittuc ceVnYrYanYar eVnYrYu pAjaka walEvar amiw RA kurYrYam cAttinYAr . 
varYumEk kottukkuk kIlYY vacikkum peVNkalYukku ilavaca camEyal eVrivAyu iNEppukalYE iraNtAm kattamAka valYYafkum vilYYA kujarAwwil FAyirYrYukkilYYamE natEpeVrYrYawu . 
iwil , mawwiya peVtroliyaw wurYE amEccar warmenwira pirawAnY , mAnila muwalvar AnYanwipeVnY patel , rAjaswAnY muwalvar vacunwarA rAje ulYlYittor pafkerYrYanYar . 
nikalYYcciyil amiw RA peciyawAvawu : mawwiyil pirawamar narenwira moti walEmEyilAnYa pAjaka aracu Atci amEwwa pirYaku , elYYEkalY marYrYum peVNkalY nalanYE mempatuwwa palverYu natavatikkEkalY eVtukkappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
elYYEp peVNkalYukku awikAramalYikkum vakEyil , avarkalYukku ilavaca camEyal eVrivAyu iNEppu valYYafkum wittawwE moti arYimukappatuwwiyulYlYAr . 
iwanY mUlam 6 koti peVNkalY payanYatEvar . 
camEyal eVrivAyu mAnYiyawwE vacawi patEwwavarkalY kEvita veNtum eVnYrYu pirawamar korikkE vituwwAr . 
iwarYku munYpu eVnwap pirawamarum iwwakEya veNtukolYE makkalYitam munYvEwwawillE . 
lAl pakawUr cAswiri pirawamarAka irunwapowu , uNavu wAnYiyafkalYukkuw wattuppAtu erYpattawu . 
arici , paruppu cArnwa uNavukalYE oVruvelYEkkAvawu makkalY wavirkka veNtum eVnYrYu appowu avar korikkE vEwwAr . 
awu makkalYAl erYrYukkoVlYlYappattawu . 
awepol , moti vituwwa korikkEyE erYrYu cumAr 1 koti per camEyal eVrivAyu mAnYiyawwEk kEvittulYlYanYar . 
kAfkiras walEmEyilAnYa Ekkiya murYpokkuk kUttaNi aracu mawwiyil 10 ANtu kAlam woVtarnwu Atciyil irunwawu . 
AnYAl , avarkalYawu Atcik kAlam nirYEvatEnwapowu aracuk karuvUlam kAliyAka irunwawu . 
awanY pirYaku Atcip poVrYuppukku vanwa pAjaka walEmEyilAnYa mawwiya aracAl elYYEkalY nalanYukkAnYa nalaw wittafkalYE merYkoVlYlYa powiya niwi illE . 
motiyinY Atci nirvAkawwAl UlYYal oVlYYikkappattawu . 
muwalIttu niwikalY wirattappattanYa . 
kalYlYaccanwEyil camEyal eVrivAyu urulYEkalY virYkappatuvawEw watuwwawutanY , payanYAlYikalYinY vafkik kaNakkukalYil neratiyAka mAnYiyam ceVluwwappattu varukirYawu eVnYrYAr amiw RA . 
kAnwi - moti oVppItu : 
inwa nikalYYcciyil pafkerYrYa mawwiyappiraweca muwalvar civarAj cif cOhAnY , makAwmA kAnwiyutanY pirawamar narenwira motiyE oVppittup pecinYAr .

awepol , warYpowu motiyE ulakam kavanYiwwu varukirYawu ' ' eVnYrYu avar kurYippittAr . rottari aNiyE vIlYYwwiyawu mArYrYuwwirYanYAlYikalY aNi - 
wi inwu inwiya

inwa woVtarEyoVtti inwiya mArYrYuwwirYanYAlYikalY kirikkeVt aNiyE pirapalappatuwwum viwamAka ceVnYnYE nufkampAkkawwil ulYlYa layolA kallUri mEwAnYawwil nerYrYu kirikkeVt potti natawwappattawu .

cukunYeR 91 ranY eVtuwwAr .

inwiya aNiyinY melAlYAr cumanw reVtti , oVrufkiNEppAlYar asvarwanY reVtti kalanwu koVNtanYar . varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa 4 kulYYukkalY amEppu 
ciwwarAmEyA petti peVfkalYUru ,

UlYYal watuppu patE 
muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA nerYrYu peVlakAvi mAvattawwil curYrYuppayaNam ceVywAr . 
iwarYkAka vimAnYam mUlam peVlakAvikku ceVnYrYAr . 
afku ciwwarAmEyA niruparkalYukku alYiwwa pettiyil kUrYiyawAvawu : 
nAnY makkalYAl muwal-manwiriyAka wernwu eVtukkappattulYlYenY . 
lok ayukwA amEppAl nAnY inwa pawavikku varavillE . 
nAnY muwal-manwiri AvawarYku makkalY wAnY kAraNam . 
lok ayukwA amEppE mUtuvawarYkAka UlYYal watuppu patE uruvAkkappattu iruppawAka kAfkiras mUwwa walEvar janYArwwanYa pUjAri kUrYi iruppawu parYrYi nIfkalY ketkirYIrkalY . 
makkalYukku nallawu ceVyvawu wAnY eVnYawu velE . 
nallawE ceVywe wIruvenY . 
varYatci pakuwikalY Ayvu karnAtakawwil nilavum varYatciyE Ayvu ceVyyavum , nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYavum manwirikalY atafkiya 4 kulYYukkalYE amEwwulYlYenY . 
inwa kulYYuvinYar mAnilam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu varYatciyE Ayvu ceVywu varukirYArkalY . 
inwa kulYYukkalY arYikkE valYYafkiya pirYaku varYatci nivAraNa paNikalY inYnYum vekamAka merYkoVlYlYappatum . 
nAnY erYkanYave pala mAvattafkalYil varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYEyum , afku merYkoVlYlYappattu varum nivAraNa paNikalYEyum neril Ayvu ceVywenY . 
ippowu 2-vawu kattamAka varYatci pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyyum paNiyE woVtafkiyulYlYenY . 
ivvArYu ciwwarAmEyA kUrYinYAr . 
AyvukkUttam peVlakAvi vimAnYa nilEyawwilirunwu ciwwarAmEyA nerAka varYatci pakuwikalYE pArvEyituvawarYkAka ampevAti kirAmawwirYku ceVnYrYAr . 
afku varYatci pakuwiyE Ayvu ceVywa pinY afkirunwu hukkeri wAlukAvil ulYlYa naracifkapurA , kArimatam marYrYum cikkoti wAlukAvukku ceVnYrYAr .

walEvarkalY karuwwu - wi inwu

muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA petti 
mEcUru , 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalY mutiyum varE manwiri capEyil mArYrYam irukkAwu eVnYrYu muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kUrYinYAr . 
ciwwarAmEyA mEcUru varukE 
mEcUruvil natanwa palverYu nikalYYccikalYil kalanwu koVlYvawarYkAka muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA nerYrYu wanYi vimAnYam mUlam peVfkalYUruvilirunwu mEcUruvukku vanwAr . 
mEcUru maNtakalYlYi vimAnYa nilEyawwirYku vanwa avar afku niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
katumEyAnYa varYatci 
karnAtakawwil warYpowu katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
kurYippAka rAyccUr , peVfkalYUru , mEcUru , peVlakAvi , kalapuraki Akiya mAvattafkalYil awEc curYrYiyulYlYa pakuwikalYilum varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
varYatcip pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya 4 kulYYukkalY amEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
iwil rAyccUr pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya manwiri eVc.ke.pattIl walEmEyilum , peVfkalYUru marYrYum awanY curYrYuvattArap pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya manwiri cInYivAca piracAw walEmEyilum , mEcUru pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya manwiri ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA walEmEyilum , peVlakAvi marYrYum kalapuraki pakuwikalYil Ayvu merYkoVlYlYa manwiri Ar.vi.weRpANte walEmEyilum kulYYukkalY amEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
2–m katta Ayvu atuwwa mAwam ( me ) 2–n wewikku pirYaku inwa kulYYukkalY varYatcip pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVywu arYikkE camarppippArkalY . 
awanY pirYaku varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYukku nivAraNa niwikalY valYYafkappatum . 
erYkanYave mAnilawwil 7 mAvattafkalYil varYatci kurYiwwu Ayvu natawwi ulYlYenY . 
mINtum varukirYa 25–nwewi muwal 27–nwewi varE 2–m kattamAka varYatci pAwiwwulYlYa pakuwikalYukku ceVnYrYu Ayvu ceVyya irukkirYenY . 
mawwiya aracitam niwi varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYukku rU. 1,416 koti valYYafkumArYu mawwiya aracitam korikkE vituwwulYlYenY . 
mawwiya aracum iwukurYiwwu Alociwwu varukirYawu . 
katanwa cila mAwafkalYukku munYpu palawwa malYYE peVywawu . 
appowu nirYEya vivacAyikalY veVlYlYawwAl naRtam atEnwanYar . 
avarkalYukku nivAraNa niwi valYYafkuvawarYkAka mawwiya aracu rU. 1,500 koti niwi koVtuwwawu . 
anwa niwi , veVlYlYawwAl pAwikkappatta anYEwwu vivacAyikalYukkum valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
kutinIr valYYafka erYpAtu varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil mAnila aracu cArpil warYpowu rU. 350 koti ceVlavil kutinIr valYYafka erYpAtu ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
inwa ANtu kotE kAlawwil kutinIr paFcam erYpatAwapati pArwwuk koVlYlYa natavatikkE eVtukkappattu varukirYawu . 
karnAtaka kAfkiracAr itEye cila karuwwu verYupAtukalY irunwu varukirYawu . 
iwukurYiwwu ifkeye peci mutikkappatum . 
ulYkatci piraccinYE kurYiwwu peca teVlli ceVllap povawillE . 
manwiri capEyil mArYrYam irukkAwu 
inwa mAwa mutivil manwiricapEyil mArYrYam merYkoVlYlYappata irunwawu . 
AnYAl mAnilawwil warYpowu varYatci nivAraNap paNikalYE kEyAlYa veNti iruppawAl ippowEkku manwiri capEyil mArYrYam irukkAwu . 
varYatci nivAraNap paNikalY mutiyum varEyil manwiri capE mArYrYam walYlYi vEkkappatum . 
melum muwal–manwiri pawaviyilirunwu eVnYnYE mArYrYuvawAka parappappattu varum wakaval oVru poVyyAnYa wakavalAkum . 
awE yArum nampa veNtAm . 
cattawwinY munY anYEvarum camam eVtiyUrappA mIwu ulYlYa UlYYal valYYakkukalY kurYiwwu cuprIm korttil melmurYEyItu ceVyyappatum . 
nAfkalY palYYivAfkum araciyal ceVyyavillE . 
cattawwinY munYpu anYEvarum camam . 
eVnYave , wavarYu ceVywavarkalY yArAka irunwAlum waNtikkappata veNtum . 
UlYYal watuppu patEkku patippatiyAka awikAram valYYafkappattu varukirYawu . 
warYpowu avarkalY uRArAka paNiyArYrYi varukirYArkalY . 
virEvil lok ayukwA ponYrYu UlYYal watuppu patEyum wirYamEyAka ceVyalpatum . 
ivvArYu muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kUrYinYAr . 
pArvEyittAr 
iwEyatuwwu mEcUru mAnYacakafkowwirikku ceVnYrYa avar afku natanwa makalYirukkAnYa cattafkalY parYrYiya karuwwarafkE woVtafki vEwwAr . 
melum makalYir cattafkalY woVtarpAnYa puwwakawwEyum veVlYiyittAr . 
pinYnYar mEcUru makArAjA kallUri mEwAnYawwil natanwa vivacAya marYrYum vivacAya poVrutkalY virYpanYE kaNkAtciyEyum woVtafki vEwwu pArvEyittAr .

arakkoNam , me 10– 
muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA inYrYu pirYpakalil arakkoNawwil werwal piraccAram ceVykirYAr . 
muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY peccE ketkavum avarE kANavum latcApa latcam makkalY AvalutanY kAwwirukkirYArkalY . 
ceVnYnYEyil katanwa 9–nwewi anYrYu jeVyalaliwA werwal piraccArawwE wuvakkinYAr . 
woVtarnwu avar cUrYAvalYi curYrYuppayaNam merYkoVNtu varukirYAr . 
katanwa 8–nwewi anYrYu waFcAvUril 13–vawu nAlYAka piraccAram ceVywAr . 
inYrYu 14–vawu nAlYAka arakkoNawwil piramANta poVwukkUttawwil pecukirYAr . 
velUr , aNEkkattu , kutiyAwwam ( wanYi ) , vANiyampAti , AmpUr , jolArpettE , wiruppawwUr , arakkoNam ( wanYi ) , colYifkar , kAtpAti , rANippettE , ArYkAtu , kIlYYvEwwiyaNAnYkuppam ( wanYi ) , pAlYUr , AraNi , ceVfkam ( wanYi ) , kalacapAkkam Akiya 17 woVkuwi vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu jeVyalaliwA pecukirYAr .

me 22-l piciciE walEvar wervu - 
wi inwu 
piciciE walEvar poVrYuppilirunwu RacAfk manYokar vilakiyawE atuwwu puwiya walEvarE wervu ceVyvawarYkAka varum 22-m wewi piciciEyinY cirYappu poVwukkulYYu mumpEyil kUtukirYawu . 
piciciE walEvarAka irunwa RacAfk manYokar katanwa 10-m wewi pawavi vilakinYAr . 
iwEw woVtarnwu Ecici-yinY muwal wanYnYiccEyAnYa walEvarAka RacAfk manYokar me 12-m wewi poVrYupperYrYukkoVNtAr . 
iwanYAl puwiya piciciE walEvarE wernweVtukka varum 22-m wewi piciciEyinY cirYappu poVwukkulYYu mumpEyil kUtum eVnYa kovA kirikkeVt cafka poVwucceVyalAlYar vinYow pAwke weVriviwwAr . 
inwa poVwukkulYYuvil puwiya walEvarE wervu ceVyyum paNi mattume natEpeVrYum eVnYrYum avar kUrYinYAr . 
anekamAka anYurAk wAkUr puwiya walEvarAka wervu ceVyyappatalAm eVnYaw weVrikirYawu .

puwuteVlli , 
varYatciyAl pAwiwwa marAttiya mAnilawwilirunwu E.pi.eVl. pottiyE mArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYa mumpE EkorttinY uwwaravE eVwirwwu appIl ceVywa manYuvE cuprIm korttu walYlYupati ceVywawu . 
E.pi.eVl. mArYrYawwE eVwirwwu appIl 
katum varYatciyum , 
waNNIr wattuppAtum nilavi varum marAttiya mAnilawwil E.pi.eVl. 20 ovar kirikkeVt pottiyE natawwuvawAl awika alYavil waNNIr vINAvawAkavum , inwa pottiyE marAttiya mAnilawwilirunwu verYu mAnilawwukku mArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu woVtarappatta poVwunala manYuvE erYrYu , epral 30–n wewikku pirYaku marAttiya mAnilawwil natakka irunwa E.pi.eVl. kirikkeVt pottikalYE verYu mAnilawwukku mArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu mumpE Ekorttu camIpawwil uwwaravittawu . 
inwa uwwaravE eVwirwwu mumpE marYrYum marAttiya kirikkeVt cafkafkalY cArpil cuprIm korttil appIl manYu wAkkal ceVyyappattawu . 
awil E.pi.eVl. pottikalYukku cuwwikarikkappatta kalYYivunIr wAnY payanYpatuwwappatukirYawu . 
eVnYave marAttiyawwil E.pi.eVl. pottiyE natawwa anYumawikka veNtum eVnYrYu anwa manYuvil korappattu irunwawu . 
cuprIm korttil walYlYupati 
inwa manYu cuprIm korttu walEmE nIwipawi ti.eVs.wAkkur , nIwipawikalY Ar.pAnYumawi , laliw Akiyor atafkiya peVFc munYpu nerYrYu vicAraNEkku vanwawu . 
manYu wArarkalY cArpil vakkIlkalY pa.ciwamparam , e.eVm.cifvi Akiyor AjarAnYArkalY . 
marAttiya mAnilawwil E.pi.eVl. pottiyE natawwa anYumawikka veNtum eVnYrYu iruvarum vAwittanYar . 
katum nipanwanYEkalYutanY E.pi.eVl. pottiyE marAttiya mAnilawwil anYumawippawu woVtarpAka woVtakkawwil walEmE nIwipawi ti.eVs.wAkkur pitc parAmarippukku payanYpatuwwappatum waNNIrinY alYavu vikiwam ulYpata cila kelYvikalYE eVlYYuppinYAr . 
iruppinYum waNNIr parYrYAkkurYEyAl waviwwu varum marAttiya mAnilawwil E.pi.eVl. pottiyE natawwakkUtAwu . 
awE verYu mAnilawwukku niccayam mArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu weVriviwwa nIwipawikalY appIl manYuvE walYlYupati ceVywu uwwaravittanYar . 
jeVyppUr piraccinYE 
iwarYkitEyil rAjaswAnY mAnilawwil waNNIr parYrYAkkurYE nilavuvawAl jeVyppUril E.pi.eVl. pottiyE natawwa watE viwikka veNtum eVnYrYu rAjaswAnY Ekorttil manYu wAkkal ceVyyappattawu . 
inwa manYu nerYrYu vicAraNEkku vanwa powu nIwipawikalY ajay raswoki , comAnYi Akiyor atafkiya peVFc , varukirYa 30–n wewi mAnila aracu pawil manYu wAkkal ceVyya veNtum eVnYrYu uwwaravittanYar . 
inwa valYYakku vicAraNE varukirYa 3–n wewikku walYlYi vEkkappattawu . wamilYYakawwil AtciyEp pitikkap povawu yAr ?

ceVnYnYE : 
wamilYYakawwil 232 cattamanYrYaw woVkuwikalYukkAnYa vAkkuppawivu mutinwulYlYa nilEyil , vAkkuppawivukku pinwEya karuwwukkaNippu mutivukalY veVlYiyAki araciyal kalYawwil paraparappE awikariwwulYlYanYa . 
anwa vakEyil tEms nav - cI ottar natawwiya karuwwukkaNippu mutivukalY a.wi.mu.ka.vE urYcAkam atEyac ceVywulYlYawu . 
AlYufkatciyAnYa a.wi.mu.ka. 139 itafkalYEp pitiwwu AtciyEw wakka vEkka vAyppu ulYlYawAka anwa karuwwuk kaNippil weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
wi.mu.ka. 78 woVkuwikalYilum , pirYa katcikalY 17 woVkuwikalYilum veVrYrYi peVrYalAm eVnYa anwa karuwwuk kaNippu kUrYukirYawu . 
pA.ja.ka.vukku oVru itamkUta kitEkkAwu eVnYrYum inwa karuwwuk kaNippil weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
e.pi.pi. niyUs veVlYiyittulYlYa karuwwukkaNippil wi.mu.ka.vukku awika woVkuwikalY kitEkkum eVnYa weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi 132 woVkuwikalYEyum , a.wi.mu.ka. 95 woVkuwikalYEyum , pA.ja.ka. oVru woVkuwiyEyum , pirYa katcikalY 6 woVkuwikalYEyum kEpparYrYa vAyppu ulYlYawAka anwak karuwwuk kaNippu kUrYukirYawu . 
AnYAl , inwa iraNtu karuwwukkaNippukalYEyum purYanwalYlYum vakEyil eVnY.ti.ti.vi. karuwwuk kaNippil mArYupatta mutivu veVlYiyAki ulYlYawu . 
a.wi.mu.ka. 110 woVkuwikalYilum , wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi 109 woVkuwikalYEyum kEpparYrYi ilYYuparYi erYpatalAm eVnYa weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
wamilYYakawwil pA.ja.ka. oVru woVkuwiyil kUta veVrYrYi peVrYa vAyppillE eVnYrYum , pirYa katcikalY 15 woVkuwikalYE kEpparYrYum eVnYrYum anwa karuwwuk kaNippu kUrYukirYawu . 
inwiyA tute -

wi inwu . 
riyo oVlimpik pottikku cAnYiyA neVvAl , juvAlA kattA utpata 7 inwiyarkalY wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYanYar . 
ulaka petmiNtanY peVtareRanY , nerYrYu petmiNtanY waravaricEp pattiyalE veVlYiyittawu . 
inwa pattiyalinYpati inwiyAvinY cAynYA neVvAl , pi.vi.cinwu , juvAlA kattA , ke.kAnw , asvinYi poVnYnYappA , manYu atri , cumiw reVtti Akiyor oVlimpik pottiyil palverYu pirivukalYil kalanwukoVlYlYa wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYanYar . 
katanwa oVlimpik pottiyil petmiNtanYil inwiyAvinY cArpil 5 per kalanwu koVNtanYar eVnYpawu kurYippitawwakawu . makArARtirAvil varYatci nivAraNawwirYku caccinY marYrYum peVpci nirYuvanYam uwava munYvanwulYlYanYar mumpE , makArARtirAvinY marawvAtA pakuwiyil varYatci nilEyinYAl makkalY pAwippatEnwulYlYanYar . 
kutinIr parYrYAkkurYEyE pokkuvawarYkAka cirYappu reVyil oVnYrYinY uwaviyutanY latcakkaNakkAnYa littar nIr afku koVNtu ceVllappatukirYawu . 
innilEyil munYnYAlY kirikkeVt vIrar caccinY weVNtulkar marYrYum peVpci nirYuvanYam iNEnwu mAnila aracinY nivAraNa paNikku uwavita munYvanwulYlYanYar . 
ivvivakAram kurYiwwu makArARtirA muwalmanwiri wevenwira patnYAvis inYrYu caccinYutanY canwippu natawwinYAr . 
iwu parYrYi avar veVlYiyittulYlYa tuvittar ceVywiyil , pAraw rawnYA viruwu peVrYrYa caccinY weVNtulkarE canwiwwawil makilYYcci . 
marawvAtA pakuwiyil varYatci nivAraNawwirYku wittam oVnYrYE ceVyalpatuwwita caccinY weVNtulkar marYrYum peVpci nirYuvanYam iNEnwu munYvanwulYlYanYar eVnYa weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
varYatciyinYAl makArARtirAvil mocamAnYa nilEyil pAwikkappattulYlYa pakuwikalYil marawvAtAvum oVnYrYu .

ceVnYnYEyil mu.ka.stAlinY wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar 
mu.ka.stAlinY ceVnYnYEyil 2 nAtkalY wIvira piracAram ceVyya erYkanYave mutivu ceVywirunwAr . 
awanYpati muwal nAlYAnYa nerYrYu kAlEyil ceVnYnYE eVlYYumpUr , wiyAkarAyanakar , wurYEmukam woVkuwikalYil wIvira vAkku cekarippil ItupattAr . 
eVlYYumpUr woVkuwiyil pottiyitum wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar raviccanwiranYukku AwaravAka cUlYE natarAj wiyettar arukil woVtafki mowilAl neru weVruvalYYiyAka pulYiyanwoppu neVtuFcAlE varE vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu mu.ka.stAlinY vAkku cekariwwAr . 
mAti vItukalYil irunwavarkalYitam anwa vIttukku patikalYil erYic ceVnYrYu uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwukku ottu kettAr . 
pinYnYar , anwa cAlE valYYiyAka natanwu ceVnYrYa avar , afku kUti irunwa poVwumakkalYitam kEkalYE acEwwavArYu vAkku kettAr . 
kEkkulYYanwEyE kEyil vEwwirunwa oVruvaritam kulYYanwEyE vAfki koVFcinYAr . 
wiyAkarAyanakar woVkuwi 
awEyatuwwu , wiyAkarAyanakar woVkuwi wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar tAktar kanYimoVlYYikku AwaravAka vatapalYYanYi ArYkAtu cAlEyil wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY vAkku cekarikka woVtafkinYAr . 
appowu afku valYYi neVtuka makkalY kUttam alEmowiyawu . 
mu.ka.stAlinY afku irunwavarkalYitam kE kulukki uwayacUriyanY cinYnYawwukku vAkku kettAr . 
vatapalYYanYi ArYkAtu cAlEyil natanwu ceVnYrYu vAkku cekariwwuk koVNtu irunwa powu , anwa valYYiyAka vanwa ilYampeVNkalY 2 per ‘ ceVlpi ’ patam eVtuwwukkoVlYlYa avaritam anYumawi kettanYar . 
utanYe avarum wArAlYamAka eVtuwwukkoVlYlYufkalY eVnYrYu kUrYinYAr . 
awEw woVtarnwu anwa ilYampeVNkalY iruvarum mu.ka.stAlinYutanY ‘ ceVlpi ’ eVtuwwukkoVNtanYar . 
oVru kutumpawwinYar mu.ka.stAlinYukku Arawwi eVtuwwu varaverYrYanYar . 
vIwi , vIwiyAka natanwu ceVnYrYa mu.ka.stAlinY wAymArkalYEyum , peVriyavarkalYEyum wetic ceVnYrYu ottu vettEyAtinYAr . 
wurYEmukam woVkuwi wiyAkarAyanakaril ottu cekariwwa mu.ka.stAlinY afkirunwu purYappattu , wurYEmukam woVkuwikku ceVnYrYAr . 
wurYEmukam woVkuwi wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar pi.ke.cekar pApuvukku AwaravAka ottu kettAr . 
wurYEmukam woVkuwi maNNati , eVnY.eVs.ci.pos cAlE , pArimunYE Akiya pakuwikalYil wIvira vAkku cekarippil mu.ka.stAlinY ItupattAr . 
anwa pakuwikalYil irunwa katE urimEyAlYarkalY , katEkalYil paNipuriyum UlYYiyarkalYitam vAkku cekariwwAr . 
pinYnYar , cAlE orawwil ninYrYu koVNtirunwavarkalYitam , anwa pakuwi vAlYY makkalYitam ottu kettAr . 
appowu avarukku anwa pakuwi makkalY malar wUviyum , poVnYnYAtE porwwiyum varaverYrYArkalY . 
maNNati pakuwiyil natanwu vAkku cekariwwu koVNtu irunwa powu , anwa valYYiyAka vanwa AttokkalY , mAnakara aracu paskalYil irunwa payaNikalYitamum mu.ka.stAlinY kE kulukki vAkku cekariwwAr . 
uriya natavatikkE 
iwarYkitEyil , wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr .

avarawu walEmEyil ifkilAnwu aNi 2009–m ANtil oVrunAlY marYrYum 20 ovar ulaka koppEyE kEpparYrYiyawu .

pAlawwirYku mel waNNIr ceVlvawAl pokkuvarawwu nirYuwwam

ampawwUr ,

karuNAniwi muwalamEccar AvAr 
ceVnYnYEyil peVywa malYYEyAl pAwikkappattu wafkalY utamEkalYE ilYYanwu weVruvil ninYrYa makkalYE jeVyalaliwA canwiwwu ArYuwal kUrYinYArA ? .

velE koVtuppom 
ampawwUr woVkuwi woVlYYirYcAlEkalY mikunwa pakuwi . 
inYrYEkku woVlYYil nalivatEnwu cirYu , kurYu woVlYYirYcAlEkalY mUtappatukirYawu .

ivvArYu I.vi.ke.eVs. ilYafkovanY pecinYAr . oVlimpikkil pawakkam : pi.vi.cinwu viruppam - 
wi inwu . 
oVlimpik pottiyil pawakkam veVlla virumpuvawAka pi.vi.cinwu kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
inwiyAvinY munYnYaNi pAtmiNtanY vIrAfkanYEkalYil oVruvar pi.vi.cinwu . 
ulaka pAtmiNtanY cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil 2 murYE veVNkalap pawakkam veVnYrYa ivar , muwal murYEyAka oVlimpik pottikku wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYAr . 
iwuparYrYi mumpEyil nerYrYu niruparkalYitam cinwu kUrYiyawAvawu : 
oVlimpik pottiyil vilYEyAta nAnY wernweVtukkappattiruppawu makilYYcci alYikkirYawu . 
ulaka cAmpiyanYRip pottikalYil 2 murYE veVNkalap pawakkam veVnYrYirunwAlum oVlimpikkil pawakkam veVlla virumpukirYenY . 
oVlimpikkil pawakkam veVlvawu wAnY oVvvoVru vIrarukkum kanYavAka irukkum . 
eVnYakkum appatiwwAnY . 
riyo oVlimpikkil petmiNtanY pirivil vilYEyAta inwiyAvilirunwu 7 per wernweVtukkappattiruppawu makilYYcci alYikkirYawu . 
nAfkalY anYEvarum oVlimpik pottikkAka wIvira payirYciyil ItupattulYlYom . 
oVlimpikkil pawakkam veVlla utalalYavilum manYawalYavilum nAfkalY wayArAka irukka veNtum . 
iwil kalanwu koVlYlYum oVvvoVru vIrarkalYum mikac cirYanwavarkalYAka iruppArkalY eVnYpawil canwekamillE . 
avarkalYE eVwirkoVlYlYa nAfkalY wayArAka irukkaveNtum . 
oVlimpikkil kalanwukoVlYlYum nam vIrarkalY anYEvarukkum eVnYawu vAlYYwwukalY . 
ivvArYu pi.vi.cinwu kUrYinYAr . inwukuR pakuwiyil cakwi vAynwa nilanatukkam : pAkiswAnY , teVlli , vatamAnilafkalYilum awirvu -

inwukuR malEppakuwiyil , vatamerYku pAkiswAnY , ApkAnY - wajikiswAnY eVllEppakuwiyil cakwi vAynwa nilanatukkam erYpattawu . 
iwanYEyatuwwu pAkiswAnY , ApkAnY walEnakarafkalYil kattitafkalY kulufkinYa eVnYrYu muwarYkatta wakavalkalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . 
teVlliyilum inwa nilanatukka alEkalYAl awirvu erYpattawil meVtro rayil cevE warYkAlikamAka nirYuwwappattulYlYawu . 
inwa nilanatukkam riktar alYavukolil 6.6 eVnYrYu pawivAkiyulYlYawAka ameVrikka puviyiyal Ayvu mEyam ( yu.eVs.ji.eVs ) weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
inYrYu mawiyam 3.58 maNiyalYavil ApkAnY walEnakar kApUlukku vatakilYYakke 282 kimI woVlEvil inwa nilanatukkam erYpattawu . 
pUmikku atiyil 210 kimi woVlEvil iwanY mEyam irunwawAka yu.eVs.ji.eVs. weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
inwa nilanatukka alEkalYinY wAkkam 200 kimi parappukku irunwawu . 
teVlli , kARmIr , uwwarAkaNt Akiya pakuwikalYilum nilanatukka alEkalYinY wAkkam irunwawu . 
pAkiswAnY vAnYoVli nilEyac ceVywiyinY pati peVRAvar , ciwral , svAt , kiljiw , pEcalApAw , lAkUr Akiya pakuwikalYilum nilanatukka awirvu erYpattulYlYawu . 
islAmApAwwil vItukalY , aluvalakafkalYE vittu pIwiyil veVlYiyerYiya makkalY cAlEkalYileye valYYipAtu ceVywawEyum pArkka mutinwawAka ejeVnYci ceVywikalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . 
iwuvarE uyirccewa , poVrutcewa vivarafkalY eVwuvumillE . 
imAlayappakuwikalYil atikkati nilanatukkam erYpatak kAraNam , inwiya , yureciya kaNtawwattukalY mowikkoVlYlYum itamAkum iwu . 
yureciya kaNtawwattukku atiyil inwiya kaNtawwattu ceVluwwappatum oVru cakwi vAynwa natavatikkEye payafkara nilanatukkap pakuwiyAka imAlayam wikalYYvawarYkuk kAraNamAka ulYlYawu . wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarinY uruvam poVrYiwwa 5 Ayiram ‘ tI kappukalY ’ ; polIcAr parYimuwal ceVywanYar 
ceVnYnYE , 
ceVnYnYE aNNAnakar woVkuwi wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar eVm.ke.mokanY AwaravAlYarkalY nerYrYu kAlE eVm.ji.Ar.kAlanYi 10-vawu meVyinY rottil minYi venY oVnYrYil paNappattuvAtA ceVyvawAka a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar pukAr weVriviwwanYar . 
pukArE woVtarnwu , campava itawwukku virEnwu ceVnYrYa polIcAr anwa pakuwiyil nirYuwwi vEkkappattu irunwa minYi venYE cowanYE ceVywanYar . 
cowanYEyil , anwa vaNtiyil aNNAnakar wi.muka. vetpAlYar eVm.ke.mokanYinY uruvam marYrYum uwayacUriyanY cinYnYam poVrYiwwa 5 Ayiram ‘ tI kappukalY ’ irunwanYa . 
avarYrYE polIcAr parYimuwal ceVywanYar . 
minYivenYil pitipatta anwa tI kappukalYil paNam vEwwu vAkkAlYarkalYukku vinYiyokam ceVyya irunwawAka a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar polIcAritam pukAr kUrYinYArkalY . 
iwEyatuwwu , anwa minYi venY marYrYum 5 Ayiram tI kappukalY aNNAnakar polIs nilEyawwil vEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
pukArkalY uNmEyAnYawA ?
