payirYciyAlYar awirupwi - 
wi inwu 
katanwa EeVseVl kAlpanwu pottiyinY irYuwi AttawwinYpowu ceVnYnYE aNiyinY natcawwira vIrar ilonYA , wanYnYEw wAkkiyawAka kUrYi kovA aNiyinY urimEyAlYarkalYil oVruvar polIsil pukAr alYiwwAr . 
iwEyatuwwu ilAnYovE polIsAr kEwu ceVywanYar . 
awanY eVwiroVliyAka inwiyanY cUppar lIk kAlpanwu pottikku avappeVyarE erYpatuwwiyawAka kUrYi kovA aNikku rU. 11 koti aparAwam viwikkappattulYlYawu . 
awanY 2 urimEyAlYarkalYukkum watE viwikkappattulYlYawu . 
iwarYku eVp.ci.kovA aNiyinY payirYciyAlYar ciko awirupwi weVriviwwulYlYAr . pacipik katalpakuwiyil ulYlYa vanYuvAttu nAttil 7.2 riktar alYavil payafkara nilanatukkam - cunYAmi eVccarikkE 
portvilA : vatakku AswireliyA pakuwiyilirunwu cumAr 1350 kilomIttar wUrawwil amEnwulYlYa wIvukkUttafkalYE koVNta vanYuvAttu nAttil inYrYu riktar alYavil 7.2 alakilAnYa payafkara nilanatukkam erYpattawu . 
ifkulYlYa cAnYtto wIvilirunwu 151 kilomIttar wUrawwil pUmiyinY atiyil cumAr 35 kilomIttar AlYYawwil uruvAnYa nilanatukkawwEyatuwwu cunYAmi eVccarikkEyum vitukkappattulYlYawu . 
cumAr 12 Ayiram cawura kilomIttar parappalYavu koVNta vanYuvAttu nAttil cumAr mUnYrYu latcam makkalY vAlYYnwu varukinYrYanYar . 
ifkilAnwu marYrYum pirAnYs nAtukalYitam katanwa 1980-m ANtu cuwanwiram peVrYrYa vanYuvAttuvE wAkkiya inYrYEya nilanatukkawwAl erYpatta uyirilYYappu marYrYum poVrulYilYYappu woVtarpAnYa utanYati wakavalkalY ewum veVlYiyAkavillE . wi.mu.ka.vukku eVnYnYE payanYpatuwwa weVriyavillE ; inwa murYE ottalYikka mAttenY 
mu.ka.alYYakiri Afkila pawwirikE oVnYrYukku woVlEpeci valYYiyAka pettiyalYiwwa mu.ka.alYYakiri kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
nAnY stAlinY , kanYimoVlYYi ponYrYoritam peci kurYEnwawu 3 varutafkalYAvawu irukkum . 
eVwarYkAkavum , avarkalYutanY peca vAyppu varavillE . 
eVnYnYE eVppati payanYpatuwwa veNtum eVnYpawu wimukavukku weVriyavillE . 
eVnYave akkatcikku kurYiwwu awikamAka karuwwu kUrYa virumpavillE . 
iwu ponYrYa araciyalil nAnY Arvam kAttavillE . 
mawurEyil ulYlYa 10 woVkuwikalYilum wimuka veVrYrYi peVrYappovawillE eVnYpawu mattum weVrikirYawu . 
nAnY varum cattacapE werwalil eVnwa katcikkum vAkkalYikka povawillE . 
ivvArYu alYYakiri kUrYiyulYlYAr . pilYe Ap curYrYu vAyppE wakkavEppawu yAr ? 
peVfkalYUru - punYe inYrYu palapparItcE - 
wi inwu 
pilYe Ap curYrYu vAyppE wakkavEkka porAtum peVfkalYUru marYrYum punYe aNikalY EpieVllil inYrYu mowukinYrYanYa . 
iwanYAl ippotti paraparappAka irukkum eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
inwa EpieVl woVtaril iwu varE 9 pottikalYil AtiyulYlYa punYe aNi 3 veVrYrYikalYE mattume peVrYrYu pulYlYippattiyalil 6-vawu itawwil irukkirYawu . 
peVfkalYUru aNi 7 pottikalYil Ati 2 pottikalYil mattume veVnYrYu pulYlYippattiyalil 7-vawu itawwil irukkirYawu . 
iwanYAl pilYe Ap curYrYukku wakuwipeVrYa inYrYEya pottiyil veVnYrYe AkaveNtum eVnYrYa nilEyil iru aNikalYum ulYlYanYa . 
ippotti peVfkalYUruvil mAlE 4 maNikku natakkirYawu . 
peVfkalYUru aNiyEp poVrYuwwavarE awu keptanY virAt koli , tivilliyars AkiyorEye peVriwum nampiyirukkirYawu . 
kirYis keVyil , vAtcanY Akiyor awirati AttakkArarkalYAka irunwAlum katanwa EpieVl pottikalYE pola avarkalY acurawwanYamAka AtAwawu peVfkalYUru aNikku palavInYamAkave ulYlYawu . 
iwu powAweVnYrYu anwa aNiyinY panwuvIccAlYarkalYum woVtarnwu coVwappi varukirYArkalY . 
pala AttafkalYil 180 ranYkalYukku mel kuviwwum peVfkalYUru aNi veVrYrYi peVrYAwawu iwarYku cAnYrYAka ulYlYawu . 
inwa kurYEkalY nIfki inYrYEya pottiyil peVfkalYUru veVrYrYipeVrYum eVnYrYu anwa aNiyinY racikarkalY eVwirpArwwu kAwwirukkirYArkalY . 
awe camayam katanwa pottiyil teVlliyE veVnYrYawAl urYcAkamAka irukkum punYe aNi , awe vekawwil inYrYu peVfkalYUruvE veVlla kAwwirukkirYawu . 
kavAjA , peVyli Akiya iru vIrarkalY anwa aNiyil puwiwAka cernwiruppawu avarkalYinY urYcAkawwE awikariwwulYlYawu . 
iwEp payanYpatuwwi anwa aNi veVrYrYipeVrYumA eVnYpawE poVrYuwwirunwu pArppom . 
teVlli - paFcAp mowal moVkAliyil inYrYu natakkum marYrYoVru pottiyil teVlli terteVvils aNi , kifs leVvanY paFcAp aNiyE eVwirkoVlYkirYawu . 
pulYlYippattiyalil 3-vawu itawwil ulYlYa teVlli aNi , katanwa pottiyil jAkirkAnY utpata wafkalYinY mukkiyamAnYa 4 vIrarkalYukku oyvu koVtuwwawu . 
appottiyil wolvi atEnwawE woVtarnwu avarkalY mINtum inYrYu kalYam irYafkuvArkalY eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
marYupurYam pilYe Ap curYrYukku wakuwi peVrYa veNtumAnYAl inYrYu kattAyam veVnYrYAka veNtiya kattAyawwil paFcAp aNi ulYlYawu . varYatci kurYiwwu Alocikka anYEwwu katci kUttam : mawwiya aracukku inwiya kamyUnYist valiyurYuwwal 
puwuteVlli : 
inwiyAvinY palverYu mAnilafkalYil warYpowu katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavi varukirYawu . 
iwanYAl vivacAyam katumEyAka pAwikkappattulYlYawotu , kutinIr wattuppAtum pala pakuwikalYil erYpattulYlYawu . 
makArARtirA ulYlYitta palverYu mAnilafkalYil ulYlYa varYatci pAwippu kurYiwwu svarAj apiyAnY eVnYrYa amEppu cArpil ucca nIwimanYrYawwil poVwunala valYYakku woVtarappattawu . 
ivvalYYakku nerYrYu vicAraNEkku vanwa powu 10 mAnilafkalYil ulYlYa 256 mAvattafkalYil vacikkum 33 koti makkalY varYatciyAl pAwikkappattiruppawAka mawwiya aracu weVriviwwawu . 
innilEyil , varYatci kurYiwwu AlocanYE ceVyya mawwiya aracu anYEwwu katci kUttawwE kUtta veNtum eVnYrYu inwiya kamyUnYist katci valiyurYuwwiyulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu akkatciyinY weciya ceVyalAlYar cuwAkar reVtti kUrYiyawAvawu : 
katanwa 25 ANtukalYil iwu ponYrYawoVru varYatci nilEmE erYpattawillE . 
varYatciyE camAlYikka mawwiya aracitam wIvira wittam eVwuvum illE . 
varYatciyAnYa pakuwikalYE kaNtarYinwu kutinIr viniyokam ceVyya veNtum . 
varYatci niwiyAka vivacAyikalYukku walA rU. 3 Ayiramum , vivacAya woVlYYilAlYarkalYukku ilavaca uNavum valYYafka veNtum . 
cila mAnilafkalYil woVtarnwu mUnYrYu varutafkalYAka waNNIr paFcam nilavi varukirYawu . 
awil , makArARtirA mAnilawwinY marawvAtA ulYlYitta pakuwikalY mukkiyamAnYavE . 
koVlYuwwum veVyilinY kAraNamAka nUrYrYukkum merYpattor iwuvarE uyirilYYanwulYlYanYar . 
katanwa 25 ANtukalYil iwuponYrYa nilEmE vanwawillE . 
veVtpanilE kittawwatta 42 tikiri ceVlciyasAka ulYlYawu . 
akila inwiya alYavil vivacAyikalY pAwukAppu - waNNIr cemippu - kAlnatEkalY pAwukAppu winYawwE inwiya kamyUnYist katci me 5 marYrYum 6-m wewikalYil anYucarikka ulYlYawu . 
appowu valYarcci pAwiwwa itafkalYukku waNNIr valYYafka natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
ivvArYu avar weVriviwwAr . mawwiyilum , mAnilawwilum oVre katciyinY Atci amEya veNtum mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureRpirapu peccu 
mawurE , mawwiyilum , mAnilawwilum oVre katciyinY Atci amEya veNtum eVnYa mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureRpirapu viruppam weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
piracAram mawurEyil cattapperavE werwalil pottiyitum pA.ja.ka. vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureRpirapu mawurEyil nerYrYu piracAram merYkoVNtAr . 
mawurE ArappAlYEyam kirAsrotu aruke piracAram merYkoVNta avar peciyawAvawu : 
wi.mu.ka. , a.wi.mu.ka. Atci kAlawwil wamilYYaka makkalYukku eVnwa nanYmEyum erYpatavillE . 
mInYavarkalY , vivacAyikalY , peVNkalY palverYu piraccinYEkalYE canwiwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
pirawamar narenwira moti walEmEyilAnYa mawwiya pA.ja.ka. aracu vivacAyikalY , mInYavarkalYukku palverYu wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwi varukirYawu . 
mawwiya aracu eVppowum wamilYYnAttukku AwaravAka irukkum . 
oVre katciyinY Atci mawwiyilum , mAnilawwilum oVre katciyinY Atci amEya veNtum . 
appowu wAnY mawwiya aracAl eVnwa itEyUrYum inYrYi makkalYukku palverYu wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwa mutiyum . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . 
celam 
celawwil mAlEyil natEpeVrYrYa pA.janYawA poVwukkUttawwil mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureR pirapu kalanwu koVNtu pA.janYawA vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu piracAram ceVywAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
mawwiyil katanwa 10 ANtukalYil Atci ceVywa kAfkiras - wi.mu.ka. nAttinY valYarccikkAnYa eVnwa wittafkalYEyum koVNtu varAmal pinYnYokki walYlYivittanYa . 
awanYAl peVriya mArYrYam veNtum eVnYrYu makkalY mutivu ceVywu 2014 pArAlYumanYrYa werwalil narenwira moti pirawamar Aka veNtum eVnYrYu avarukkAka vAkkalYiwwArkalY . 
anwa muwal vAyppE makkalY ippowu anYupaviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
ulaka alYavil pala nAtukalY valYarcci atEyAmal pinYnYokki ceVnYrYu koVNtirukkum inwa velYEyil , inwiyA mattum valYarcciyE nokki ceVlkirYawu . 
iwarYku pirawamar motiye kAraNam . 
mawwiya aracinY muwalItukalY wamilYYakawwirYku varaveNtum eVnYrYAl , mawwiya aracutanY oVwwupokirYa aracu wamilYYakawwil erYpata veNtum . 
ivvArYu mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureR pirapu pecinYAr . hAkkiyil inwiyA veVrYrYi - 
wi inwu 
weVnY AppirikkAvil curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu vilYEyAti varum inwiya makalYir hAkki aNi nerYrYu wanYawu katEci Attawwil skAtlAnwE eVwirwwu vilYEyAtiyawu . 
iwil inwiya aNi 3-0 eVnYrYa kol kaNakkil veVrYrYi peVrYrYawu . 
inwiya warappil pUnYam rANi iru kolkalYum , vanwanYA kattAriyA oVru kolum atiwwanYar . wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam - puwiwAka woVtafkappattulYlYa ; 
wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil ' wamilYYakawwinY waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam , makApalipuram katarYkarE koyil ulYpata 25 ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY itampeVrYrYulYlYanYa . nAttil ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYil wUymEyEp parAmarikkum vakEyil , poVwumakkalY pukArkalYEw weVrivippawarYkAka ; wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyali ' woVtafkappattulYlYawu . 
iwEyoVtti puwuwilliyil wifkalYkilYYamE natEpeVrYrYa vilYYAvil puwiya ceVyaliyE woVtafkivEwwu mawwiya curYrYulA marYrYum kalAcAra iNEyamEccar ( poVrYuppu ) tAktar makeR carmA peciyawAvawu : nAttil ulYlYa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYEw wUymEyAka vEwwiruppawil curYrYulAp payaNikalYum , poVwumakkalYum mukkiyap pafkalYippu ceVyya veNtiyulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl , curYrYulA itafkalY , awEc curYrYiyulYlYa pakuwikalY AkiyavE cukAwAramarYrYa vakEyil irunwAlo , kuppEkalY irunwAlo awu kurYiwwa pukArkalYE poVwumakkalY weVrivikka vacawiyAka mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakam inwa wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyE uruvAkkiyulYlYawu . 
inwaw wittam veVrYrYipeVrYa anYEvarawu oVwwulYYEppum avaciyamAkum . 
aNmEyil woVtafkappatta curYrYulA ; inYpolEnY ' mUlam winYamum 18 Ayiram pawilkalY varukinYrYanYa . 
iwu ponYrYu curYrYulAp payaNikalYinY vacawikkAka palverYu wittafkalY curYrYulA amEccakam mUlam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
ulYnAttu curYrYulAw wurYEyum panYnYAttu curYrYulA pola awikamAnYa vAyppukalYEp peVrYrYulYlYawu . 
awanYAlwAnY inwa ceVllitappeci ceVyali valYYiyAka poVwumakkalY , curYrYulAp payaNikalY Akiyoritamirunwu AlocanYEkalY ketkappatukinYrYanYa eVnYrYAr amEccar . 
curYrYulA ucci mAnAtu 
mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakawwinY ceVyalar vinYow sutRi peciyawAvawu : 
2016 ANtAnYawu curYrYulAw wurYEkku nalla vAypputanY woVtafkiyulYlYawu . 
inwa ANtu mApeVrum curYrYulA ucci mAnAtu jUlE , Akastil natEpeVrYum eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
inwa mAnAtu curYrYulAw wurYEyE Ukkuvikkum . 
warYpowu arYimukappatuwwappattulYlYa wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyE veVrYrYikaramAnYawAka uruvAkka mawwiya curYrYulA marYrYum kalAcAra amEccakam iNEnwu natavatikkEkalYE merYkoVlYlYum . 
ceVyaliyinY payanYpAtu 
inwa ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil inwiyaw woVlliyal wurYEyAl pAwukAkkappatum 
nAttil ulYlYa 25 cirYanwa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY cerkkappatum . 
melum , cila ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalYum woVtarnwu inwac ceVyaliyil cerkka natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY ulYlYa pakuwikalYil cukAwAram illAmal irunwAlo , kuppEkalY ewum irunwAlo awE curYrYulAp payaNikalY marYrYum poVwumakkalY inwac ceVyaliyEp payanYpatuwwi pukEppatam eVtuwwu , wafkalYawu kurYippukalYutanY pawiverYrYam ceVyyalAm . 
iwEyatuwwu , ceVyaliyAnYawu campanwappatta inwiyaw woVlliyal wurYEyinY oVrufkiNEppAlYarukku kurYunwakavalAka anYuppappatum . 
awanYpirYaku , campanwappatta itawwil wUymEp paNi merYkoVlYlYa natavatikkE eVtukkappatum . 
awu woVtarpAnYa wakavalum pukArwArarukku kurYunwakaval mUlam anYuppivEkkappatum . 
inwac ceVyali kUkulY wetuwal poVrYi iyanwirawwil " svac paryattanY " ( ‘ najhasrItt tahalYYhharYhay ’ ) eVnYum peVyaril ulYlYawu eVnYrYAr avar . 
wamilYYakak koyilkalY : 
inwaw wUymE curYrYulA ceVllitappeci ceVyaliyil williyil ulYlYa kuwUpminYAr valYAkam , himAyUnY kallarYE , willi ceVfkottE , wamilYYakawwil ulYlYa waFcE pirakawIsvarar Alayam , makApalipuram katarYkarEkkoyil , AkrAvil ulYlYa wAjmakal , HpawepUr cikri , karnAtakawwil ulYlYa hampi ulYpata 25 cirYanwa ninYEvuc cinYnYafkalY itampeVrYrYulYlYanYa . 
peVfkalYUru , varYatciyE nirvakippawil mAnila aracu wolvi atEnwu vittawAka kavarnYar vajUpAy vAlAvE pA.janYawA walEvarkalY neril canwiwwu paraparappu pukAr weVriviwwanYar . 
kavarnYarutanY canwippu 
karnAtaka kavarnYar vajUpAy vAlAvE pA.janYawA mAnila walEvar eVtiyUrappA walEmEyil akkatciyinY walEvarkalY nerYrYu peVfkalYUruvil ulYlYa rAjpavanYil neril canwiwwu pecinYar . 
appowu karnAtakawwil katum varYatci nilavuvawAkavum , pala pakuwikalYil kutinIr paFcam erYpattu iruppawAkavum , inwa piraccinYEyE wIrkka mAnila aracu uriya natavatikkE eVtukkavillE eVnYrYum , eVnYave iwukurYiwwu uriya uwwaravE karnAtaka aracukku pirYappikkumArYum kori pA.janYawA walEvarkalY manYu koVtuwwanYar . 
kavarnYarE canwiwwu peciya pirYaku rAjpavanYE vittu veVlYiye vanwa eVtiyUrappA niruparkalYitam kUrYiyawAvawu : 
karnAtakawwil katum varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
iwarYkAka pA.janYawA cArpil 12 kulYYukkalY amEkkappattu mAnilam mulYYuvawum varYatciyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyyappattawu . 
inwa 12 kulYYukkalYum wanYiwwanYiyAka arYikkEyE wayAriwwu eVnYnYitam valYYafkiyulYlYanYa . 
anwa arYikkEkalYE oVrufkiNEwwu oVre arYikkEyAka wayAriwwu kavarnYaritam valYYafki ulYlYom . 
karnAtaka aracukku uwwaravita... kavarnYitam valYYafkiyulYlYa arYikkEyil mAnilawwil nilavum varYatci kurYiwwu mulYYumEyAnYa wakavalkalY itampeVrYrYulYlYanYa . 
mawwiya aracu varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa awikalYavil niwi oVwukkiyulYlYawu . 
appati irunwum varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE mAnila aracu cariyAka merYkoVlYlYavillE . 
eVnYave , wAfkalY ( kavarnYar ) utanYatiyAka walEyittu varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYumpati karnAtaka aracukku uwwaravitumArYu nAfkalY kUrYiyulYlYom . 
katum varYatciyAl vivacAyikalY pAwikkappattulYlYawAl vivacAyikalYinY katanYE walYlYupati ceVyyumArYu mAnila aracukku arYivurYuwwumArYu kavarnYaritam eVtuwwuk kUrYiyulYlYom . 
varYatciyE nirvakippawil mAnila aracu mulYYumEyAka wolvi atEnwu iruppawE kavarnYaritam virivAka vivariwwu ulYlYom . 
reVyilkalY mUlam waNNIr kutinIr paFcam ulYlYa pakuwikalYil reVyilkalY mUlam waNNIr koVNtu ceVlla natavatikkE eVtukkumArYu koriyulYlYom . 
kAlnatEkalYukku wevEyAnYa wIvanYawwE vata mAnilafkalYilirunwu reVyilkalY mUlam koVNtu vara natavatikkE eVtukkumpati karnAtaka aracukku uwwaravitumArYu korikkE vituwwulYlYom . 
paruvamalYYE woVtafkuvawarYku munYpAka vivacAyikalYukku viwEkalY marYrYum uram AkiyavarYrYE koVtukka veNtum . 
wevEyAnYa itafkalYil kocAlE , minYcArawwE vinYiyokam ceVyya veNtum . 
mAnilawwil 150 wAlukAkkalY varYatci pakuwikalYAka arYivikka veNtum . 
3 ANtukalY Akiyum inwa kAfkiras aracinY cAwanYE pUjjiyam . 
eVnwa valYarcci paNikalYum natEpeVrYavillE . 
mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavinYAlum awE parYrYi kavalEppatAmal muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA wanYawu nArYkAliyE pAwukAwwuk koVlYlYa manwiricapEyE mArYrYi amEppawAka coVlkirYAr . 
iwu veVtkakketAnYawu . 
rU. 1,000 kotiyE ... mawwiya aracE kurYE kUrYuvawE vittuvittu ciwwarAmEyA varYatciyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa makkalYukku uwava veNtum . 
mAnila aracu wanYawu coVnwa niwiyilirunwu rU. 1,000 kotiyE ceVlavu ceVyya veNtum . 
ivvArYu eVtiyUrappA kUrYinYAr . 
inwa pettiyinYpowu pA.janYawA walEvarkalY Ar.acok , IcuvarappA , ci.ti.ravi , cureRkumAr ulYlYittor utanY irunwanYar . a.wi.mu.ka. peVN vetpAlYar vIttil rU. 14 latcam parYimuwal wamilYYakawwil cattamanYrYa werwal vAkkuppawivu varum wifkatkilYYamE ( 16-nwewi ) oVre kattamAka natEpeVrYa ulYlYawu . 
werwalE munYnYittu vetpAlYarkalY marYrYum avarkalY cArnwa araciyal katciyinYar vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam marYrYum paricu poVrutkalY pattuvAtA ceVyvawE watukka werwal ANEyam palverYu natavatikkEkalY eVtuwwu varukirYawu . 
inwa nilEyil vANiyampAti woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. peVN vetpAlYar nilopar ( vayawu 53 ) vIttil vAkkAlYarkalYukku pattuvAtA ceVyvawarYkAka paNam kattukkattAka pawukki vEwwiruppawAka parYakkumpatEyinYarukku nalYlYiravu rakaciya wakaval kitEwwawu . 
iwEyatuwwu parYakkumpatEyinYar marYrYum varumAnYa variwwurYEyinYar , vANiyampAti tavunY kacceri rottil ulYlYa a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar niloparukku coVnwamAnYa Aspawwiri marYrYum awe valYAkawwil ulYlYa avarutEya vIttil awiratiyAka cowanYE merYkoVNtanYar . 
cowanYEyinY powu , a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar nilopar vIttil irunwAr . 
awikArikalYinY cowanYEkku avar oVwwulYYEppu koVtuwwAr . 
wakavalarYinwa a.wi.mu.ka. nirvAkikalY marYrYum woVNtarkalY erAlYamAnYor vetpAlYar vIttinY munYpu wiraNtanYar . 
iwanYAl afku paraparappAnYa cUlYYal kANappattawu . 
nalYlYiravu 11.30 maNikku woVtafkiya cowanYE cumAr 2 maNi nerawwukkum melAka natanwawu . 
wIviramAka natawwappatta cowanYEyil , a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar nilopar vIttilirunwu 14 latcawwu 8 Ayirawwu 820 rUpAy roVkkappaNawwE awikArikalY kEpparYrYinYar . 
paNawwirYkAnYa uriya AvaNam niloparitam illE .

mawwiya aracu mIwu ciwwarAmEyA kurYE coVlvawE erYka mutiyAwu eVtiyUrappA petti 
peVfkalYUru , 
mAnilawwil varYatci nivAraNa niwikku rU. 723 kotiyE oVwukkiya mawwiya aracu mIwu muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kurYE coVlvawE erYka mutiyAwu eVnYrYu pA.janYawA mAnila walEvar eVtiyUrappA weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
eVtiyUrappA AlocanYE kalapuraki mAvattawwil nilavum varYatci kurYiwwu , anwa mAvattawwE cernwa pA.janYawA nirvAkikalY marYrYum varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya amEkkappatta pA.janYawA kulYYuvinYarutanY peVfkalYUru mallecuvarawwil ulYlYa katci aluvalakawwil nerYrYu mAnila walEvar eVtiyUrappA AlocanYE natawwinYAr . 
pinYnYar eVtiyUrappA niruparkalYitam kUrYiyawAvawu : 
erYka mutiyAwu 
mAnilawwil katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavuvawAl palverYu mAvatta makkalY kutinIr kitEkkAmal peVrum ciramawwE anYupaviwwu varukirYArkalY . 
AnYAl muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYAmal mawwiya aracu mIwu kurYEkalYE kUrYi varukirYAr . 
varYatci parYrYi Ayvu ceVyya mawwiya aracu erYkanYave kulYYuvE anYuppi vEwwirunwawu . 
melum varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa rU. 723 koti niwiyE pirawamar narenwira moti oVwukkiyulYlYAr . 
AnYAl varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa mawwiya aracu niwi valYYafkavillE eVnYrYu muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kurYE coVlkirYAr . 
nAttil 10 mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
AnYAl namawu mAnilawwil varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYavum , vivacAyikalYukku uriya parikAramum valYYafkavum mawwiya aracu niwi oVwukki irukkirYawu . 
anwa niwiyE muwal–manwiri murYEyAka payanYpatuwwAmal mawwiya aracE kurYEcoVlvawE erYka mutiyAwu . 
melum muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA , pirawamarE canwiwwu varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa niwi oVwukkumpati ketka ulYlYAr . 
iwu wevEyarYrYawu . 
ivvArYu eVtiyUrappA kUrYinYAr . ceVnYnYE , 
wamilYYnAttirYku vacanwam vIcum eVwirkAlawwE uruvAkka tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAcE muwalvar AkkufkalY eVnYa tAktar rAmawAs poVwumakkalYukku veNtukolY vituwwulYlYAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu pA.ma.ka. nirYuvanYar tAktar rAmawAs veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
lok ayukwA wamilYYnAttinY valYarccikku peVrum watEyAka irukkum iru wImEkalYE pattiyalittAl muwalitawwil iruppawu UlYYal , iraNtAvawu itawwil iruppawu mawu Akum . 
ivviru wImEkalYEyum uram pottu valYarwwavE wamilYYakawwE 50 ANtukalYAka Atci ceVywu varum a.wi.mu.ka.vum , wi.mu.ka.vum wAnY . 
wamilYYakawwE puwEkulYYiyil walYlYiya inwa iru katcikalYinY pitiyilirunwu wamilYYaka makkalYE mItpawarYku unYnYawamAnYa ceVyalwittawwE uruvAkkiyirukkirYAr 
pA.ma.ka. muwal-amEccar vetpAlYar tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs . 
aracu nirvAkawwil UlYYalE oVlYYippawarYkAka lok ayukwA amEppu erYpatuwwappatum , poVwu cevE peVrYum urimEc cattam koVNtu varappatum eVnYrYu avar vAkkurYuwi alYiwwulYlYAr . 
powE mItpu maruwwuvam 
muwal-amEccaro , amEccarkalYo UlYYal ceVyvawAka weVriyavanwAl yArutEya anYumawiyEyum peVrYAmal wanYnYiccEyAka valYYakku woVtara mutiyum eVnYrYa alYavukku lok ayukwA amEppukku awikAram alYikkappatum . 
muwalamEccarAka tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs pawaviyerYrYawum muwal kEyeVlYYuwwe mawu oVlYYippukkAnYa ANEyil wAnY irukkum . 
wamilYYakawwil anYEwwu mawu AlEkalYum mUtappatum . 
mawukkatEkalY mUtappatuvawAl erYpatum varuvAy ilYYappE Itukatta cirYappuwwittafkalY , mawu atimEkalYE mItka powE mItpu maruwwuvam alYikkappatum , mawukkatEkalYil paNiyArYrYiyavarkalYukku mArYrYu aracu velE valYYafkappatum eVnYa mawuvilakkE veVrYrYikaramAka ceVyalpatuwwuvawarYkAnYa anYEwwu wittafkalYum pA.ma.ka.vAl vakukkappattulYlYanYa . 
vacanwam vIcum eVwirkAlam . 
wamilYYnAttil mawuvE oVlYYikka 35 ANtukalYAka nAnY porAti varukirYenY . 
eVnYawu kanYavum , mawu illA wamilYYakam amEya veNtum eVnYrYu ninYEkkum peVNkalY ulYlYitta anYEvarinY kanYavum nirYEverYa veNtumAnYAl tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs muwalamEccar AnYAl wAnY mutiyum . 
oVru pEcA UlYYal illAwa wamilYYakam ; 
oVru coVttu mawu illAwa wamilYYakawwE uruvAkka tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAcAl wAnY mutiyum . 
eVnYave , wamilYYnAttirYku vacanwam vIcum eVwirkAlawwE uruvAkka tAktar anYpumaNiyE muwalamEccarAkka veNtum . 
awarYkAka varum cattapperavEw werwalil anYEvarum mAmpalYYam cinYnYawwil vAkkalYiwwu veVrYrYi peVrYac ceVyya veNtum eVnYrYu kettuk koVlYkirYenY . 
ivvArYu awil kUrYappattulYlYawu . caccinYutanY oVppita virAt koli inYnYum katumEyAka ulYYEkka veNtum : 
yuvarAj cif karuwwu 
wi inwu . 
caccinY teVNtulkarinY cAwanYEkalYE murYiyatippawu katinYam , caccinYutanY oVppitappatuvawarYku virAt koli inYnYum neVtunwoVlEvu ceVlla veNtiyulYlYawu eVnYrYu yuvarAj cif weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
camIpawwil wanYiyAr woVlEkkAtci oVnYrYil yuvarAj cif kUrYiya powu , “ 100 cawafkalY eVnYpawu cinwippawarYke neVtunwUrawwil ulYlYa cAwanYEyAkum . 
caccinY teVNtulkar oVru kiret pilYeyar , inwiyAvinY wUwar 
eVnYave virAt koliyE caccinYutanY oVppita veNtumeVnYil awarYku virAt koli inYnYum katumEyAka ulYYEwwu neVtunwUram ceVlla veNtiyulYlYawu . 
caccinY teVNtulkarinY kirikkeVt cAwanYEkalYE oVppitappata mutiyAwawu . 
avarawu pArampariyam nINta nAtkalYukku nItippawAkum .

natappu EpieVl kirikkeVttil canY rEcars hEwarApAw aNikkAka natappu EpieVl woVtaril muwal pottiyil yuvarAj kalYamirYafkuvAr eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavuvawAl vitumurYE nAtkalYilum palYlYi mANavarkalYukku mawiya uNavu manwiri ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA petti 
peVfkalYUru , 
mAnilawwil katum varYatci nilavuvawAl vitumurYE nAtkalYilum palYlYi mANavarkalYukku mawiya uNavu valYYafka manwiricapE kUttawwil mutivu eVtuwwiruppawAka manwiri ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
manwiricapE kUttam peVfkalYUru 
viwAnYacavuwAvil muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA walEmEyil nerYrYu manwiricapE kUttam natEpeVrYrYawu . 
inwa kUttawwil karnAtakawwil nilavum varYatci kurYiwwu virivAnYa AlocanYE natawwappattawu . 
inwa nilEyil , manwiricapE kUttam mutinwawum manwiri ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
palYlYikalYil mawiya uNavu mAnilawwil katumEyAnYa varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
varYatciyAl palverYu mAvattafkalYil kutinIr wattuppAtu , kAlnatEkalYukku wIvanYafkalY illAwa nilE erYpattulYlYawu . 
varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYil nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa rU. 50 koti niwi erYkanYave oVwukkappattawu . 
warYpowu anwa niwiyE rU. 100 kotiyAka uyarwwa mutivu eVtukkappattulYlYawu . 
kAlnatE wIvanYafkalYukku rU. 15 koti niwi oVwukkappattulYlYawu . 
awwutanY varYatci pAwiwwa mAvattafkalYil nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa , anwanwa mAvatta kaleVktarkalYukku rU. 357 koti niwi oVwukkappatum . 
varYatciyE camAlYikka mawwiya aracitam mAnilawwirYku uriya niwi oVwukki warumpati ketkappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl mawwiya aracitam irunwu rU. 800 koti kitEkkalAm eVnYrYu eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
kurYippAka varYatci pAwiwwa mAvattafkalYil ulYlYa palYlYikalYil 39 nAtkalY kotE vitumurYE vitappattulYlYawu . 
AnYAlum anwa mAvattafkalYil ulYlYa palYlYikalYil patikkum mANavarkalYukku mawiya uNavu valYYafka wIrmAnYikkappattu irukkirYawu . 
malYYEnIr cemippu kawak mAvattawwil rU. 12 koti ceVlavil 3 ekkar nilawwil kaNkAtci mEyam katta mutivu eVtukkappattulYlYawu . 
melum aracu cArpil natakkum rU. 50 latcam varEyilAnYa valYarcci paNikalYukkAnYa teVNtarkalYE eVtukka waliw , palYYafkutiyinYarukku 24 cawavIwam oVwukkItu ceVyyappatum . 
peVfkalYUruvil malYYEnIr cemippu kattAyamAkka mutivu ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
peVfkalYUruvil 1,200 cawura atiyil kattappatum vItukalYil malYYEnIr cekarippu kattAyamAkkappattulYlYawu . 
inwa wittawwE murYEyAka ceVyalpatuwwa wIrmAnYamum nirYEverYrYappattu irukkirYawu . 
ivvArYu manwiri ti.pi.jeVyaccanwirA kUrYinYAr . wirucci , we.mu.wi.ka. , makkalY nalakkUttaNi - wa.mA.kA . cArpil wirucciyil natanwa mAnAttil 6 katci walEvarkalY kalanwukoVNtu pecinYar . 
makkalY nalakkUttaNi natEpeVrYa ulYlYa cattamanYrYa werwalil we.mu.wi.ka. , makkalY nalakkUttaNi - wa.mA.kA. cArpil oVru kUttaNi amEkkappattu 234 woVkuwikalYilum vetpAlYarkalY kalYawwil ulYlYanYar . 
kUttaNiyinY muwal-amEccar vetpAlYarum , we.mu.wi.ka. nirYuvanYa walEvarumAnYa vijayakAnw , ma.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , kUttaNiyinY oVrufkiNEppAlYarumAnYa vEko , mArkcist kamyUnYistu katciyinY mAnila ceVyalAlYar ji.rAmakiruRNanY , inwiya kamyUnYistu katciyinY mAnila ceVyalAlYar muwwaracanY , vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katciyinY walEvar woVl.wirumAvalYavanY , wa.mA.kA. walEvar ji.ke.vAcanY Akiyor vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum wanYiwwanYiyAka cUrYAvalYi piracAram ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . 
mAnAtu 6 katci walEvarkalYum oVnYrYAka cernwu mAmaNtUril katanwa cila nAtkalYukku munYpu piracAram ceVywu pecinYar . 
awanYpinY oVnYrYAka iNEnwu oVre metEyil piracAram ceVyyAmal wanYiwwanYiyAka kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu wIvira piracAram ceVywu vanwanYar . 
inwa nilEyil 6 katci walEvarkalYum oVre metEyil piracAram ceVyyum vakEyil wirucciyil mArYrYu araciyal veVrYrYi kUttaNi mAnAtu natawwa akkUttaNi katci walEvarkalY mutivu ceVywanYar . 
iwarYkAka wirucci - ceVnYnYE weciya neVtuFcAlEyoram paFcappUril itam wervu ceVyyappattu 15 ekkar parappalYavil mAnAttu wital amEkkappattawu . 
awanYpati mArYrYu araciyal veVrYrYi kUttaNi mAnAtu nerYrYu mAlE natanwawu . 
mAnAttu witalil 6 katci walEvarkalYinY uruvappatafkalY atafkiya kat-avutkalY , vilYampara pawAkEkalY vEkkappattirunwanYa . 
vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu.. walEvarkalY pecum metEyum piramANtamAka amEkkappattirunwanYa . 
woVNtarkalY amaruvawarYku vacawiyAka nArYkAlikalY potappattirunwanYa . 
mawiyam muwale woVNtarkalY varawwoVtafki mAnAttu witalil amarnwanYar . 
mAnAtu natEpeVrYum itawwE curYrYi minYvilYakkukalY potappattirunwanYa . 
woVNtarkalYinY vAkanYafkalYE nirYuwwa wanYiyAka vacawi erYpatuwwappattirunwanYa . 
mAnAtu mAlE 6 maNikku mel woVtafkiyawu . 
mAnAttil wirucci kilYYakku woVkuwi vetpAlYar tAktar roVkEyA ( ma.wi.mu.ka ) , merYku woVkuwi vetpAlYar jocap jeVrAltu ( we.mu.wi.ka ) , wiruveVrYumpUr woVkuwi vetpAlYar ceVnwilkumAr ( we.mu.wi.ka ) , srIrafkam woVkuwi vetpAlYar vE.puRpam ( inwiya kamyUnYistu ) , mucirYi woVkuwi vetpAlYar rAjacekaranY ( wa.mA.kA ) , lAlkuti woVkuwi vetpAlYar jeVyacIlanY ( mArkcist kamyUnYistu ) , maNNaccanallUr woVkuwi vetpAlYar pApu ( we.mu.wi.ka ) , wurYEyUr woVkuwi vetpAlYar cujAwevi ( vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katci ) , maNappArYE woVkuwi vetpAlYar kiruRNakopAl ( we.mu.wi.ka ) AkiyorE arYimukappatuwwi katci walEvarkalY pecinYar . 
vijayakAnw walEmE mAnAttirYku vijayakAnw walEmE wAfki pecinYAr . 
wirucci mAnakar mAvatta wa.mA.kA. walEvar cArupAlA woVNtEmAnY munYnYilE vakiwwu pecinYAr . 
awanYpinY vEko , ji.ke.vAcanY , rAmakiruRNanY , woVl.wirumAvalYavanY , muwwaracanY , weciya weVnYnYinwiya nawikalY iNEppu cafka walEvar ayyAkkaNNu Akiyor pecinYar . 
munYnYawAka wirucci mAnakar mAvatta ma.wi.mu.ka. ceVyalAlYar veVllamaNti comu varaverYrYu pecinYAr . 
mutivil mAnakar mAvatta we.mu.wi.ka. ceVyalAlYar vijayarAjanY nanYrYi kUrYinYAr . 
mAnAttil 6 katcikalYE cernwa mAnila , mAvatta nirvAkikalY , woVNtarkalY wiralYAka kalanwu koVNtanYar . jAkIr kAnY illAwa teVlli aNiyE vIlYYwwiyawu punYe - 
wi inwu 
teVlliyil natEpeVrYrYa EpieVl kirikkeVt pottiyil punYe cUppar jeVyaNts aNi , teVlli ter teVvils aNiyE 7 vikkeVttukalY viwwiyAcawwil vIlYYwwiyawu . 
muwalil pet ceVyya alYYEkkappatta teVlli aNi 20 ovarkalYil 7 vikkeVttukalY ilYYappukku 162 ranYkalY eVtukka punYe aNi ilakkE viratti 166 / 3 eVnYrYu veVrYrYi peVrYrYawu . 
ivvakEp pottikalYeVllAm EpieVl woVtarukku eVnYrYe pirawyekamAka vativamEkkappatta potti , iwanY warkkam EpieVl kirikkeVttukkAnYa pirawyeka warkkam . 
jAkIr kAnY , kuviNtanY ti kAk illE . 
teVlli aNikku keptanY tuminYi . 
teVlli aNi veVrYrYi peVrYuvawarYkAka Atiyawu pol weVriyavillE . 
wonYi aNiyE avvalYavu eVlYiwAka veVlYiyerYrYivittAl EpieVl ‘ mAtal ’ eVnYpawe kelYvikkurYiyAkivitume ? 
amiw misrA no-pAl vIcukirYAr 
awuvum mikappeVriya no-pAl , atuwwa panwe neVFcuyara pultAs vIcukirYAr . 
moVkamawu Rami patumocamAka vIci 3.1 ovarkalYil 50 ranYkalY koVtukkirYAr . 
awuvum 18-vawu ovaril Rami vIciya vEtukkAkave avarE 6 vArafkalY kirikkeVttilirunwu watE ceVyya veNtum . 
leVk stampilirunwu arE ki.mI. walYlYi oVru panwE vIcukirYAr inwiya aNiyinY munYnYaNi pavular . 
awu 5 vEtAka mArYiyawu . 
tuminYi katEci nerawwil pavanY neVkiyE panwu vIca alYYEkkirYAr . 
ivE eVllAmwAnY EpieVl kirikkeVttinY pirawyeka kuNAmcafkalY . 
imrAnY wAhir , amiw misrAvinY nutpamAnYa panwu vIccinYAl katEci 3 ovarkalYil 37 ranYkalY eVnYrYu punYe aNikkuw wevEyAka irunwa powu iruwarappirYkum veVrYrYi cAwwiyamAka irunwawu . 
appowuwAnY moVkamawu Rami AttawwinY 18-vawu ovaril mocamAnYa 5 vEtukalYutanY wonYikku eVfku panwu vIcakkUtAwo afku vIcinYAr . 
avarum oVru pavuNtari oVru ner ciks atiwwAr . 
iwanYAl 3 ovarkalY 37 ranYkalY eVnYrYa camanYpAtu RamiyinY kEfkaryawwinYAl 12 panwukalYil 17 ranYkalY eVnYrYu AnYawu . 
19-vawu ovarinY muwal panwil 27 ranYkalY eVtuwwa wonYi imrAnY wAhir panwE wUkki atiwwu pavuNtari aruke cAm pillifsinY arumEyAnYa ketcukku veVlYiyerYinYAr . 
AnYAl wicara peVrerA irYafki 2 mikappeVriya cikcarkalYE vilYAca katEci ovaril 3 ranYkalY wevE eVnYrYa nilEyil rahAnYe pilYikkil pavuNtari atiwwu mutiwwu vEwwAr . 
rahAnYe 48 panwukalYil 7 pavuNtarikalYutanY 63 ranYkalY eVtuwwu nAt avuttAka wikalYYnwAr , wicara peVrerA 5 panwukalYil 14 nAt avut . 
munYnYawAka usmAnY kavAjA 8 ranYkalYil koVtuwwa ketc vAyppu wavarYavitappata 27 panwukalYil 2 pavuNtari 1 cikcarutanY 30 ranYkalY eVtuwwu misrA panwil stamptu AnYAr . 
cavurav wivAri 21 ranYkalY eVtuwwu imrAnY wAhiritam vIlYYnwAr . 
teVlli aNiyil jeVyanw yAwav vikkeVt eVtukkAvittAlum cikkanYamAka vIcinYAr , imrAnY wAhir , amiw misrA murYEye 2 marYrYum 1 vikkeVttEk kEpparYrYinYar . 
munYnYawAka punYe aNi vekappanwu vIccAlYar tiNtA , teVlli woVtakka vIrar riRap paNttE pavultu ceVyya karuN nAyar , caFcu cAmcanY cila pavuNtarikalYE atiwwu ceVttil AyinYar 
ranY vikiwam ovarukku 8 ranYkalYukkum mel ceVnYrYawu . 
AnYAl pavar pilYeyinY katEci panwil cAmcanY eVlYiwAnYa ketccukku 20 ranYkalYil AttamilYYanwAr . 
karuN nAyar 23 panwukalYil 32 ranYkalY eVtuwwAr , tuminYi 32 panwukalYil 34 ranYkalYE eVtuwwAr . 
cAm pillifs katEciyil awiratiyAka AtinYAr . 
asvinYE ivar iraNtu woVtar cikcarkalYE atiwwAr . 
pirAwveVyt , murukanY asvinYE iraNtu cikcarkalY atiwwAr . 
AnYAl rahAnYe , cavurav wivAriyinY arYpuwamAnYa pIltifkinYAl 2 ranY avutkalY erYpattawu . 
pavanY neVki 12 panwukalYil 19 ranYkalY eVtukka teVlli aNi oralYavukku cavAlAnYa ilakkE nirNayiwwawu . 
Atta nAyakanYAka rahAnYe wervu ceVyyappattAr . makkalY varYatciyil wavippu , 
muwal-manwiri varukEkkAka cAlEyil waNNIr weVlYippu 
peVfkalYUr , 
karnAtakawwil makkalY varYatciyil waviwwuvarum nilEyil muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varukEkkAka cAlEyil waNNIr weVlYikkappattawu carccEyE erYpatuwwi ulYlYawu . 
karnAtaka mAnilawwilum varYatci erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
makkalY waNNIr parYrYAkkurYEyinYAl waviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
karnAtakawwil 27 mAvattafkalYil 136 wAlukAkkalYil varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
anwap pakuwikalYil nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa aracu wIvira natavatikkE eVtuwwu varukirYawu . 
inwa pakuwikalYil kutinIr piraccinYEyE wIrkka wevEyAnYa niwi oVwukkappattulYlYawu . 
kutinIr piraccinYEyE wIrkkavum , kAlnatEkalYukku wIvanYam valYYafkavum uriya natavatikkE eVtukkumpati mAvatta kaleVktarkalYukku uwwaravitappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwarYkitEye karnAtaka aNEkalYil ulYlYa waNNIrE kutinIrukku mattume payanYpatuwwa veNtum eVnYrYu uyar awikArikalYukku ciwwarAmEyA uwwaravittulYlYAr . 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE Ayvu ceVyya eVnwa manwiriyum mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVyyavillE eVnYrYu eVtiyUrappA kurYrYam cAttinYAr . 
karnAtakawwil nilaviya varYatciyE camAlYikka mawwiya aracu valYYafkiya niwiyE muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA cariyAka payanYpatuwwavillE eVnYrYu munYnYAlY muwal–manwiri eVtiyUrappA , mawwiya manwiri anYanwakumAr marYrYum pA.janYawA walEvarkalY kurYrYamcAtti irunwArkalY . 
AnYAl karnAtaka varYatci nivAraNawwirYkAka mawwiya aracu eVnwaviwa niwi uwaviyum valYYafkavillE eVnYrYu muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA kurYrYam cAttinYAr . 
karnAtakAvil varYatci araciyalAkkappattu oVruvarE oVruvar kurYrYam cAtti varukinYrYanYar . 
makkalY varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu varum innilEyil muwal-manwiri varukkEkkAka waNNIr cAlEyil weVlYikkappatta vivakAram carcEyE erYpatuwwi ulYlYawu . 
muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA varYatci pAwippE pArvEyita pAkAlkot ceVnYrYAr . 
ciwwAramEyA afku ceVlvawarYku munYnYawAka cAlEyil vINAka waNNIr weVlYikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
vAttar tefkaril waNNIr nirYappattu cAlE kulYirvikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwu woVtarpAnYa pukEppatafkalY camUka valEwalYafkalYil veVlYiyAki vimarcanYawwirYku ulYlYAkiulYlYawu . ceVnYnYE , ceVnYnYEyil mu.ka.stAlinY inYrYu ( viyAlYYakkilYYamE ) natanwu ceVnYrYu vItu , vItAka piracAram ceVykirYAr . 
mu.ka.stAlinY wIvira piracAram 
wamilYYaka cattamanYrYa werwalil pottiyitum wi.mu.ka. - kAfkiras marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu wi.mu.ka. poVrulYAlYar mu.ka.stAlinY katanwa mAwam 15-nwewi muwal wIvira piracArawwil Itupattu varukirYAr . 
ceVnYnYEyil katanwa 28-nwewi rAyapuram , Ar.ke.nakar , wiruvoVrYrYiyUr , mAwavaram , peVrampUr , aNNAnakar , ceppAkkam - wiruvallikkeNi , AyiramvilYakku Akiya 8 woVkuwikalYilum , 4-nwewi , mayilAppUr , AyiramvilYakku , wiyAkarAyanakar , cEwAppettE , virukampAkkam , AlanwUr , velYacceri , colYYifkanallUr Akiya woVkuwikalYilum venY mUlam vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu wi.mu.ka. kUttaNikku vAkku cekariwwAr . 
ceVnYnYEyil natanwu piracAram 
wamilYYakawwil nAlYE marYuwinYam 5 maNiyutanY piracAram oyvatEya ulYlYanilEyil , mu.ka.stAlinY inYrYu ( viyAlYYakkilYYamE ) ceVnYnYEyil mINtum piracAram merYkoVlYlYa ulYlYAr . 
wamilYYakawwinY pirYa mAvattafkalYil natanwu ceVnYrYu vAkku cekarippil Itupattawu pol , ceVnYnYEyilum avar vItu , vItAka ceVnYrYu piracAram ceVyya ulYlYAr . 
awanYpati , eVlYYumpUr woVkuwikku utpatta natrAj wirEyarafkam arukil kAlE 7 maNikku piracArawwE woVtafkum mu.ka.stAlinY anwa woVkuwiyil kAlE 8 maNi varEyil vItu , vItAka ceVnYrYu vAkku cekarikkirYAr . 
awanYpinYnYar wiyAkarAyanakar woVkuwikku utpatta wafkalkarE pakuwiyil 9 maNi muwal 10 maNi varEyilum , wurYEmukam woVkuwikku utpatta maNNatiyil kAlE 10.15 maNi muwal 11 maNi varEyilum , cEwAppettE woVkuwikku utpatta neru nakaril mAlE 4 maNi muwal 5 maNi varEyilum vItu , vItAka natanwu ceVnYrYu wi.mu.ka.vukku Awaravu wirattukirYAr . 
wirYanwa venYil.. 
awanYpinYnYar mu.ka.stAlinY wirYanwa venY mUlam vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu mAlE 6 maNiyalYavil pUnwamalli woVkuwiyilum , 7.30 maNiyalYavil wAmparam woVkuwiyilum , 8.30 maNiyalYavil pallAvaram woVkuwiyilum , 9.15 maNiyalYavil colYYifkanallUr woVkuwiyilum piracAram ceVykirYAr . mAtrit opanY teVnYnYis : 
3-vawu curYrYil jokovik - 
wi inwu . 
mAtrit opanY teVnYnYis pottiyinY 3-vawu curYrYukku ceVrpiya vIrar novAk jokovik wakuwi peVrYrYulYlYAr . 
mAtrit opanY teVnYnYis pottikalY mAtrit nakaril natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
iwil nerYrYu munYwinYam natanwa 2-vawu curYrYup pottiyil ceVrpiyAvinY jokovik kuroRiyAvinY pornYA korikkE eVwirwwu AtinYAr . 
ippottiyil jokovik 6-2 , 6-4 eVnYrYa nerceVtkalYil veVnYrYu 3-vawu curYrYukku wakuwipeVrYrYAr . 
3-vawu curYrYup pottiyil speVyinY vIrar rApeVrto patistA akattE eVwirwwu avar AtavulYlYAr . 
marYrYoVru pottiyil AswireliyAvinY nikkirjiyos 7-6 , 7-6 eVnYrYa ceVtkaNakkil cuvitcarlAnwinY stAnY vAvrifkAvE veVnYrYAr . 
peVNkalYukkAnYa pottiyilirunwu muwukuvali kAraNamAka viktoriyA acareVnYkA vilakinYAr . 
marYrYoVru pottiyil peVtrAkvitovAvE 6-3 , 6-4 eVnYrYa ner ceVtkalYil AswireliyAvinY tAriyA kAvrilovA vIlYYwwinYAr . usmanYapAw , marawvAtAvil varYatciyinY uccamAka , powiya waNNIr illAwawAl cikiccEkku varum noyAlYikalYE anYumawippawE aracu Aspawwiri nirvAkam nirYuwwi vEwwulYlYawu . 
powiya waNNIr illE 
marAttiyawwil nilavum varYatci makkalYE vAtti vawEwwu varukirYawu . 
kurYippAka marawvAtA maNtalawwil katum varYatci nilavukirYawu . 
iwanYAl inwa pakuwikalYil vAlYYum makkalY kutikka waNNIr kUta illAmal waviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
melum afkulYlYa kiNarYukalYum , kulYafkalYum varYaNtu pAlEvanYafkalYAka kAtci warukinYrYanYa . 
inwanilEyil marawvAtA maNtalawwil ulYlYa usmanYApAw aracu Ayurvewa Aspawwiriyil powiya waNNIr illAwawAl noyAlYikalYE anYumawippawE Aspawwiri nirvAkam nirYuwwi ulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu Aspawwiri tInY pirakAR hapArte kUrYiyawAvawu : 
varYaNta AlYYwulYE kiNarYukalY Aspawwiri valYAkawwil ulYlYa 2 AlYYwulYE kiNarYukalYum varYaNtu vittanYa . 
iwanYAl Aspawwiri maruwwuva kallUri vituwi mANavarkalY 150 perukku 2 nAtkalYukku munYnYare vitumurYE alYikkappattu vIttirYku anYuppi vEkkappattulYlYanYar . 
Aspawwiriyil moVwwam 170 patukkEkalY ulYlYanYa . 
warYpowu 80 noyAlYikalY mattume wafki cikiccE peVrYrYu varukinYrYanYar . 
avarkalYukku wevEyAnYa waNNIr kUta warYpowu illE . 
eVnYave puwiwAka varum noyAlYikalYE Aspawwiriyil anYumawikka mutiyAwa nilEkku walYlYappattulYlYom . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . 
AspawwiriyinY inwa mutivu kurYiwwu civacenYA mAvatta walEvar cuwIr pAttIl kUrYukEyil , 
‘ ‘ Aspawwiri nirvAkam wanYnYiccEyAka noyAlYikalYE anYumawippawE nirYuwwiyulYlYawu . 
iwu kurYiwwu vicAraNEkku uwwaravita korikkE vituwwulYlYom . 
civacenYA cArpil Aspawwirikku tefkar lArikalYil waNNIr valYYafkappatum ’’ eVnYrYAr . wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum veVrYrYi peVrYum ; 
I.vi.ke.eVs. ilYafkovanY petti 
Irotu , wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum veVrYrYipeVrYum eVnYrYu I.vi.ke.eVs.ilYafkovanY kUrYinYAr . 
I.vi.ke.eVs.ilYafkovanY Irotu mAvattawwil ulYlYa 8 cattamanYrYa woVkuwikalYilum nerYrYu amEwiyAka werwal natanwawu . 
wamilYYnAtu kAfkiras katciyinY walEvar I.vi.ke.eVs.ilYafkovanY Irotu kacceri vIwiyil ulYlYa mAnakarAtci woVtakkappalYlYikkUtawwil kutumpawwinYarutanY vanwu wanYawu vAkkE pawivu ceVywAr . 
munYnYawAka vAkkuccAvatikku vanwa avar varicEyil ninYrYu vAkku alYiwwAr . 
vAkkalYiwwa pinY vAkkuccAvatikku veVlYiye niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwa avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi wi.mu.ka. - kAfkiras kUttaNi anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum veVrYrYi peVrYum . 
a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalY paNam koVtuwwawAka werwal ANEyame aravakkurYicci , waFcAvUr Akiya itafkalYil werwalE walYlYivEwwu ulYlYawu . 
paNam koVtuwwa a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalYE pottiyilirunwu wakuwi nIkkam ceVyya veNtum . 
illEyeVnYrYAl werwal mutinwa pinYnYar paNam koVtuwwawAka kUrYappatum vetpAlYarkalY veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl anwa werwal mutivE rawwu ceVyya veNtum . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYinYAr . inwiya oVrunAlY kirikkeVt aNiyinY keptanYAka virAtkoliyE niyamikka veNtum 
kafkuli karuwwu 
puwuteVlli , 
inwiya oVrunAlY kirikkeVt aNiyinY keptanYAka virAtkoliyE niyamikka veNtum eVnYrYu munYnYAlY keptanY kafkuli karuwwu weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
virAtkoliyE keptanYAkka veNtum 
inwiya kirikkeVt aNiyinY munYnYAlY keptanYum , peVfkAl kirikkeVt cafka walEvarumAnYa kafkuli alYiwwa oVru pettiyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
eVllA kirikkeVt aNikalYum wafkalYawu eVwirkAlam kurYiwwu wittam wItti vEwwu irukkum . 
2019–m ANtu natEpeVrYum atuwwa ulaka koppE potti varE tonYiyE keptanYAka woVtara inwiya kirikkeVt vAriya wervu kulYYu mutivu ceVywu irukkirYawA ? 
eVnYpawu wAnY eVnYawu kelYviyAkum . 
teVst pottiyilirunwu tonYi oyvu peVrYrYu vittAr . 
oVrunAlY marYrYum 20 ovar pottiyil mattume avar vilYEyAti varukirYAr . 
tonYi keptanY pawaviyil cirYappAka ceVyalpattu varukirYAr . 
avarawu wirYamE mIwu eVnYakku canwekamillE . 
iruppinYum warYpowu inwiya oVrunAlY aNiyinY keptanY pawaviyE ilYam vIrar oVruvaritam oVppatEkka veNtum eVnYrYu nAnY karuwukirYenY . 
atuwwa keptanY pawavikku virAtkoli poVruwwamAnYavar . 
tonYi katanwa 9 ANtukalYAka inwiya aNiyinY keptanYAka irunwu varukirYAr . 
avar melum 4 ANtukalYukku keptanYAka woVtara pokirYArA ? , allawu virAtkoliyE puwiya keptanYAka niyamippawA ? 
eVnYpawu kurYiwwu inwiya kirikkeVt vAriyam wAnY mutivu ceVyya veNtum . 
oVruvelYE keptanYAka tonYiyE woVtara mutivu eVtuwwAl awu mikavum AccariyawwukkuriyawAka wAnY irukkum . 
tonYi mikaccirYanwa keptanY 
virAtkoli teVst potti keptanY poVrYuppil cirYappAka ceVyalpattu varukirYAr . 
avar Attawwil nAlYukku nAlY nalla erYrYam kaNtu varukirYAr . 
nilEyAnYa AttawwE woVtarnwu veVlYippatuwwuvawil ulakinY walEcirYanwa petsmenYAka virAtkoli vilYafki varukirYAr . 
virAtkoliyinY manYa urYuwiyum , vitAmuyarYciyum nampa mutiyAwa vakEyil cirYappAka ulYlYawu . 
AtukalYawwil arumEyAka ceVyalpattu varukirYAr . 
virAtkoliyE keptanY Akkuvawu , tonYiyE ilYYivupatuwwuvawAka yArum ninYEwwu vitakkUtAwu . 
inwiyA pArwwa mikac cirYanwa keptanYkalYil tonYi oVruvar eVnYpawE marYanwu vita mutiyAwu . 
ivvArYu kafkuli kUrYinYAr . 
27 vayawAnYa virAtkoli inwiya teVst aNiyinY keptanYAka irunwu varukirYAr . 
camIpawwil natanwa 20 ovar ulaka koppE pottiyil woVtarnAyakanY viruwu peVrYrYa virAtkoli , E.pi.eVl. pottiyilum ranY kuvippil acawwi varukirYAr . 
virAtkoli oVrunAlY aNiyinY poVrYuppu keptanYAka 17 AttafkalYil paNiyArYrYi irukkirYAr . 
anwa AttafkalYil 4 cawamum kaNtAr . 
34 vayawAnYa tonYi inwiya oVrunAlY marYrYum 20 ovar aNiyinY keptanYAka ulYlYAr . 
veVrYrYi keptanY eVnYrYu varNikkappatum tonYi camIpakAlamAka wanYawu Attawwil woVyvu kaNtu varukirYAr . varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE Ayvu ceVyya eVnwa manwiriyum mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVyyavillE 
eVtiyUrappA kurYrYaccAttu 
peVfkalYUru , 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE Ayvu ceVyya eVnwa manwiriyum mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVyyavillE eVnYrYu eVtiyUrappA kurYrYamcAttiyulYlYAr . 
araciyal ceVyyakkUtAwu 
karnAtaka pA.janYawA munYnYAlY walEvar pirakalAwjoRikku pirivu upacAra nikalYYcci peVfkalYUru mallesvarawwil ulYlYa pA.janYawA aluvalakawwil nerYrYu natEpeVrYrYawu . 
iwil pA.janYawA mAnila walEvar eVtiyUrappA kalanwu koVNtAr . 
inwa nikalYYccikku pirYaku eVtiyUrappA niruparkalYukku alYiwwa pettiyil kUrYiyawAvawu : 
muwal–manwiri ciwwarAmEyA awikArawwE wavarYAka payanYpatuwwi wanYawu makanYinY nirYuvanYawwirYku aracu Aspawwiriyil maruwwuva paricowanYE kUtam amEkka anYumawi valYYafkiyulYlYAr . 
iwu mattuminYrYi ciwwarAmEyAvinY UlYYalkalY anYEwwum oVvvoVnYrYAka veVlYiye varavulYlYawu . 
eVnYave , ciwwarAmEyA AtciyinY nAtkalY eVNNappatukinYrYanYa . 
varYatci pakuwikalYE Ayvu ceVyya pA.janYawA kulYYukkalYE amEwwawu . 
awanY pirYaku ciwwarAmEyA vilYYiwwuk koVNtu ippowu varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYil Ayvu ceVykirYAr . 
varYatci viRayawwil araciyal ceVyyakkUtAwu . 
kurYrYam coVllik koVNtu eVwuvum ceVyyAmal amEwiyAka irunwAl powAwu . 
kocAlEkalYE wirYakkavillE 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYa mawwiya aracu rU. 1,450 koti valYYafkiyulYlYawu . 
inwa niwiyE mAnila aracu ceVlavu ceVyyavillE . 
inYnYum kUtuwal niwi wevEppattAl mawwiya aracutanY peci peVrYrYuw waruvom . 
karnAtakawwil varYatci nivAraNa paNikalY cariyAka natEpeVrYavillE . 
powumAnYa eVNNikkEyil kocAlEkalYE wirYakkavillE . 
varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE Ayvu ceVyya eVnwa manwiriyum mAvattafkalYil curYrYuppayaNam ceVyyavillE . 
mAnilam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam ceVyya nAnY wittamittulYlYenY . 
awarYku munYpAka civamoVkkA mAvattawwirYku ceVnYrYu katci woVNtarkalYinY kUttawwil kalanwukoVlYlYa ulYlYenY . 
varukirYa 20–n wewi allawu 21–n wewi inwa kUttam natEpeVrYum . 
ivvArYu eVtiyUrappA kUrYinYAr . aravakkurYicci woVkuwi werwal oVwwivEppu : 
me 23-il natEpeVrYukirYawu 
wamilYYakawwil aravakkurYicci cattapperavEw werwal oVwwivEkkappattulYlYawu . 
ifku me 16Am wewi natEpeVrYavirunwa werwal , me 23Am wewi natEpeVrYum eVnYrYu walEmEw werwal ANEyam arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
iwu woVtarpAka werwal ANEyam canYikkilYYamE veVlYiyittulYlYa ceVywikkurYippil weVrivikkappattulYlYawAvawu : 
kotikkaNakkil paNam parYimuwal ceVyyappattawu ; 
vAkkAlYarkalYEk kavarvawarYkAka viniyokikkappatavirunwa kotikkaNakkAnYa rUpAy mawipputEya vetti - celE ulYlYitta ilavacap poVrulYkalY parYimuwal ceVyyappattanYa ; 
AlYum awimuka , wimuka AkiyavarYrYEc cernwa vetpAlYarkalY Akiyorukku coVnwamAnYa marYrYum neVrukkamAnYavarkalYukkuw coVnwamAnYa itafkalYil roVkkap paNam parYimuwal ceVyyappattawu ulYlYitta kAraNafkalYAl aravakkurYicciyil werwal veVlYippatEyAkavum , niyAyamAkavum natEpeVrYAwu eVnYa werwal ANEyam karuwukirYawu . 
iwEk karuwwil koVNtu aravakkurYicci woVkuwiyil me 16Am wewi natEpeVrYuvawAka arYivikkappatta werwal me 23Am wewikku walYlYivEkkappatukirYawu . 
awwoVkuwikkAnYa vAkku eVNNikkE me 25Am wewi natEpeVrYum eVnYrYu ceVywikkurYippil werwal ANEyam kUrYiyulYlYawu . 
aravakkurYicci woVkuwiyil awimuka cArpil munYnYAlY amEccar ceVnwil pAlAjiyum wimuka cArpil ke.ci.palYYanYicAmiyum pottiyitukinYrYanYar . 
iwil awimuka AwaravAlYarAnYa anYpunAwanYukkuc coVnwamAnYa vIttil rU. 4.77 koti alYavukku roVkkawwE varumAnYa variw wurYEyinYar parYimuwal ceVywanYar . 
rU. 1.30 koti mawippilAnYa vetti , celE ulYlYitta poVrulYkalYum parYimuwal ceVyyappattanYa . 
iwepola , wimuka vetpAlYar ke.ci.palYYanYicAmi , avarawu makanY ke.ci.pi.civarAmanY Akiyorukku ceVnYnYE , karUr Akiya itafkalYil ulYlYa vItukalYil rU. 1.98 koti alYavukku roVkkam parYimuwal ceVyyappattawu . 
iwEw woVtarnwu moVwwam elYYu , muwal wakaval arYikkEkalY pawivu ceVyyappattu werwal ANEya uwwaravinYpati vicAraNE natawwappattu varukirYawu . 
inwa vivakArawwil AlYum awimuka , wimuka cArpil parasparam kurYrYamcAttu eVlYYuppappattu , roVkkam parYimuwal ceVyyappattawu kurYiwwu cipiE vicAraNEkku uwwaravita veNtum eVnYrYu werwal ANEyawwitam pukAr manYukkalY alYikkappattanYa . 
inwa nilEyil aravakkurYicci werwal wewi walYlYivEkkappattulYlYawu . makalYir hAkki : inwiyAvukku 2-Avawu wolvi - 
ifkilAnwinY mArlo nakaril natEpeVrYrYa 5 pottikalY koVNta makalYir hAkkiw woVtarinY 2-Avawu Attawwil inwiya aNi 1-2 eVnYrYa kol kaNakkil pirittanYitam wolvi kaNtawu . 
erYkeVnYave muwal Attawwil wolvi kaNtirunwa inwiya aNi , ippowu atuwwa Attawwilum worYrYu pinYnYatEvEc canwiwwirukkirYawu . 
ivviru aNikalY itEyilAnYa 3-Avawu Attam FAyirYrYukkilYYamE natEpeVrYukirYawu . 
2-Avawu Attawwukkup pirYaku peciya inwiya aNiyinY walEmEp payirYciyAlYar nIl hAvkut , inwiya vIrAfkanYEkalYinY Attawwil nalla munYnYerYrYam erYpattulYlYawu . 
inwiya vIrAfkanYEkalY oVrufkiNEnwu vilYEyAtiyawotu , katanwa Attawwil ceVywa wavarYukalYE inwa Attawwil cari ceVywanYar ' eVnYrYAr . varYatciyAl vAtum makArARtira makkalYukku rU. 10 latcam niwiyuwavi valYYafkiya ' hAkki inwiyA ' 
puwuteVlli , 
katanwa 100 ANtukalYil illAwa alYavukku makArARtira mAnilam varYatciyAl waviwwu varukirYawu . 
kurYippAka , marawvAtA , viwarpA ulYlYitta pala itafkalYil kutinIr wattuppAtu vAtti varukirYawu . 
innilEyil , varYatciyAl pAwikkappatta makkalYukku uwavikkaram nIttum vakEyil ' hAkki inwiyA ' amEppu rU. 10 latcam niwiyuwavi valYYafkiyiruppawu palarawu pArAttEyum peVrYrYulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAnYa niwiyE ' hAkki inwiyA ' amEppinY poVwucceVyalAlYar mummawu muswAk akamawu , walEmE nirvAka awikAri eVlinYA nArmanY Akiyor mAnila muwalvar wevenwira patnYAvisitam valYYafkinYar . 25 cawavIwa vAkkuccAvatikalYil veVp kemarAkkalY illE . 
mA.cuppiramaNiyanY kurYrYaccAttu - 
wi inwu 
cEwAppettE woVkuwi wimuka vetpAlYar mA.cuppiramaNiyanY , woVkuwikku utpatta palverYu vAkkuccAvatikalYukku ceVnYrYu pArvEyittAr . 
merYku cEwAppettE jAnYs cAlEyil ulYlYa ceVnYnYE ANkalY melnilEp palYlYiyil vAkkuppawivE pArvEyitta pinYnYar , avar niruparkalYitam kUrYiyawAvawu , ‘ ‘ cEwAppettE woVkuwikku utpatta vAkkuccAvatikalYE pArvEyittu varukirYenY . 
25 cawavIwa vAkkuccAvatikalYil veVp kemarAkkalY poVruwwAmal ulYlYanYar . 
cila vAkkuccAvatikalYil powiya alYavil itavacawi illAmal neVrukkatiyAka irukkirYawu . 
AnYAlum , 5 ANtukalYukku oVrumurYE werwal eVnYpawAl anYEwwu inYnYalkalYEyum wANti makkalY ArvamAka vAkkalYiwwu varukinYrYanYar ’’ eVnYrYAr . vAyppE wakkavEkkum munYEppil teVlli aNi iwuvarE 11 AttafkalYil vilYEyAti 6 veVrYrYiyutanY 12 pulYlYikalY peVrYrYirukkum teVlli torteVvils aNi , ‘ pilYe-Ap ’ curYrYu vAyppE wakkavEkka eVFciya 3 AttafkalYilum veVrYrYi peVrYa veNtiyawu avaciyamAkum . 
awe camayam inYrYEya Attawwil worYrYAlum teVlli aNiyinY vAyppu oVreyatiyAka mutinwu vitAwu . 
AnYAl ranYrettE uyarwwa veNtiya neVrukkati uruvAkum . 
awarYku valYYikoVtukkAmal Atuvawil teVlli vIrarkalY munYEppu kAttuvArkalY . 
munwEya Attawwil mumpEyitam 80 ranYkalY viwwiyAcawwil worYrYAlum eVlYYucci peVrYum uwvekawwutanY kANappatukirYArkalY . 
12 AttafkalYil vilYEyAti 9-l worYrYu erYkanYave atuwwa curYrYu vAyppE parYikoVtuwwuvitta tonYi walEmEyilAnYa punYe aNiyE poVrYuwwavarE , inYi eVwiraNikalYinY vAyppE mutinwavarE cIrkulEkka veNtum eVnYpawe oVre ilakkAka irukkum . 
AnYAl punYe aNiyil pettifkil rahAnYevE ( 6 arEcawam ulYpata 419 ranY ) wavira marYrYavarkalYinY Attam cIrAka illE . 
teVlli aNi panwu vIccil valuvAka iruppawAl punYe vIrarkalYukku katum cavAl kAwwirukkirYawu . 
ivviru aNikalYum erYkanYave canwiwwa Attawwil punYe aNi 7 vikkeVt viwwiyAcawwil veVrYrYi peVrYrYirunwawu kurYippitawwakkawu . nAttil 33 koti makkalY varYatciyAl pAwippu . 
cuprIm korttil mawwiya aracu wakaval . 
puwuteVlli , 
inwiyAvinY moVwwa makkalYwoVkEyil kAlvAcikku mel 33 koti makkalY varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar eVnYrYu mawwiya aracu cuprIm korttil wakaval weVriviwwu ulYlYawu . 
nAttil varYatciyinYAl 33 koti makkalY kutinIr parYrYAkkurYE marYrYum vivacAya neVrukkatiyE eVwirkoVNtu ulYlYanYar . 
varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta mAnilafkalYukku mawwiya aracinY peritar niwiyilirunwu niwi valYYafkappattu varukirYawu eVnYrYu mawwiya aracu kUrYiyulYlYawu . 
kUtuwal coVlicittar jeVnYaral pi.eVs.naracimkA cuprIm korttil arYikkEyE wAkkal ceVywAr . 
arYikkEyil 10 mAnilafkalY itampeVrYrYulYlYawu . 
mAnilafkalYukku katanwa wifkatkilYYamE rU. 7,321 koti valYYafkappattu ulYlYawu . 
immAwa woVtakkawwil erYkanYave rU. 12,230 koti valYYafkappattu ulYlYawu . 
varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta mAnilafkalYil kirAmapurYa velEvAyppu wittam mUlam cumAr 21 latcawwirYku melAnYa kutumpawwinYarukku 100 nAtkalYukku mel velEvAyppu valYYafkappattu ulYlYawu . 
varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta makkalYinY eVNNikkEyAnYawu awikamAka irukkum , pIkAr marYrYum ariyAnYA mAnilawwil malYYE parYrYAkkurYE irunwa powilum varYatci nilEyAnYawu arYivikkappatavillE . 
cuprIm korttil aracu wAkkal ceVywulYlYa arYikkEyil 254 mAvattafkalYil 2.55 latcam kirAmafkalY varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
cuvAraciyamAka ivvalYYakkil arYikkEyil kujarAw mAnilam itampeVrYavillE . 
kujarAw mAnilawwil cumAr 637-kkum merYpatta kirAmafkalYil waNNIr parYrYAkkurYE iruppawE munwEya vicAraNEyil ammAnila aracu oVwwukkoVNta nilEyil mawwiya aracinY arYikkEyil kujarAw mAnilam itampeVrYavillE . 
varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta mAnilafkalY pattiyalil kujarAw mAnilam arYikkEyil itampeVrYAwa vivakArawwE kEyil eVtuwwuk koVNta cuprIm korttu “ kujarAw mAnilawwirYku mattum wanYippatta murYEyil natawwappatuvawu enY ” eVnYrYu mawwiya aracukku kelYvi eVlYYuppi ulYlYawu . 
iwarYku pawilalYiwwa kUtuwal coVlicittar wavarYu natanwuvittawu , ivvivakArawwinY pinY eVwuvum kitEyAwu , kujarAw mAnilam itampeVrYum arYikkEyum alYikkappatum eVnYrYu kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
nAttil nilavum varYatci aracukkalYE cirYappu tefkar reVyil mUlam waNNIrE valYYafkacceVywu ulYlYawu . 
marAttiya mAnilawwil E.pi.eVl. pottikalYEyum itamArYrYam ceVywu ulYlYawu . 
makkalYukku kutinIr valYYafkum paNiyinYE polIcAre ceVyyum nilEyum erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
uwwarapirawecam mAnilawwil awikapatcamAka 9.88 koti makkalY varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
uwwarapirawecam mAnilawwil paruvamalYYE kurYE kAraNamAka 50 mAvattafkalYil varYatci erYpattu ulYlYawu . 
varYatci piraccanYEyE camAlYikka aracu anYEwwu natavatikkEkalYEyum eVtuwwu varukirYawu eVnYrYum kUtuwal mItpu marYrYum mempAttu paNikkAnYa niwi valYYafkappatum eVnYrYum mawwiya aracu weVriviwwu ulYlYawu . 
varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta pakuwikalY weciya peritarAka , peritar melANmE cattawwinY kIlYY koVNtu varappattu ulYlYawu . 
mawwiya aracu varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta mAnilafkalYukku kUtuwal niwiyE valYYafkum . 
cuvarAj apiyAnY woVNtu nirYuvanYam woVtuwwu ulYlYa poVwunala valYYakkE cuprIm korttu vicAriwwu varukirYawu . 
uwwarapirawecam , karnAtakA , mawwiyapirawecam , Anwirapirawecam , weVlufkAnYA , marAttiyam , kujarAw , oVticA , jArkaNt , pIkAr , ariyAnYA marYrYum cawwiRkAr varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYu poVwunala manYuvil weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
mAnilafkalY , makAwmA kAnwi weciya Uraka velEvAyppu urYuwiw wittam marYrYum uNavu pAwukAppu cattawwE pinYparYrYavillE eVnYrYum weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
melum mawwiya aracinY varYatci kEyetum pinYparYrYappatavillE eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
pIkAr , ariyAnYA Akiya mAnilafkalYil peVywa malYYE wirupwiyAnYawu eVnYrYu ammAnila aracukkalY weVriviwwu ulYlYanYar . 
varYatci eVnYrYu arYivikkavillE... ... 
ivvivakArawwil mawwiya aracinY kEkalY kattappattu ulYlYawu eVnYrYu kUrYiya naracimkA , varYatci arYivikkum vivakArawwil mAnila aracukkalY kattAyappatuwwappatAwu eVnYrYum kurYippittu ulYlYAr . 
mawwiya aracu alYiwwu ulYlYa wakavalil varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappatta 10 mAnilafkalYil uwwarapirawecam , mawwiyapirawecam , marAttiyam , jArkaNt marYrYum karnAtakA muwal 5 itafkalYE pitiwwu ulYlYawu . 
uwwarapirawecam mAnilawwil ulYlYa moVwwa 75 mAvattafkalYil 50 mAvattafkalYil varYatci erYpattu 9.9 koti makkalY pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar . 
mawwiyapirawecam mAnilawwil 46 mAvattafkalYil varYatci erYpattu 4.0 koti makkalY pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar . 
marAttiyawwil moVwwam ulYlYa 36 mAvattafkalYil 21 mAvattafkalY varYatciyinYAl pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
3.7 koti makkalY pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar . 
jArkaNt mAnilawwil ulYlYa moVwwa 24 mAvattafkalYil 22 mAvattafkalYil varYatci erYpattu 3.2 koti makkalY pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar . 
karnAtakAvil ulYlYa 30 mAvattafkalYil 27 mAvattafkalYil varYatci erYpattu 3.1 koti makkalY pAwikkappattu ulYlYanYar eVnYrYu weVrivikkappattu ulYlYawu . 234 woVkuwikalYilum aNNA wi.mu.ka. veVrYrYi urYuwi : 
anYiwA kuppucAmi peccu 
wirucci , 
me 10– 
wamilYYakawwE amEwi pUfkAvAka mArYrYiyavar jeVyalaliwA . 
cattamanYrYa werwalil 234 woVkuwikalYilum aNNA wi.mu.ka. veVrYrYi peVrYrYu ammA mINtum muwalamEccarAvawu urYuwi eVnYrYu wirucciyil nAttuppurYa pAtaki anYiwA kuppucAmi pecinYAr . 
wirucci kilYYakku woVkuwikku utpatta ke.ke.nakar pakuwiyil aNNA wi.mu.ka , vetpAlYar veVllamaNti eVnY.natarAjanYE Awariwwu nAttuppurYa pAtaki anYiwA kuppucAmi vIwi vIwiyAka wirYanwa jIppil ceVnYrYu muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY cAwanYEkalYE pattiyalittu piraccAram ceVywAr . 
appowu avar peciyawAvawu : 
muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA veVlYiyittulYlYa werwal arYikkEyil makalYirkalYukku skUtti vAfka mAnYiyam , wAlikku 8 kirAm wafkam , makapperYukku 18Ayiram rupAy , vivacAyakatanY , mANavar kalvi katanY rawwu eVnYa eVNNarYrYa wittafkalYE jeVyalaliwA arYiviwwulYlYAr . 
2006 muwal 2011 varE natanwa wi.mu.ka , Atciyil oVvvoVru mAvattawwEyum kurYunila manYnYarkalY pol anwa anwa mAvattawwE cernwa wi.mu.kavinYar wafkalY kattupAttukkulY vEwwirunwanYar . 
avarkalYE mIrYi anwa mAvattawwil eVwuvum natakkAwa pati ravutiwwanYam ceVywanYar . 
poVwumakkalY wafkalY coVnwa nilawwE virYka veNti vanwAl kUta ivarkalYE kettuwwAnY virYka mutiyum eVnYrYa arAjaka Atci natawwinYar . 
ivarYrYukku murYrYupulYlYi vEwwu wamilYYakawwE amEwi pUfkAvAka mArYrYiyavar muwalvar jeVyalaliwA . 
234 woVkuwikalYilum aNNA wi.mu.ka. veVrYrYi peVrYrYu ammA mINtum muwalamEccarAvawu urYuwi . 
ilafkEyil wamilYYarkalY koVwwu koVwwAka koVlYlYapatta powu 3 maNi neram uNNAvirawa nAtakam pottu wurokam ceVywa karuNAniwi warYpowu inwa cattamanYrYa werwalEyoVtti makkalYitam anYuwApam peVrYa wanYakku utampu cariyillE eVnYrYu oVru nAtakam pottu maruwwuvamanYEyil atmittAka wittamittu ulYlYawAka oVru wakaval veVlYiyAki ulYlYawu . 
Akave poVwumakkalY avarawu nAtakawwE nampa veNtAm . 
kuRpu ifku pecum powu mawuvilakku kurYiwwu pecukirYAr . 
namawu aNtE mAnilamAnYa karnAtakAvil kAfkiras Atci wAnY natakkirYawu . 
afku erAlYamAnYa peVNkalYum mawuvukku atimE Aki vittanYar . 
kAfkiras katciyE cernwa kuRpu karnAtakAvil mawuvilakkE muwalil amal patuwwa wayArA ? 
ivarkalY mAnilawwirYku mAnilam oVvvoVnYrYu peci makkalYE emArYrYupavarkalY . 
kAnwi , neru , kAmarAjar , irAjAji ulYlYittor valYarwwa kAfkiras ippo kuRpu , nakmA kEyil cikki cinYnYApinYnYamAkirYawu . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . 
piraccArawwil pakuwi kalYYaka ceVyalAlYar veVllamaNti ji.caNmukam , poVwukkulYYu urYuppinYar cAwwUr rAmalifkam , eVm.ji.Ar.manYrYa walEvar cureR kupwA , pakuwi kalYYaka poVrulYAlYar cinwE viji , warkA kAjA utpata palar kalanwu koVNtanYar . oVlimpik vIrarkalYukku rohiw vAlYYwwu 
- wi inwu 
oVlimpik pottiyil pafkerYkavulYlYa inwiya vIrarkalYukku kirikkeVt vIrar rohiw carmA vAlYYwwu weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
carvaweca vilYEyAttu eVkspo punYe nakaril nerYrYu woVtafkivEkkappattawu . 
innikalYYcciyil peciya rohiw carmA , oVlimpik pottiyil pafkerYkum inwiya vilYEyAttu vIrarkalY marYrYum vIrAfkanYEkalYukku vAlYYwwu weVriviwwAr . 
melum oVlimpikkil pawakkam veVlla vAlYYwwu weVriviwwu kEyeVlYYuwwitta kirikkeVt pet oVnYrYE pirapala wuppAkki cutum vIrarAnYa kakanY nArafkukku rohiw carmA valYYafkinYAr . varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwiyil coVkucu kAril payaNamA ? 
eVtiyUrappAvukku eVwirAka puwiya carccE 
peVfkalYUru , varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwiyil coVkucu kAril payaNam ceVyvawA ? eVnYrYu eVtiyUrappAvukku eVwirAka eVlYYunwulYlYa puwiya carccE paraparappE erYpatuwwi ulYlYawu . 
rU. 1.15 kotiyil coVkucu kAr 
karnAtaka mAnila pArawIyajanYawA walEvarAka eVtiyUrappA katanwa 14–n wewi pawavi erYrYAr . 
avarukku munYnYAlY manwiriyum avarawu AwaravAlYarumAnYa murukeR nirAnYi rU. 1.15 koti mawippilAnYa coVkucu kArE paricalYiwwAr . 
inwa kAril mAnilam mulYYuvawum eVtiyUrappA curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu katci valYarcci paNikalYil ItupatuvAr eVnYrYum arYivikkappattawu . 
awotu karnAtakawwil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil varukirYa 27–nwewi muwal me 1–n wewi varE avar curYrYuppayaNam ceVywu pAwikkappatta makkalYE neril canwippAr eVnYrYum arYivikkappattu irunwawu . 
puwiya carccE 
inwa nilEyil varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil eVtiyUrappA coVkucu kAril payaNam ceVyvawA ? eVnYrYu puwiya carccE eVlYYunwu ulYlYawu . 
iwuparYrYi eVtiyUrappA nerYrYu pawil alYiwwu kUrYiyawAvawu : 
“ katci paNiyArYrYuvawarYkAka inwa kArE eVnYakku murukeR nirAnYi valYYafki ulYlYAr . 
nAnY katci paNikkAka mAnilam mulYYuvawum curYrYuppayaNam ceVyya ulYlYenY . 
awarYku inwa kAr vacawiyAka irukkum eVnYrYu nirAnYi kUrYinYAr . 
eVnYawu katci walEvar pawavikkAlam ( 2 ANtukalY ) mutinwawum avar mINtum inwa kArE wirumpa peVrYrYukkoVlYvAr . 
melum varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwiyil nAnY curYrYuppayaNam ceVyyumpowu inwa coVkucu kArE nAnY payanYpatuwwamAttenY ” ivvArYu eVtiyUrappA kUrYinYAr . 
katanYukku vAfkiya kAr 
varYatci pAwiwwa pakuwiyil coVkucu kAril payaNam ceVyvawu cariyA ? eVnYrYu kelYvi eVlYYunwulYlYawe eVnYrYu eVtiyUrappAvitam kettapowu “ kArinY vilEyEyum varYatciyEyum oVppitAwIrkalY ” eVnYrYAr . 
appowu arukil irunwa murukeR nirAnYi “ inwa kAr eVtiyUrappAvukku paricAka valYYafkappatavillE eVnYrYAr .

E.pi.eVl. pottikalYE verYu mAnilafkalYil natawwa veNtum : 
pArawIyajanYawA mumpE , 
makArARtirAvil varYatciyAnYa cUlYYnilE woVtarum nilEyil natEpeVrYa wittamitappattu ulYlYa E.pi.eVl. pottikalYE verYu mAnilafkalYil natawwa veNtum eVnYa mumpE pArawIyajanYawA katciyinY ceVyalAlYar vivekAnYanwA kupwA valiyurYuwwiyulYlYAr . 
iwu parYrYi pi.ci.ci.E. walEvar RaRAf manYokarukku avar eVlYYuwiyulYlYa katiwawwil , waram mikka kirikkeVt mEwAnYam oVnYrYirYku oVru murYE upayokikka kurYEnwawu 80 Ayiram littar muwal oVru latcam littar varEyilAnYa nIr wevEppatum . 
purYkalY valYarcciyE mempatuwwita marYrYum cewamatEnwa pakuwikalYE cIr ceVyya eVnYa vAram oVnYrYirYku 2l irunwu 3 murYE nIr upayokikkappatum . 
awanYAl 1 latcawwu 60 Ayiram littarilirunwu 3 latcam littar varE oVru vArawwirYku nIr wevEppatum eVnYa anwa arYikkEyil avar weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
makArARtirAvinY mumpE , punYe marYrYum nAkpUr Akiya nakarafkalYil epral 9n wewiyilirunwu me 29n wewi varE 19 E.pi.eVl. pottikalY natakka ulYlYanYa . 
inwa woVtarinY irYuwi potti vAnYkate mEwAnYawwil me 29n wewi natEpeVrYa ulYlYawu . 
iwuparYrYi pArawIya janYawA walEvar kUrYumpoVlYYuwu , 
veVppam marYrYum kArYrYu vIcum cUlYYalil awika nIr wevEppatum . 
kulYir nirYEnwa cUlYYalil kurYEvAka nIr wevEppatum . 
inwa 19 pottikalYukkum mEwAnYawwE mempatuwwita 70 latcam littarukkum kUtuwalAnYa nIr wevEppatum eVnYa kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
avar woVtarnwu kUrYumpoVlYYuwu , 
pi.ci.ci.E.yinY walEvar cArnwa inwa mAnilam AnYawu katanwa oVru nUrYrYANtil awika varYtciyAl katumEyAka pAwikkappattulYlYawu .

atuwwatuwwa kurYEnwa malYYE poVlYYivinYAl nilawwil nIrmattam kurYEnwulYlYawu .

pUw cilipputanY paNam pattuvAtA ceVywa wi.mu.ka.vinYar mIwu uriya natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYu wamilYYaka walEmE werwal awikAriyitam a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar manYu alYiwwanYar . 
cattam-oVlYYufku piraccinYE ceVnYnYE AyiramvilYakku woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. muwanYmE mukavar ci.wirumArYanY , wamilYYaka walEmE werwal awikAri rAjeR lakkAnYiyitam alYiwwulYlYa manYuvil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : - 
AyiramvilYakku woVkuwiyil vAkkuppawivinYpowu , wi.mu.ka.vinYar ravutikalYE evi vittu cattam - oVlYYufku piraccinYEyE erYpatuwwavum , vAkkuccAvatikalYE kEpparYrYavum wittamittulYlYanYar eVnYrYu nAnY erYkanYave wafkalYitam manYu alYiwwulYlYenY . 
melum pawarYrYamAnYa vAkkuccAvatikalY eVvE eVnYpawu kurYiwwum , afku kUtuwal pAwukAppu erYpatuwwa veNtum eVnYpawu kurYiwwum manYu alYiwwirunwenY . 
natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum 
inwa nilEyil katanwa 10-nwewi mAlE 6 maNi alYavil 113-vawu tivicanYE cernwa wi.mu.ka.vinYar cattavirowamAka pUw cilippukalYutanY paNawwE vAkkAlYarkalYukku vinYiyokiwwulYlYanYar . 
iwukurYiwwu eVfkalYukku weVriyavanwawum kavunYcilar cAnwi pAskar , vArtu ceVyalAlYar jeVyapAl marYrYum a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar afku ceVnYrYapowu pUw cilippukalYE vinYiyokiwwavarkalYEyum , paNam koVtuwwavarkalYEyum pitiwwu polIcil oVppatEwwom . 
iwukurYiwwu werwal awikAriyitam pukAr alYikkappattawu . 
iwEw woVtarnwu polIcAr valYYakkuppawivu ceVywulYlYanYar . 
inwa campavawwil a.wi.mu.ka kavunYcilar wAkkappattAr . 
iwu woVtarpAka wanYiyAka valYYakkuppawivu ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
cattacapE werwalil worYrYu vituvom eVnYrYa payawwil wi.mu.ka.vinYar iwuponYrYa ceVyalkalYil ItupattulYlYanYar . 
avarkalY mIwu uriya natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYu kettukkoVlYkirYom . 
ivvArYu anwa manYuvil kUrYappattulYlYawu . yUro koppE : peVljiyam keptanY vilakal - 
yUro koppE kAlpanwu pottiyilirunwu peVljiyam keptanY vinYceVnYt kampeVnYi kAyam kAraNamAka vilakiyulYlYAr . 
iwu anwa aNikku peVrum pinYnYatEvE erYpatuwwiyulYlYawu . 
iwu woVtarpAka vinYceVnYt wanYawu mukanUl pakkawwil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
yUro koppEyil nAnY vilYEyAtavillE . 
eVnYakku awu cokamAnYa ceVywiyAkum eVnYa kurYippittulYlYAr . 
kilYap pottiyil mAnYceVstar citti aNikkAka vilYEyAti varum vinYceVnYt , inwa cIcanYil kAyam kAraNamAka peVrumpAlAnYa nAlYkalY oyvileye irunwAr . 
vinYceVnYt vilakiyiruppawAl yUro koppE pottiyil pafkerYkum peVljiyam aNikku ItanY hasArtu keptanYAka ceVyalpatuvAr eVnYa eVwirpArkkappatukirYawu . 
katanwa 13 ANtukalYAka carvaweca pottikalYil vilYEyAti varum vinYceVnYt , awil 1,045 nAlYkalY kAyam kAraNamAka maruwwuvamanYEyil cikiccE peVrYrYawAka peVljiyam pawwirikE oVnYrYu weVriviwwulYlYawu . ceVnYnYE veVlYlYawwirYku kAraNam eVnYnYa ? 
veVlYlYa nIril inYnYum cikki wavikkum pakuwikalY 
ceVnYnYE , 
ceVnYnYEyil katanwa vAram peVywa kanYamalYYEyAl ceVnYnYEyinY palaverYu pakuwikalY veVlYlYawwil mUlYYkiyawu . 
mAnakarame veVlYlYak kAtAka mArYip ponYawu . 
inwa katum veVlYlYa pAwippirYku ceVmparappAkkam eriyilirunwu wirYanwuvitappatta awikappatiyAnYa nIr wAnY eVnYak kurYrYam cAttappatukirYawu . 
kutiyiruppukalYukkulY nIr pukunwawAl , patakukalY mUlam makkalY pAwukAppAnYa itafkalYukku alYYEwwuc ceVllappattanYar . 
vIttil irunwa vIttu upayokap poVrutkalY , mukkiya AvaNafkalY , vAkanYafkalY ulYlYitta anYEwwup poVrutkalYum veVlYlYa nIril UrYi vINAkinYa . 
ceVnYnYEyinY peVruvAriyAnYa pakuwikalY katalmattawwilirunwu cumAr 25 muwal 35 ati varEyilAnYa uyarawwil irukkinYrYanYa . 
wiruvallikkeNi 30 ati uyarawwilum , ceVnYtral rayil nilEyam 18 ati uyarawwilum , puracEvAkkam 23 ati uyarawwilum irukkinYrYanYa . 
iwepol , velYacceriyilulYlYa erikkuw weVrYkup pakuwi katalmattawwilirunwu veVrYum 14 ati uyarame irukkirYawu . 
koVttivAkkawwilulYlYa kaNNaki nakar katalmattawwileye ( 0 ati ) irukkirYawu . 
inwa nila amEppil , ceVmparampAkkam eriyilirunwu wirYanwu vitappatukinYrYa nIrAnYawu atEyArYrYil payaNam ceVyya veNtum . 
ArYrYinY valYYi cirYiwAka irunwAlum , woVtarcciyAka irunwAl mattume inwa nIrAnYawu murYEppati katalEc ceVnYrYu atEyum . 
AnYAl , ceVmparampAkkawwilirunwu veVlYiyerYum nIrAnYawu kurompettEkku merYke ceVnYnYE veVlYivattac cAlEyE atEkEyil , nilamattam katal mattawwilirunwu 35 ati eVnYnYum alYavukkuw wAlYYnwu vanwuvitukirYawu . 
awanYEw woVtarnwu mInYampAkkam vimAnYa nilEya otupAwEyE oVttiya atEyArYrYup patukE katal mattawwilirunwu veVrYum 12 ati eVnYrYa wAlYYnilEyE atEnwu vitukirYawu . 
afkirunwu katalEc cerumvarE atEyArYu woVtarcciyAkac carinwu irYafkuvawillE . 
atuwwatuwwu varum atEyArYrYinY patukEkalY 10 muwal 20 ativarE uyarvawum pinYpu carivawumAkave irukkirYawu . 
iwanYAl , wafkuwatEyinYrYi ceVlla veNtiya veVlYlYa nIr , pala itafkalYil wefkukirYawu . 
pinYnYar appakuwikalYE nirYEwwa pinYnYare atuwwa itawwirYku nakarkirYawu . 
iwwakEya ArYrYup patukEyAl wAnY witIreVnYrYu erYpatta mikuveVlYlYam valuvillAwa karEppakuwiyE mIrYi , UrukkulY pukunwuvittawu . 
erYkanYave erYrYawwAlYYvAnYa ArYrYuppatukE ulYlYa nilEyil , nIr pAya veNtiya itafkalYil AkkiramippukalYum , atEppukalYum awikamAka vittawu . 
iwanYAl waNNIr pokku melum watEpattawu . 
eVnYave palYlYamAnYa pakuwikalYil wefkiya nIrAnYawu nirampi valYYiya melum kAlam eVtuwwuk koVNtawu . 
iwanYAleye ceVnYnYE nakar atEyArYrYu veVlYlYawwAl inwa peVrum pAwippukalYEc canwiwwulYlYawu . 
awikArikalY ceVywa Ayvil ceVnYnYEyil 859 itafkalYil veVlYlYam cUlYYnwawu kaNtupitikkap pattawu . 
awirRtavacamAka katanwa vAra irYuwiyilirunwu woVtar palawwa malYYE illAwa kAraNawwAl veVlYlYam pAwiwwa pakuwikalYilirunwu waNNIr vatiyaw woVtafkiyawu . 
awu pola atEyArYu , kUvam ArYrYafkarEkalYil upari nIr wirYanwu vitappatuvawu kurYEnwawAlum karEyorap pakuwikalYil veVlYlYam vatinwawu . 
cila pakuwikalYil mAnakarAtci awikArikalY pampu mottArkalY uwaviyutanY waNNIrE akarYrYinYArkalY . 
katanwa 3 nAtkalYil 90 cawavIwa pakuwikalYil veVlYlYam vatinwu vittawu . 
veVlYlYa pAwippu erYpatta 859 pakuwikalYil nerYrYu varE 787 pakuwikalYil veVlYlYam mulYYumEyAka akanYrYu vittawu . 
mIwamulYlYa 72 itafkalY inYnYamum veVlYlYawwil ulYlYawu . 
kurYippAka wAmparam , muticcUrinY purYanakar pakuwikalY , mukalivAkkam , velYacceriyil cila itafkalY vata ceVnYnYEyil ulYlYa cila pakuwikalY inYnYamum veVlYlYam cUlYYnwu nirYkirYawu . 
inwa pakuwikalYil peVrumpAlAnYavarYrYil veVlYlYa nIr vativawarYku uriya vatikAl vacawikalY illE 
weVrukkalYil wefki ulYlYa waNNIrE verYu itawwukku veVtti vitavum valYYi illE . 
eVnYave veVlYlYawwil miwakkum pakuwikalYil ulYlYa waNNIrE mArYrYu valYYikalYil akarYrYa AlocanYE natanwu varukirYawu . 
awanY oVru pakuwiyAka rAtcawa mottArkalY mUlam waNNIrE urYiFci eVtukka mutivu ceVyyappattawu .

vAnYUr ,

kAyawwinYAl veVlYiyerYinYAr 3vawu Aswireliya vIrar mArR meVlpornY , 
E.pi.eVl. pottiyil kifs leVvanY paFcAp aNikkAka vilYEyAti varum Aswireliya kirikkeVt vIrar RAnY mArR muwukil erYpatta kAyawwinYAl wanYawu coVnwa Urukku wirumpukirYAr . 
9vawu E.pi.eVl. kirikkeVt pottikalY inwiyAvinY palverYu nakarafkalYil natanwu varukinYrYanYa . 
innilEyil , kAyawwinYAl mArRinY ilYEya cakowarar mitceVl katanwa FAyirYrYukilYYamE pottiyilirunwu vilakinYAr . 
Aswireliya aNiyinY keptanY stIv smiw maNikkattu kAyawwinYAl nerYrYu pottiyilirunwu vilakinYAr . 
innilEyil , teVst potti vIrarAnYa AswireliyAvinY mArR kAyawwinYAl wanYawu coVnwa Urukku wirumpukirYAr . 
kAyawwinYAl pottiyilirunwu veVlYiyerYum 3vawu Aswireliya vIrar mArR AvAr . 
katanwa epral 19n wewi koVlkawwA nEt rEtars aNikku eVwirAnYa pottiyil kifs leVvanY paFcAp aNi 6 vikkeVttukalY viwwiyAcawwil vIlYYnwawu . 
inwa pottikku pinYnYar itawu kE petsmenYAnYa mArR nilE mocamatEnwawu eVnYa kirikkeVt AswireliyA wanYawu iNEyawalYawwil ( cricket.com.au ) weVriviwwulYlYawu . 
varukirYa jUlE marYrYum Akastil 3 teVst pottikalY koVNta woVtaril vilYEyAtuvawarYkAka Aswireliya kirikkeVt aNi ilafkEkku ceVlkirYawu .

avarawu cakowararAnYa mitceVl marYrYum smiw AswireliyAvukkAka atuwwa mAwam karIpiyanYil natEpeVrYa ulYlYa weVnYnYAppirikkA marYrYum merYku inwiya wIvukalY kalanwu koVlYlYum muwwarappu oVru nAlY potti woVtaril vilYEyAta kUtum eVnYa wakaval weVrivikkinYrYawu . peVriyakulYam aruke kumpakkarE aruvikku nIrvarawwu 
curYrYulA payaNikalY kulYikka anYumawi 
peVriyakulYam aruke kumpakkarE aruviyil nIrvarawwu kANappatukirYawu . 
nINta nAtkalYukku pirYaku curYrYulA payaNikalY kulYikka vanYawwurYEyinYar anYumawi alYiwwanYar . 
kumpakkarE aruvi wenYi mAvattam , peVriyakulYam aruke cumAr 8 kilo mIttar wUrawwil kumpakkarE aruvi ulYlYawu . 
inwa aruvi iyarYkE eVlYYil cUlYYa merYku woVtarcci malEyativAra pakuwiyil amEnwu ulYlYawu . 
inwa aruvikku koVtEkkAnYal malEppakuwiyil malYYE peVyvawanY mUlam nIr varawwu irukkum . 
inwa aruvikku palverYu pakuwiyilirunwu erAlYamAnYa curYrYulA payaNikalY vanwu kulYiwwu ceVlkinYrYanYar . 
katanwa oVru mAwawwirYkum melAka aruvi pakuwi marYrYum koVtEkkAnYal pakuwiyil malYYE illAwawAl aruvikku nIrvarawwu murYrYilumAka kurYEnwuvittawu . 
iwanYAl curYrYulA payaNikalY kulYikka mutiyAwa cUlYYnilE erYpattawu . 
katanwa cila nAtkalYAkave peVriyakulYam pakuwi marYrYum kumpakkarE pakuwiyil malYYE peVywu varukirYawu . 
iwanY kAraNamAka aruvikku nIrvarawwu kANappattawu . 
waNNIr kalafkalAka vanwawAl curYrYulA payaNikalY kulYikka vanYawwurYEyinYar anYumawi alYikkavillE . 
kulYikka anYumawi 
warYpowu aruviyil kulYippawarYku ukanwawAka waNNIr ulYlYawAl curYrYulA payaNikalY kulYikka vanYawwurYEyinYar anYumawi alYiwwulYlYanYar .

iwanYAl curYrYulA payaNikalY makilYYcci atEnwulYlYanYar . eVwwiyoppiyA nAttil kanYamalYYE , veVlYlYam nilaccarivil cikki 41 per pali 
atis apApA ,

iwil afku ulYlYa 5 mAvattafkalY peVrum pAwippukku ulYlYAki ulYlYanYa . 
afku veVlYlYam karEpuraNtotukirYawu . 
voVlEttA–wavro nakarafkalYukku itEyeyAnYa pirawAnYa cAlE marYrYum voVlEttA–citamA nakarkalYE iNEkkum pAlam AkiyavE veVlYlYawwil atiwwucceVllappattanYa . 
nUrYrYukkaNakkAnYa vItukalY nIril mUlYYki ulYlYanYa . 
makkalYinY iyalpu vAlYYkkE peVriwum pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu .

patukAyam atEnwavarkalY anYEvarum mItkappattu , maruwwuvamanYEkalYil cerkkappattu cikiccE peVrYrYu varukinYrYanYar .

pAwikkappatta pakuwikalYil mulYYu vIccil mItpuppaNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . ceVnYnYE , pulYiyanwoppu AttirYEcci kUtam navInYamayamAkkappatum eVnYrYu wiru.vi.ka.nakar woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar vAkkurYuwi alYiwwulYlYAr .

oVru vArawwirYku ilavaca cevE valYYafka pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. mutivu - 
kanYa malYYEyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa ceVnYnYE makkalYukku oVru vAram ilavaca cevE valYYafkappatum eVnYa mawwiya aracu woVlEwwoVtarpu nirYuvanYamAnYa pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
iwuwoVtarpAka ceVywiyAlYarkalYitam peciya mawwiya woVlEwwoVtarpu wurYE amEccar ravicafkar piracAw , malYYEyAl pAwikkappattulYlYa ceVnYnYE makkalYukku , pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. oVru vAram ilavaca cevE valYYafkum eVnYrYAr . 
inwa vacawi inYrYu muwal amalukku varukirYawu eVnYrYAr amEccar . 
erteVl calukE iweponYrYu wanYiyAr woVlEwwoVtarpu nirYuvanYamAnYa erteVl , wanYawu ceVnYnYE vAtikkEyAlYarkalYukku 30 rUpAykku ' tAktEm ' valYYafkappatum eVnYa arYiviwwulYlYawu .

melum , 50 eVm.pi. ilavaca inYtarneVt tettAvum alYiwwulYlYawu .

appowu avar , a.wi.mu.ka. Atciyil koVNtu varappatta ammA uNavakam , ammA marunwakam , muwiyor , viwavE uwavi woVkE , minYipas vacawi , camuwAya nalakkUtam ulYlYittavEkalY kurYiwwu poVwumakkalYitam eVtuwwu kUrYi vAkku cekariwwAr . 
wittafkalY nirYEverYrYappatum

108-vawu vArtu eVm.eVm.ti.e. kAlanYi aracu melnilEppalYlYi mANavarkalYinY nalanY karuwi rU. 72 latcam ceVlavil kUtuwal vakupparYEkalY kattiyawu ulYlYittavEkalY kurYiwwu poVwumakkalYitam eVtuwwu kUrYinYAr .
