malYYE kottum , kulYirkAlafkalYil mANava , mANaviyarinY utalnalawwE pAwukAkkum vakEyil anYEvarukkum walA oVru kampalYic cattEyum valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
* AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa mANAkkarkalYukkAka , peVrampalUr mAvattawwil iraNtu vituwikalY , puwukkottE , waFcAvUr , mawurE , velUr , koyampuwwUr , wiruccirAppalYlYi , wiruneVlveli marYrYum ceVnYnYE Akiya 8 mAvattafkalYil walA oVnYrYu vIwam 8 vituwikalY eVnYa moVwwam 10 kallUri vituwikalY wuvafkappattulYlYanYa . 
* AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nala vituwikalY marYrYum aracu palYYafkutiyinYa uNtiurYEvitap palYlYikalYil payanYpAttil ulYlYa kulYYal vilYakku , minYvicirYi marYrYum waNNIrk kulYYAy AkiyavarYrYinYE parAmarippawarYkAka 2.47 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , parAmarippu paNikalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * velE vAyppu aluvalakawwil pawivu ceVywulYlYa , 16 mAvattafkalYEc cernwa 906 palYYafkutiyinYa pi.eVt. pattawArikalYukku avarkalY Aciriyar wakuwiw wervil wercci peVrYa valYYivakE ceVyyum vakEyil mAnilak kalviyiyal ArAycci nirYuvanYam mUlam payirYci alYippawarYkAnYa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattu varukirYawu * 160 palYYafkutiyinYar uNti urYEvitap palYlYikalYukkum , 100 AwiwirAvitar nala palYlYikalYukkum , AkamoVwwam 260 palYlYikalYil 260 nIrAvi koVwikalanYkalY valYYafkuvawarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * 1,314 AwiwirAvitar nala vituwikalYil wafkip payilum 98,039 mANava / mANaviyarukku eVvarcilvar wattu marYrYum tamlYar valYYafka natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * ceVnYnYE , kAFcipuram , wiruvalYlYur , koyampuwwUr marYrYum wirucci mAvattafkalYil paNipuriyum makalYirukkAnYa puwiya vituwikalY wuvafka natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * 5 AwiwirAvitar / palYYafkutiyinYar uNtiurYEvita uyarnilEp palYlYikalY , melnilEppalYlYikalYAka nilE uyarwwa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * 15 AwiwirAvitar / palYYafkutiyinYar uNtiurYEvita natunilEp palYlYikalY , uyarnilEp palYlYikalYAka nilE uyarwwa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa * nIlakiri mAvattawwil ulYlYa 32,873 palYYafkutiyinYarkalY **lYuayacava **UtayalYalYa **cutitia amEkka natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYawu . 
3. curYrYuccUlYYal marYrYum vanYawwurYE * vanYa vilafkukalYAl erYpatum uyir / payir / utamEkalY cewafkalYukkAka valYYafkappatum ilYYappIttuw woVkE uyarwwi valYYafkappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
* wekkumarafkalY valYarkkum wittawwinY kIlYY , 2011-12 ANtu muwal 2014-15 ANtu varE 14,335 heVkter parappalYavil wekku maraw wottafkalY erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
* wamilYYnAttinY uyirppanYmEyEp pAwukAkkavum , peVrumalYavilAnYa pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinYE ceVyalpatuwwitavum , witta melANmE alaku aluvalakawwirYkAnYa puwiya kattatam nanYmafkalam kAppukAtu pakuwiyil rU. 6.90 koti ceVlavil kattappattulYlYawu . 
* wamilYYnAtu vanYawwurYEyil vanYavar , vanYakkAppAlYar , vanYakkAvalar ponYrYa pawavikalYil nerati niyamanYawwirYku eVnYa erYpatum kAlip paNiyitafkalYE nirappita wamilYYnAtu vanYaccIrutEppaNiyAlYar wervu kulYYumam eVnYrYa amEppu erYpatuwwappattu anwa amEppinYAl paNiyAlYarkalY wervu paNi natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYawu . 
* wamilYYnAtu vanYaw wottak kalYYakawwinY paNikalY melum cirYakkum vakEyil , 4,500 eVkter parappalYavil , marakkUlYY wottafkalYum , 800 eVkter parappil uyar vilYEccal oVttu munwiri kanYrYukalYum natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
* wamilYYnAtu weyilE wottak kalYYakawwil paNipuriyum woVlYYilAlYarkalY payanYpeVrYum vaNNam , wevAlYA , pANtiyAr , kunYnYUr , ceranYkotu marYrYum natuvattam kottawwil cAlE vacawi , kutinIr vacawi , kutiyiruppu pakuwikalYE mempatuwwuwal ponYrYa paNikalY ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYanYa . * mAnilawwil vanYa uyirinYafkalY awikamAka vAlYYum pakuwikalYE iNEwwu , puwiya vanYa uyirinYa caraNAlayafkalY erYpatuwwa mutivu ceVywu , awanYpati , warmapuri , kiruRNakiri mAvattafkalYil kAveri vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiruneVlveli mAvattawwil kafkEkoVNtAnY pulYlYimAnY caraNAlayamum , waFcAvUr marYrYum wiruvArUr mAvattafkalYil , kotiyakkarE vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiNtukkal , wenYi mAvattafkalYil , koVtEkkAnYal vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . * vanYawwurYEyil paNipuriyum vanYappaNiyAlYarkalYukku kAvalwurYE paNiyAlYarkalYukku iNEyAka cIrutEppati , calavEppati marYrYum itarpati AkiyavarYrYE valYYafkita ANEyitappattu , ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukinYrYanYa . * wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY , 1018 varuvAy kirAmafkalYil 1.82 koti marakkanYrYukalY natappattulYlYanYa . * wamilYYnAttil vanYafkalYinY mempAttirYkum vanYa valYafkalYEp pAwukAwwitavum , 2013-14Am ANtirYku , vanYa parAmarippu paNikalYAnYa , uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu , wIwwatuppu melANmE , ponYrYa paNikalY 34 kotiye , 89 latcam rUpAy ceVlavil ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . * manYiwa - kAttu yAnYE mowalkalYinYAl eVlYiwil pAwippirYkulYlYAkak kUtiya pakuwikalY kaNtarYiyappattu , 461.44 ki.mI wUrawwirYku yAnYE pukA akalYYikalY 19 kotiye 64 latcam rUpAy ceVlavil erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . * civakafkE , wiNtukkal , nAmakkal , marYrYum viruwunakar mAvattafkalYil ceVyalpatum wamilYYnAtu mAcuk kattuppAtu vAriyawwinY mAvatta aluvalafkalYukku coVnwamAka puwiya aluvalaka kattitafkalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . * wamilYYnAtu mAcu kattuppAtu vAriya paNiyAlYarkalYukku vIttuk katanY peVrYum vacawi erYpatuwwi koVtukkappattulYlYawu . * nuNNuyiri mUlam Utti eriyinYE cuwwappatuwwuwal , colE vanYakkAtukalYE marYu urYpawwi ceVywal , manYnYAr valYEkutA palluyir pAwukAppakam mUlam vilYYippuNarvup paNikalY marYrYum iwara wittafkalY 36.67 koti rUpAy ceVlavil ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYanYa . * wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu , wanYiyAr nilafkalYil marafkalY valYarwwal ulYlYitta wittafkalYukku 109.6 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , pirYa paNikalYutanY 1,000 kirAmafkalYil 1.02 koti marak kanYrYukalY natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . * 13-vawu niwik kulYYumaw wittawwinY kIlYY , uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu , utkattamEppu mempAtu marYrYum kAtu valYarppu ponYrYa paNikalY woVtarnwu ceVyalpatuwwa 35.62 koti rUpAy oVppalYippu ceVyyappattu , iwuvarEyil , 29.93 koti rUpAy ceVlavitappattu iwwittam ceVyalAkkappattulYlYawu . * vanYawwurYEyil paNipuriyum 1,439 mikEp paNiyita wottak kAvalarkalY marYrYum 137 mikEp paNiyita vettEw watuppuk kAvalarkalYukku iwara vanYawwurYE paNiyAlYarkalYukku valYYafkappatuvawu pola , itarpati mAwanworYum walA 400 rUpAy vIwam valYYafkappattu varukirYawu . * wiruneVlveli mAvattawwil uyirpanYmE ceVrinwulYlYa pakuwikalYE ulYlYatakki ' neVllE vanYa uyirinYa vanYaccaraNAlayam ' erYpatuwwappattulYlYawu . * vilYYuppuram mAvattawwil , vAnYUr vattawwil ulYlYa ocUtu erippakuwi ' ocUtu parYavEkalY caraNAlayam ' eVnYa AkkappattulYlYawu . * AnYEmalE pulikalY kAppakam , attakkatti marYrYum muwumalE pulikalY kAppakam weVppakkAtu Akiya pakuwiyilulYlYa atippatE payirYci mEyafkalYE , mempatuwwappatum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . * wamilYYnAtu vanYac cIrutE paNiyAlYar wervu kulYYumawwAl vanYavar / kalYappaNi uwaviyAlYar Akiya pawavikalYil kAliyAka ulYlYa paNiyitafkalYE nirappa wakuwiyAnYa naparkalYEw wervu ceVyya uriya natavatikkE eVtukkappattu varukirYawu . * manYiwa - vanYa uyirinYa mowalkalYE eVwirkoVlYlYum vakEyil , Utti , kiruRNakiri , marYrYum wiruneVlveli Akiya itafkalYil mUnYrYu awivirEvu kulYYukkalY erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . * marapu valYYiyAka canwanYa marafkalY valYarum pakuwikalYAnYa javvAwumalE , cervarAyanY malE , koVllimalE , paccEmalE marYrYum ciwweri malEppakuwikalYil canwanYa marafkalYE valYarkkum wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukinYrYawu . * mAnilam mulYYuvawum ulYlYa nakaram marYrYum woVlYYirYcAlEp pakuwikalYil 25 itafkalYil woVtar kArYrYu **wara kaNkANippu nilEyafkalY amEppawarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalY eVtukkappattu varukinYrYanYa . mawwiya ceVnYnYEyum mUlYYkiyawu kUvam ArYrYil veVlYlYam karEpuraNtu otukirYawu ceVnYnYE , kUvam ArYrYil veVlYlYam karEpuraNtu otuvawAl mawwiya ceVnYnYEyum veVlYlYawwil pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
atEyArYu ArYrYil erYpatta veVlYlYam weVnYceVnYnYEyE erYkanYave mUlYYkatiwwu vittawu . 
weVnYceVnYnYEyinY anYEwwu pakuwikalYum peVrufkalYawwUril woVtafki wAmparam , celEyUr , muticcUr , pIrkkanYkaraNE , matippAkkam , metavAkkam , palYlYikkaraNE , velYacceri , AwampAkkam , AlanwUr , parafkimalE , acoknakar , ke.ke.nakar , mAmpalam , wiyAkarAyanakar , mayilAppUr , atEyArYu , cEwAppettE , eVm.ji.Ar.nakar , mawuravAyal , porUr , valYacaravAkkam , virukampAkkam , pUnwamalli , mAfkAtu , kunYrYawwUr , marYrYum wurEppAkkam , wiruvAnYmiyUr , waramaNi ponYrYa pakuwikalY erYkanYave veVlYlYawwil mUlYYki miwakkinYrYanYa . 
anwa pakuwiyil vAkanYa pokkuvarawwu , wakaval woVtarpu , ponYrYa vacawikalY wuNtikkappattu pAwikkappattu vittanYa . 
inwa nilEyil kAlEyil kUvam ArYrYil veVlYlYappeVrukku erYpattawu . 
kUvawwEyoVtti ulYlYa mawwiya ceVnYnYE pakuwi mulYYuvawilum veVlYlYam pukunwawu . 
arumpAkkam , amEnwakarE , cewwuppattu , eVlYYumpUr , cinwAwirippettE , nufkampAkkam , aNNAnakar , wirumafkalam , je.je.nakar , mukapper ponYrYa pakuwikalYil kUvawwil karEpuraNtu otiya veVlYlYanIr pukunwu vittawu . 
cewwuppattu eriyum nirampi valYYikirYawu . 
anwa waNNIrum UrukkulY pukunwu vittawu . 
iwanYAl cewwuppattu spartAfkcAlEyil veVlYlYam cUlYYnwawAl , anwa cAlEyil vAkanYa pokkuvarawwu nirYuwwappattawu . 
minYcAra iNEppum merYkaNta pakuwikalYil illE . 
awwiyAvaciya poVrutkalY kitEkkAmal makkalY pAwippukkulYlYAnYArkalY . ottunar payirYciyE alYiwwu Atto vAfka makalYirukku mAnYiyam valYYafkappatum : werwal piracArawwil jeVyalaliwA peccu waFcE , wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalE munYnYittu a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA waFcEyil werwal piracAra kUttawwil pecinYAr . 
avar woVtarnwu pecumpoVlYYuwu , • a.wi.mu.ka. aracAl anYEvarukkum palanY • kAviri melANmE vAriyam , natuvar manYrYa kulYYuvE amEwwita natavatikkE eVtukkappatum • kAviri piracnYEyE oVru poVruttAkave karuNAniwi karuwavillE • munwEya wi.mu.ka. Atciyileye mIwwenY eVrivAyu wittawwirYku oVppuwal valYYafkappattawu • mIwwenY wittawwinYE ceVyalpatuwwa kUtAwu eVnYa a.wi.mu.ka. aracu uwwaravu pirYappiwwawu . 
makalYirukku mAnYiyam • ottunar payirYciyE alYiwwu Atto vAfka makalYirukku mAnYiyam valYYafkappatum • cuya woVlYYil woVtafkavum natavatikkE • peVNkalY skUttar vAfka 50 cawavIwam mAnYiyam . pirawAnYa curYrYil inwiya aNi - wi inwu ulaka tepilY teVnYnYis cAmpiyanYRip 2vawu tiviRanY pottiyil inwiya makalYir aNi 3-0 eVnYrYa kaNakkil kuroRiyAvE vIlYYwwi pirawAnYa curYrYukku wakuwi peVrYrYawu . 
kolAlampUril natEpeVrYrYu varum inwa pottiyinY katEci lIk Attawwil inwiyAvinY manYikA pawrA , mavumA wAs , RAminYi Akiyor veVrYrYi peVrYrYanYar . 
inwiya Atavar aNi 3-0 eVnYrYa kaNakkil svitcarlAnwE worYkatiwwawu . 
Atavar aNi katEci Attawwil slovekkiyAvE eVwirkoVlYkirYawu . atuwwa ANtil weciya & # 034 ; tirAval mArt # 039 ; kaNkAtci - puwuwilli , ceVp . 8 : mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakam cArpil weciya tirAval mArt kaNkAtci atuwwa ANtil natawwappata ulYlYawu eVnYrYu awwurYE amEccar cupow kAnw cahAy weVriviwwAr . 
pacipik eciyA tirAval acociyeRanY cArpil " pAtA tirAval mArt 2011 ' eVnYum walEppil pirakawi mEwAnYawwil natEpeVrYrYuvarum ulaka curYrYulA wakaval kaNkAtciyE mawwiya curYrYulA amEccar cupow kAnw cahAy viyAlYYakkilYYamE pArvEyittAr . 
munYnYawAka avar kUrYiyawAvawu : inwa tirAval mArt kaNkAtci carvaweca alYavil vAfkuvorEyum , virYporEyum , curYrYulAw wurYEyinYarEyum iNEkkum vakEyil natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
camuwAyafkalY , nAtukalY itEye ulakalYAviya cakowarawwuvawwEyum , valuvEyum erYpatuwwum karuviyAka curYrYulA vilYafkukirYawu . 
ikkaNkAtci , nAtukalY itEye oVwwulYYEppE mempatuwwuvawarYkum , palverYu nAtukalYinY , poVrulYAwAra valYarccikkAnYa curYrYulAvE mempatuwwuvawarYkum oVru muyarYciyAka amEnwulYlYawu . 
pacipik AciyAvinY palawarappatta nAtukalY pirAnwiyawwE mempatuwwuvawarYkAka natEpeVrYum " pAtA tirAval mArt ' kaNkAtci , pirAnwiya oVwwulYYEppinY oVru veVrYrYikaramAnYa uwAraNamAka ulYlYawu . 
curYrYulAwwurYE , woVlYYilwurYE itEye oVwwulYYEppu , wirYanYmiku peccuvArwwE irunwAl mattume curYrYulAvE cirYappAka mempatuwwa mutiyum . 
curYrYulAw wurYEyinYar ulYkattamEppu vacawi , atippatE valYarccip paNi , mArkkeVttif AkiyavarYrYE uruvAkka mutiyum . 
AnYAl , irYuwiyAnYa payanY eVnYpawu palawarappatta curYrYulAw walafkalY , curYrYulAvE mempatuwwa curYrYulA woVlYYil wurYE eVppati ceVyalpatukirYawu eVnYpawEp poVruwwe amEyum . 
inwiyA oVru palam vAynwa , wirYanYmikka curYrYulA , payaNam , virunwompal woVlYYilwurYE AkiyavarYrYEk koVNtulYlYawu . 
awE veVlYippatuwwum viwamAka ikkaNkAtciyil arafkukalY amEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
katanwa 10 ANtukalYil inwiya curYrYulAw woVlYYil wurYE inwiyac curYrYulAvE atuwwa kattawwirYkuk koVNtu ceVlla cirYappAnYa pafkalYippEc ceVywulYlYawu . 
iwu pArAttukkuriyawu . 
niwinilE pAwippAl ulakam mulYYuvawum poVrulYAwArawwil pinYnYatEvEc canwiwwuk koVNtirunwa kAlakkattawwil , curYrYulAw wurYEyum pAwippukku ulYlYAnYawu . 
iwil , inwiyA ulYlYitta oVru cila nAtukalYe virEvAnYa mItci kaNtanYa . 
inwiyAvinY valuvAnYa ulYnAttu curYrYulA , wIviramAnYa mArkkeVttif Akiya amcafkalY virEvAnYa mItci peVrYa kAraNamAka irunwanYa . 
ANtu mulYYuvawum verYupatta curYrYulA wayArippukalYE alYikkum curYrYulA itafkalYEk koVNta itamAka inwiyA afkIkarikkappattulYlYawu . 
ANtu mulYYuvawum curYrYulA vanwu ceVllum itamAka inwiyAvE uruvAkka veNtum eVnYpawu curYrYulA amEccakawwinY nokkam . 
curYrYulA varwwakawwE mempatuwwum vakEyil inwiya aracinY curYrYulA amEccakam 2012 - 2013-m ANtil weciya tirAval mArt kaNkAtciyE natawwum . 
cila ANtukalYil ikkaNkAtci , anYEwwu munYnYaNi panYnYAttuk kaNkAtcikalYukku oVppitakkUtiya vakEyil irukkum eVnYrYAr amEccar . 
pacipik eciyA tirAval acociyecanY ( carvaweca ) walEvar hiranY kUre , muwanYmE ceVyal walEvar pil kAltar ut , mawwiya curYrYulA amEccakac ceVyalar Ar.eVc. kuvAjA ulYlYittor utanYirunwanYar . a.wi.mu.ka. - wi.mu.ka. paNam viniyokippawE watukka veNtum werwal ANEyawwukku tAktar anYpumaNi veNtukolY ceVnYnYE , vAkkAlYarkalYukku a.wi.mu.ka. - wi.mu.ka.vinYarinY paNa viniyokawwE watukka veNtum eVnYrYu werwal ANEyawwukku tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs veNtukolY vituwwulYlYAr . 
iwukurYiwwu , pA.ma.ka. ilYEFaraNiw walEvar tAktar anYpumaNi rAmawAs veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : - wamilYYaka cattapperavE werwalukku inYnYum oVru vAram irukkum nilEyil , a.wi.mu.ka.vum , wi.mu.ka.vum pottipottuk koVNtu paNa viniyokawwE woVtafkiyulYlYanYa . 
valYYakkam polave werwal ANEyam iwE watukkAmal vetikkE pArwwuk koVNtiruppawu kaNtikkawwakkawAkum . 
wamilYYnAttil eVnwa woVkuwiyilum a.wi.mu.ka.vo , wi.mu.ka.vo makkalYE canwiwwu koVlYkEkalYEk kUrYi vAkku cekarikkum paNiyil ItupatavillE . 
mArYAka woVkuwiyil ulYlYa vAkkAlYarkalY anYEvarukkum paNawwEk koVtuwwu vAfki vitalAm eVnYrYa eVNNawwil paNam viniyokikkum velEyil wAnY ItupattirukkinYrYanYar . 
iwarYkAka oVvvoVru weVruvilum eVwwanYE vAkkAlYarkalY ulYlYanYar ; avarkalYinY araciyal nilEppAtu eVnYnYa ? ; yArutEya vAkkukalYEyeVllAm paNam koVtuwwu vAfkalAm eVnYpawE iru katcikalYum kaNakkeVtuwwu vEwwulYlYanYa . 
awanYatippatEyil 25 vAkkukalYukku oVru nirvAki vIwam niyamikkappattu avarkalY mUlam poVwumakkalYukku paNam viniyokikkappattu varukirYawu . 
werwal neVrukkawwil kaNkANippu awikamAka irukkum eVnYpawAl , awarYku munYpAkave paNa viniyokawwE mutiwwuvita veNtum eVnYrYa eVNNawwil paNikalY wIvirappatuwwappattirukkinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYakawwE 50 ANtukalYAka Atci ceVywu varum a.wi.mu.ka.vum , wi.mu.ka.vum cAwanYEkalYEk kUrYi vAkku cekarippawarYku pawilAka makkalYukku paNawwEk koVtuwwu avarkalYinY vAkkukalYE vilEkku vAfkuvawu aruvarukkawwakka mocamAnYa kalAcAram Akum . 
werwalil anYEwwu katci vetpAlYarkalYukkum camavAyppu valYYafkappata veNtiyawu werwal ANEyawwinY katamEyAkum . 
vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam warappatuvawE watuwwum , vAkkAlYarkalYukku waruvawarYkAka pawukki vEkkappattirukkum paNawwE parYimuwal ceVywum werwal ANEyam awanY katamEyE nirYEverYrYa veNtum .

mawurE ArappAlYEyam kirAsrotu aruke piracAram merYkoVNta avar peciwAvawu : - wi.mu.ka. , a.wi.mu.ka. Atci kAlawwil wamilYYaka makkalYukku eVnwa nanYmEyum erYpatavillE .

manwiricapE mArYrYi amEkkappatum . 
warYpowu patjeVt kUttawwoVtar mutinwu 2 vAram Akivittawu . 
manwiri pawaviyE eVwirpArwwu kAwwirukkum kAfkiras mUwwa eVm.eVl.e.kkalY oVnYrYukUti AlocanYE natawwinYar . 
manwiricapEyE mArYrYiye wIra veNtum eVnYrYu avarkalY ciwwarAmEyAvukku korikkE vituwwanYar . 
iwarYku pawil alYiwwa ciwwarAmEyA , inwa mAwawwirYkulY manwiricapE mArYrYi amEkkappatum eVnYrYu arYiviwwAr . 
iwanYAl manwiri pawavi mIwu kaN vEwwulYlYa kAfkiras eVm.eVl.e.kkalY mikunwa makilYYcciyil irunwanYar . 
inwa nilEyil karnAtaka melita poVrYuppAlYar wikvijaycif nerYrYu peVfkalYUru vanwAr . 
manwiricapEyE mArYrYa veNtAm 
manwiricapE mArYrYam woVtarpAka wikvijaycifkutanY muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyA AlocanYE natawwinYAr . 
appowu karnAtakawwil katum varYatci nilavukirYa inwa cUlYYnilEyil manwiricapEyil mArYrYam ceVyvawu cariyAka irukkAwu eVnYrYum , puwiya manwirikalY vanwAl avarkalY wurYE woVtarpAnYa vivarafkalYE arYinwukoVlYlYa cirYiwu kAlam Akum eVnYrYum , eVnYave warYpowEkku manwiricapEyE mArYrYa veNtAm eVnYrYum , ippowu ulYlYa manwirikalYe varYatci nivAraNa paNikalYE merYkoVlYlYattum eVnYrYum ciwwarAmEyAvitam wikvijaycif kUrYiyawAka weVrikirYawu . 
varYatci nIfkiya pirYaku , wamilYYnAtu ulYpata 5 mAnila cattacapE werwal mutivatEnwa pinYnYare manwiricapEyE mArYrYalAm eVnYrYu wikvijaycif AlocanYE weVriviwwu iruppawAka kUrYappatukirYawu . 
awepol muwal-manwiri ciwwarAmEyAvE mArYrYum peccukke itam illE eVnYrYum wikvijaycif kUrYiyawAkavum wakaval veVlYiyAkiyulYlYawu . 
katum emArYrYam atEnwanYar 
iwukurYiwwu wikvijaycif niruparkalYukku alYiwwa pettiyil , 
“ ciwwarAmEyAvE mArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu eVm.eVl.e.kkalY yArum ketkavillE .

iwil eVnYakku eVnwa AtcepanYEyum illE .

wanwE witIr cAvu 
celam mAvattam vAlYYappAti nakara a.wi.mu.ka. ceVyalAlYarAka iruppavar civakkumAr ( vayawu 45 ) 
ivarawu vItu vAlYYappAti reVyil nilEyam arukil ulYlYawu . 
civakkumAr vIttil vAkkAlYarkalYukku koVtukka rU. 2 koti paNam pawukki vEwwiruppawAka anwa pakuwi wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kAfkiras nirvAkikalYukku nerYrYiravu rakaciya wakaval kitEwwawu . 
utanYe afku virEnwu ceVnYrYa wi.mu.ka , kAfkiras katciyinYar 50-kkum merYpattor civakkumAr vIttE murYrYukEyittu porAttawwil ItupattanYar . 
wakaval arYinwa a.wi.mu.ka.vinYarum erAlYamAnYor afku kuvinwawAl pawattamAnYa cUlYYal nilaviyawu . 
utanYe afku virEnwu ceVnYrYa vAlYYappAti polIcAr murYrYukE porAttawwil Itupatta wi.mu.ka , kAfkiras katciyinYaritam peccuvArwwE natawwinYar . 
appowu vAkkAlYarkalYukku koVtukka civakkumAr vIttil paNam pawukki vEwwulYlYawAkavum , anwa paNawwE werwal awikArikalY marYrYum parYakkumpatEyinYar cowanYE ceVywu parYimuwal ceVyya veNtum eVnYrYu korikkE vituwwanYar . 
iwarYkitEye muwalmAtiyil patuwwirunwa civakkumArinY wanwE nakArAjanY kIlYYe irYafki vanwAr . 
appowu wanYawu vIttu munYpu erAlYamAnYor wiraNtiruppawEyum polIcAr kuvikkap pattulYlYawEyum pArwwa nAkarAjanY awircci atEnwAr . 
pinYnYar cirYiwu nerawwil vIttu munYpu mayafki vilYYunwa nAkarAjanY campava itawwileye irYanwAr . 
iwE pArwwa urYavinYarkalY kawarYi wutiwwanYar . 
iwE woVtarnwu murYrYukE porAttawwE kEvitta wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kAfkiracAr afkirunwu kalEnwu ceVnYrYanYar . 
inwa campavam kurYiwwu erYkAtu woVkuwi werwal awikArikalYukku wakaval weVrivikkappattawu . 
awanYperil erYkAtu woVkuwi parYakkumpatE awikAri kanwacAmi walEmEyil awikArikalY inYrYu awikAlE 3 maNiyalYavil civakkumArinY vIttukku ceVnYrYu vicAraNE natawwinYar . 
appowu afku wiraNtirunwa a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar nAkarAjanY cAvukku wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kAfkiracAr wAnY kAraNam eVnYrYum avarkalYE kEwu ceVyya veNtum eVnYrYum koRam pottanYar 
afku pawattamAnYa cUlYYal nilavuvawAl kUtuwal pAwukAppu potappattu ulYlYawu . 
iwarYkitEye nakara ceVyalAlYar civakkumAr vAlYYappAti polIcil inYrYu kAlE oVru pukAr koVtuwwAr . 
anwa pukAril wanYawu wanwE nAkarAjanYE wittamittu wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kAfkiras katciyinYar atiwwu koVlE ceVywulYlYawAkavum , avarkalY mIwu natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYum kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
inwa campavawwAl anwa pakuwiyil woVtarnwu pawattam nItiwwu varuvawAl 100-kkum merYpatta polIcAr vAlYYappAti nakaram mulYYuvawum pAwukAppu paNiyil ItupattulYlYanYar . atEyArYu ArYrYil varalArYu kANAwa veVlYlYam wi.nakar , ke.ke.nakarukkulY pukunwawu 
ceVnYnYE 
ceVnYnYE atEyArYrYilirunwu veVlYiyerYum veVlYlYanIr wi.nakar , ke.ke.nakar Akiya pakuwikalYukkulY pukunwulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl wi.nakar , ke.ke.nakar , merYku mAmpalam Akiya pakuwikalYilirunwu makkalY veVlYiyerYi varukinYrYanYar . 
wi.nakaril ulYlYa natcawwira ottalukkulYlYum veVlYlYanIr pukunwulYlYawAl jeVnYarettarkalY iyakka mutiyAwa nilE erYpattulYlYawu . 
ottalkalYil wafkiyirunwavarkalY veVlYiyerYaw woVtafkiyulYlYanYar . 
wi.nakarukkulY nulYYEnwulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl perunwu nilEyawwinY ulYlYe mulYYafkAl alYavukku waNNIr wefkiyulYlYawu . 
wi.nakar mArkkeVt , natecanY weVru Akiya itafkalYil wefkiyulYlYa malYYE nIril kalYYivunIrum kalanwu wurnArYrYam vIcukirYawu . 
mukkiya varwwakap pakuwiyAnYa rafkanAwanY weVruvilum malYYEnIr wefkiyulYlYawu . 
afkulYlYa cila mukkiya katEkalYukkulY malYYEnIr pukunwulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl , anwap pakuwiyil varwwakam veVkuvAka pAwikkappattulYlYawu . 
atEyArYu ArYrYinY veVlYlYanIr mattam vekamAka uyarnwu varuvawAl wi.nakarvAcikalY accawwil AlYYnwulYlYanYar . 
makAlatcumi nakaril ulYlYa vItukalYukkulY veVlYlYanIr pukunwulYlYawu . 
patakukalY mUlam wafkalYE mItka veNtum eVnYrYu erAlYamAnYor valiyurYuwwi varukinYrYanYar . 
atEyArYu ArYrYinY veVlYlYam , ke.ke.nakarE mUlYYkatiwwulYlYawu . 
erAlYamAnYa vItukalY waNNIril mUlYYki varukinYrYanYa . 
mItpukkulYYuvinYar utanYatiyAka vara veNtum eVnYrYu poVwumakkalY korikkE vituwwulYlYanYar . 
veVlYlYam pAwiwwa pakuwikalYil cikki iruppor katarYkarE cAlEkku vanwu , pUnwamalli valYYiyAka ceVnYnYEyE vittu veVlYiyerYalAm eVnYrYu arYivurYuwwappattulYlYawu . 
kotampAkkam , vatapalYYanYi , cAlikirAmam , valYacaravAkkam , IkkAtuwAfkal pakuwikalYilwAnY natikar , natikEkalY , tEraktarkalY , wayArippAlYarkalY , wirEppata woVlYYilAlYarkalY erAlYamAnYor vacikkinYrYanYar . 
inwa pakuwikalYil malYYE veVlYlYam vItukalYukkulY pukunwawu . 
atEyArYil cIrYikkoVNtu ceVllum veVlYlYam cEwAppettEyE mUlYYkatiwwu wiyAkarAyanakar , kotampAkkam pakuwikalYEyum purattippottawu . 
IkkAttuwAfkal pAlam , kottUrpuram pAlam , cEwAppettE marYEmalEatikalY pAlam , atEyArYu wiruvika pAlam ponYrYavarYrYil pokkuvarawwu nirYuwwappattulYlYawu . 
cAlEyE vita uyaramAka kattappattulYlYa pAlawwE woVtum alYavirYku veVlYlYanIr ceVlvawAl ArYrYafkarEkalYil ulYlYa vItukalY mulYYumEyAka waNNIril mUlYYkiyulYlYanYa . wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar ke.ci.palYYanYiccAmi makanY vIttil 1.5 koti parYimuwal ; 
rU 10 koti vari eyppu 
ceVnYnYE 
karUr mAvattam aravakkurYicci woVkuwiyil wi.mu.ka. cArpil ke.ci.palYYanYiccAmi pottiyitukirYAr . 
karUril ulYlYa avarawu lAtjil vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam koVtukka pawukki vEwwiruppawAka vanwa rakaciya wakavalEyatuwwu varumAnYa variwwurYE awikArikalY cowanYE natawwinYar . 
appowu cila AvaNafkalY kEpparYrYappattanYa . 
iwanY atippatEyil ceVnYnYE AlYYvArpettEyil ulYlYa ke.ci.palYYanYi cAmiyinY makanY civarAmanY vIttil inYrYu varumAnYa variwwurYE awikArikalY cowanYE natawwinYar . 
appowu rU. 1.5 koti parYimuwal ceVyyappattawu . 
inwa paNawwirYku uriya kaNakku , AvaNafkalY illAwawAl avarYrYE varumAnYa variwwurYE awikArikalY parYimuwal ceVywawAka kUrYappatukirYawu . 
melum avar rU. 10 koti varE vari eyppu ceVywawAka kaNtu pitikkappattulYlYawu . 
parYimuwal ceVyyappatta paNam vAkkAlYarkalYukku koVtuppawarYkAka pawukki vEkkappattulYlYawA ? eVnYrYu vicAraNE natawwap patukirYawu . 
werwalukku inYnYum 4 nAtkalYe ulYlYa nilEyil araciyal katcikalY vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam koVtukkum muyarYciyil Itupattu varukinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYakawwinY palverYu itafkalYil natanwa cowanYEyil pala koti rUpAy oVre nAlYil parYimuwal ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
parYakkumpatEyinYar wIviramAka cowanYEyil Itupattu varuvawAl paNam parYimuwal natavatikkE awikariwwu varukinYrYanYa . ceVnYnYE malYYE , irYEvanY alYiwwa waNtanYE : ilYEyarAjA - 
ceVnYnYE 
kanYamalYYEyAl wirEppataw woVlYYilAlYarkalYinY vAlYYvAwAram pAwikkappattulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl wirEppataw woVlYYilAlYarkalYukku nivAraNam valYYafka weVnYnYinwiya wirEppata woVlYYilAlYarkalY cammelYanYam mutivu ceVywawu . 
wamilYY wirEppata wayArippAlYarkalY cafkam , weVnYnYinwiya wirEppata varwwaka capE , weVnYnYinwiya natikar cafkam marYrYum icEyamEppAlYarkalY ilYEyarAjA , e.Ar.rakumAnY , hAris jeVyarAj , ti.imAnY Akiyor mUlam nivAraNap poVrulYkalY peVrYappattanYa . 
muwarYkattamAka 5 Ayiram perkalYukku nivAraNap poVrulYkalY nerYrYu valYYafkappattanYa . 
inwa vilYYAvil ilYEyarAjA pecumpowu kUrYiyawAvawu : 
ifke koVtuppawum vAfkuvawum cinYimA kalEFarkalYwAnY . 
nAm oVvvoVruvarum oVvvoVruvakEyil wavarYu ceVywulYlYom . 
camIpawwil peVywa malYYE , irYEvanY alYiwwa waNtanYE . 
iwE nAnY mattume coVlla mutiyum . 
inwa malYYE nammEp pAtAyp patuwwivittawu . 
malYYEyAl pAwikkappatta paNakkArarukku pirat koVtuwwAl , avar atuwwavarukkum koVtufkalY eVnYrYu coVlkirYAr . 
iwu nam kaN munY natakkum nikalYYvu . 
oVvvoVruvarukkum koVtuwwup palYYakufkalY . 
malYYE , manYiwaneyawwE valYarwwulYlYawu eVnYrYAr . jeVyalaliwA inYrYu ‘ witIr ’ piracAram . 
ceVnYnYEyil 15 woVkuwikalYilum wirYanwa venYil Awaravu wirattukirYAr . 
ceVnYnYE , 
muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA inYrYu ( puwanYkilYYamE ) witIreVnYa ceVnYnYEyil ulYlYa woVkuwikalYil piracAram ceVyvawAka a.wi.mu.ka. walEmE kalYYakam arYiviwwawu . 
ceVnYnYE mAvatta a.wi.mu.ka. nirvAkikalYukku iwu inYpa awircciyAka irunwawu . 
neram mika kurYEvAka ulYlYa powilum jeVyalaliwAvE varaverYka AfkAfke ulYlYa a.wi.mu.ka. nirvAkikalY cirYappAnYa erYpAtukalY ceVywulYlYanYar . 
ceVnYnYE mAvattawwil moVwwam 16 woVkuwikalY ulYlYanYa . 
iwil muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA wanY coVnwa woVkuwiyAnYa Ar.ke.nakar woVkuwiyil katanwa 6-nwewi vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu Awaravu wirattinYAr . 
mIwamulYlYa ceppAkkam - wiruvallikkeNi , AyiramvilYakku , velYacceri , mayilAppUr , eVlYYumpUr , wurYEmukam , rAyapuram , kOwwUr , villivAkkam , peVrampUr , wiru.vi.ka.nakar , virukampAkkam , aNNAnakar , cEwAppettE , wi.nakar Akiya 15 woVkuwikalYilum muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA inYrYu pirYpakal woVtafki iravu varE Awaravu wirattukirYAr . 
ceVnYnYEyil inYrYu avar eVnweVnwa valYYiwwatafkalYil ceVnYrYu makkalYE canwikkirYAr eVnYpawE a.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam veVlYiyittulYlYawu . 
awanY vivaram varumArYu : 
muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA inYrYu pirYpakal tAktar rAwAkiruRNanY cAlE , natecanY cAlE , Esavus kAval nilEyam canwippu , wiruvallikkeNi neVtuFcAlE , aNNAcAlE , vels wotta cAlE , I.vi.ke.campaw cAlE , cUlYE wapAl nilEyam , cUlYE neVtuFcAlE , yAnYEkkavunYi pAlam - vAltAks rotu canwippu , mUlakkoVwwalYam canwippu . 
pecinYpiritj , cawwiya mUrwwi nakar , eVm.ke.pi.nakar ceVnYtral aveVnYyU , tAktar ampewkar kallUri cAlE , steVrAnYs rotu , otteri pAlam , koVnYnYUr meVyinY rotu , ayanYAvaram pas nilEyam , reVtti weVru canwippu , pAti mempAlam , wirumafkalam meVyinY rotu , koyampetu pas nilEyam , vinAyakapuram pirawAnYa cAlE , eVm.eVm.ti.e. kAlanYi , aNNA Arc , neVlcanY mANikkam rotu , puRpA nakar , vatakku usmAnY rotu , wiyAkarAyanakar pas nilEyam , weVrYku usmAnY rotu , cEwAppettE panYakal mAlYikE , kiNti pAlam , aNNA cilE , kawwippArA mempAlam , mawwiyakElAR , malar maruwwuvamanYE , wiru.vi.ka. pAlam , Ar.ke.matam rotu , mayilE mAfkoVllE , laskArnYar , AlYYvArppettE canwippu Akiya itafkalYil piracAram ceVykirYAr . 
ivvArYu awil kUrYappattulYlYawu . 
muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA tAktar rAwAkiruRNanY cAlEyil pirYpakal 3 maNikku wanY cUrYAvalYi piracArawwE woVtafkuvAr eVnYrYu arYivikkappattulYlYawu . 
cumAr 3 maNi nerawwukkum mel avar 15 woVkuwikalYEyum curYrYi varuvAr . 
mukkiya itafkalYil avar wirYanwa venY mUlam Awaravu wirattuvAr . 
marYrYa itafkalYil avar venYil amarnwapati vAkkAlYarkalYE canwippAr . 
muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY inwa witIr cUrYAvalYi piracArawwAl ceVnYnYE mAvatta a.wi.mu.ka.vinYar mikunwa urYcAkam atEnwulYlYanYar . 
nAlYE ( viyAlYYakkilYYamE ) muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA neVllE mAvattawwil erYpAtu ceVyyappattulYlYa piramANta poVwuk kUttawwil kalanwu koVNtu neVllE , wUwwukkuti , kanYnYiyAkumari Akiya 3 mAvatta 20 a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalYukkAka piraccAram ceVyya ulYlYAr . 
nAlYEyutanY avarawu werwal piracAra curYrYuppayaNam nirYEvu peVrYuvawAka a.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam erYkanYave veVlYiyittirunwa ceVywik kurYippil weVrivikkappattirunwawu . 
nAlYE neVllE mAvatta poVwukkUttam mutinwa pirYaku 13 , 14-nwewikalYil melum 2 nAtkalY piracAram ceVyya jeVyalaliwAvukku avakAcam ulYlYawu . 
eVnYave katEci iru winYafkalYil avar wanY coVnwa woVkuwiyAnYa ceVnYnYE Ar.ke.nakar woVkuwiyil piracAram ceVyyakkUtum eVnYrYu kUrYappattawu . 
awarYkAnYa erYpAtukalYE a.wi.mu.ka. nirvAkikalY ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . ameVrikkAvil veVlYlYam : 
inwiya peVN eVnYjinYIyar ulYpata 6 per pali hUstanY : 
ameVrikkAvil teVkcAs mAkANawwil ulYlYa wurYEmuka nakarAnYa hUstanYil palawwa malYYE peVywawu . 
iwanY kAraNamAka erYpatta veVlYlYam , afku peVruwwa cewawwE erYpatuwwi vittawu . 
1 latcawwu 20 Ayiram vItukalY minY iNEppu wuNtikkappattu irulYil mUlYYkinYa . 
cAlEkalY veVlYlYawwil atiwwucceVllappattanYa . 
inwa veVlYlYawwil 6 per pariwApamAka uyirilYYanwanYar . 
avarkalYil oVruvar , inwiyap peVNNAnYa cunYiwA cif ( vayawu 47 ) AvAr . 
ivar afku peVkteVk eVNNeVy marYrYum kiyAs nirYuvanYawwil mUwwa minYcAra eVnYjinYIyarAka velE pArwwu vanwAr . 
nerYrYu munYwinYam avar valYYakkampola velEkku ceVnYrYu koVNtirunwapowu , kArotu atiwwu ceVllappattAr . 
iwil avar kArileye piNamAnYAr . 
cunYiwAvukku kaNavarum , 15 vayawil oVru makanYum ulYlYanYar . 
inwa wuyara campavam kurYiwwu avarawu kaNavar rAjIv cif kUrYukEyil ,

nAnY Apawwil irukkirYenY ’’ eVnYa kUrYinYAr .

arakkoNam piracAra kUttawwil jeVyalaliwA wAkku . 
arakkoNam , 
makkalY nalanYukkAkave wayArikkappattulYlYa a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyE eVwirppavarkalY makkalY mIwu akkarYE illAwavarkalY eVnYrYu arakkoNam piracAra kUttawwil muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA kAttamAka wAkki pecinYAr . 
jeVyalaliwA piracAram 
wamilYYaka cattamanYrYa werwalEyoVtti , a.wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu katanwa mAwam ( epral ) 9-nwewi ceVnYnYEyil muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA piracArawwE woVtafkinYAr . 
woVtarnwu , viruwwAcalam , aruppukkottE , celam , wirucci , puwucceri , kovE , peVrunwurYE , waFcAvUr Akiya nakarafkalYil natanwa piracAra poVwukkUttawwil jeVyalaliwA pecinYAr . 
inwa nilEyil , nerYrYu mAlE arakkoNawwil natanwa piramANta werwal piracAra poVwukkUttawwil muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA pafkerYrYu , wiruvaNNAmalE marYrYum velUr mAvattafkalYil ulYlYa 21 woVkuwikalYil pottiyitum a.wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu pecinYAr . 
appowu avar peciyawAvawu : 
UlYYal kUttaNi kAfkiras - wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi eVnYrYAle UlYYal kUttaNi eVnYpawu wAnY poVrulY . 
nilakkari UlYYal ; 
2ji speVktram UlYYal ; 
AwarR vIttu vacawi UlYYal eVnYa palverYu UlYYalkalYE ceVywu , makkalYAl waNtikkappatta kUttaNi wAnY kAfkiras - wi.mu.ka. kUttaNi . 
kAmanYveVlw vilYEyAttile kUta vilYEyAtiyavarkalY eVnYrYAl anwak kUttaNi eVppatippatta UlYYal kUttaNi eVnYpawE nIfkalY purinwukoVlYlYa veNtum . 
wi.mu.ka. afkam vakiwwa kAfkiras kUttaNi , pawaviyil irunwa powu iwwAliyEc cernwa oVru nirYuvanYawwitam irunwu heVlikAptarkalY vAfkiyawil UlYYal natEpeVrYrYawu parYrYi warYpowu vicAraNE natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
ippatiw wAnY eVfkum UlYYal , eVwilum UlYYal eVnYa UlYYal AtciyEye wi.mu.ka.vum , kAfkiracum cernwu mawwiyilum , mAnilawwilum natawwi vanwanYar . 
munwEya wi.mu.ka. Atciyil kirAnYEt koVlYlYE , maNal koVlYlYE , wAwu maNal koVlYlYE , woVlYYil wuvafka anYumawippawil UlYYal , minY koVlYmuwalil UlYYal , nilakkari irYakkumawiyil UlYYal , velE vAyppu valYYafkuvawil UlYYal , paNi mArYrYawwil UlYYal eVnYa eVfkum eVwilum UlYYal wAnY . 
ota , ota virattufkalY . 
1,76,000 koti rUpAy ilYYappu erYpatuwwiya 2ji speVktaram eVnYrYa imAlaya UlYYalE nikalYYwwiyawu wi.mu.ka.vEc cernwa mawwiya manwiri wAnY . 
erceVl-mekcis UlYYal , pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. woVlEpeci iNEppukalYE woVlEkAtci nirYuvanYawwirYku payanYpatuwwiyawil UlYYal eVnYa , eVllAvarYrYilum UlYYal purinwavarkalY wAnY wi.mu.ka.vinYar. UlYYalEye woVlYYilAkak koVNtulYlYa wi.mu.ka. - kAfkiras kUttaNi vAkku cekarikka ufkalYEw weti varum powu avarkalYawu UlYYalkalYE eVtuwwuc coVlli ota , ota viratti atiyufkalY . 
ceVyvIrkalYA ? 
nIfkalY ceVyvIrkalYA ? 
werwal arYikkEyil illAwa cila puwiya arYivippukalYE ippowu ceVyya virumpukirYenY . 
inwu camaya arYanilEyawwurYEyinY nerati AlYukEyinY kIlYY koVNtuvarappatAwa wirukkovilkalYil , 20 ANtukalYAka paNipurinwu 60 vayawinYE nirYEvu ceVywu oyvu peVrYrYa kirAma kovil pUcArikalYukku 750 rUpAy eVnYa valYYafkappattu vanwa mAwa oyvUwiyawwE , 1,000 rUpAyAka uyarwwi valYYafkiyawu eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa a.wi.mu.ka. aracu . 
inwa oyvUwiyam kAlawwirYkerYpa uyarwwappatum . 
kirAma kovil pUcArikalYukku Uwiyam valYYafkappata veNtum eVnYrYa korikkE paricIlikkappattu Uwiyam valYYafkuvawarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalY eVtukkappatum . 
puwu vAlYYvu wittam kirAmap purYafkalYil ulYlYa elYYmEyE nIkkuvawarYkAka , ‘ ‘ puwu vAlYYvu ‘ ‘ eVnYnYum oVru puwumEyAnYa wittam ulaka vafki katanYuwaviyutanY eVnYawu munwEya Atcik kAlawwil 2005-m ANtu muwal ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
inwaw wittam inYnYum oVru cila mAwafkalYil nirYEvatEyum . 
eVnYave , 900 koti rUpAy mawippIttil ‘ ‘ iraNtAm puwu vAlYYvu wittam‘ ‘ ulaka vafkiyinY uwaviyutanY ceVyalpatuwwita natavatikkEkalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
inYnYum oVru cila mAwafkalYil iwarYkAnYa anYumawiyE ulaka vafki valYYafkivitum . 
warYpowu puwu vAlYYvu wittawwil paNipuriyum paNiyAlYarkalY iraNtAvawu wittawwilum woVtarnwu paNiyil Itupatuwwappatuvar . 
a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyEp parYrYi palverYu katcikalYum woVtarnwu palverYu karuwwukalYE weVriviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
warYpowu nAfkalY veVlYiyittulYlYa werwal arYikkEyil , elYYE - eVlYiya makkalYukku vilEyillAmal cilavarYrYE valYYafkuvom eVnYrYa urYuwiyE alYiwwirukkirYom eVnYrYu pirYa katcikalY coVlvawE nAnY marYukkavillE . 
awu uNmE wAnY . 
elYYEkalY pakkam 
enYeVnYil , eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa a.wi.mu.ka. aracu eVppowum iruppawu elYYEkalYinY pakkam wAnY . 
eVnYave , elYYE eVlYiyorukkAnYa wittafkalYAka , avarkalYE vAlYYvil kE wUkki vitum wittafkalYAka , avarkalYum wafkalY coVnwak kAlkalYile ninYrYu varuvAy Ittum wittafkalYAka , eVfkalY werwal vAkkurYuwikalY amEnwulYlYanYa . 
iwarYku mukkiya kAraNam , eVnYakku eVnYrYu kutumpam illE . 
eVnYakku eVnwaviwa cuyanalamum illE . 
ilavaca vaNNaw woVlEkAtcippeVttiyE koVtuwwu pala Ayiram koti rUpAy kepilY ti.vi. kattaNamAka apakarikka veNtum eVnYrYa eVNNam eVnYakku illE . 
eVnYave wAnY , eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkEyil makkalYawu eVwirpArppukalYE nirYEverYrYum vakEyil vAkkurYuwikalYE alYiwwulYlYom . 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi , wi.mu.ka.vinYar , pA.ma.ka , makkalY nala kUttaNiyil ulYlYa katcikalY eVnYa palarum eVnY mIwu wanYippatta murYEyil kurYrYaccAttukalYE iwunAlYvarE coVllivanwanYar . 
eVnYawu walEmEyilAnYa a.wi.mu.ka. aracinY mIwum , kurYEkalY coVlvawotu mattumallAmal , kurYrYaccAttukalYE cumawwi vanwanYar . 
warYpowu awEyeVllAm nirYuwwivittu eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkEyE parYrYi mattume peci varukinYrYanYar . 
iwil ulYlYa vAkkurYuwikalY nirYEverYrYa iyalAwavE eVnYa ivarkalY eVllorum weVriviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
jeVyalaliwA makkalYE emArYrYap pArkkirYAr . 
vAkkurYuwi inwa ammEyAr koVtuwwa vAkkurYuwikalYE nirYEverYrYave mutiyAwu . 
anwa ammAvE nampi emAnwu pokAwIrkalY eVnYrYu wirumpaw wirumpak kUkkural itukinYrYanYar . 
eVnwa oVru vAkkurYuwiyE koVtuppawarYku munYnYAlum , awEpparYrYi 100 watavE alla , Ayiram watavE yociwwu vAkkurYuwi warupavalY wAnY inwa jeVyalaliwA . 
eVnYnYAl nirYEverYrYa mutiyum eVnYrYAl wAnY nAnY eVnwa vAkkurYuwiyEyum alYippenY . 
iwu wamilYYaka makkalYukkum nanYrYAkaw weVriyum . 
eVfkalYawu werwal arYikkEyil weVriviwwulYlYa vAkkurYuwikalY anYEwwEyum nAnY nirYEverYrYuvenY eVnYrYa urYuwiyE inwa nerawwil ufkalYukku alYikkirYenY . 
makkalY nalanYukkAkave wayArikkappattulYlYa inwaw werwal arYikkEyE eVwirppavarkalY , uNmEyileye makkalY mIwu akkarYE illAwavarkalY wAnY . 
iwE nIfkalY purinwukoVlYlYa veNtum . 
makkalY virowa ceVyalkalYinY uccawwirYke ceVnYrYu inwa werwal arYikkEyE watEceVyya veNtum eVnYrYu nIwimanYrYawwirYke wi.mu.ka. ceVnYrYulYlYawu . 
ivarkalY wAnY makkalYinY eVwirikalY . 
atEyAlYam kaNtu koVlYlYufkalY . 
ippowu inwaw werwalEyoVtti 2016-l nAnY veVlYiyittulYlYa werwal arYikkEyil erAlYamAnYa arYivippukalY irunwAlum , vAkkurYuwikalY irunwAlum , ivvalYavu wAnY eVnYrYu karuwivitAwIrkalY . 
oVru wAykkuw wAnY wanY pilYlYEkalYukku eVnYnYeVnYnYa ceVyya veNtum ; 
eVppowu ceVyya veNtum ; 
awE eVppati ceVyya veNtum eVnYpawu weVriyum . 
eVnYave , ivvalYavu wAnY eVnYrYu karuwivitAwIrkalY . 
nIfkalYe eVwirpArkka mutiyAwa ; 
nIfkalYe karYpanYE ceVywu pArkka mutiyAwa , inYnYum cirYanwa wittafkalYE , inYnYum unYnYawamAnYa wittafkalYE nAnY koVNtu vanwu ufkalYukkAka ceVyalpatuwwuvenY eVnYrYa urYuwiyE inwa nerawwil ufkalYukku alYikkirYenY . 
ivvArYu jeVyalaliwA pecinYAr . ‘ 6-vawu murYEyAka nAnY muwal-amEccarAka veNtum eVnYa ninYEkkum muwal AlY mu.ka.stAlinY ’ 
karuNAniwi petti 
ceVnYnYE , 
werwalil inwa murYEyum veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl 6-vawu murYEyAka nAnY muwal-amEccarAka veNtum eVnYa ninYEkkum muwal AlY mu.ka.stAlinY wAnY eVnYrYu wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi kUrYinYAr . 
karuNAniwi petti 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi , ceVnYnYEyil nerYrYu wanYiyAr Afkila woVlEkkAtci oVnYrYirYku cirYappu pettiyalYiwwAr . 
appowu ketkappatta kelYvikalYum , awarYku avar alYiwwa pawilkalYum varumArYu : 
kelYvi : 
ufkalY araciyal vAlYYkkEyil nIfkalY eVwwanYEyo werwalkalYE canwiwwu irukkirYIrkalY . 
munYpu natanwa werwalukkum , ippowulYlYa werwalukkum eVnYnYa verYupAtu iruppawAka uNarkirYIrkalY ? 
pawil : 
iwuvarE 12 murYE cattamanYrYa werwalil wi.mu.ka. cArpil nAnY pottiyittulYlYenY . 
eVwirkoVNta anYEwwu werwalilum nAnY veVrYrYi peVrYrYulYlYenY . 
inwa werwalil paNa palawwAl veVrYrYi peVrYa a.wi.mu.ka. wittamittulYlYawu . 
AnYAl , jeVyalaliwAvinY kanYavu palikkAwu . 
kelYvi : 
werwal arYikkEyil a.wi.mu.ka. arYiviwwulYlYa ilavaca wittafkalY eVppati ? . 
pawil : 
oVnYrYukkum uwavAwawu . 
makkalYE emArYrYum viwamAka ilavacafkalYE arYiviwwulYlYanYar . 
a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkE eVppati ? 
kelYvi : 
a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkEyE poVwuvAka eVppati pArkkirYIrkalY ? . 
pawil : 
a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkE veVlYivanwawe peVriya viRayam . 
werwal mutinwa pirYaku wAnY varumo eVnYrYu ninYEkka wonYrYiyawu . 
awE a.wi.mu.ka.vinYarum eVwirpArwwu irunwanYar . 
AnYAl , wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkE appatiye kAppi atikkappattu a.wi.mu.ka. werwal arYikkE wayArikkappattulYlYawu . 
kelYvi : 
poVwumakkalYAkiya vAkkAlYarkalYukku eVnYnYa kUrYa virumpukirYIrkalY ? . 
pawil : 
nAnY wamilYYanY . 
wirAvitanY . 
wamilYYanY uyarvukku pAtupatupavanY . 
wirAvitarkalY wiyAka uNarvotu paNiyArYrYa veNtum . 
wi.mu.ka.vil nAnY peVrYrYa anYupavafkalY , wiyAkafkalY eVnYnYE inwa alYavukku veVrYrYi peVrYa ceVywulYlYawu . 
wamilYY camuwAyam vAlYYa anYEvarum eVwEyum ilYYakka wayArAka irukka veNtum . 
ivvArYu karuNAniwi kUrYinYAr . 
mu.ka.stAlinY viruppam 
iwepol , marYrYoVru Afkila woVlEkkAtcikkum wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi pettiyalYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
nAnY 6-vawu murYEyAka muwal-amEccarAki cAwanYE patEkka veNtum eVnYrYu mu.ka.stAlinY virumpukirYAr . 
wAnY muwal-amEccarAka veNtum eVnYa mu.ka.stAlinY ninYEwwawu illE . 
werwalil iwuvarE nAnY worYrYawillE . 
inwa murYEyum veVnYrYAl , nAnY 6-vawu murYEyAka muwal-amEccar pawavi erYka veNtum eVnYa ninYEkkum muwal AlY mu.ka.stAlinY wAnY . 
eVnYakku iyarYkEyAka ewAvawu nernwAl wAnY mu.ka.stAlinY wamilYYaka muwal-amEccarAvAr . 
wamilYYakawwil 3-vawu aNiyE nampuvawu eVnwa viwawwilum palanYalYikkAwu . 
3-vawu aNikku makkalY vAyppu alYiwwanYar .

jeVyalaliwA poVy piracAram ceVywu varukirYAr . 
mawurEyil wamilYYanYnYEkku rU. 100 kotiyil cilE amEkkappatum eVnYrYu kUrYinYAr .

ceVnYnYE , 
wi.mu.ka.vinY veVrYrYi vAyppu pirakAcamAka irukkirYawu eVnYrYu vAkkalYiwwapinY karuNAniwi kUrYinYAr . 
karuNAniwi vAkkalYiwwAr 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi nerYrYu kAlE 7.15 maNikku kopAlapurawwil ulYlYa cArawA natunilEppalYlYiyil amEkkappattu irunwa vAkkuccAvatiyil vAkkalYippawarYkAka vanwAr . 
valYYakkawwE vita cIkkiramAkave vAkkalYippawarYkAka vanwa karuNAniwiyE woVNtarkalY mukamalarcciyutanY varaverYrYanYar . 
pinYnYar karuNAniwi wanYawu vAkkE pawivu ceVywAr . 
vAkkuccAvatiyE vittu veVlYiye vanwa karuNAniwi makilYYcci poVfka kANappattAr . 
niruparkalY avaritam , ‘ petti veNtum eVnYrYu kettapowu , 
avar ciriwwapati , kelYufkalY coVlkirYenY ’ eVnYrYu kUrYiyapati niruparkalY kUtiyirunwa pakuwikku vanwAr . 
pirakAcamAka ulYlYawu .

awu oralYavu wavirkkap pattirukkirYawu . 
wavirkkappattawotu vituvArkalYA ? 
waNtanYE warukinYrYa alYavukku werwal ANEyam natavatikkE eVtukkumA eVnYrYa Avalotu wamilYYnAtu eVwirpArkkirYawu . 
veVrYrYi vAyppu kelYvi : 
wi.mu.ka. eVwwanYE woVkuwikalYil veVrYrYi peVrYum eVnYrYu ninYEkkirYIrkalY ? 
pawil : 
wevEyAnYa alYavukku . 
ivvArYu avar pawil alYiwwAr . miyAnYmaril cakwivAynwa nilanatukkam - 
miyAnYmar nAttil cakwivAynwa nilanatukkam erYpattawu . 
riktar alYavukolil 7.4Aka pawivAnYa inwa nilanatukkam inwiyAvinY willi , kolkattA ulYlYitta palverYu pakuwikalYilum uNarappattawAkavum wakavalkalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . 
eVnYinYum nilanatukkawwAl erYpatta pAwippukalY kurYiwwa utanYati wakavalkalY ewum veVlYiyAkavillE . ceVnYnYE , 
vAkkAlYarkalYE kavarum puwiya piracAramAka jeVyalaliwAvinY peccE oVliparappi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar veVrYrYivel ottu kettu varukirYAr . 
melum peVrampUr woVkuwiyinY valYarccikku pAtupatuvenY eVnYrYu makkalYitam kUrYukirYAr . 
piracAra viyUkam 
peVrampUr woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarAka , anwa katciyinY vataceVnYnYE , vatakku mAvatta ceVyalAlYar pi.veVrYrYivel pottiyitukirYAr . 
avar piracArawwil puwumEyAka , anYEwwu warappu makkalYE kavarum vakEyil puwiya piracAra viyUkawwE katEpitiwwu varukirYAr . 
awAvawu muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY cattacapE peccukalY , makkalY nalawwittafkalY kurYiwwa arYivippukalY , a.wi.mu.ka.vinY werwal arYikkEyE veVlYiyittu peciya peccukalY ponYrYavarYrYE oVliparappi makkalYitam ottuvettE natawwi varukirYAr . 
nottIcu peVrampUr woVkuwikku utpatta pakuwiyil wIvira piracArawwil ItupattulYlYa vetpAlYar veVrYrYivel , wanYnYutanY muwal-amEccar peccE oVliparappum vacawiyutanY kUtiya vAkanYawwE utanY koVNtu ceVlkirYAr . 
avar makkalYitam ottu ketkum powu , jeVyalaliwAvinY peccum oVlikkirYawu . 
eVnYave poVwumakkalYum awanYE ArvawwutanY ketkinYrYanYar . 
kurYippAka vItukalYukkulY irukkum peVNkalYum , jeVyalaliwA oVlinAtA peccE ketka mika ArvamAka veVlYiye vanwu nirYkinYrYanYar . 
melum veVrYrYivel jeVyalaliwAvinY cAwanYE wittafkalY atafkiya wuNtu piracAra nottIcEyum valYYafki varukirYAr . 
pasnilEyam 
peVrampUr woVkuwikkutpatta kaNecapuram , pAlacuppiramaNiyapuram , pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. kutiyiruppu ponYrYavarYrYil veVrYrYivel piracAram ceVyyumpowu , erAlYamAnYa peVNkalYum a.wi.mu.ka. koVtiyutanY UrvalamAka vanwanYar . 
piracArawwinY powu veVrYrYivel kUrYiyawAvawu : 
jeVyalaliwA arYiviwwulYlYa anYEwwu wittafkalYEyum peVrampUr woVkuwi makkalYukku ceVyalpatuwwuvenY . 
ifkulYlYa pakkifkAm ulYpata anYEwwu kAlvAykalYEyum wUrvAri cIramEkka natavatikkE eVtuppenY . 
iwanY mUlam inwa pakuwiyil koVcuwwoVllE irukkAwu . 
300 ekkaril ulYlYa kuppE kitafkAl piraccinYE ulYlYawu . 
inwa kuppE kitafkE navInYappatuwwuvenY . 
vataceVnYnYE pakuwikku eVnYrYu wanYiyAka peVrampUril purYanakar pas nilEyam koVNtu vara pAtuvenY . 
kirYiswuva makkalYukku mayAnYa vacawi illE . 
eVnYave ifku puwiya mayAnYam amEkkappatum . 
peVrampUr woVkuwikku eVnYnYE arppaNiwwu pAtupatuvenY . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . Aciya skuvAR cAmpiyanYRip : 
jappAnYitam vIlYYnwawu inwiya aNi . 
Aciya skuvAR cAmpiyanYRip pottiyil inwiya Atavar aNi jappAnYitamum , makalYir aNi maleciyAvitamum vIlYYnwawu . 
munYnYawAka , Atavar pirivinY muwal Attawwil jappAnYinY riyoceVy koVpAyARiyE eVwirkoVNta inwiyAvinY kuR kumAr 6-11 , 11-13 , 9-11 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYnwAr . 
marYrYoVru Attawwil inwiyAvinY harInwar pAl canwu , jappAnYinY yunYosuke cukiyUvitam 11-5 , 8-11 , 10-12 , 7-11 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYnwAr . 
mUnYrYAvawu Attawwil jappAnYinY tEki kEtovE 9-11 , 11-4 , 11-6 , 11-6 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYwwinYAr inwiyAvinY velavanY ceVnwil kumAr . 
iwEw woVtarnwu , makkAvukku eVwirAnYa Attawwil , muwalil kalYam kaNtAr harInwar pAl canwu . 
makkAvinY stIvanY liyu cunYmAnYE eVwirkoVNta avar , 11-7 , 11-4 , 11-6 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil veVrYrYi peVrYrYAr . 
atuwwa Attawwil inwiyAvinY kuR kumAr , makkAvinY vAnY keVf heVyyE 11-3 , 11-1 , 11-2 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYwwinYAr . 
mUnYrYAvawu Attawwil , manYuvel cAnY kAsmanY ti oVliviyarAvE , 11-6 , 11-4 , 11-4 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYwwinYAr inwiyAvinY vijaykumAr mInYA . 
makalYir : 
iwanYitEye , maleciyAvE eVwirkoVNta makalYir pirivinY muwal Attawwil kalYamirYafkiya akafkRA calunYke , civacafkari cupramanYiyawwitam 11-13 , 4-11 , 8-11 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYnwAr . 
iraNtAvawu Attawwil reccal arnYAltE eVwirkoVNta inwiyAvinY wIpikA palikkal , 2-11 , 11-3 , 11-4 , 11-3 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil veVrYrYi peVrYrYAr . 
mUnYrYAvawu Attawwil , teVliyA arnYAltitam 11-7 , 7-11 , 9-11 , 11-5 , 9-11 eVnYrYa ceVt kaNakkil vIlYYnwAr inwiyAvinY joRnYA cinYnYappA . ciwwanYnYavAcalil kuvinwa curYrYulA payaNikalY . 
puwukkottE mAvattawwil ulYlYa curYrYulA mEyamAnYa ciwwanYnYavAcalil FAyirYrYukkilYYamE ulaka curYrYulA winYawwEyoVtti , curYrYulA payaNikalYinY varukE awikamAka irunwawu . 
wirucciyilirunwu 60 ki.mI , puwukkottEyilirunwu 12 ki.mI. woVlEvilum ulYlYawu ciwwanYnYavAcal . 
cumAr 16 ekkar parappalYavil amEnwulYlYa ciwwanYnYavAcal curYrYulA walawwil cirYuvarkalY vilYEyAti makilYYum vakEyil vilYEyAttu upakaraNafkalY , pacumEyAnYa pulwarEkalY , nIrUrYrYukalY , pataku kulYYAm eVnYa curYrYulA payaNikalYE kavarum vakEyil inwa curYrYulA mEyawwE mAvatta Uraka valYarcciwwurYEyinYar parAmariwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
nUlYYEvu kattaNam rU. 10-m , miwippataku kattaNam 10-m , wutuppu pataku 20-m , ceVyarYkE nIrUrYrYukalYE kaNtukalYikka napar oVnYrYukku rU. 50-m kattaNamAka vacUlikkappatukirYawu . 
awotu , ifkulYlYa kukE koyilAnYa camaNar patukkEkalY , palYYafkAla wamilYY pirAmi kalveVttu , oviyafkalY ( patakAtciyakam ) ulYlYittavEkalYE mawwiya aracinY weVlliyal wurYEyinYarum parAmariwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
camaNar patukkE , wamilYYpirAmi kalveVttu , oviyafkalYE kANpawarYku , 2 nulYYEvu vAyilukkum rU. 10 vacUlikkappattu varukirYawu . 
innilEyil , inwa ANtu ulaka curYrYulA winYam FAyirYrYukkilYYamE ( ceVp . 27 ) koVNtAtappattawEyoVtti , anYrYu oVrunAlY mattum curYrYulA payaNikalY ilavacamAka anYumawikkappattanYar . 
palYlYi vitumurYE nAlYkalY , kotE vitumurYE , vinAyakar cawurwwi , Ati 18 , weVlufkuvarutappirYappu , AfkilavarutappirYappu , wIpAvalYi , kirYiswumas , pakrIw ponYrYa vilYYAk kAlafkalYil ciwwanYnYavAcal curYrYulA walawwukku payaNikalYinY varukE awikamAka irukkum . 
katanwa ANtEk kAttilum inwa ANtu curYrYulA payaNikalYinY varukE awikariwwulYlYawu . keralYawwil pAjaka oritawwil kUta veVrYrYi peVrYAwu - 
keralYa cattapperavEw werwalil pAjaka oritawwil kUta veVrYrYi peVrYAwu eVnYrYu anwa mAnilawwinY muwalvarum , kAfkiras katciyinY mUwwa walEvarumAnYa ummanY cANti weVriviwwAr . 
keralYa cattapperavEyil ulYlYa 140 woVkuwikalYukku varum 16Am wewi oVre kattamAka werwal natEpeVrYavulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAnYa werwal piracAram canYikkilYYamE mAlEyutanY nirYEvatEnwawu . 
iwEyoVtti , kottayawwil ummanY cANti ceVywiyAlYarkalYitam canYikkilYYamE kUrYiyawAvawu : 
keralYaw werwalEyoVtti piracArawwukku vanwa pirawamar narenwira moti , mAnilawwil palYYafkutiyinYar pakuwikalYil nikalYYum irYappu vikiwam kurYiwwu pecumpowu comAliyAvutanY keralYawwE oVppittAr . 
iwanYmUlam , keralYawwE avar avamawiwwu vittAr . 
iwarYku werwalinYpowu pirawamar motikku keralYa makkalY wakunwa pawilati koVtuppArkalY . 
keralYa werwalil oritawwil kUta pAjaka veVrYrYi peVrYAwu . 
pAjakavinY piriwwAlYum araciyalE keralYa makkalY oVrupowum erYka mAttArkalY . 
iwepol , mArkcist kamyUnYist katciyinY kurYrYaviyal araciyalukku eVwirAkavum werwalil makkalY wafkalYawu vAkkukalYEp pawivu ceVyvArkalY . 
keralYa werwalil veVrYrYi peVrYuvom eVnYrYa nampikkE kAfkiras walEmEyilAnYa Ekkiya janYanAyaka munYnYaNikku ulYlYawu . 
munwEya werwalkalYil kitEwwa itafkalYEk kAttilum inwaw werwalil Ekkiya janYanAyaka munYnYaNikku awika itafkalY kitEkkum eVnYrYAr ummanY cANti . 
eVrNAkulYam mAvattam , peVrumpAvUril 30 vayawAnYa waliw peVN pAliyal palAwkAram ceVyyappattu koVlE ceVyyappatta campavawwil kurYrYavAlYikalY kEwu ceVyyappatuvawil wAmawam erYpattiruppawu kurYiwwu cANtiyitam ketkappattawu . 
awarYku avar pawilalYikkEyil , quot ; 
vicAraNE cariyAnYa wicEyil ceVnYrYu koVNtirukkirYawu ; 
virEvil kurYrYavAlYikalY kEwu ceVyyappatuvArkalY ' eVnYrYAr . wiruppUr - kaNteVynYar paNam vivakAram : 
vEko canwekam 
wi inwu 
wiruppUril kaNteVynYaril pitipatta rU. 570 koti woVkEyAnYawu araciyal pera paNamAka irukkalAm eVnYa mawimuka poVwucceVyalAlYar vEko canwekam eVlYYuppiyulYlYAr . 
iwu woVtarpAka inYrYu avar veVlYiyitta arYikkEyil , 
' ' wiruppUr mAvattawwil pitipatta , avarkalY kaNakkup pati rU. 570 koti kurYiwwa mikak katumEyAnYa UlYYalil wanYnYEk kAppArYrYikkoVlYlYa veNtum eVnYpawarYkAka mawwiyil AlYum narenwira moti aracutanY , muwalvar jeVyalaliwA palverYu vakEkalYil muyanYrYu araciyal peram pecukirYAr eVnYpawu mika nampakamAkaw weVriya vanwulYlYawu . 
mawwiya aracu inwa mocatikkuw wuNE ponYAl , uNmE vicuvarUpam eVtuwwu veVlYiye varum . 
eVnYave , inYnYum afke nirYuwwappattirukkum kaNteVynYarkalYil irukkum paNawwE eVNNumpowu , nermEyAnYa awikArikalYEk koVNtu anYEwwuk katci pirawiniwikalY munYnYilEyil wAnY paNam eVVMappata veNtum . 
aNNA wimuka UlYYal ampalawwukku vanwuvittawAl , wimuka UlYYal piraccinYEyil wappivittawAka eVvarum eVVMa veNtAm . 
oVru ilatcawwu eVlYYupawwu Ayiram koti 2ji speVktram UlYYalil mattuminYrYi , kirAnYEt koVlYlYE , ArYrYu maNal koVlYlYE , wAwu maNal koVlYlYEyilum wimuka karYpanYE ceVyya mutiyAwa kotikalY UlYYalil koVlYlYEyatiwwawE wamilYYaka makkalY eVnYrYum marYakka mAttArkalY . 
wimukavinYarum , aNNA wimukavinYarum potti pottuk koVNtu wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum 234 woVkuwikalYilum vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam koVtuwwuvittArkalY . 
awarYku cariyAnYa uwAraNamwAnY aravakkurYicci woVkuwi . 
katanwa 14-m wewi mAlE muwal inYrYu kAlE varE paNam koVtukkappattawu . 
oVppukkAka cila itafkalYil parYakkumpatE cowanYEyittapowu , kaNtupitikkappatta paNawwEw wavira , rAjeR lakkAnYi oVttumoVwwamAka paNam koVtuppawEw watukka eVnwa natavatikkEyum eVtukkavillE . 
uNmEyAnYa janYanAyakam veVllumA eVnYpawu me 19-m wewi wAnY weVriya varum . 
paNa veVlYlYawwE eVwirwwu wemuwika - makkalY nalak kUttaNi - wamilYY mAnilak kAfkiras iNEnwu amEwwa mArYrYu araciyal veVrYrYik kUttaNi janYanAyakawwEk kAwwu veVrYrYi peVrum eVnYa nampukirYenY ' ' eVnYrYu vEko weVriviwwulYlYAr . pirawamar moti eVnwa Uril pi.e. wervu eVlYYuwinYAr ? 
Am Awmi puwiya kelYvi 
puwuteVlli , me . 10 – 
pirawamar narenwira moti pi.e , marYrYum eVm.e , pattafkalYE peVrYrYawarYku AwAramAka nerYrYu pArawIya janYawA walEmE veVlYiyitta AvaNafkalYil avarawu tikiri cAnYrYiwalYYkalYil peVyar marYrYum ANtukalYil mArYrYam kANappatuvawE cuttik kAttiya Am Awmi katci eVnwa Uril moti pi.e. wervE eVlYYuwinYAr ? kelYvi eVlYYuppiyulYlYawu . 
pirawamar narenwira moti peVrYrYa kallUri pattafkalY parYrYi teVlli muwalvarum , Am Awmi katci walEvarumAnYa aravinw keVjrivAl , mawwiya wakaval ANEyawwitam kelYvi eVlYYuppi irunwAr . 
inwa carccEkku murYrYuppulYlYi vEkkum viwamAka motikku teVlli palkalEkkalYYakam alYiwwa pi.e. pattam marYrYum kujarAw palkalEkkalYYakam alYiwwa eVm.e. pattawwE teVlliyil nerYrYu natanwa pawwirikEyAlYar canwippinY powu pArawIya janYawA walEvar amiw RA , mawwiya niwi amEccar aruN jeVtli pakirafkamAka veVlYiyittanYar . 
kalvic cAnYrYiwalYYkalYinY nakalkalYEyum veVlYiyittanYar . 
AnYAl , inwa cAnYrYiwalYYkalY anYEwwum poliyAka uruvAkkappattavE eVnYa Am Awmi ceVywi woVtarpAlYar acuwoR kurYrYamcAttiyulYlYAr . 
iwuwoVtarpAka , teVlliyil niruparkalYEc canwiwwa avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
motiyinY pi.e . tikiri mawippeVN pattiyalil kalviyANtu 1977 eVnYa kurYippitappattulYlYawu . 
AnYAl , pattac cAnYrYiwalYYil patippE 1978-m ANtu patiwwu mutiwwawAka kAttukirYawu . 
avarawu eVm.e. tikiri pattac cAnYrYiwalYYil mANavar cerkkE eVN kurYippitappatavillE . 
iwu mikap peVriya muraNpAtAka ulYlYawu . 
1975-m ANtu camarppikkappatta kalvic cAnYrYiwalYYutanY kUtiya mawippeVN pattiyalil avarawu peVyar narenwira kumAr wAmowarawAs moti eVnYrYu kANappatukirYawu . 
1976-m ANtil narenwira wAmowarawAs moti eVnYrYum ulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAnYa awwAtci urYuwimoVlYYi pawwirawwE ( apitavit ) wAkkal ceVyyAmal oVru peVyarinY oVru pakuwiyE witIr nIkkam ceVyya mutiyAwu . 
nAttil avacaranilE cattam ( micA ) natEmurYEyil irunwa ( 1975-1977 ) kAlakattawwil walEmarYEvu vAlYYkkE vAlYYnwuvanwawAka moti erYkanYave palamurYE kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
1977-m ANtil pi.e. pattampeVrYrYawAka kUrYum avar , appowu eVnwa Uril ulYlYa wervu mEyawwil parItcE eVlYYuwinYAr ? eVnYpawE weVlYivuppatuwwa veNtum . 
motiyinY kalviwwakuwi woVtarpAka kelYvi eVlYYuppiya aravinw keVjrivAl nAttu makkalYitam manYnYippu ketka veNtum eVnYa kUrYuvawE vittuvittu , iwEpponYrYu mocatiyAka wayArikkappatta poli AvaNafkalYE veVlYiyittawarYkAka makkalYitam amiw RAvum , aruN jeVtliyumwAnY manYnYippu ketka veNtum . 
enYeVnYrYAl , amiw RA marYrYum motiyinY katanwakAlam eVnYnYa ? eVnYrYu inwa nAttukke weVriyum . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYiyulYlYAr . jeVyalaliwAvinY coVwwu mawippu rU. 118.58 koti . 
karuNAniwikku rU. 62.99 kotikku coVwwu ulYlYawAka vetpu manYuvil wakaval . 
ceVnYnYE : 
wamilYYakawwil cattamanYrYaw werwalukkAnYa vetpu manYu wAkkal woVtafki natEpeVrYrYu varukirYawu . 
iraNtAm nAlYAnYa inYrYu , Ar.ke.nakaril pottiyitum muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA , wiruvArUr woVkuwiyil pottiyitum wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi marYrYum mukkiya piramukarkalY wafkalY woVkuwikalYil vetpu manYukkalYE wAkkal ceVywanYar . 
vetpu manYukkalYutanY werwal viwimurYEp pati wafkalY coVwwu vivarafkalYEyum wAkkal ceVywanYar . 
anwa vakEyil , muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA wanYakku 118.58 koti rUpAy mawippilAnYa coVwwukkalY iruppawAka weVriviwwulYlYAr . 
iwil acEyum coVwwukkalY rU. 41.63 kotikkum , acEyA coVwwukkalY rU. 76.95 kotikkum iruppawAka kUrYiyulYlYa avar , wanYawu peVyaril rU. 2.04 kotikku vafkik katanY iruppawAkavum kurYippittulYlYAr . 
wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi wAkkal ceVywa vetpu manYuvil wanY peVyarilum , wanY manYEviyar peVyarilum moVwwam rU. 62.99 koti mawippilAnYa coVwwukkalY iruppawAka kurYippittulYlYAr . 
iwil , karuNAniwi , avarawu manYEviyarkalYAnYa wayAlYu , rAcAwwi Akiyor peVyarkalYil acEyum coVwwu rU. 58.77 kotikku iruppawAka weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . 
manYEviyar peVyarkalYil rU. 4.21 koti mawippil acEyA coVwwukkalY ulYlYanYa . 
karuNAniwi peVyaril acEyA coVwwukkalY eVwuvum illE . 
avar peVyaril kArkalY , nilafkalY , vafkik katanY eVwuvum illE . 
rAcAwwi peVyaril 11.94 koti rUpAy vafkik katanY ulYlYawAkavum weVrivikkappattulYlYawu . wiruvArUr woVkuwiyil karuNAniwi inYrYu muwal 2 nAlY piracAram . 
venY mUlam vIwi , vIwiyAka vAkku cekarippu . 
ceVnYnYE , 
ceVnYnYEyilirunwu reVyil mUlam wiruvArUr vanwulYlYa wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi inYrYum , nAlYEyum woVkuwiyil venY mUlam vIwi , vIwiyAka ceVnYrYu vAkku cekarikkirYAr . 
karuNAniwi piracAram . 
cattamanYrYa werwalil pottiyitum wi.mu.ka. marYrYum kUttaNi katci vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu , wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi ceVnYnYEyil katanwa mAwam ( epral ) 23-nwewi wanYawu piracArawwE woVtafkinYAr . 
woVtarnwu , 25-nwewi wiruvArUr ceVnYrYa avar , vetpumanYu wAkkal ceVywuvittu , afku natanwa poVwukkUttawwil pecinYAr . 
awanYpinYnYar , wamilYYakawwil palverYu nakarafkalYil piracArawwE merYkoVNta karuNAniwi , mINtum wanYawu coVnwa woVkuwiyAnYa wiruvArUril 2 nAtkalY piracAram merYkoVlYlYa irukkirYAr . 
reVyil mUlam payaNam . 
iwarYkAka avar , nerYrYu iravu 11.15 maNikku ceVnYnYE eVlYYumpUrilirunwu kampanY eVkspiras reVyil mUlam wiruvArUr payaNam merYkoVNtAr . 
inYrYu ( puwanYkilYYamE ) kAlE wiruvArUr vanwa karuNAniwi , inYrYum , nAlYEyum wiruvArUril vIwi , vIwiyAka venYil ceVnYrYu vAkku cekarikkirYAr . 
wiruvArUr woVkuwiyil ulYlYa vilYamalilirunwu mAlE 5 maNikku piracArawwE woVtafkum karuNAniwi , wevarkaNtanallUr ( mAlE 5.15 maNi ) , kulYikkarE ( 5.30 maNi ) , ammEyappanY ( 6 maNi ) , mukanwanYUr ( 6.30 maNi ) , eVNkaN ( iravu 7 maNi ) , kAppaNAmafkalam ( 7.30 maNi ) , aracavanYafkAtu ( 8 maNi ) , maNakkAl ( 8.30 maNi ) , wirukkaNamafkE ( 9 maNi ) , paviwwiramANikkam ( 9.30 maNi ) Akiya itafkalYil venY mUlam piracAram merYkoVlYkirYAr . 
12-nwewi ( nAlYE ) mAlE 5.30 maNikku pulivalawwilirunwu venY mUlam piracArawwE woVtafkum wi.mu.ka. walEvar karuNAniwi , woVtarnwu mAfkuti ( 6 maNi ) , kamalApuram ( 6.30 maNi ) , kaNkoVtuwwavaNiwam ( iravu 7 maNi ) , wirumawikunYnYam ( 7.30 maNi ) , wAlYYEkkuti ( 8 maNi ) , koVratAcceri ( 8.30 maNi ) , ceVllUr ( 9 maNi ) , ilEyUr ( 9.10 maNi ) Akiya itafkalYil piracAram ceVykirYAr . weVnYnYinwiya wirEppataw woVlYYilAlYarkalY cammelYanYam ; 
a.wi.mu.ka.vukku Awaravu . 
ceVnYnYE , a.wi.mu.ka. walEmEk kalYYakam cArpil nerYrYu veVlYiyitappattulYlYa ceVywik kurYippil kUrYappattulYlYawAvawu : 
wamilYYnAtu cattamanYrYap peravE poVwuwwerwal 16-5-2016 anYrYu natEpeVrYa ulYlYawE munYnYittu , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwuc ceVyalAlYarum , muwal-amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwAvE 10-5-2016 anYrYu ( nerYrYu ) weVnYnYinwiya wirEppataw woVlYYilAlYarkalY cammelYanYam ( peVpci ) marYrYum akila inwiya wirEppataw woVlYYilAlYarkalY cammelYanYawwinY walEvar ji.civA , ceVyalAlYar ke.Ar.ceVlvarAj , poVrulYAlYar eVs.Ar.canwiranY , wuNEw walEvarkalY ke.campaw , e.capari kiricanY , vi.rAmanY , ti.ke.mUrwwi , ke.ji.jIvAnYanwam , eVs.cunwar , iNEc ceVyalAlYarkalY Ar.wanYapAl , Ar.eVs.rAjA , eVnY.rAwA , pi.ramaNapApu Akiyor neril canwiwwu , a.wi.mu.ka.vukku , wamilYYnAtu cattamanYrYap peravE poVwuw werwalil , wafkalYutEya amEppukalYinY AwaravE weVriviwwanYar . 
awarYku , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwuc ceVyalAlYarum , muwal-amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA wamawu nanYrYiyinYE weVriviwwukkoVNtAr .

ilYEFarkalYAl mutiyum 
makkalY nala kUttaNiyAl mattume mawukkatEkalYE niranwaramAka mUta mutiyum .

mawuvilakkE amalpatuwwa wanYicattam

tAktar wamilYYicE veNtukolY . 
ceVnYnYE , iwu mArYrYawwinY kAlam , emArYrYawwinY kAlam alla eVnYrYum , mawwiyil UlYYalarYrYa nirvAkawwE warum pA.ja.ka.vukku Awaravu wara veNtum eVnYrYum tAktar wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanY veNtukolY vituwwulYlYAr . 
iwu kurYiwwu , pA.ja.ka. mAnila walEvar tAktar wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanY veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
karuwwu kaNippu karuwwu kaNippukalY ulA varukinYrYawu . 
marAttiyam , jammu kARmIr , ariyAnYA , teVlli , pIkAr mAnilafkalYil veVlYiyAnYa karuwwu kaNippukalY uNmE nilEyE kaNikkaw wavarYukirYawu eVnYpawE uNarwwiyirukkirYawu . 
AnYAl oVru tAktar eVnYrYa murYEyil iwwakEya wakavalkalY vAkkAlYarinY manYanilEyE mArYrYum vAyppum uNtu eVnYpawE arYivenY . 
veVrYrYi peVrYakkUtiya vetpAlYarukku vAkkalYikka veNtum eVnYrYa manYanilEyE peVrumpAlum vAkkAlYarkalY koVNtiruppawAl iwwakEya karuwwu kaNippukalY makkalYinY uNmEyAnYa kaNippukalYE AttamkANa vEkka vAyppirukkirYawu . 
woVNtarkalY corvatEya vAyppu . 
awumattumalla woVNtarkalYEyum corvatEyac ceVyya vAyppirukkirYawu . 
AnYAl , eVnYawu veNtukolY karuwwu kaNippukalYukku watE viwikka mutiyAwu . 
AnYAl , anwa kaNippukalY nam vekawwirYkum , veVrYrYikkum watE pota mutiyAwu eVnYpawE uNara veNtum .

awanYAlwAnY wirAvita katcikalY makkalYE emArYrYa Arampiwwu vittArkalY . 
katanwa 5 ANtukalYAka mika mocamAnYa nirvAkawwEp pArwwa inwa wamilYYnAtu inYrYu cila ilavacafkalYAl marYupatiyum wamilYYakawwE ilE vacamAkkappArkkirYawu . 
awe camayawwil wAnY eVwE eVllAm ceVywArkalYo inYimel ceVyyamAttom eVnYrYum vAyppu koVtukkum poweVllAm ceVyyAmal , inYimel vAyppu koVtufkalY ceVykirYom eVnYrYu coVllum wi.mu.ka. niccayam mArYrYAkAwu . 
karuwwu kaNippukalY eVllAm wirAvita katcikalYitam irunwu mArYrYame illE eVnYrYa rIwiyil veVlYiyitappattu koVNtiruppawu vewanYE . 
UlYYal or poVrutte illE . 
2 katcikalYum UlYYalil awika poVrulY cerwwawAl valYYakkil mAttik koVNtirukkirYa nilEyil , UlYYal or poVrutte illE eVnYrYa nilEyil karuwwu kaNippukalY kUrYuvawu makkalYinY karuwwirYkum , viruppawwirYkum eVwirAnYawAkave nAnY pArkkirYenY . 
eVppati ilavacafkalY makkalYinY elYYmEyE payanYpatuwwikkoVlYkirYawo ? 
awepol iwwakEya karuwwu , makkalYinY natunilEwwanYmEyE kulEwwu oVru pakkamAka mutiveVtukka vEkkum yukwiyAkave karuwappatukirYawu . 
kotikkaNakkAnYa vAkkAlYarkalYinY manYanilEyE weVrukkotiyil nirYkum oVnYrYiraNtu per nirNayikkirYArkalY eVnYrYAl awu nampawwakunwawalla . 
awanYAl woVNtarkalY nampikkEyutanY paNiyArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu paNivanYputanY kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
poVwumakkalYum iwwakEya karuwwu wiNippukalYAl kaNippukalY mArYrYAmal ufkalYukku UlYYalarYrYa nirvAkawwE erYkanYave iraNtANtukalYAka wanwu varum pA.ja.ka.vukku AwaravEw wara veNtum eVnYak kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
iwu mArYrYawwinY kAlam , emArYrYawwinY kAlamalla eVnYpawE makkalY wiraNteVlYYunwu wamilYYakawwil or mArYrYawwE koVNtuvara veNtum eVnYavum kettukkoVlYkirYenY .

a.wi.mu.ka. kavunYcilar

Aswireliya kirikkeVt aNiyinYarukku eVccarikkE meVlpornY : 
weVnY AppirikkA , AswireliyA , veVst iNtIs aNikalY itEyilAnYa oVru nAlY kirikkeVt potti woVtar veVst iNtIcil jUnY 3-nwewi muwal 26-nwewi varE natakkirYawu . 
kayAnYA , ceVyinYt kits , pArpatos Akiya itafkalYil inwa potti natakkirYawu . 
camIpawwil kayAnYAvil jikA vEras pAwippu iruppawu kaNtupitikkappattawu . 
iwanYAl veVst iNtIs ceVlla irukkum , Aswireliya kirikkeVt aNiyinYarukku , anwa nAttu kirikkeVt vAriya maruwwuva kulYYu eVccarikkE vituwwu irukkirYawu . 
jikA vEras uruvAka kAraNamAka vilYafkum koVcuvinY katiyilirunwu wappippawu ulYpata palverYu AlocanYEkalY vIrarkalYukku valYYafkappattu irukkirYawu . curYrYulA payaNikalYE kavarnwilYYukka kalYamirYafkukirYawu kARmIr mumpE , ceVnYrYa ANtu mattum 11 latcam curYrYulA payaNikalY kARmIrukku vanwu ceVnYrYulYlYanYar . 
avarYrYil 50 Ayiram per veVlYinAttu curYrYulA payaNikalYAvar .

katanwa ANtu ceVptampar mAwam erYpatta varalArYu kANAwa veVlYlYawwil kARmIrinY mukkiya curYrYulA mEyafkalY ciwEnwuvittanYa . 
innilEyil , mINtum kARmIril curYrYulA payaNikalYE kuviya vEkka ammAnila aracu 2015-E ' Visit Jammu and Kashmir Year ' ANtAka arYiviwwulYlYawu . 
kARmIrE pirapalappatuwwa pAlivut amEppukalYutanY peccuvArwwE natawwi varukirYawu . 
afku wirEppatafkalY marYrYum cinYnYawirEkalYukkAnYa patappitippukalYE natawwumArYum kettukkoVNtulYlYawu . 
iwarYkAka , cAlE vilYYippuNarvu nikalYYvukalY , wiruvilYYAkkalY , kaNkAtcikalY , kulYirkAla vilYEyAttu pottikalY , nIrnilE pottikalY , malEyerYuwal ponYrYa atveVnYcar nirYEnwa cAkacafkalYEyum natawwa ulYlYawu .

muwarYkattamAka inwa ANtu 10 cawavIwawwE ilakkAka koVNtu ceVyalpatukirYawu kARmIr curYrYulA amEccakam . wi.mu.ka.vinYar woVtarnwu poVy piracAram ceVykinYrYanYar :

jeVyalaliwA vilYakkam . 
ceVnYnYE ,

iwu woVtarpAka , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwal-amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA nerYrYu veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : 
poVy piracAram 
katanwa 5 ANtukalYil cattapperavE viwi 110-nY kIlYY nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVwuvume nirYEverYrYappatavillE eVnYa kurYrYaFcAtti karuNAniwiyum , wi.mu.ka.vinYarum poVy piracAram ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . 
17 wurYEkalYil veVlYiyitappatta arYivippukalYinY mIwu eVtukkappatta natavatikkEkalY kurYiwwu nAnY erYkanYave eVnYawu arYikkEkalYil weVriviwwirunwenY . 
warYpowu , melum 3 wurYEkalYil nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVvvArYu nirYEverYrYappattirukkinYrYanYa eVnYpawu parYrYiya vivarafkalYE nAnY alYikka virumpukirYenY . 
kEwwarYi , kEwwirYanY , wuNinUl marYrYum kawarwwurYE kEwwarYi , kEwwirYanY , wuNinUl marYrYum kawarwwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
kUtturYavu kEwwarYi neVcavAlYar cemippu marYrYum pAwukAppu wittawwinY kIlYY ceVluwwappatum mAnila aracinY pafkAnYa 4 cawavIwawwinYE , 8 cawavIwamAka uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
malpari natavu mAnYiyam uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
navInYa pulYYuvalYarppu walYavAtafkalY marYrYum paNNE upakaraNafkalYukkAnYa mAnYiyam uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
wiruvaNNAmalE , kAFcIpuram , wiruvalYlYUr , wiruneVlveli , katalUr , velUr , wirucceVfkotu , celam marYrYum mawurE pakuwikalYil ulYlYa neVcavAlYarkalYukku ½ kuwirE wirYanY koVNta mottAr poVruwwappatta 6 Ayiram peVtal warYikalY aracinY mAnYiyawwutanY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
pacumE vItukalY wittam EnwANtukalYukku mel paNipurinwu varum woVkuppUwiyam peVrYum paNiyAlYarkalYukku avarkalY paNipuriyum cafkafkalYinY vakEpAtukalYukkerYpa pawavi nilE nAnYkil ulYlYa kAlamurYE Uwiyam 1-1-2013 muwal valYYafkappatuvawarYkAnYa ANE veVlYiyitappattulYlYawu . 
cafkafkalYil ulYlYa 25 Ayiram kEwwarYi neVcavAlYarkalYukku minY mottAr poVruwwiya wAr curYrYum eVnwirafkalY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
muwal-amEccarinY pacumE vItukalY wittawwinY kIlYY 60 Ayiram vItukalYum , kUtuwalAka neVcavAlYarkalYu eVnYa 10 Ayiram vItukalYum kattum paNikalY mulYYumEyAka mutivatEnwulYlYanYa . 
paFcAyawwirYku oVru pattu vivacAyi - wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattulYlYawu . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nalawwurYE . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nalawwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
mAnila aracAl ceVyalpatuwwappatum mAnila post meVtrik kalvi uwaviwwoVkE wittam , vituwikalYil mANAkkar cerkkE , uyarkalvi cirYappu uwaviwwoVkE ponYrYa wittafkalYukku , peVrYrYor allawu pAwukAvalarinY ANtu varumAnYa varampu oVru latcam rUpAyilirunwu 2 latcam rUpAyAka uyarwwappattulYlYawu . 
mulYYunera munYEvar pattappatippE merYkoVlYlYum AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa mANava - mANaviyarkalYukku UkkawwoVkE 50 Ayiram rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu , 4 ANtukalYukku valYYafkum wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
vAtakE kattitafkalYil iyafki varum AwiwirAvita nala vituwikalY marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa nala vituwikalYukku , muwarYkattamAka 23 vituwikalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
melum , 31 vituwikalY kattum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu aracup paNiyAlYar wervANEyawwAl natawwap peVrYum woVkuwi - 1 , awAvawu , kurUp - 1 muwanYilEw wervil wercci peVrYum AwiwirAvita mANAkkarkalYukku , avarkalY muwanYmEw wervE cirYappAka eVwirkoVlYlYum vakEyil , cirYanwa kalvi nirYuvanYafkalYil payirYci peVrYa ewuvAka walA 50 Ayiram rUpAy valYYafka ANEyitappattu , iwuvarE 32 naparkalY payanY peVrYrYulYlYanYar . 
smArt kilYAs rUm . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar inYawwEc cArnwa pattayak kaNakkarkalY , ceVlavuk kaNakkarkalY , wercci peVrYrYa pinY , avarkalY cuyamAkaw woVlYYil woVtafkita walA 50 Ayiram rUpAy mAnYiyamAka valYYafka ANEkalY veVlYiyitappattulYlYanYa . 
2013-14-m ANtu muwal AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa nalawwurYEyinY kIlYY iyafkum 98 palYlYikalYil smArt kilYAs rUm arYimukappatuwwappattulYlYawu . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nala vituwikalY marYrYum uNti urYEvitappalYlYikalYil payilum 1,23,895 mANavarkalYukku 4.93 koti rUpAy ceVlavil urYEyutanY kUtiya walEyaNEkalY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nala vituwikalY marYrYum aracu palYYafkutiyinYa uNti urYEvitap palYlYikalYil payanYpAttil ulYlYa kulYYal vilYakku , minYvicirYi marYrYum waNNIrk kulYYAy AkiyavarYrYinYE parAmarippawarYkAka 2.47 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , parAmarippu paNikalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
velE vAyppu aluvalakawwil pawivu ceVywulYlYa , 16 mAvattafkalYEc cernwa 906 palYYafkutiyinYa pi.eVt. pattawArikalYukku avarkalY Aciriyar wakuwiw wervil wercci peVrYa valYYivakE ceVyyum vakEyil mAnilak kalviyiyal ArAycci nirYuvanYam mUlam payirYci alYippawarYkAnYa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattu varukirYawu . 
160 palYYafkutiyinYar uNti urYEvitap palYlYikalYukkum , 100 AwiwirAvitar nala palYlYikalYukkumAka moVwwam 260 palYlYikalYil 260 nIrAvi koVwikalanYkalY valYYafkuvawarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
curYrYuccUlYYal marYrYum vanYawwurYE curYrYuccUlYYal marYrYum vanYawwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : 
vanYa vilafkukalYAl erYpatum uyir , payir , utamEkalY cewafkalYukkAka valYYafkappatum ilYYappIttuw woVkE uyarwwi valYYafkappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
wekkumarafkalY valYarkkum wittawwinY kIlYY , 2011-12-m ANtu muwal 2014-15-m ANtu varE 14,335 heVkter parappalYavil wekku marawwottafkalY erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAttinY uyirppanYmEyEp pAwukAkkavum , peVrumalYavilAnYa pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinYE ceVyalpatuwwitavum , witta melANmE alaku aluvalakawwirYkAnYa puwiya kattitam nanYmafkalam kAppukAtu pakuwiyil rU. 6.90 koti ceVlavil kattappattulYlYawu . 
wamilYYnAtu vanYawwurYEyil vanYavar , vanYakkAppAlYar , vanYakkAvalar ponYrYa pawavikalYil nerati niyamanYawwirYkeVnYa erYpatum kAlip paNiyitafkalYE nirappita “ wamilYYnAtu vanYaccIrutEppaNiyAlYar wervu kulYYumam ” eVnYrYa amEppu erYpatuwwappattu anwa amEppinYAl paNiyAlYarkalY wervu paNi natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYawu . 
vanYawwottak kalYYakam . 
wamilYYnAtu vanYawwottak kalYYakawwinY paNikalY melum cirYakkum vakEyil , 4,500 heVkter parappalYavil , marakkUlYY wottafkalYum , 800 heVkter parappil uyar vilYEccal oVttu munwiri kanYrYukalYum natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu weyilE wottakkalYYakawwil paNipuriyum woVlYYilAlYarkalY payanYpeVrYum vaNNam , wevAlYA , pANtiyAr , kunYnYUr , ceranYkotu marYrYum natuvattam kottawwil cAlE vacawi , kutinIr vacawi , kutiyiruppu pakuwikalYE mempatuwwuwal ponYrYa paNikalY ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
mAnilawwil vanYa uyirinYafkalY awikamAka vAlYYum pakuwikalYE iNEwwu , puwiya vanYa uyirinYa caraNAlayafkalY erYpatuwwa mutivu ceVywu , awanYpati , warmapuri , kiruRNakiri mAvattafkalYil kAveri vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiruneVlveli mAvattawwil kafkEkoVNtAnY pulYlYimAnY caraNAlayamum , waFcAvUr marYrYum wiruvArUr mAvattafkalYil , kotiyakkarE vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiNtukkal , wenYi mAvattafkalYil , koVtEkkAnYal vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
marakkanYrYukalY natavu wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY , 1018 varuvAy kirAmafkalYil 1.82 koti marakkanYrYukalY natappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu , wanYiyAr nilafkalYil marafkalY valYarwwal ulYlYitta wittafkalYukku 109.6 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , pirYa paNikalYutanY 1,000 kirAmafkalYil 1.02 koti marakkanYrYukalY natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
ivvArYu jeVyalaliwA kUrYiyulYlYAr . moti lApawwirYku valYYi coVnYnYAl , jeVyalaliwA naRtawwirYku valYYi wetuvawu enY ? 
mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal kelYvi ceVnYnYE , ‘ ‘ uway ’’ wittawwE wamilYYakawwil enY nirYEverYrYavillE . 
moti aracu lApawwirYku valYYi coVnYnYAl , jeVyalaliwA aracu naRtawwirYku valYYi wetuvawu enY ? eVnYrYu mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal kUrYinYAr . 
piracAram ceVnYnYE cEwAppettE woVkuwiyil pottiyitum pA.janYawA katci vetpAlYar kAlYiwAcE Awariwwu mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal nerYrYu anwa woVkuwikkutpatta pakuwikalYil piracAram ceVywAr . 
munYnYawAka avar niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : 
katanwa 2 winYafkalYAka ceVnYnYEyinY palverYu pakuwikalYukku ceVnYrYenY . 
inYrYu ( nerYrYu ) kAlE Ar.ke.nakar pakuwikku ceVnYrYu vanwenY . 
mawwiya aracu eVppowum wamilYYnAttukku AwaravAka irukkum . 
oVre katciyinY Atci mawwiyilum , mAnilawwilum oVre katciyinY Atci amEya veNtum . 
appowu wAnY mawwiya aracAl eVnwa itEyUrYum inYrYi makkalYukku palverYu wittafkalYE ceVyalpatuwwa mutiyum . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . 
celam celawwil mAlEyil natEpeVrYrYa pA.janYawA poVwukkUttawwil mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureR pirapu kalanwu koVNtu pA.janYawA vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu piracAram ceVywAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : - mawwiyil katanwa 10 ANtukalYil Atci ceVywa kAfkiras - wi.mu.ka. nAttinY valYarccikkAnYa eVnwa wittafkalYEyum koVNtu varAmal pinYnYokki walYlYivittanYa . 
awanYAl peVriya mArYrYam veNtum eVnYrYu makkalY mutivu ceVywu 2014 pArAlYumanYrYa werwalil narenwira moti pirawamarAka veNtum eVnYrYu avarukkAka vAkkalYiwwArkalY . 
anwa muwal vAyppE makkalY ippowu anYupaviwwu varukinYrYanYar . 
ulaka alYavil pala nAtukalY valYarcci atEyAmal pinYnYokki ceVnYrYu koVNtirukkum inwa velYEyil , inwiyA mattum valYarcciyE nokki ceVlkirYawu . 
iwarYku pirawamar motiye kAraNam . 
mawwiya aracinY muwalItukalY wamilYYakawwirYku varaveNtum eVnYrYAl , mawwiya aracutanY oVwwupokirYa aracu wamilYYakawwil erYpata veNtum . 
ivvArYu mawwiya reVyilve manwiri cureR pirapu pecinYAr . wamilYYakawwil kUttaNi Atci amEvawu urYuwi wirumAvalYavanY peccu vAnYUr , wamilYYakawwil kUttaNi Atci amEvawu urYuwi eVnYrYu werwal piracArawwil woVl.wirumAvalYavanY kUrYinYAr . 
woVl.wirumAvalYavanY vilYYuppuram mAvattam vAnYUr cattamanYrYa woVkuwiyil makkalY nala kUttaNi cArpil vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katciyE cernwa wurE ravikkumAr pottiyitukirYAr . 
ivarE Awariwwu vituwalE cirYuwwEkalY katci walEvar woVl.wirumAvalYavanY wirYanwa venYil ninYrYapati nerYrYu piracAram ceVywAr . 
appowu avar peciyawAvawu : - valuvAnYa kUttaNi wi.mu.ka. , a.wi.mu.ka. iraNtu peVriya katcikalYE eVwirwwu muwanYmurYEyAka oVru valuvAnYa kUttaNiyE uruvAkkiyulYlYom . 
wamilYYakawwil wi.mu.ka , a.wi.mu.ka. Atcikku vanwAl mawukkatEkalYE mUtuvom eVnYkirYArkalY . 
avarkalYAl mutiyAwu . 
kAraNam 80 cawavIwa cArAya AlEkalY wi.mu.ka , a.wi.mu.ka. katciyinYaritam ulYlYawu . 
iwanYAl iraNtu katcikalYum makkalYE emArYrYum velEyil ItupatukirYawu . 
kUttaNi Atci wi.mu.ka , a.wi.mu.ka. wAfkalY koVlYlYEyatiwwa paNawwE kotikkaNakkil werwalil ceVlavu ceVykirYawu . 
kUttaNi Atci kitEyAwu eVnYrYu stAlinY kUrYiyulYlYAr . 
AnYAl we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar vijayakAnw , makkalY nala kUttaNi veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl kaNtippAka kUttaNi Atci amEppom eVnYkirYAr . 
wamilYYakawwil kUttaNi Atci amEvawu urYuwi . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . ceVnYnYE , vAkkAlYarkalYE kavarum puwiya piracAramAka jeVyalaliwAvinY peccE oVliparappi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYar veVrYrYivel ottu kettu varukirYAr . 
melum peVrampUr woVkuwiyinY valYarccikku pAtupatuvenY eVnYrYu makkalYitam kUrYukirYAr . 
piracAra viyUkam peVrampUr woVkuwi a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarAka , anwa katciyinY vataceVnYnYE , vatakku mAvatta ceVyalAlYar pi.veVrYrYivel pottiyitukirYAr . 
avar piracArawwil puwumEyAka , anYEwwu warappu makkalYE kavarum vakEyil puwiya piracAra viyUkawwE katEpitiwwu varukirYAr . 
awAvawu muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwAvinY cattacapE peccukalY , makkalY nalawwittafkalY kurYiwwa arYivippukalY , a.wi.mu.ka.vinY werwal arYikkEyE veVlYiyittu peciya peccukalY ponYrYavarYrYE oVliparappi makkalYitam ottuvettE natawwi varukirYAr . 
nottIcu peVrampUr woVkuwikku utpatta pakuwiyil wIvira piracArawwil ItupattulYlYa vetpAlYar veVrYrYivel , wanYnYutanY muwal-amEccar peccE oVliparappum vacawiyutanY kUtiya vAkanYawwE utanY koVNtu ceVlkirYAr . 
avar makkalYitam ottu ketkum powu , jeVyalaliwAvinY peccum oVlikkirYawu . 
eVnYave poVwumakkalYum awanYE ArvawwutanY ketkinYrYanYar . 
kurYippAka vItukalYukkulY irukkum peVNkalYum , jeVyalaliwA oVlinAtA peccE ketka mika ArvamAka veVlYiye vanwu nirYkinYrYanYar . 
melum veVrYrYivel jeVyalaliwAvinY cAwanYE wittafkalY atafkiya wuNtu piracAra nottIcEyum valYYafki varukirYAr . 
pasnilEyam peVrampUr woVkuwikku utpatta kaNecapuram , pAlacuppiramaNiyapuram , pi.eVs.eVnY.eVl. kutiyiruppu ponYrYavarYrYil veVrYrYivel piracAram ceVyyumpowu , erAlYamAnYa peVNkalYum a.wi.mu.ka. koVtiyutanY UrvalamAka vanwanYar . 
piracArawwinY powu veVrYrYivel kUrYiyawAvawu : - jeVyalaliwA arYiviwwulYlYa anYEwwu wittafkalYEyum peVrampUr woVkuwi makkalYukku ceVyalpatuwwuvenY . 
ifkulYlYa pakkifkAm ulYpata anYEwwu kAlvAykalYEyum wUr vAri cIramEkka natavatikkE eVtuppenY . 
iwanY mUlam inwa pakuwiyil koVcuwwoVllE irukkAwu . 
300 ekkaril ulYlYa kuppE kitafkAl piraccinYE ulYlYawu . 
inwa kuppE kitafkE navInYappatuwwuvenY . 
vataceVnYnYE pakuwikku eVnYrYu wanYiyAka peVrampUril purYanakar pas nilEyam koVNtu vara pAtuvenY . 
kirYiswuva makkalYukku mayAnYa vacawi illE . 
eVnYave ifku puwiya mayAnYam amEkkappatum . 
peVrampUr woVkuwikku eVnYnYE arppaNiwwu pAtupatuvenY . 
ivvArYu avar pecinYAr . elYYE makkalYinY pakkam iruppawu a.wi.mu.ka : werwal piracArawwil jeVyalaliwA peccu waFcE , wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalE munYnYittu a.wi.mu.ka. vetpAlYarkalYE Awariwwu muwal amEccar jeVyalaliwA waFcEyil werwal piracAra kUttawwil pecinYAr .

iwwAliyil akastA veVstleNt heVlikAptar oVppanwa pera UlYYalil woVtarputEyavarkalY waNtikkappattiruppawE cuttikkAttiya avar , iwepol inwiyAvil anwa UlYYalil woVtarputEyavarkalY niccayam waNtikkappatuvArkalY eVnYrYum , awecamayam appAvikalY waNtikkappata mAttArkalY eVnYrYum kUrYinYAr . anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum awimuka paNam viniyokam : ilYafkovanY kurYrYaccAttu - wi inwu wamilYYakawwinY anYEwwu woVkuwikalYilum awimuka paNam koVtuwwirukkirYArkalY eVnYrYu kAfkiras mAnilaw walEvar I.vi.ke.eVs. ilYafkovanY kurYrYamcAttinYAr .

paNam koVtuwwawu nirUpaNamAl , veVrYrYi peVrYrYAlum avarkalYE wolviyurYrYavarkalYAka arYivikka veNtum " eVnYrYu weVriviwwAr . jeVyalaliwA inYrYu waFcAvUril piraccAram ceVnYnYE , me 8 – muwalamEccar jeVyalaliwA inYrYu waFcAvUril piramANta werwal piraccAra kUttawwil pecukirYAr . 
jeVyalaliwAvE kANavum avarawu peccE ketkavum latcopalatcam makkalY wiraNtirukkirYArkalY .

waFcAvUril inYrYu 13–vawu nAlYAka werwal piraccAram ceVykirYAr . 
ceVnYnYEyil katanwa mAwam 9–nwewi anYrYu werwal piraccArawwE wuvakkiya jeVyalaliwA iwuvarE 12 nAtkalY piraccAram ceVywirukkirYAr .
