iwukurYiwwu , pA.ja.ka. mAnila walEvar tAktar wamilYYicE cavunwararAjanY veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : - karuwwu kaNippu karuwwu kaNippukalY ulA varukinYrYawu . 
marAttiyam , jammu kARmIr , ariyAnYA , teVlli , pIkAr mAnilafkalYil veVlYiyAnYa karuwwu kaNippukalY uNmE nilEyE kaNikkaw wavarYukirYawu eVnYpawE uNarwwiyirukkirYawu . 
AnYAl oVru tAktar eVnYrYa murYEyil iwwakEya wakavalkalY vAkkAlYarinY manYanilEyE mArYrYum vAyppum uNtu eVnYpawE arYivenY . 
veVrYrYi peVrYakkUtiya vetpAlYarukku vAkkalYikka veNtum eVnYrYa manYanilEyE peVrumpAlum vAkkAlYarkalY koVNtiruppawAl iwwakEya karuwwu kaNippukalY makkalYinY uNmEyAnYa kaNippukalYE AttamkANa vEkka vAyppirukkirYawu . 
woVNtarkalY corvatEya vAyppu awumattumalla woVNtarkalYEyum corvatEyac ceVyya vAyppirukkirYawu . 
AnYAl , eVnYawu veNtukolY karuwwu kaNippukalYukku watE viwikka mutiyAwu . 
AnYAl , anwa kaNippukalY nam vekawwirYkum , veVrYrYikkum watE pota mutiyAwu eVnYpawE uNara veNtum . 
mArYrYawwEw wamilYYakam eVwirnokka Arampiwwu vittawu . 
awanYAlwAnY wirAvita katcikalY makkalYE emArYrYa Arampiwwu vittArkalY . 
katanwa 5 ANtukalYAka mika mocamAnYa nirvAkawwEp pArwwa inwa wamilYYnAtu inYrYu cila ilavacafkalYAl marYupatiyum wamilYYakawwE ilE vacamAkkappArkkirYawu . 
awe camayawwil wAnY eVwE eVllAm ceVywArkalYo inYimel ceVyyamAttom eVnYrYum vAyppu koVtukkum poweVllAm ceVyyAmal , inYimel vAyppu koVtufkalY ceVykirYom eVnYrYu coVllum wi.mu.ka. niccayam mArYrYAkAwu . 
karuwwu kaNippukalY eVllAm wirAvita katcikalYitam irunwu mArYrYame illE eVnYrYa rIwiyil veVlYiyitappattu koVNtiruppawu vewanYE . 
UlYYal or poVrutte illE 2 katcikalYum UlYYalil awika poVrulY cerwwawAl valYYakkil mAttik koVNtirukkirYa nilEyil , UlYYal or poVrutte illE eVnYrYa nilEyil karuwwu kaNippukalY kUrYuvawu makkalYinY karuwwirYkum , viruppawwirYkum eVwirAnYawAkave nAnY pArkkirYenY . 
eVppati ilavacafkalY makkalYinY elYYmEyE payanYpatuwwikkoVlYkirYawo ? 
awepol iwwakEya karuwwu , makkalYinY natunilEwwanYmEyE kulEwwu oVru pakkamAka mutiveVtukka vEkkum yukwiyAkave karuwappatukirYawu . 
kotikkaNakkAnYa vAkkAlYarkalYinY manYanilEyE weVrukkotiyil nirYkum oVnYrYiraNtu per nirNayikkirYArkalY eVnYrYAl awu nampawwakunwawalla . 
awanYAl woVNtarkalY nampikkEyutanY paNiyArYrYa veNtum eVnYrYu paNivanYputanY kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
poVwumakkalYum iwwakEya karuwwu wiNippukalYAl kaNippukalY mArYrYAmal ufkalYukku UlYYalarYrYa nirvAkawwE erYkanYave iraNtANtukalYAka wanwu varum pA.ja.ka.vukku AwaravEw wara veNtum eVnYak kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
iwu mArYrYawwinY kAlam , emArYrYawwinY kAlamalla eVnYpawE makkalY wiraNteVlYYunwu wamilYYakawwil or mArYrYawwE koVNtuvara veNtum eVnYavum kettukkoVlYkirYenY . 
ivvArYu avar kUrYiyulYlYAr . wi.mu.ka vetpAlYar vIttil cowanYE ; a.wi.mu.ka kavunYcilar vIttil rU 40 latcam parYimuwal ceVnYnYE wamilYYaka cattacapE werwalukku inYnYum 5 nAtkalYe ulYlYanYa . 
iwEw woVtarnwu vAkkAlYarkalYukku paNam koVtukkum velEyE cila katcikalY woVtafki iruppawAka wakavalkalY veVlYiyAkiyulYlYanYa . 
vAkkAlYarkalYukku araciyal katcikalY paNam marYrYum paricu poVrutkalY koVtuppawE watukka wamilYYakam mulYYuvawum parYakkum patEkalY amEkkappattulYlYanYa . 
avarkalY iravu - pakalAka awirati cowanYE natawwi varukirYArkalY . 
iwuvarE AvaNam inYrYi eVtuwwu ceVllappatta cumAr rU. 90 koti varE parYimuwal ceVyyappattu ulYlYawu . 
a.wi.mu.ka. kavunYcilar inwa nilEyil matippAkkam , poVnYnYiyammanY kovil aruke vaciwwu varum 169-vawu vArtu mAnakarAtci kavunYcilar jeVyaccanwiranY vIttil kattu kattAka paNam pawukki vEkkappattu ulYlYawAka werwal parYakkum patE awikArikalYukku wakaval kitEwwawu . werwal awikAri ceVnwil vel walEmEyil awikArikalY nerYrYu iravu jeVyaccanwiranY vIttil awirati cowanYE natawwinYar . 
inwa cowanYE inYrYu awikAlE varE nItiwwawu . 
appowu kattukattAka rU. 40 latcawwu 38 Ayirawwu 148 roVkkam irunwawu . 
paNawwirYkAnYa AvaNam illE . 
iwEyatuwwu awanYE awikArikalY parYimuwal ceVywanYar .

iwu pol karUril ulYlYa aravakkurYicci wi.mu.ka vetpAlYar ke.ci.palYYanYicAmikku coVnwamAnYa karUril ulYlYa wafkumvituwiyil paNam pawukkiyulYlYawAka vanwa pukArinY peril , avarawu vItu marYrYum vituwikalYil varumAnYa variwwurYE marYrYum werwal parYakkumpatE awikArikalY cowanYE natawwukinYrYanYar . wi.mu.ka.vinYar woVtarnwu poVy piracAram ceVykinYrYanYar : melum 3 wurYEkalYil viwi eVN 110-nY kIlYY nirYEverYrYappatta wittafkalY eVnYnYa ? 
jeVyalaliwA vilYakkam ceVnYnYE , wi.mu.ka.vinYar woVtarnwu poVy piracAram ceVyvawAkavum , melum 3 wurYEkalYil viwi eVN 110-nY kIlYY nirYEverYrYappatta wittafkalY eVnYnYa ? 
eVnYpawu kurYiwwum muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA vilYakkam alYiwwulYlYAr . 
iwu woVtarpAka , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwal-amEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA nerYrYu veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : - poVy piracAram katanwa 5 ANtukalYil cattapperavE viwi 110-nY kIlYY nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVwuvume nirYEverYrYappatavillE eVnYa kurYrYaFcAtti karuNAniwiyum , wi.mu.ka.vinYarum poVy piracAram ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . 
17 wurYEkalYil veVlYiyitappatta arYivippukalYinY mIwu eVtukkappatta natavatikkEkalY kurYiwwu nAnY erYkanYave eVnYawu arYikkEkalYil weVriviwwirunwenY . 
warYpowu , melum 3 wurYEkalYil nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVvvArYu nirYEverYrYappattu irukkinYrYanYa eVnYpawu parYrYiya vivarafkalYE nAnY alYikka virumpukirYenY . 
kEwwarYi , kEwwirYanY , wuNinUl marYrYum kawarwwurYE kEwwarYi , kEwwirYanY , wuNinUl marYrYum kawarwwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : - kUtturYavu kEwwarYi neVcavAlYar cemippu marYrYum pAwukAppu wittawwinY kIlYY ceVluwwappatum mAnila aracinY pafkAnYa 4 cawavIwawwinYE , 8 cawavIwamAka uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
malpari natavu mAnYiyam uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
navInYa pulYYuvalYarppu walYavAtafkalY marYrYum paNNE upakaraNafkalYukkAnYa mAnYiyam uyarwwi valYYafkappattulYlYawu . 
wiruvaNNAmalE , kAFcIpuram , wiruvalYlYUr , wiruneVlveli , katalUr , velUr , wirucceVfkotu , celam marYrYum mawurE pakuwikalYil ulYlYa neVcavAlYarkalYukku ½ kuwirE wirYanY koVNta mottAr poVruwwappatta 6 Ayiram peVtal warYikalY aracinY mAnYiyawwutanY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
pacumE vItukalY wittam EnwANtukalYukku mel paNipurinwu varum woVkuppUwiyam peVrYum paNiyAlYarkalYukku avarkalY paNipuriyum cafkafkalYinY vakEpAtukalYukkerYpa pawavi nilE nAnYkil ulYlYa kAlamurYE Uwiyam 1-1-2013 muwal valYYafkappatuvawarYkAnYa ANE veVlYiyitappattulYlYawu . 
cafkafkalYil ulYlYa 25 Ayiram kEwwarYi neVcavAlYarkalYukku minY mottAr poVruwwiya wAr curYrYum eVnwirafkalY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
muwal-amEccarinY pacumE vItukalY wittawwinY kIlYY 60 Ayiram vItukalYum , kUtuwalAka neVcavAlYarkalYukkeVnYa 10 Ayiram vItukalYum kattum paNikalY mulYYumEyAka mutivatEnwulYlYanYa . 
paFcAyawwirYku oVru pattu vivacAyi - wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattulYlYawu . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nalawwurYE AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nalawwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : - mAnila aracAl ceVyalpatuwwappatum mAnila post meVtrik kalvi uwaviwwoVkE wittam , vituwikalYil mANAkkar cerkkE , uyarkalvi cirYappu uwaviwwoVkE ponYrYa wittafkalYukku , peVrYrYor allawu pAwukAvalarinY ANtu varumAnYa varampu oVru latcam rUpAyilirunwu 2 latcam rUpAyAka uyarwwappattulYlYawu . 
mulYYunera munYEvar pattappatippE merYkoVlYlYum AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa mANava - mANaviyarkalYukku UkkawwoVkE 50 Ayiram rUpAyAka uyarwwappattu , 4 ANtukalYukku valYYafkum wittam ceVyalpatuwwappattu varukirYawu . 
vAtakE kattitafkalYil iyafki varum AwiwirAvita nala vituwikalY marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa nala vituwikalYukku , muwarYkattamAka 23 vituwikalY katti mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
melum , 31 vituwikalY kattum paNikalY natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu aracup paNiyAlYar wervANEyawwAl natawwappeVrYum woVkuwi - 1 , awAvawu , kurUp - 1 muwanYilEw wervil wercci peVrYum AwiwirAvita mANAkkarkalYukku , avarkalY muwanYmEw wervE cirYappAka eVwirkoVlYlYum vakEyil , cirYanwa kalvi nirYuvanYafkalYil payirYci peVrYa ewuvAka walA 50 Ayiram rUpAy valYYafka ANEyitappattu , iwuvarE 32 naparkalY payanY peVrYrYulYlYanYar . 
smArt kilYAs rUm AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar inYawwEc cArnwa pattayak kaNakkarkalY , ceVlavuk kaNakkarkalY , wercci peVrYrYa pinY , avarkalY cuyamAkaw woVlYYil woVtafkita walA 50 Ayiram rUpAy mAnYiyamAka valYYafka ANEkalY veVlYiyitappattulYlYanYa . 
*2013-14-m ANtu muwal AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYa nalawwurYEyinY kIlYY iyafkum 98 palYlYikalYil smArt kilYAs rUm arYimukappatuwwappattulYlYawu . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nala vituwikalY marYrYum uNti urYEvitappalYlYikalYil payilum 1,23,895 mANavarkalYukku 4.93 koti rUpAy ceVlavil urYEyutanY kUtiya walEyaNEkalY valYYafkappattulYlYanYa . 
AwiwirAvitar marYrYum palYYafkutiyinYar nala vituwikalY marYrYum aracu palYYafkutiyinYa uNti urYEvitap palYlYikalYil payanYpAttil ulYlYa kulYYal vilYakku , minYvicirYi marYrYum waNNIrk kulYYAy AkiyavarYrYinYE parAmarippawarYkAka 2.47 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , parAmarippu paNikalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
velE vAyppu aluvalakawwil pawivu ceVywulYlYa , 16 mAvattafkalYEc cernwa 906 palYYafkutiyinYa pi.eVt. pattawArikalYukku avarkalY Aciriyar wakuwiw wervil wercci peVrYa valYYivakE ceVyyum vakEyil mAnilak kalviyiyal ArAycci nirYuvanYam mUlam payirYci alYippawarYkAnYa natavatikkE merYkoVlYlYappattu varukirYawu . 
160 palYYafkutiyinYar uNti urYEvitap palYlYikalYukkum , 100 AwiwirAvitar nala palYlYikalYukkum , AkamoVwwam 260 palYlYikalYil 260 nIrAvi koVwikalanYkalY valYYafkuvawarYkAnYa natavatikkEkalY merYkoVlYlYappattulYlYanYa . 
curYrYuccUlYYal marYrYum vanYawwurYE curYrYuccUlYYal marYrYum vanYawwurYEyil nirYEverYrYappatta paNikalY varumArYu : - vanYavilafkukalYAl erYpatum uyir , payir , utamEkalY cewafkalYukkAka valYYafkappatum ilYYappIttuw woVkE uyarwwi valYYafkappattu varukinYrYanYa . 
wekkumarafkalY valYarkkum wittawwinY kIlYY , *2011-12-m ANtu muwal *2014-15-m ANtu varE 14,335 heVkter parappalYavil wekku marawwottafkalY erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAttinY uyirppanYmEyEp pAwukAkkavum , peVrumalYavilAnYa pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinYE ceVyalpatuwwitavum , witta melANmE alaku aluvalakawwirYkAnYa puwiya kattitam nanYmafkalam kAppukAtu pakuwiyil rU. 6.90 koti ceVlavil kattappattulYlYawu . 
wamilYYnAtu vanYawwurYEyil vanYavar , vanYakkAppAlYar , vanYakkAvalar ponYrYa pawavikalYil nerati niyamanYawwirYkeVnYa erYpatum kAlip paNiyitafkalYE nirappita “ wamilYYnAtu vanYaccIrutEppaNiyAlYar wervu kulYYumam ” eVnYrYa amEppu erYpatuwwappattu anwa amEppinYAl paNiyAlYarkalY wervu paNi natEpeVrYrYu varukinYrYawu . 
vanYawwottak kalYYakam wamilYYnAtu vanYawwottak kalYYakawwinY paNikalY melum cirYakkum vakEyil , 4,500 heVkter parappalYavil , marakkUlYY wottafkalYum , 800 heVkter parappil uyar vilYEccal oVttu munwiri kanYrYukalYum natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu weyilE wottakkalYYakawwil paNipuriyum woVlYYilAlYarkalY payanYpeVrYum vaNNam , wevAlYA , pANtiyAr , kunYnYUr , ceranYkotu marYrYum natuvattam kottawwil cAlE vacawi , kutinIr vacawi , kutiyiruppu pakuwikalYE mempatuwwuwal ponYrYa paNikalY ceVywu mutikkappattulYlYanYa . 
mAnilawwil vanYa uyirinYafkalY awikamAka vAlYYum pakuwikalYE iNEwwu , puwiya vanYa uyirinYa caraNAlayafkalY erYpatuwwa mutivu ceVywu , awanYpati , warmapuri , kiruRNakiri mAvattafkalYil kAveri vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiruneVlveli mAvattawwil kafkEkoVNtAnY pulYlYimAnY caraNAlayamum , waFcAvUr marYrYum wiruvArUr mAvattafkalYil , kotiyakkarE vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum , wiNtukkal , wenYi mAvattafkalYil , koVtEkkAnYal vanYa uyirinYac caraNAlayamum erYpatuwwappattulYlYanYa . 
marakkanYrYukalY natavu wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY , 1018 varuvAy kirAmafkalYil 1.82 koti marakkanYrYukalY natappattulYlYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu marYrYum pacumEyAkkuwal wittawwinY kIlYY uyirppanYmE pAwukAppu , wanYiyAr nilafkalYil marafkalY valYarwwal ulYlYitta wittafkalYukku 109.6 koti rUpAy valYYafkappattu , pirYa paNikalYutanY 1,000 kirAmafkalYil 1.02 koti marakkanYrYukalY natavu ceVyyappattulYlYanYa . 
ivvArYu jeVyalaliwA kUrYiyulYlYAr . moti lApawwirYku valYYi coVnYnYAl , jeVyalaliwA naRtawwirYku valYYiwetuvawu enY ? 
mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal kelYvi ceVnYnYE , ‘ ‘ uway ’’ wittawwE wamilYYakawwil enY nirYEverYrYavillE . 
moti aracu lApawwirYku valYYi coVnYnYAl , jeVyalaliwA aracu naRtawwirYku valYYiwetuvawu enY ? 
eVnYrYu mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal kUrYinYAr . 
piracAram ceVnYnYE cEwAppettE woVkuwiyil pottiyitum pA.janYawA katci vetpAlYar kAlYiwAcE Awariwwu mawwiya minYwurYE manwiri piyUR koyal nerYrYu anwa woVkuwikku utpatta pakuwikalYil piracAram ceVywAr . 
munYnYawAka avar niruparkalYukku petti alYiwwAr . 
appowu avar kUrYiyawAvawu : - katanwa 2 winYafkalYAka ceVnYnYEyinY palverYu pakuwikalYukku ceVnYrYenY . 
inYrYu ( nerYrYu ) kAlE Ar.ke.nakar pakuwikku ceVnYrYu vanwenY . 
anwa woVkuwi muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwA eVm.eVl.e.vAka irukkum woVkuwi . 
afkirukkum makkalYukku kUta kutinIr vacawi kitEkkavillE . 
kalYYivu nIr vacawi illE . 
afkeye inwa nilEmE eVnYrYAl , wamilYYakawwinY palverYu pakuwikalYinY nilEmE eVppati irukkum eVnYpawanYE eVnYnYAl purinwu koVlYlYa mutikirYawu . 
wamilYYarkalYinY naRtam wamilYYaka minYvAriyawwirYku ANtukku rU. 14 Ayirawwu 200 koti naRtam erYpatukirYawu . 
inwa naRtawwE kurYEwwu ANtukku rU. 8 Ayiram koti lApam IttuvawarYku mawwiya aracinY uway wittawwE ceVyalpatuwwa coVlkirYom . 
AnYAl ifkulYlYa aracu awanYE erYka marYukkirYawu . 
wamilYYaka minYcAra vAriyawwinY naRtam , ifkulYlYa oVvvoVru wamilYYarkalYinY naRtam . 
nAnY werwalukkAka wamilYYaka aracu mIwu eVnwa kurYrYaccAttum vEkkavillE . 
katanwa ANte nAnY uway wittawwE ceVyalpatuwwa veNtum eVnYrYu valiyurYuwwinYenY . 
iwanYE wamilYYaka aracu enY erYrYukkoVlYlYavillE eVnYpawu puriyavillE . 
mawwiya moti aracu lApawwirYku valYYi coVnYnYAl , ifkulYlYa jeVyalaliwA naRtawwirYku valYYiweti koVNtu irukkirYAr . 
awu enY ? 
eVnYrYum eVnYakkum puriyavillE . 
ilavaca poVrutkalY mawwiya aracu 24 maNi neramum , wamilYYaka makkalYukku minYcAram koVtuppawarYkAnYa paNiyinYE merYkoVNtu varukirYawu . 
awe pol pA.janYawA vetpAlYarkalY veVrYrYi peVrYrYAl ufkalYukkAka 24 maNi neramum paNiyArYrYuvArkalY . 
ufkalYukku kitEwwa ilavaca mikci - kirENtar - minYvicirYiyAl eVnYnYa palanY kitEwwu vittawu coVllufkalY pArppom . 
ilavaca poVrutkalYAl oVru payanYum ufkalYukku illE . 
wamilYYaka makkalYukku nermEyAnYa vetpAlYarkalY wevE . 
UlYYalarYrYa pA.janYawA aracuwAnY wevE . 
cinwikkAwa - canwikkAwa... muwal-amEccar jeVyalaliwAvE oVru mawwiya manwiriyAnYa eVnYnYAl kUta canwikka mutiyAwa powu , cAwAraNa makkalY canwiwwu eVppati wafkalYawu kurYEkalYE coVlla mutiyum . 
nAnY ufkalYE ketkirYenY , pawwirikEyAlYarAnYa nIfkalY eVnYnYitam petti eVtuppawu pol , jeVyalaliwAvE canwiwwu petti eVtukka mutiyumA ? 
niccayam mutiyAwu . 
makkalYE parYrYi cinwikkAwa , canwikkAwa oVru walEvar namakku wevEyA ? 
eVnYrYu mutivu ceVyyum neram vanwu vittawu .

27 : kurYrYAlawwil inwa ANtu cIcanYil cumAr 30 latcam curYrYulA payaNikalY varukE wanwulYlYanYar . 
mulYYu alYavil irunwa cIcanY , curYrYulA payaNikalY mattumanYrYi , viyApArikalYEyum makilYYccik katalil AlYYwwiyulYlYawu . 
weVnYnYakawwinY *&quot ; spA ' eVnYrYalYYEkkappatum kurYrYAlawwil ANtuworYum jUnY muwal Akast varE cIcanY nilavum . 
2 Ayirawwukkum merYpatta mUlikEkalYutanY kalanwurYavAti peraruviyil koVttum waNNIril AnYanwa kulYiyal potuvawarYku wamilYYakam mattumanYrYi pirYa mAnilafkalYilirunwum curYrYulA payaNikalY kuvivawu valYYakkam . 
cIcanY mUnYrYu mAwa kAlam eVnYrYAlum , jUlE 15 muwal Akast 15 varE mattume curYrYulA payaNikalYinY varukE awikamAka irukkum . 
katanwa nAnYku ANtukalYil murYEye 16 latcam , 18 latcam , 20 latcam , 23 latcam per varukE wanwulYlYa nilEyil , nikalYYANtil iwuvarE 30 latcam per vanwulYlYawAka aracuw warappil awikArikalY weVriviwwanYar . 
ippowum winYamum 5 Ayiram muwal 7 Ayiram curYrYulA payaNikalY kurYrYAlam aruvikalYukku vanwu ceVlkinYrYanYar . 
vitumurYE winYafkalYil inwa eVNNikkE iraNtu matafkAka uyarum . 
kurYrYAlawwil nikalYYANtilwAnY anYEwwu aruvikalYilum ceVlYYippAka waNNIr vilYYunwulYlYawu . 
ippowu ceVptampar irYuwi Akiyum kUta peraruvi , Enwaruvi , cirYrYaruvi , palYYEya kurYrYAlam , puliyaruvi ulYlYitta anYEwwu aruvikalYilum waNNIr nanYrYAka vilYYukirYawu . 
cIcanYukkAka canniwi pajAril wArYkAlikamAka katE amEkkum viyApArikalY , Akast irYuwiyil katEkalYEk kAliceVywuvituvar . 
AnYAl , inwa ANtil curYrYulA payaNikalYinY varukE woVtarvawAl , wArYkAlika katEkalYum woVtarnwu ceVyalpattu varukinYrYanYa . 
inYnYum eVnYnYa wevE ? 
kurYrYAlawwil 3 mAwa kAlame cIcanY nItikkirYawu . 
awEw wavira , avvappowu peVyyum malYYE , cAral kAraNamAka wArYkAlikamAka cila nAlYkalYukku mattume aruvik kulYiyalukku vAyppu irukkirYawu . 
curYrYulA payaNikalYE nampi irukkum uNavu vituwikalY , wafkumvituwikalY , vAkanYacevE , cirYu vaNikarkalYukku cIcanY kAlafkalYil mattume varuvAy kitEkkum . 
eVnYave pirYa nakarafkalYil ulYlYawupol *&quot ; wIm pArkkukalYE ' uruvAkkavum , keralYa mAnila curYrYulA walafkalYil iruppawupol ciwwa , Ayurvewa mEyafkalYE nirYuvavum natavatikkE eVtukkalAm . 
cIcanY illAwa kAlafkalYilum , vitumurYE nAlYkalYilum malEyerYrYap payirYci mukAmkalYE natawwalAm . 
inwa nAlYkalYil palYlYi , kallUri mANavarkalYukku wafkumitam , pokkuvarawwu ponYrYavarYrYil cirYappu calukEkalY valYYafkuvawanY mUlam awikamAnYor ifku varuvawarYkAnYa vAyppE erYpatuwwalAm . 
pataku kulYYAmil wevEyAnYa alYavu waNNIrEw wekki ANtu mulYYuvawum pataku cavAri ceVyyavum , mInY kAtciyakawwE mempatuwwavum natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum . 
ippakuwiyilulYlYa aNEkalY marYrYum pirYa curYrYulA walafkalYE kaNtukalYikkumviwamAka *&quot ; carkular tUrE ' aracu erYpatuwwalAm . 
curYrYulA valYarcciyil wanYiyAr muwalItukalYE Ukkappatuwwa veNtum , weVnYkAcikku kUtuwal cirYappu rayilkalY , pas vacawikalY iwuwavira cAwwiyamAnYa curYrYulA wittafkalYE Alociwwu kurYrYAlawwE mulYYumEyAnYa curYrYulA walamAka mArYrYa mulYYu muyarYcikalYE merYkoVlYlYa veNtum eVnYpawu anYEwwu warappinYarinY eVwirpArppu . ceVnYnYEyil malYYE kurYEnwulYlYawAl makkalY nimmawi : mItpu paNikalY wIviram ceVnYnYE , ceVnYnYE nakarilum , curYrYu vattAra pakuwikalYilum nerYrYu munYwinYam itEvitAmal kanYamalYYE koVttiyawu . 
iravilum vitiya vitiya malYYE peVywawu . 
nerYrYum avvappowu malYYE peVywawu . 
iwanYAl ceVnYnYE mAnakarame veVlYlYakkAtAnYawu . 
iwanYAl ceVnYnYE marYrYum purYanakar pakuwiyil vacikkum makkalYinY iyalpu vAlYYkkE peVriwum pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu . 
eVfkeVfku kANinYum veVlYlYamatA eVnYrYu coVllum alYavukku eVfku pArwwAlum waNNIr cUlYYanwu iruppawAl vAkanYa pokkuvarawwu , minYcAra reVyil pokkuvarawwu pAwikkappattawu . 
minYcAram illE . 
awanYAl pokkuvarawwu wakaval woVtarpu eVllAm pAwikkappattu ulYlYawAl poVwu makkalYinY iyalpu vAlYYkkE mikavum pAwikkappattu ulYlYawu .

mItpu paNikku kappal vanwulYlYawu . 
wefkiyirukkum veVlYlYa nIrE veVlYiyerYrYum paNikalYilum makkalYE mItkum paNiyil mItpu patEyinYar ItupattulYlYanYar .

inwa vAkku kaNippukalY uNmEyAkum patcawwil vatakilYYakku mAnilafkalYil muwanYmuwalAka pA.ja.ka. veVrYrYiyE rucikkum nilE erYpatum . 
awu mattuminYrYi katanwa 15 ANtukalYAka acAmil Atci ceVywu varum kAfkiracE pA.ja.ka. virattum eVnYrYu vAkku kaNippukalY coVlkinYrYanYa . 
wamilYYnAtu wamilYYnAttil eVnwa kUttaNikku eVwwanYE itafkalY kitEkkum eVnYrYa werwalukku pinwEya karuwwu kaNippu vivaram varumArYu : - tEms nav ti.vi. a.wi.mu.ka . -139 wi.mu.ka. -78 marYrYavE - 17 niyUs eVks wi.mu.ka. -129-151 a.wi.mu.ka. -81-89 marYrYavE -2-6 eVnY.ti.ti.vi. wi.mu.ka. -132 a.wi.mu.ka. -95 inwiyA tute wi.mu.ka. -124-140 awi.mu.ka. -89-101 marYrYavE -4-11 e.pi.pi. wi.mu.ka. -135 a.wi.mu.ka. -95 marYrYavE -7 niyUs neRanY wi.mu.ka. -114-118 a.wi.mu.ka. -95-99 marYrYavE -27 ci ottar a.wi.mu.ka. - 139 wi.mu.ka. - 78 pA.janYawA - 0 marYrYavE - 17 pol Ap pols a.wi.mu.ka. - 110 wi.mu.ka. - 109 pA.janYawA - 0 marYrYavE - 15 puwucceri puwucceri mAnilawwil wi.mu.ka. - kAf. kUttaNi 15 muwal 21 itafkalYEyum , eVnY.Ar.kAfkiras 8 muwal 12 itafkalYEyum , a.wi.mu.ka. 1 muwal 4 itafkalYEyum kEpparYrYum eVnYa werwalukku pinwEya karuwwu kaNippukalY weVrivikkinYrYanYa . arjUnYA viruwukku riwu rANi , rakunAw parinwurE - wi inwu arjUnYA viruwukku inwiya makalYir hAkki aNiyinY keptanY riwu rANiyinY peVyar parinwurE ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
inwiya aNiyE cirYappAka valYYinatawwi varum riwu rANi , 36 ANtukalYukku pirYaku oVlimpik pottiyil vilYEyAta wakuwi peVrYac ceVywavar . 
cirYanwa vIrarkalYukkAnYa arjUnYA viruwukku inwiya Atavar hAkki aNi vIrarkalY rakunAw , waramvIr cif Akiyorawu peVyarkalY parinwurE ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
katanwa 2005-l pAkiswAnYukku eVwirAnYa pottiyinY mUlam arYimukamAnYa rakunAw 2007 aslAnY RA koppEpil veVNkala pawakkam , Aciya koppEkalYil 2007l wafkam , 2008l veVlYlYi , 2013l veVlYlYi pawakkafkalY veVlla mukkiya kAraNamAka vilYafkinYAr . 
2010 Aciya vilYEyAttu pottiyil veVNkalam , 2014l wafkam , kAmanYveVlw pottiyil 2014l veVlYlYi , aslAnY RA koppEyil 2014l veVNkala pawakkam peVrYrYawil waramvIrar cif mukkiya pafkArYrYinYAr . 
mejar wayAnY canw vAlYYnAlY cAwanYEyAlYar viruwukku munYnYAlY vIrar taf taf peVyar parinwurE ceVyyappattulYlYawu . 
katanwa 1980l mAskovil natEpeVrYrYa oVlimpikkil wafkam veVnYrYa inwiya aNiyil taf taf itam peVrYrYirunwAr . 
cirYanwa payirYciyAlYarukkAnYa wuronYAccAriyA viruwukku ci.Ar.kumAr parinwurEkkap pattulYlYAr . vAlpArYEkku veVlYinAttu curYrYulA payaNikalY varukE awikarippu wakaval mEyam amEkka korikkE vAlpArYE vAlpArYEkku veVlYinAttu curYrYulA payaNikalY varukE awikariwwulYlYawu . 
eVnYave vAlpArYEyil curYrYulA wakaval mEyam amEkka veNtum eVnYrYu korikkE eVlYYunwulYlYawu . 
veVlYinAttu curYrYulA payaNikalY vAlpArYE pakuwikku winYamum palverYu itafkalYilirunwu curYrYulA payaNikalY varukirYArkalY . 
avarkalY ifkulYlYa weyilE wottafkalY , kUlYYAfkal ArYu , nallamuti pUFcolE kAtcimunYE ulYpata palverYu curYrYulA walafkalYE kaNtu raciwwu ceVlkirYArkalY . 
inwa nilEyil camIpa kAlamAka veVlYinAttu curYrYulA payaNikalYinY varukE awikariwwulYlYawu . 
kurYippAka laNtanY , neVwarlAnwu , ameVrikkA , isrel , jeVrmanY , AswireliyA ponYrYa nAtukalYilirunwu curYrYulA payaNikalY vanwu ceVlkirYArkalY . 
AnYAl avarkalYukku curYrYulA cArnwa wakaval kitEppawu illE eVnYrYa pukAr eVlYYunwulYlYawu . 
curYrYulA wakaval mEyam amEkka veNtum iwanYitEye vAlpArYE pakuwikku isrel nAttilirunwu vanwirunwa curYrYulA payaNikalY ifkulYlYa iyarYkE alYYakE kaNtu raciwwanYar . 
iwu kurYiwwu avarkalY kUrYiyawAvawu : – nAfkalY eVfkalYitamulYlYa varEpatafkalYinY uwaviyutanY vAlpArYE pakuwikku vanwu ulYlYom . 
ifkulYlYa pakuwikalY anYEwwum iyarYkE alYYaku nirYEnwavE . 
AnYAl vAlpArYEkku vanwavutanY eVnwa itawwirYku eVppati ceVlla veNtum , wafkum vacawikalY eVfku kitEkkum marYrYum vAlpArYE pakuwiyinY cirYappu amcafkalY eVvE eVnYpawu kurYiwwa curYrYulA cArnwa wakavalkalY kitEppawillE . 
eVnYave vAlpArYE pakuwiyil curYrYulA wurYE cArpil curYrYulA wakaval mEyam amEkkappattAl veVlYinAtukalYilirunwu varum curYrYulA payaNikalYukku mikavum vacawiyAka irukkum . 
melum curYrYulA walafkalYukku alYYEwwucceVnYrYu kANpippawarYku valYYikAttikalYEyum erYpAtu ceVyyaveNtum ivvArYu avarkalY kUrYinYArkalY . 
curYrYulA valYarcci valYAkam iwu woVtarpAka poVwumakkalY kUrYum powu , vAlpArYE kurYiwwu wakaval arYinwu palverYu nAtukalYilirunwu erAlYamAnYa curYrYulA payaNikalY varukirYArkalY . 
veVlYinAtukalYilirunwu avarkalYukku ifku wakaval mEyam illAwawAl ciramappatukirYArkalY . 
eVnYave curYrYulA cArnwa wakaval mEyam marYrYum puwiya pasnilEyam aruke rU. 1 koti mawippil kattimutikkappattu pala ANtukalYAka wirYakkappatAwa nilEyil ulYlYa oVrufkiNEnwa curYrYulA valYarcci valYAkawwE wirYakka natavatikkE eVtukka veNtum eVnYrYu kUrYinYArkalY . nAnY hIro... karuNAniwi villanY... jeVyalaliwA villi... vijayakAnw petti puwuteVlli , eVnY.ti.ti.vi.kku alYiwwu ulYlYa pettiyil we.mu.wi.ka. walEvar vijayakAnw , nAnY hIro... karuNAniwi villanY... jeVyalaliwA villi... eVnYrYu kUrYiulYlYAr . 
vijayakAnw petti viparam : - kelYvi : - makkalY nalak kUttaNiyinY muwal-amEccar vetpAlYar... iwuvarE nIfkalY palverYu poVrYuppukalYE vakiwwirukkirYIrkalY . 
ippowu wAfkalY erYrYuk koVNtu ulYlYa inwa poVrYuppuwAnY mikap peVriyawu eVnYrYu karuwukirYIrkalY ? 
pawil : - nAnY hIro... karuNAniwi eVnYakku villanY . 
jeVyalaliwA eVnYakku villi . 
nAnY 93 vayawAnYa karuNAniwiyutanYum , 65 vayawu mawikkawwakka jeVyalaliwAvutanYum potti potukinYrYenY... eVnYnYutEya vayawu eVnYnYa eVnYrYu eVnYakke weVriyAwu... ufkalYukku weVriyume eVnYnYaveVnYrYu.. itEyil ceVywiyAlYar cAr... ufkalYukku 25 cAr... illE... illE.. nIfkalY 70 , 80 eVvvalYavu veNtumAnYAlum coVlli koVlYlYalAm . 
AnYAl eVnY manYawu eVppowu ilYamEyAnYawu ( eVnYnYutEyE iwayam ilYamEyAnYawu ) 
kelYvi : - werwalil wi.mu.ka.vum , a.wi.mu.ka.vum ufkalYutanY kUttaNi vEwwuk koVlYlYa virumpinYArkalY , AnYAl nIfkalY avarkalYutanY kUttaNi vEkkAwawu enY ? 
pawil : - muwalil nAnY awimukavutanY kUttaNiyil irunwenY . 
mUnYrYe mAwawwil anwak kUttaNiyilirunwu veVlYiyerYinYenY . 
( muwalil nAnY mattum veVrYrYi peVrYrYenY... pinYnYar 41 woVkuwiyil pottiyittu 29 woVkuwiyil veVrYrYi peVrYrYenY ) pAl vilE , pas kattaNa vilEyE awimuka aracu erYrYiyawu . 
appowuwAnY eVnYakku kopam vanwawu . 
AnYAlum avarkalY vilEyerYrYawwE vApas peVrYavillE . 
awarYku nAnY eVwirppu weVriviwwenY . 
kUttaNiyilirunwu vilakinYenY . 
appowuwAnY cafkaranY kovil itEwwerwal natEpeVrYrYawu... itEwwerwalil AlYumkatciwAnY veVrYrYi peVrYum eVnYpawu weVrinwawe . 
AnYAl peVnYnYAkaram itEw werwalil avarkalY ( a.wi.mu.ka ) teVppAcit ilYYanwArkalY... appowu wi.mu.ka. Atciyil irunwawu . 
ippowu , werwal vAkkurYuwiyil pAl vilEyE kurYEppawAka kUrYiulYlYArkalY... iwEwwAnY nAnY appowu valiyurYuwwinYenY . 
AnYAl mutiyAwu eVnYrYu kUrYinYArkalY... inYrYu kurYEppawAka kUrYukinYrYanYar . 
awarYku kAraNam eVnYnYaveVnYrYAl werwal payam... kelYvi : - jeVyalaliwA , karuNAniwiyE nerukkuner canwiwwAl ? 
pawil : - jeVyalaliwA eVnYnYEp pArwwAl mukawwE wiruppik koVlYvAr . 
nAnYum avvArYe ceVyvenY . 
( ceVywiyAlYar : nIfkalY karuNAniwiyE pArwwAl ) karuNAniwiyE pArwwAlum awewAnY cAr... nAnY erYkanYave eVm.ji.Ar.wAnY cAr... eVm.ji.Ar.rE pArwwAl poccu... karuNAniwiyitam pecinYAl poccu.. karuNAniwi pecanYum eVnYpAr . 
awanYAl wAnY iraNtu perEyum pArwwAl pecamAttenY... nAnYum eVnYnYutEya mukawwE wiruppi koVlYvenY . 
avaritam peca veNtiya cUlYYnilE vanwAl , avar ( karuNAniwi ) pecuvAr.. pecinYAl eVnYnYa cAr eVnYrYu ninYrYu mariyAwE koVtuppenY... awAnY avarinY araciyal nAkarikam . 
eVwEyum avarukku cAwakamAkki koVlYvAr . 
kelYvi : - makkalY nalakkUttaNiyil nIfkalY mattumwAnY palamAnYavarkalYAka weVrikirYIrkalY... eVppati Atci amEppIrkalY aracAfkawwE kattamEppIrkalY ? 
pawil : - aracAfkawwE amEppawarYku nalla eVNNafkalY irunwAle powum... jeVyalaliwAvirYku eVwuvum weVriyAwu... kalEFar kat - Ap , jeVyalaliwA kat , kat eVnYrYu nallA puriyum... avafkalYukku eVnYnYa eVnYnYa ceVyvArkalY... awikArikalY wittam vakuwwuw wara aracAfkam natawwukirYAr . 
eVnYave , aracAfkam amEkka munYanYupavam veNtum eVnYrYu kUrYuvaweVllAm oVru piwarYrYal . 
eVfkalY werwal arYikkE muwalil veVlYiye vanwawu... eVfkalYutEya werwal arYikkEyE wimuka marYrYum awimuka kAppiyatiwwuvittawu... payam kAraNamAka wAnY ilavacafkalYE alYlYi , alYlYi vitukirYArkalY . 
( eVwwanYE woVkuwi eVnYrYu ivar ketkirYAr ) werwalil eVwwanYE cIt veVrYrYi peVrYupom eVnYrYu wulliyamAka kaNiwwuc coVlla nAnY jowitanY alla . 
AnYAl niccayamAka eVfkalY kUttaNi veVrYrYi peVrYum . 
( 120 cIt ) 120 cIt eVnYrYAl awuvum veVrYrYiwAnYe.... kelYvi : - nIfkalY awikam kutippawAka kurYrYaccAttu eVlYYukirYawu... ufkalYukku kutipiraccanYE iruppawAka kurYrYam cAttappatukirYawu . 
pawil : - illEye . 
nAnYwAnY paricowanYE ceVywu pArppom eVnYrYu kUrYivittenYe .

awu palYYEya kurYrYaccAttu .

yArum varavillE .

ilYEFarkalYukku eVppati velE vAyppE uruvAkkuvIrkalY ? 
ippa vanwu... uwAraNawwirYku vItuworYum reRanY poVrutkalY neratiyAka viniyokikkappatum eVnYrYu kUrYiulYlYenY , iwanY mUlam velE vAyppu kitEkkum . 
melum nUrYu nAlY velEw wittam ulYlYawu , mawwiya aracu mAnYiyam valYYafkukirYawu , mAnila aracum ceVyyum awupoka kUtuwal varumAnYawwE peVrYa natavatikkE merYkoVlYvenY . 
300 allawu 500 rUpAyE nAnY vAfki koVtuppenY . 
kelYvi : - wamilYYakawwil jeVyalaliwA kAlil vilYYunwu vaNafkum palYYakkam kurYiwwu ufkalY karuwwu ? 
laFcam vAfki awikamAka ceVlavu ceVykirYArkalY... oVru woVkuwikku rU. 10 koti ceVlavu ceVyvArkalY eVnYrYu ninYEkkinYrYenY... oVru peVNNinY kAlil AN vilYYunwu vaNafkuvawu wamilYYnAttE walE nimirac ceVyyumA ? 
wamilYYnAtu walE nimira veNtumAnYAl , muwalil wamilYYaka amEccarkalY walE nimira veNtum . 
kAlil vilYYuvawE anwa ammA virumpukirYAr . 
awarYkAnYa kAraNam eVnYnYaveVnYrYu eVnYakku weVriyavillE . 
eVllorum kAlil vilYYunwu vaNafkaveNtum . 
iwuvarEyil anwa ammA eVwirppu weVriviwwawA ? 
ippowEya werwal piracArawwil pArufkalY . 
piracAra metEyil anwa ammA uyare amarnwuk koVNtu , vetpAlYarkalYE kIlYYe amara vEkkirYAr . 
AnYAl , nAnY eVnY vetpAlYarkalYE caricamamAka natawwukirYenY . 
eVllorEyum oVre lEnYil irukka vEyufkalY... anwa ammA leti , ANkalY veNtumeVnYrYAl carYrYu walYlYi utkArnwuk koVlYlYalAm... eVnYrYu kUrYiulYlYAr . cattap peravE viwi 110-nY kIlYY arYivippukalY mUnYrYu wurYEkalYil nirYEverYrYappatta wittafkalY jeVyalaliwA arYikkE ceVnYnYE , iwu woVtarpAka , a.wi.mu.ka. poVwucceVyalAlYarum , muwalamEccarumAnYa jeVyalaliwA veVlYiyittulYlYa arYikkEyil kUrYiyiruppawAvawu : - katanwa 5 ANtukalYil cattapperavE viwi 110-nY kIlYY nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVwuvume nirYEverYrYappatavillE eVnYa kurYrYaFcAtti wiru.karuNAniwiyum , wi.mu.ka.vinYarum poVy piraccAram ceVywu varukinYrYanYar . 
17 wurYEkalYil veVlYiyitappatta arYivippukalYinY mIwu eVtukkappatta natavatikkEkalYE kurYiwwu nAnY erYkeVnYave eVnYawu arYikkEkalYil weVriviwwirunwenY . 
warYpowu , melum mUnYrYu wurYEkalYil nAnY ceVywa arYivippukalY eVvvArYu nirYEverYrYappattirukkinYrYanYa eVnYpawu parYrYiya vivarafkalYE nAnY alYikka virumpukirYenY .
